Pauṣkarasaṃhitā 

atha saptaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ śrībhagavānuvāca 

evaṃ kṛtvā yathāśāstraṃ divyamabjaja vai purā ।
pitryaṃ tadanu vai kuryāt vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।।

pauṣkarauvāca

jñātum icchāmi bhagavān tvacchāsanasthitaiḥ ।
samuddiśya pitṛśrāddhaṃ kāryam ācāryapūrvakaiḥ ।।

keṣāṃ keṣāṃ ca tat kāryaṃ kasya kasya ca kīdṛśam ।
vidadhāti pañca pañcaiva samyaṅnirvartitaṃ hi yat ।।

śrī bhagavānuvāca 

kartavyatvena vai kuryāt karmasanyāsināṃ sadā ।
nirvāṇadīkṣitānāṃ ca bhaktānām api cābjaja ।।

anirdiṣṭakramāṇāṃ ca caturthāśramiṇāṃ tu vai ।
bhagavad padalipsūnāṃ jñānināṃ ca tathaiva hi ।।

prītaye manyasiddhānāṃ sādhakānāṃ tu pauṣkara ।
śubhajanmāptaye śaśvanmanyasāmukhyasiddhaye ।।

kāryaṃ tatputrakāṇāṃ tu kṛpayā deśikādikaiḥ ।
kuryād vai samayajñānāṃ nityaṃ saddharmavṛddhaye ।।

bhūyaḥ sujanmalābhāya sadvidhādhigamāya ca ।
bāndhavānāmāto anyeṣāṃ bhaktānām evam eva hi ।।

sadyo duṣkṛtaśāntyarthaṃ kṛpayā nityam ācaret ।
kartānā karmasaṃnyāsī parivṛddho vratāśrayī ।।

na nivāṇapadaṃnīto dīkṣāyāṃ bhogalālasa ।
tīvrabhāvaṃ vinā yastu na siddho manyasevanāt ।।

niḥ santāno api vai mantrī na yāti siddhigocaram ।
nūnam etat dvijaśreṣṭha sanmārgasyaiḥ kriyāparaiḥ ।।

satkartavyaprakāreṇa tvanugrāhayāḥ sadaiva hi ।
samāsādyātra saṃyāti yathā divyaṃ paraṃ padam ।।

ātastuḥ dīkṣitānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ sā mayājinām ।
avaktavyaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ etat nirvartanāya ca ।।

śrāddhakāle tu vai muktavā tair apyanyatra padmaja ।
mantramudrākriyā dhyānamajñānādikriyāṃ vinā ।।

nābhyastavyā na yoktavyā bhaktaiḥ sāmayikādibhiḥ ।
samāśritya nimittaṃ vai deśakālādiktaṃ dvija ।।

kriyate yat pitṝṇāṃ ca bhavatyanṛṇavān naraḥ ।
prayāti tṛptim atulāṃ tena karmavaśād api ।।

āgate gatim āyānti śrāddhād āhlādasaṃyutām ।
sakṛdvaikaṃ tu bahudhā kālamādehalakṣaṇam ।।

yuktaṃ tithigaṇena eva vātsarīyeṇa pauṣkāra ।
kṣetrāptipūrveṇānnena sannimittagaṇena tu ।।

saṃsāraduḥkhaśāntyarthaṃ duṣkṛtakṣapaṇāya ca ।
।।

vyakte ca indriyacakrasya duḥkhajaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ hi yat ।
save dyanantakalpaṃ ca karmātmā ye? yato abjajī ।।

ato bhūtamayaṃ dehaṃ samantaram asya vai ।
duḥkhopalambhanaṃ kalpaṃ yasmāt kamalasaṃbhava ।।

duḥkhena śāmyate duḥkha sanyaskandhagate yathā ।
skandhādgurutaraṃ bhāraṃ nṛṇāṃ duṣkṛtakāriṇām ।।

nidrakrāntasvapiṇḍāt vai yathā nirgatya pauṣkara ।
vāsanādeham āśritya nānāceṣṭāṃ karoti ca ।।

bhūtapiṇḍaṃ vinā tāsāṃ na śāntim anuvindati ।
evam annāśritaṃ pūrvaṃ prāṇam indriyasaṃgraham ।।

vyaktikṛtaṃ na vai deva dehabhāvena dehinām ।
tāvat karmakṣayaṃ teṣāṃ kathameti mahāmate ।।

antastad upacārārthaṃ jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā ।
saṃpādya yadvaśāt śīghram anantaṃ sukhamedhate ।।

sāmānyaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca gurvādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
sādhāraḥ saṃpradhānākhyaḥ sāṃprataṃ vidhiḥ ucyate ।।

nimantritaṃ vā saṃprāptaṃ nityam aṅgīkṛtaṃ tvatha ।
dvijendraṃ pañjakālajñaṃ ṣaṭkarmanirataṃ tu vā ।।

snānādinā purā kṛtvā prayataḥ saṃviśet punaḥ ।
svayam ardhyāmbunā vipra pavitrīkṛtya pāṇinā ।।

santāya kusumāstreṇa mantrāraścādhiṣṭhitena ca ।
samuddharan netramantraṃ mantrārthādhiṣṭhitena ca ।।

samuccaran netramantram avalokya atha kadviti ।
niveśya bhagavatyagre praṇavādhiṣṭhitāsane ।।

pūjite vitate pūte saṃmukhaṃ vottarānanam ।
udakdigkṣamāṇaṃ ca viniveśya tathā ca tat ।।

yathā mantreśadigraśmiprasareṇa abhividhyate ।
mantreṇa ārādhya taṃ dhyātvā brūyāt saṃyatā vāgbhava ।।

samādhāya jagannāthra hṛtpadmagaganer'kavat ।
saptātrasyātha pātrāṇāṃ pātrābhyāṃ vābjasaṃbhava ।।

evaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhānaṃ prāg yatnenātra karmaṇi ।
samuddiśya pitṝn dadyāt dānama ntaravedikam ।।

niveśitaṃ dvijendraṃ yad vṛttistham api mantrarāṭ ।
antarvedī tu sā jñeyā tvābhyām abhyantaraṃ hi tat ।।

saṃpradānaṃ pitṝṇāṃ yat kuryāt satpātrapiṇḍakam ।
tad divyam amalaṃ yasmāt caitanyam avalaṃbyate ।।

tatkālaṃ saṃvibhajyāśca tiṣṭhanti kamalodbhava ।
pradātṛsaṅkalpavaśāt dattaṃ puṣkarasaṃbhava ।।

ekasya vā bahūnāṃ vā pradadyād āsanopari ।
punarevāsanaṃ dābhamigranthi bahubhiḥ kuśaiḥ ।।

vibhoḥ yajñāṅgadehasya lomāni tu kuśāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
tā eva nāyaḥ sarvā tasya bhūtaśarīragāḥ ।।

raśmayo bhūtadehe tu cinmūrteḥ śaktayo akhilāḥ ।
ata eva hi viprendra pitṝṇāṃ tu kuśāsanam ।।

śrāddhakāle tu vihitam āhūtānāṃ tadūrdhvataḥ ।
yat kiṃcid dīyate bhaktayā brahmabhūtaṃ tu tadbhavet ।।

purā vai hetunānena nṛṇām aviditātmanām ।
karmavyatra kuśājālaṃ vihitaṃ kamalodbhava ।।

yeṣāṃ sarvagataṃ brahman mantrarūpīśvaro acyutaḥ ।
bhāvasthatatvatastābhisteṣāṃ vai na prayojanam ।।

athāścaparijaptena bhūtināvātmaśaṅkunā ।
masṛṇenāśmacūrṇena parighāsu yathāthavā ।।

bahistadāsane kāryā tvagre dairghyācchamādhikā ।
vaipulyācchamamānaṃ tu prāgvat pāvanatāṃ nayet ।।

nyaset tatrāpyabhagnāgrān udaṅmūlān kuśān dvija ।
yasmād divyam udagbhāgaṃ pitryaṃ dakṣiṇasaṃjñakam ।।

svakenāmṛtavīryeṇa nityaṃ saṃvardhayanti ca ।
darbhamārgacchatenaiva pitṝṇāṃ te amarān dvija ।।

vasatyantaḥ pitṛgaṇo bhāgamāśritya dakṣiṇam ।
citkalāṃśasvarūpeṇa nṛṇāmevaṃ hi cottare ।।

kṛtāspadāmalā nityā tvamṛtākhyākṣayā kalā ।
ata evaṃ hi yatkiñcid ābrahmaviditaiḥ dvija ।।

pradīyate pitṝṇāṃ ca tat satyena tu pāṇinā ।
ye adhikṛtya jagadyoniṃ mantrātmānamajaṃ harim ।।

prayacchanti pitṝṇāṃ ca toyatarpaṇapūrvakam ।
teṣāṃ tadāśrayatvā yaduktaṃ nānakāraṇam ।।

kartavyasya ca pāramyaṃ prakṛtasya mahāmate ।
sphuratyantargataṃ yeṣāṃ mantrārādhanapūrvakam ।।

tat svottaravaśādyeṣāṃ mantrasāṃmukhyadigvaśāt ।
cetasā nirvikalpena kṛtaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ।।

kintu puṣkarasambhūta durlabhā bhuvi cetanāḥ ।
iti cetasi vai yeṣāṃ niścayīkṛtya vartate ।।

satyatāmupanīye tvevanyasye kuśācaye ।
tilāṃstathāścajaptāśca tadūrdhve vikiret punaḥ ।।

kuruvindastu darbhāgrairyasmādetad dvayaṃ dvija ।
sarvasya bhogajālasya janakaṃ bhuvanatraye ।।

viśeṣāt pitṛdevasya śraddhāpūtasya vastunaḥ ।
agnīṣomasvarūpeṇa śāntyātmā bhagavāna svayam ।।

vyaktaḥ karmātmaka tvānāṃ mūrtitvenātmasiddhaye ।
sa pitryasya ca divyasya vyāpārasyātivaddhaye ।।

tattejastilabhāvena hlādo vartatyapātmanā ।
ata evāprabuddhānāṃ prabuddhānāmapi dvija ।।

tilodakena bhāvaṃ tu gacchataḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi ।
śrāddhasya ca parā rakṣā te dve nityamamārntraṇām ।।

tatsvarūpavidāṃ cai va viśeṣo mantravedinām ।
nyastra strāṇyabhijaprāni tatra pātrāṇi vinyaset ।।

tatrādyaṃ cakavṛttāni hemādyutthāni saṃbhave ।
pālāśakadalīpatratamālacchadanānyatha ।।

purānya strāmbuśaddhāni śubhaparṇamayāni ca ।
pādayorapi pādyārthaṃ kaṃ kṣiped dakṣiṇāditaḥ ।।

āmūrdham arcayet paścād ardhyapuṣpānulepanaiḥ ।
vastrastragdhūpadīpaiḥ tu dadhyannaṃ phalavādiṇā ।।

satāmbūlena vittena yathāśakti mahāmate ।
samuddiśya pitṝn sarvān sanābhīyān yathākramam ।।

śabdabhāvasvarūpāstu jñavṛttisthānavigrahān ।
bahutve sati viprāṇāṃ pitṛṇāmevamācaret ।।

yatra dvijadvayaṃ vipra pitrarthaṃ viniveśitam ।
ekāsmin svapitṛṇāṃ tu tadā kāryaśca sannidhiḥ ।।

dvitīye jananīyānāṃ tatha'nyeṣāṃ tu saṃsthitim ।
sarveṣāmekaprāptaṃ tu tṛpraye yadi yojitam ।।

omādyamasmacchabdaṃ tu pitṛbhyastadanantaram ।
idam ardhyam idaṃ pādyaṃ tadante saṃsmaret svadhām ।।

sarvāsmin upacārānte vaṃ vā saṃsmaran naram ।
namaḥ svadhāthavā brūyānnamontāṃ tvathavā svathavā svadhām ।।

evameva hi yaḥ kuryāt kartavyatvena pauṣkara ।
tulyānāṃ ca svakulyānāṃ namastatra ca kevalam ।।

satyukte vyatyaye nityaṃ vihitaṃ ca svadhā dvija ।
svayameva hi sanyāsī dadāti ca phalārthinām ।।

kāryastena namaskāraḥ svadhānte nityameva hi ।
dadāti phalakāmastu yo nityaphalamārthinām ।।

svadhākārāvasāne tu hitaṃ tasya sadā namaḥ ।
evam icchavaśenai va saṃvibhajya pitṝn dvija ।।

pṛṣṭvā pātramukhenaiva satṛptiṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ।
tato ambhaśculakaṃ pāṇau hranmantreṇāmṛtopamam ।।

dadyāt pūrṇendutulyaṃ taddhyātavyaṃ tatkalāḥ paḍhan ।
sānusvāram akārādyairbhinnaṃ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ svaraiḥ ।।

tvaṅkārananiniṣṭaṃ ca tatra prākasthaḥ satārakam ।
ityuktaṃ sakalasyendora vācakaṃ mantramabjaja ।।

pāṇiprakṣakanāt pūrvaṃ pātavyaṃ tena pūrvavat ।
yenāmṛtapurāntastham annavīryam anaśvaram ।।

bhavatyāpyāyakṛd brahman pitṛdevagaṇasya ca ।
māṣacūṇādinā pāṇiṃ prakṣālyāmaṇibandhanāt ।।

samācamyopasaṃhṛtya ūcchiṣṭaṃ tu yathāvidhi ।
pavitrīkṛtya vasudhāṃ pāṇau kṛtvā tilodakam ।।

prīṇanaṃ bhagavatyagre samutthāyācaret tataḥ ।
tavāstu bhagavan pūrvaḥ prītaḥ pitṛgaṇastathā ।।

śārīro devatāvyūha a padā dyā vyavasthitaḥ ।
evaṃ suvitate kuryāt karmatvārādhanālaye ।।

saṅkaṭe punaraanyatra yāyādabhyarcya mantrarāṭ ।
sthānaṃ saṃskārasaṃśudhdaṃ kṛtvā prāktānādinā ।।

vyāptiśaktayāritaṃ bhūtastoyādhāragataṃ smaret ।
manyamarcanapūrvaṃ tu tadagra sarvamācaret ।।

pātrāghrāṇapareṇaiva tatpātrasthena bhāvayet ।
mādhuyuktena haviṣā darbhakāṇḍaistilaiḥ saha ।।

nirdeṣaṃ vahninā kṛtvā hṛdā darbhāgrakeṇa tu ।
dhyātvā dhāma drumākāraṃ jñasvabhāvaṃ mahat prabham ।।

dravyadoṣagaṇa kṛtsnaṃ nirdahantaṃ samantataḥ ।
devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ yat tṛptaye annaṃ mahāmate ।।

tat sādhanaṃ ca vihitaṃ saṃskṛtena purānninā ।
dvābhyāṃ deśikapūrvābhyāme tad viṣayam abjaja ।।

pradāpanamato anyeṣāṃ tatkālaṃ tasya vai hitam ।
sadaiva vidhinānena tadarthaṃ śubhasiddhaye ।।

ekasyā śrayabījasya nānākarmavaśāt tu vai ।
nānātvaṃ bhāvayed buddhayā pitṛkarmavyataḥ purā ।।

tenaiva tarpaṇīyaṃ tat svayaṃbhūtā tadātmanā ।
matpravāhavadantastho bhāvayed annapātragau ।।

arhaṇāgrahagarbhau tu dvau darbhau tālasammitau ।
hranmantramantritau kṛtvā tābhyāṃ saha samuddharet ।।

rasarūpasvabhāvaṃ tat stha latvenānnatāṃ gatam ।
caturaṅgulamātraṃ tu grāsaṃ grāsaṃ mahāmate ।।

agnīṣomāśrayasthasya pūrvaṃ pitṛgaṇasya ca ।
pitṝṇāṃ bījabhūtasya jñasvabhāvasya tattvataḥ ।।

daghāt piṇḍadvayaṃ cai va tvagnīṣomasamudbhavam ।
nāḍīsvarūpau tau darbhau piṇḍena saha tatra vai ।।

layaṃ nītvā dvitīyena vyavahāradhiyāṃ tataḥ ।
pitṝṇāṃ kalpayet tena piṇḍānyanye na sāṃpratam ।।

krameṇa prāgadṛṣṭānāṃ hradā saṃjñāpadena tu ।
evaṃ dṛṣṭasvarūpaṃ ca jñātvā teṣāṃ sthitiṃ sphuram ।।

prāgvat svadhāvasānāghairmantrair oṃkārapūrvakaiḥ ।
hranmantrālaṅkṛnairvipra tadā saṃjñāpadānvitaiḥ ।।

piṇḍaṃ prakalpayāmīti tataḥ pūrvavadācaret ।
añjanābhyañjanādyaistu hyupacāraiḥ prapūjanam ।।

krameṇa tarpaṇaṃ kuryāt satilaiścā mbhasā tataḥ ।
śirasā vanate kṛtvā jānupādau kṣitau gatau ।।

pāṇiyugme lālārasthe ekacintaḥ paḍhed imam ।
oṃ namo vaḥ pitaro namo vāḥ puruṣottama ।।

namo viṣṇupadasthebhyaḥ svadhā vaḥ pitaro namaḥ ।
haraye pitṛnāthāya hyagnīṣomātmane namaḥ ।।

satsomapātmane viṣṇo namo barhiṣadātmane ।
āsaṃsārābhijanakā agniṣvāttā athācyuta ।।

pitāmahāḥ somapāstvaṃ tvamanye pratitāmahāḥ ।
tubhyaṃ namo bhagavate pitṛmūrte anyutāya ca ।।

nārāyaṇāya haṃsāya viṣṇo tripuruṣātmane ।
muttavā tvāmeva bhagavan na namāmi arcayāmi ca ।।

na tarpayāmi sarveśa nānyam āvāhayāmyaham ।
stutvā evaṃ hi pitṛvyūhaṃ bhaktayā paramayā punaḥ ।।

saṃbhave sati sandhānaṃ piṇḍamūrteḥ samācaret ।
tadagratopaviṣṭasya kramāt pitṛgaṇasya ca ।।

anusandhāya vai dvābhyām ekasmin vā dvijottama ।
ūṣmāgrāvasthitaṃ dhyātvā pitrayaṃ pitṛgaṇaṃ kramāt ।।

praṇavena svarūpaṃ tu samutthāya tataḥ svayam ।
madhyatiryaksthitau sthitvā hyadūraṃ nā nyadṛksthinaiḥ ।।

uttarābhimukhaiśca eva dakṣiṇasyāthavā dvija ।
taduttarānanavaśād hranmantraṃ hradayān nyaset ।।

namo antaṃ praṇavādyaṃ tu marudambaravigraham ।
piṇḍāgre hyupaviṣṭasya prāṇaśakti dvijasya vā ।।

bahūnāṃ vā prayatnena svātantrān nirgato bahiḥ ।
dhyātvā tayā saha kṣipramekībhūtatvamāgatam ।।

ātmaśaktau layaṃ nītvā yadi hyūṣmākhyalakṣaṇā ।
kṛtvaivaṃ prāṇasaṅghaṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ vipravigrahe ।।

prāgvadāsanasaṃruddha bhojayet pūrvavat tataḥ ।
oṃ namatvamṛtāyānnamidaṃ viṣṇupuraḥsarāḥ ।।

devā nadyastathā gāvaḥ sūryaḥ somo vanaspatiḥ ।
oṃ mādhavo atha bhagavān mantramūrtimayo mahān ।।

madhubhāvena vo anyasmin sthitvā tṛptiṃ karotu vai ।
anujjhitāsanaṃ kuryāt pitṝṇāṃ prīṇanāya ca ।।

tasminnevāsmi bhūbhāge vastvā tatpiṇḍavikṣitau ।
sthitiḥ sarvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca sāṃprataṃ kamalāsana ।।

yāvat prāṇavimuktānāṃ piṇḍānāṃ nopasaṃhṛtiḥ ।
socchiṣṭānāṃ kṛtā samyak tadante saṃvrajanti te ।।

svasthānāmāśiṣaṃ datvā śrāddhakarturdhiyā dvija ।
sāmṛtaṃ sodakaṃ sthāne satilaṃ mantratejasā ।।

viviktaṃ vivṛtaṃ mārgaṃ punarāgamanāya ca ।
nārāyaṇākhyasanmantrakarma brahmajavīkṛte ।।

sve svondriyarathe kṛtvā tṛptā yātācyutāspadam ।
prājāpatyamidaṃ proktaṃ saṃpradāyasamanvitam ।।

saṃpradānaṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca pūrvoktaphalavardhanam ।
samācaret sadā vyūhya mantrāṇāṃ mantrakarmaṇā ।।

nityaṃ bahutve dvitve vā prayogaṃ kamalodbhava ।
yadyetadapyanaṅgaṃ ca tadā vai pratikarmaṇi ।।

hradādyaṅgāṅgato yojyamaṅgi pūrvavadabjaja ।
ārādhyānāmamunetrāṇām oṃṅkāraḥ tatkriyāntare ।।

asminnarthe vikārastu ya ukto mantrapūrvakaḥ ।
samayaḥ putrakādīnāmanyeṣāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

gurośca sādhakendrasya mantro mama mahāmate ।
pradāne sa viruddhaśca tvato anyastvaviruddhakṛt ।।

samayī putrakādīnāṃ vaiṣṇavānāmapi dvija ।
caturṇāṃ maugdalāntānāṃ tathaivāśramiṇā tu vai ।।

dīkṣayā saṃskṛtānāṃ ca dīkṣitānāṃ mahāmune ।
sāmānyastvatha sarvatra sāṅgaḥ siddhaḥ supūjitaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ yaścopadeṣṭavyo mantravyūho hi taṃ śṛṇu ।
sadvādaśākṣaro mantraḥ kavacaṃ brahmaṇe namaḥ ।।

evaṃ viśvātmane netramastraṃ ca paramātmane ।
ete sapraṇavāḥ sarve śūdrāṇāṃ yogyatāvaśāt ।।

samyagvā dīkṣitānāṃ ca teṣāṃ vai praṇavojjhitāḥ ।
vihitāca yathā strīṇāṃ sadācāravaśāt tu vai ।।

asamyak pratipannānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ tu mahāmate ।
na khaṇḍayet tu mantrāṇāṃ namaskāro bhavet punaḥ ।।

sajāterdvādaśārṇasya tadvadaṣṭākṣarasya ca ।
ṣaḍakṣarasya vai pūrvaṃ prayojyaṃ pūraṇārthataḥ ।।

yadā tvabhihito aṣṭārṇe tvaṣṭārṇena avatāritaḥ ।
mukhyatā dvādaśārṇasya mantrasya vihitā tadā ।।

ṣaḍakṣarasya mukhyatvaṃ bhavedubhāvavaśād api ।
yojyasvaṣṭākṣaro mantro nityameva śikhāvadhau ।।

praṇavasya ca mukhyatvaṃ dviṣaḍaṣṭaṣaḍakṣarāḥ ।
mantrā hṛdayapūrvāstu parijñeyāstataḥ kramāt ।।

mantrāṇāṃ varmapūrvāṇāṃ vācyatvaṃ yadi kalpyate ।
tadātmatā ca vihitā tatsthāne praṇavasya ca ।।

devo jitaṃtāmantreṇa cittasthaḥ sannidhīkṛtaḥ ।
yoktavyaṃ tatra ca aṅgānāṃ mantraṣaṭkaṃ yathā sthitam ।।

dvādaśākṣarapūrvaṃ tu tṛtīyaṃ yat prakīrtitam ।
tṛtīyaṃ brahmapūrvaṃ tu dharmādīnāṃ hi vācakam ।।

praṇavaḥ sarvamantrāṇāmitaśca āsanakarmaṇi ।
dvādaśākṣarapūrvāṇāṃ mantrasāmānyakarmaṇām ।।

darbhātilodakādīnāṃ dravyāṇāṃ pratikarmaṇi ।
jāyate ca visṛṣṭānāmvupaśāntiśca taijasī ।।

ata evopayuktānāṃ bhogānāṃ kamalodbhava ।
viruddhasaṃgraho bhūyastvanyāsmin hi kriyāntare ।।

gauṇī vyaktiḥ yatasteṣāmāmūlāccidādhiṣṭhitā ।
vartate paramāśritya tat kartuḥ phalasiddhaye ।।

citsāmānyavinirmuktā hyayomyāste śarīravat ।
mantrāṇāṃ sthāyino bhāgā yānti vai yogyatāṃ punaḥ ।।

kadācinmantrasāmarthyāt jñānabhāvanayā dvija । 

- atha naimittikaśrāddhavidhiḥ -

naimittakamataḥ śrāddhavidhānamavadhāraya ।
gatipradaṃ pitṝṇāṃ yat karmaṇāṃ siddhibhūridam ।।

sadyaḥ satpātrasaṃprāptiṃ vinā naiva samācaret ।
evamādyairvinirmuktaṃ śrāddhamabjasamudbhava ।।

tiṣṭhatyanugrahārthaṃ ca yadi saṃprārthitaṃ hi yat ।
tadā niyamamātiṣṭhe[dagni]kāṣṭhād anādikam ।।

mānamātsaryakārpavyakrodhalobhādayo akhilāḥ ।
doṣā dūratare tyājyā hyāniṣpattidināvadhi ।।

śuddhipūrveṇa vidhinā suprayatnena cetasā ।
pradattaṃ phalamūlādyaṃ bhavet tadamṛtādhikam ।।

deśapātravaśenaiva saṃpatto sati padmaja ।
ekāhāt saptarātraṃ tu śraddhayā tat samācaret ।।

samāśritya śubhaṃ kālamekāhaṃ kamalodbhava ।
nirvartya parayā prītyā naiti kālaṃ yathānyathā ।।

trayamāśritya te śrāddhaṃ sānukampena cetasā ।
satvasthena kṛtaṃ śaktyā śuddhena draviṇena ca ।।

nayatyavaśyamacirāt satyalokaṃ tadarthitam ।
deśakālakṛtaṃ tvetat tapolokaṃ dadāti ca ।।

deśapātrāśritu śrāddhaṃ jana lokaṃ dadāti ca ।
phalaṃ maharlokagati kālapātravaśāt kṛtam ।।

kevalaṃ deśamāsādya dattaṃ svargaṃ prayacchati ।
kṛtaṃ yat kālamaśritya bhuvarlokaṃ dvijayāte? ।।

saumyapātrāśritaṃ śrāddhaṃ tadbhūlokagatipradam ।
sāmānyasya ca deśādestritayasya phalaṃ tvidam ।।

tatra puṣkara puṣṭiṃ hi prasiddhaṃ dehamabjaja ।
kālaṃ grāhyoparāgādyaṃ pātraṃ tanmayamabjaja ।।

tathā niyamavān samyak śrāddhahetorna cānyathā ।
yaduktaṃ tritayaṃ śrāddhe saviśeṣaṃ hi tat punaḥ ।।

bhavatyutārakaṃ nṝṇāṃ savijñānena janmanā ।
prasiddhayā vaiṣṇavaṃ deśaṃ pātrastradbhgavanmayā ।।

dvādaśyākhyo bṛhatkālaḥ saṅkāntyādyaiḥ pariṣkṛtaḥ ।
trayametanmahābuddhe saviśeṣataraṃ yadi ।।

bhavatyuttārakaṃ nūnaṃ dehāntaranivāsinām ।
svayaṃvyaktena vibhunā tvekamūrtyādinābjaja ।।

adhiṣṭhitaṃ hi sargādāvekadeśāt sahāmbunā ।
tadviśeṣāntaraṃ deśaṃ siddhikṛt sarvakarmaṇām ।।

tasmin dvijocite kāle dvādaśyākhye bhavedyadi ।
samuhūrtaṃ sanakṣatraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tena tadbhavet ।।

prottārakaṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca savyabāhusamanvitam ।
samyaksiddhitrayopetaṃ pañcakālaparāyaṇam ।।

labdhalakṣaṃ pare tattve pātramekāyanaṃ dvija ।
saṃyamādyairupetaṃ ca tanmahārthāyanāttu vai ।।

pitṛṇāṃ sugatiprāptiḥ śaśvadeva hi jāyate ।
vetaṃ ca taṃ mahāvegāt[tulyavegaṃ hi]jāyate ।।

deśe śubhe śubhaṃ janma jñānasatkarmaṇā saha ।
phalaṃ śubhatarān bhinnān pitṝṇāṃ tritayāt kramāt ।।

jñātvaivaṃ śrāddhadāne tu deśakālādayo guṇāḥ ।
cittaśuddhisametāśca samāsannāḥ prasannataḥ ।।

etadastrādinā sarvamupakāraṃ hi karmaṇām ।
kevalaṃ bhaktipūtānāṃ lokadharmaratātmanām ।।

jñānakarmaratānāṃ ca dvijānāmadhikāriṇām ।
pañcakālaratānāṃ ca svakarmavyabjasaṃbhava ।।

yānti ?vyāghāramantreṇa parikrāmyena vai tataḥ ? ।
prabandhabrahmavarṇatvaṃ ?teṣāṃ tadbhagavān hariḥ ।।

ṣāḍguṇyavigraho devaḥ prabhavāpyayakṛt svayam ।
guṇamuktasamūhena svarūpādacyutena ca ।।

kālādīnāṃ samutthānaṃ ṣāḍguvyād ata eva hi ।
na vindanti paratvena te cānyasyācyutaṃ vinā ।।

kālādeḥ sūkṣmabhūtasya tvāśrayasyāmalasya ca ।
ato anayadbhagavadbhaktāstanmantrajñānatatparāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ kamalasaṃbhūta kālādyamakhilaṃ hi yat ।
sarvam antaḥsthitaṃ bhāti tatprabhāvavaśāt sphuṭam ।।

bahirantaravaścāpi yasmādetadadhīśva[rāt] ।
viśvasya cāpi dehatvaṃ purā te saṃprakāśitam ।।

adhvopadeśadvāreṇa vistareṇa ta[d]eva hi ।
dehajñaṃ satkriyāniṣṭhaṃ jñāninaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ sthiram ।।

icchantyutārakaṃ śuddhaṃ pitaraḥ svakule pumān ।
deśakālādayastvevamaśritya prayataḥ svayam ।।

nistuṣairujjvalaiḥ śuddhaiḥ sakṣīraid abjasaṃbhava ।
savdyañjanasamopetaṃ saṃsādya śraddhayā purā ।।

hṛdā vā dvādaśārṇena bhāṇḍeṣvabhinaveṣu vai ।
vinirgateṣu vā pākād bhūyaḥ snehokṣiteṣvatha ।।

evaṃ vā sādhanīyaṃ ca putraśiṣyātmanā dvija ।
bhaginyā dharmasā ?pantyā suhṛtsambandhavartmanā ।।

śuklāṃbaradhareṇaiva dakṣeṇa śucinā'tmanā ।
śārīravyādhihīnena kṣuttṛṣṇāvigatena ca ।।

kāsaśvāsa svabhāvātha dṛkśrutihīnakharvaṭaiḥ ।
evaṃ vimuktādoṣeṇa bhāvabhaktipareṇa ca ।।

saṃsādhanīyaṃ śrāddhārthaṃ svajātīyena vai caruḥ ।
anulomena vihitaṃ varṇānāṃ carusādhanam ।।

divye pitraye abjasaṃbhūta pratilomaśca doṣakṛt ।
tadalābhāt krayakrītamaduṣṭaṃ kārukā śucim ।।

pūrvoktādośanirmuktaṃ tenāpi kamalodbhava ।
apikṣayavidhūnā vā lausyaikaniratātmanām ।।

rajasvalānāṃ ṣaṇḍānāṃ ṛtvādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
śvānasūkaramārjāramarkaṭānāṃ tathaiva hi ।।

viḍvarāhaśivāgṛdhrapūrvāṇāṃ tu svacāriṇām ।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena nivātasthagitāmbare ।।

niḥśasye kuṭṭime bhūyaḥ sulipte dhavalīkṛte ।
sthāne mantrārcanaṃ devapitṛdevasya sādhanam ।।

vihitaṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ saṃbhave sati sarvadā ।
annavyañjanabhāṇḍānāṃ sarveṣāṃ kramaśo dvija ।।

antaścārambhakālo tu madhvājyaiḥ sakuśāstilāḥ ।
kṣeptavyā dvādaśārṇena bhūyaḥ siddhena saṃgrahe ।।

aṣṭārṇenātha vastreṇa sthagayet tān prayatnataḥ ।
yathā na bahiranyotthaṃ bāṣpaṃ niryāti padmaja ।।

ūrdhvapuṇḍre kṛte lipte kṣālite stha likācaye ।
varmaṇā vāsasā cchanne maryādābhyantarīkṛte ।।

rakṣapālaṃ ca tatpaṅktau datvā snānādyamācaret ।
agnervipramavāsānāṃ ?pūjāsthānasya pauṣkara ।।

bhāṇḍānāṃ bhāgapūrvāṇāṃ satsahāyagaṇasya ca ।
viniyogaṃ purā kṛtvā pūrṇāntaṃ nityamācaret ।।

apā nāt pratiśāṭakam ।
tasyādhaḥ śāṭikāyāṃ tu vidhūyāt tanuveṣṭanam ।।

adhūtaṃ vimalaṃ svacchaṃ[visūtraṃ]valkalīdikam ।
nīlāñcitaṃ ca catkiṃcidvidyate cāmbarādikam ।।

sarvatra viṣayāṃ caiva?tvapāsya bhuvanādbahiḥ ।
tato dhiyābhisandhāya mantramūrtigataṃ param ।।

yajāmyanugrahārthaṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ punareva hi ।
niveśya prāgvadāhūya hyāsaneṣu kramād dvijān ।।

tebhyaḥ prāgānanau pūrvaṃ niveśyau dvau dvijottamau ।
dvādaśāro dharo dhāma tritayādhiṣṭhitāsane ।।

athoktān sarvasāmānyān ṣaḍaṅgā dvijavāsvarāḥ ? ।
astramantraśikhāyuktaḥ kramādbi ṣaḍanvitam ।।

niyojya prāṅmukhasthābhyāṃ dehatādātmyatāptaye ।
svavācakena saddhāmno hyekamūrtyādikātmanā ।।

nyastavyaṃ devatāvyūhaṃ phaḍvauṣaṭkārasaṃyutam ।
nṛsiṃhākhyaṃ savārāhaṃ mantramūrtidvayaṃ hi yat ।।

agnīṣomākhyadaivatyaṃ rakṣārthaṃ sarvadaiva hi ।
avīkṣayannudagbhāga ato anye viniveśya ca ।।

tatrādau hṛdayadīnāmadhaḥpaṅktau niveśya ca ।
dṛśā sadvarṇajānāṃ tu saṅghānāmevameva hi ।।

tasya dakṣiṇataścordhve jananīyakulasya ca ।
kavacenāparaṃ yojyamekāntaṃ bhagavanmayam ।।

pitṛnāmnā[dvitīyaṃ]ca tasya dakṣiṇatastataḥ ।
tṛtīyamāptikārī ? ca caturthaṃ hṛdayena tu ।।

pitāmahābhidhānena mūrtimantreṇa pañcamam ।
pratitāmahanāmnā vai yojyamekāyanaṃ dvija ।।

janake jīvabhāvena tadatītatrayaṃ kramāt ।
niveśanīyaṃ tairmantrairvartate ca dvayaṃ kramāt ।।

pratitāmahapūrvaṃ tu samatītatrayaṃ nyaset ।
sāmānyena ṣaḍaṅgena tvevamuktaṃ svakena vā ।।

mantreṇa śrāddhadāne tu viniyogaṃ dvijārcane ।
caturmūrtādhikāreṇa dvidhāvasthamathocyate ।।

sabhogamapavargaṃ ca mantraikasmādavāpyate ।
kaivalyaṃ kevalaṃ caiva dvitīyādamalekṣaṇa ।।

sasuhṛnmantravargasya nyasedavyaktamantrarāṭ ।
trayāṇāṃ vāsudevāntaṃ pradyumnādyamataḥ kramāt ।।

na tadvai saviśeṣaṃ ca punareva[ca]me śṛṇu ।
suhṛtprapūrvamiśrāṇāmaniruddhaṃ hi vācakam ।।

pradyumnamantravargasya kāmād dvābhyāṃ dvayaṃ tataḥ ।
praṇavena paraṃ brahmasvarūpaṃ pratitāmaham ।।

maha dāptamukhenaiva tarpaṇaṃ yanmahāmate ।
navamūrtyadhikāreṇa triprakāramathocyate ।।

samitrāṇāṃ ca vātsalyād dvijānāṃ viṣṇunā nyaset ।
tato vairājamantreṇa mātṛvargasya pauṣkara ।।

tribhirnārāyaṇadyaistu pitrādīnāṃ trayaṃ kramāt ।
viddhi viddhā khyametaddhi śrāddhajñānaṃ phalapradam ।।

pitṝṇā yajamānasya dehalābhe vinaiva hi ।
vairājamantrādārabhya sāṅkarṣaṇāntamabjaja ।।

samantrapañcakaṃ viddhi ।
pratitāmahaniṣṭhānāṃ yatacchrāddhaṃ hi pauṣkara ।।

prayacchatyātmalābhaṃ tu śrāddhakartuḥ pitṛṣvapi ।
ādhārāṇāṃ mantrādvai ।।

niyojanaṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ pañcānāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi ।
mitravargāt samārabhya parametaddhi vaśvaram ।।

sāmagrībhiḥ samopetaṃ kartuḥ pitṛgaṇasya ca ।
paraṃ yacchati nirvāṇaṃ sakṛtsnaṃ ca kiṃ punaḥ ।।

kālamājīvitaṃ vipra śraddhāpūtena cetasā ।
kṛpayā ca samānānāṃ saṃbhave sati pauṣkara ।।

kāmye asmiñśrāddhadāne tu paṅktayā nānyatra yojayet ।
samūhamekaṃ pūrvaṃ tu viprāṇāmuttarānanam ।।

hṛnmantreṇābjasaṃbhūta sarveṣāṃ vinyaset tataḥ ।
praṇavena svanāmnā ca jñāta hṛdādiṣu ।।

astrabhūṣaṇahetīśa pūrvamantrān sagocare ।
evaṃ vā prāṅmukhaṃ śaktayā cakramantreṇa yojayet ।।

vipramekamudagvakraṃ mukhyamantreṇa yojayet ।
dvayaṃ codaṅmukhaṃ tatra hranmantreṇānusandhya ca ।।

suhṛmnitraṃ dvivetaṃ tu ?mātṛvaṃśamathābjaja ।
pitṛvaṃśaṃ hi niḥśeṣaṃ smaredaparadehagam ।।

maṇḍale tvambupātrastha cakraṃ vā nṛhariṃ yajet ।
[vipramekamudagvaktraṃ mukhyamantreṇa vinyaset ।।

tṛptaye pitṛvargasya yathā mātṛkulasya ca ।
sarvaṃ janamāto anyeṣāṃ prītaye ca svaśaktitaḥ ।।

gavā grāsaṃ samuddhṛtya dadyād ghṛtamadhuplutam ।
darbhaistilodakairmiśraṃ na kṣāraṃ lavaṇotkaṭam ।।

ātmavaṃśādhikāreṇa karyādevamato anyathā ।
paurohityena kṛpayā prītyā vānyasya kasya cita ।।

nirvartane tadīyaṃ hi tatpūrvaṃ vihitaṃ kulam ।
āpādājjānuparyantamājānormadhyamasta kam ।।

āvastimūrdhno hṛdayamāhṛdo masatakāvadhi ।
aniruddhādayo mantrāścatvāro viniveśya ca ।।

sugatiprāptaye vipra pitṝṇāṃ nityameva hi ।
tṛptaye vāsudevādyādāmūrdhnastvaṅ ghrigācaram ।।

catvāraścāniruddhānto yoktavyā vā mahāmate ।
praṇavena hṛdi brahman śāntaṃ saṃvinmayaṃ tu vā ।।

samīśanalatoyakṣmābhūtānāṃ vya pakaṃ kramāt ।
nyastavyaṃ vāsudevādyamadhyakṣāntaṃ catuṣṭayam ।।

apekṣayāniruddhādyaṃ pṛthivyādicaturṣvatha ।
rakṣārthaṃ nṛhariṃ nyastvā navamūrteḥ paraṃ dvija ।।

mūrdhāsyakaṇṭhahṛnnābhiguhyajānudveya tvatha ।
pādayoḥ kṣmādharāntaṃ tu nyastavyaṃ tvaṣṭakaṃ kramāt ।।

hṛdambare tu bhagavān vāsudevo apyadhokṣajaḥ ।
kṣmāntānāṃ buddhipūrvāṇāṃ kramāt saṅkarṣaṇādikam ।।

yā ktavyamathavā vipra pṛthivyādikrameṇa tu ।
saptakaṃ bhūdharākhyaṃ tu saṅkarṣaṇāntameva hi ।।

atha ciddhṛtvadhiṣṭhāne vāsudevaṃ tu bhāvayet ।
rasalohitamāṃsānāṃ medomajjāsthiṣu dvija ।।

krameṇa śukladhātvantaṃ nyaset saṅkarṣaṇādikam ।
saptakaṃ ca varāhāntamāśuklād dvārasiddhaye ।।

varāhamantrādāramya saṅkarṣaṇāntamabjaja ।
evaṃ duṣṭanirāsārthaṃ pūrvavat pātrakaṃ nyaset ।।

vyāpakatvena bhagavān bahirabhyantare svavat ।
jīvavat sāṅkarṣaṇaṃ ca bījaṃ hṛtkamalodare ।।

sṛṣṭisaṃhārayogena saptakaṃ dhātusaptake । pauṣkara uvāca

sāmānyena svamantreṇa sati sannihitena vai ।
kārayo?rvigrahe vṛttau jvālantābhyantare tu vā ।।

nyāsārcanādimuktānāṃ mantrāṇāṃ yujyate katham ।
viniyogaṃ caturṇāṃ vā navānāṃ mantrakarmaṇi ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca

saṣaḍaṅgo hi sāmānyaḥ sarveṣāṃ vihitaḥ sadā ।
sādhakasya hi mantro hi viṣamaḥ syādvirodhakṛt ।।

anujñātaḥ sasarvasya cāturātmyādikaṃ hi yat ।
guroricchā svakīyātra svamantrādau mahāmate ।।

tatrāpi hi viśeṣāya śrāddhe dvābhyāṃ sa ucyate ।
mantragrāme tu vinyaste viprāṇāmicchayā purā ।।

svamantramupasaṃhṛtya svadhāmnā ca dhiyā satā ।
brahmabhāvanayā vyāpta evaṃ kṛtvā'śrayādikam ।।

yadvipravigrahe vyastaṃ mantravyūhaṃ tadātmani ।
athāniyojanīyaṃ ca kṣantu ?tatpāṇipūrvakam ।।

tatrāyaṃ vihitaṃ vipra viśeṣaṃ tannibodhatu ।
vyāpakatvena bhagavān prāk savyetarayostataḥ ।।

dakṣiṇe karaśākhāsu dvitīyaṃ pañcasunyaset ।
tadandvā me tṛtīyaṃ hi tvaṅguṣṭhādikrameṇa tu ।।

taladvaye dakṣiṇādāvaniruddhamato nyaset ।
ekaṃ vā vāsudevāntaṃ nyasedicchāvaśena tu ।।

yadā navātmā karayostadaṅguṣṭhadvaye acyutaḥ ।
aṣṭhakaṃ ca varāhantaṃ prāgvadātarjaneḥ kramāt ।।

vāmatarjana niṣṭhaṃ tu vāsudevāntameva vā ।
svāhāmadhyoditaṃ kṛtvā pūjāsāre ? tathā nale ।।

hutamapyanalaṃ bhūtaṃ prāgvat pāva katāṃ nayet ।
evamicchāvaśenaiva mantrāṇāṃ parivartanam ।।

svārādhyā navaniṣṭhānāṃ śrāddhakāle avirodhakṛt ।
evaṃ niyojanaṃ kṛtvā śirasābhyarcya sāṃpratam ।।

sāsanaṃ puṣpapātreṇa samūhaṃ bhagavanmayam ।
tanmadhyembhaścalaṃ cittaṃ pañcendriyasamanvitam ।।

kuryāttāṃma ntrapīṭhasthaṃ madhye pāre athavā hṛdi ।
kālamācamanāntarṃ tu madanugrahakāmyayā ।।

sannidhāne dvijānāṃ ca vibhoḥ sajvalanasya ca ।
bhāvyaṃ suyantritenaiva sarvajñenāpi jantunā ।।

evaṃ bhūtaiḥ dvijendraistu buddhayā tu suviśaddhayā ।
śraddheyamakhilaṃ tasya sānukampena cetasā ।।

yasmādabjasamudbhūta mānaṃ yadubhayātmakam ।
nāsakṛt sarvabhāvānāṃ viśeṣācchrāddhakarmaṇi ।।

samaye[tasya]yojyaṃ tat pūraṇa sarvakarmaṇām ।
pāvanaṃ tṛptijananaṃ kiṃ punaḥ pitṛkarmaṇi ।।

ādāya manasā māntrīmājñāṃ vai śirasā saha ।
hārdamāpādya vai śrāddhaṃ dravyotthaṃ yadvaśād dvija ।।

saphalaṃ syāt pitṝṇāṃ tu jñānamūlaṃ hi tattvataḥ ।
anyathā hetunā kena pitṝṇāṃ tadgatipadam ।।

mūlaṃ vinā kṣmāṃ nābhyeti pādapānāṃ yathā tathā ।
jñānamāhlādapūrveṇa phalatyāśu ca vartmanā ।।

kāraṇaṃ sarvendriyāgrāmaṃ bahirvṛttigataṃ hi yat ।
svayamātmani saṃlīnaṃ kṛtvā hṛtkamalāmbare ।।

svabhāvaśaktyā saṃpūrya samāste sāṃprataṃ tu tat ।
svarūpād vandanaṃ kuryādvibhoḥ sarveśvarasya ca ।।

śāntasaṃvitsvarūpasya spandānandamayātmanaḥ ।
tāvacyutaṃ hi cit spandaṃ svayaṃ pariṇataṃ smaret ।।

sahastraśaśisūryāgniprabhayā projvalaṃ sthiram ।
marīcicakrasaṃpūrṇacidgarbhaṃ sarvatomukham ।।

cidambarāntarāvasthaṃ suśāntaṃ bhagavatpadam ।
tacchakti jñānanāḍervai vilakṣaṇataraṃ hi yat ।।

smarenmarīcikoṇasthaṃ svabhāvāhlādapiṇḍakam ।
svakaṃ pitṛsamūhaṃ tu sphurantaṃ karmaśāntaye ।।

mahataḥ pāvakādyadvacchaktirdahanalakṣaṇā ।
aṅgārakaṇamāśritya bāhyamāyāti pauṣkara ।।

tadvadeva hi niryātaḥ kintu saṅkspaniścayāt ।
agnīṣomau samāśritya pitaraśceśvarecchayā ।।

prakāśamantrarāḍbāhyaṃ māyākāśava[śād]dvija ।
krameṇa yat tataḥ sveṣāṃ sukhaduḥkhataraṃ tu vā ।।

mūlāntaḥkaraṇenaiva sendriyeṇa samābjaja ।
māyākāśavṛtenaiva hṛnmantraṃ bhrāmayekttataḥ ।।

tadduḥ khādupaśāntyarthaṃ raśmirandhreṇa kenacit ।
jñānatastvaravindākṣa tadākāśāvadheḥ punaḥ ।।

tatkālaṃ tatkulodbhetamanubhāvavaśād dvija ।
agnīṣomāśrayasthaṃ ca citpiṇḍaṃ tattu vai kramāt ।।

antaḥkaraṇabījaṃ tu mahāmohabalojjhitam ।
jñānāntamaṃbarāntasthaṃ susūkṣmaṃ satatoditam ।।

kṣmāntaṃ nārāyaṇādyaistu hyadhyakṣāntairadhiṣṭhitam ।
prāṇabrahmāvasānairvā vāsudevādikaiḥ kramāt ।।

buddhayā vyāptairyathāvasthaiḥ prabhavasthitilakṣaṇaiḥ ।
mantrāṅgairjñasvarūpairvā pañcabhirlocanojjhitaiḥ ।।

yadvaśāt pratipattirvai karturbhavati susphuṭā ।
sanniveśavaśenāto hārde asmin pitṛtarpaṇe ।।

svānuṣṭhānavaśenāpi mantrāṇāmmudayān smaran ।
amūrtamathavā mūrtamadhidaivavyavasthayā ।।

cidbījanicayādhāra bdyātmakaṃ yat puroditam ।

tābhiḥ saṃpūrṇamantaḥkaraṇaśaktibhiḥ ।।

abhinnalakṣaṇenaiva praṇavena mahāmate ।
dhyāyoccitkarṇikāmadhye bhūmau bījatvamāgatam ।।

saturyamapṛthagbhūtaiḥ satvādyairanupaplutam ।
tasmādvinirgataṃ dhyāyet tritayenābhirañjitam ।।

pratitāmahasaṃjñaṃ tu caitanyatvena pauṣkara ।
suṣuptirūpa tāprāptamīṣatkāluṣyamāgatam ।।

viśrāntaṃ karṇikākāśadeśe cidbhāskarodare ।
taduddeśaṃ tatastamāccaitanyānnirgataṃ smaret ।।

svenāntaḥkaraṇenaiva rañjitaṃ svaṃ pitāmaham ।
ekāreṇa svanāmnā ca svapnenāviṣvakṛtasya ca ।।

saṃsthitiṃ saṃsmarettasya dvayātmanā māśritasya ca ।
cidaṃśasya vai kaṇṭhadeśe nābhyantarāmbare ।।

manobuddhirahaṅkārarañjitaṃ saṃsmarettataḥ ।
jāgreṇākūlitenaiva pitā caitanyamabjaja ।।

brahmanāyantarākāśe brahmarandhrapathāvanau ।
vdyātmake jīvakośe tu kāraṇe turyalakṣaṇe ।।

daivatyaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca sākāraṃ vār'kabimbavat ।
tadātmanā ca boddhavyau vibudhau viśvasaṃjñakau ।।

tanmūlaṃ hi yataḥ sarvaṃ karmiṇāṃ pitṛsaṃgrahaḥ ।
pratitāmahasaṃjñaṃ vai tvadhiṣṭhāyāthavā bhavet ।।

madhyāhnabhāskarākāraṃ mūrtaṃ vā jñānamūrtibhṛt ।
paitāmahīyamevaṃ hi caitanyaṃ kamalodbhava ।।

pradyumnādhiṣṭhitaṃ dhyāyet svasthānena puroditam ।
pitā dhidevatārūpamaniruddhamataḥ smaret ।।

mūrdhnaśchidrapraveśe tu amūrtaṃ mūrtameva vā ।
ārādhya mantreṇāḍhyaṃ vā sthānaṃ kuryādadhidhiṣṭhitam ।।

hṛnmantreṇāparaṃ vipra śirasā tat paraṃ tu tat ।
śikhādhidaivataṃ dhyāyeccaturthaṃ sarvadaiva hi ।।

śaktimantreṇa tanutīṃ hṛnmantrānugatāṃ smaret ।
śirasā saha cāstrākhyaṃ śikhayā saha locanam ।।

navamūrteścatuṣkaṃ tu cidrūpaṃ kevalaṃ hṛdi ।
sattāmātrasvarūpābhirvibhinnaṃ guṇaśaktibhiḥ ।।

oṃ tatsaditi caitadvat karṇikāgahanāntare ।
vyaktaṃ kaṇṭhāvadhoddeśaṃ kuryādgaruḍagādinā ।।

brahmarandhragrataṃ dhyāyet khavarāhanṛkesari[ ?m] ।
bhinnatve bhedabuddhayā tu yathaikasmin hi jāyate ।।

svabhāvaśītalaṃ coṣṇaṃ svādu bhinnajaladvayam ।
evaṃ bhogāptaye kuryādetasmādvamatyayaṃ hi ye ।।

jñeyaṃ tanmokṣadaṃ vipra nityamevāphalārthinām ।
tanutrāstradṛśo mantrāḥ hṛdayānmasatakāvadhi ।।

nyasyādhidevatātvena śaktitvena hṛdādayaḥ ।
jñānādīnāṃ hi vai yasmādbhogyāstrīṇi balādayaḥ ।।

te ca ṣaḍ hṛdayādīni nirṇītāni ca vai purā ।
evaṃ kāraṇamūlaṃ tu dehe pitṛgaṇaṃ kramāt ।।

nyastvā manīṣitairanyaiścidrūpaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha ।
santarpaṇaṃ tataḥ pārśve viśvedevapurassaram ।।

jalakṣaṇena santarpyau praṇavena tu tau purā ।
paramānandagarbheṇa sahastraśaśiraśminā ।।

hṛdiprāṇakalāmūle proccarat praṇavaṃ smaret ।
dugdhabudbudasaṅkāśamamṛtaṃ himaśītalam ।।

tarasāratayaṃ taṃ ca jñānanāḍīkramaṃ mahat ।
yamāśritya ca tiṣṭhanti viśvedevapurassarāḥ ।।

pitaro bhagavadrūpāḥ sākārā vahnirākṛtiḥ ।
brahmarandhrāvadhiṃ yāvadvisarpantaṃ smareta tat ।।

saṃpūrṇendutvamāpannaṃ bhāvayettatra tad dvija ।
yat pitryadaivataṃ mantraṃ brahmarandhropari sthitam ।।

prāṇaśaktirjvaladrūpā tadīyā tacchiropari ।
sūryamaṇḍalamadhyasthā yugāntānalavat smaret ।।

tattejasāvalīnaṃ taddhayāyenmaṇḍalamāmṛtam ।
janakīyakarandhreṇa pratistrotīkṛtaṃ punaḥ ।।

mūlaniṣṭhaṃ kramāddhayāyet cetasā nirmalena tu ।
evaṃ gatapipāsārthaḥ prāgvadoṅkāramuccaran ।।

turyabhūmiṃ tu pitrādilayadhyānadhiyā nayet ।
iti bhogāptaye kuryād bhūyo bhūyo dvijottama ।।

pitṝṇāmamṛtaṃ śrāddhaṃ sarvaduḥkhakṣayapradam ।
prakāśāhlādapiṇḍasthaṃ kṛtvā pitṛgaṇaṃ tu vai ।।

antarmāyāmbarādyantaṃ kṣīṇasaṃskāralakṣaṇam ।
āmūlādullasantaṃ ca ūrdhvadehavyapekṣayā ।।

audayena krameṇaiva sūryabimbamivāmbare ।
tat punarvilayīkuryāccandrabhāvanayā yathā ।।

na rogamāyāti punaḥ karmabhamau sacitphalaḥ ।
evaṃ yat pātayet piṇḍaṃ brahmakṣetrasamāścite ।।

anante vipule pūrṇe cidrūpe tvasphuṭaṃ dvija ।
svavaṃśottārakaṃ viddhi jñānakarmaparāyaṇam ।।

kintvasau durlabho yasya bhāvanaiṣāṃ hi tattvataḥ ।
bhagavadbhaktipūtā tanmantraika parāyaṇaḥ ।।

pravartetātha siddhayarthaṃ bāhyataśśrāddhakarmaṇi ।
mantreśavahniviprāṇāṃ sannidhāne yathākramam ।।

abhyarthāsanakarmākhyaṃ mantraṃ yadavatāritam ।
bhagavan puṇḍarīkākṣa pitryaṃ vargaṃ hi māmakam ।।

svayaṃ śrāddhātmanā bhūtvā proddharasva bhavārṇavāt ।
bhuṅkṣa tvaṃ śaktiniṣṭhena svayaṃ jñānādikena vai ।।

karaṇena balādyaṃ hi bhogajālaṃ trilakṣaṇam ।
evamabhyarthayitvā ca hyabhisandhāya cetasā ।।

kramāt pitṛgaṇaṃ sarvamidamuccārya vai tataḥ ।
oṃ oṃ oṃ oṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca tṛptaye parameśvara ।।

uttāraṇārthamapi vai yajāmyomoṃ namo nāmaḥ ।
sakṛccaturdhā navadhā tvimuccārya cetasā ।।

smaran bāhyāmbarāvasthaṃ vinyastaṃ yat parātmani ।
tato vibhavataḥ sarvairardhyapādyapurassaraiḥ ।।

bhogaistāmbūlaparyantairmantranāthaṃ yajed dvija ।
tatredaṃ sarvasāmānyaṃ bhogopādānakarmaṇi ।।

mantramuccāraṇīyaṃ ca śrāddhadāneṣu sarvadā ।
oṃ vauṣaḍamṛtābhaṃ tu balavīryamayaṃ tvidam ।।

tejaḥsvabhāvamamalaṃ bhogaṃ bhuṅkṣvoṃ namo namaḥ ।
naivedyaṃ vidyamānaṃ tu prokṣayitvā dṛśā bṛhat ।।

evaṃ yadabṛhadrūpaṃ pāṇau kṛtvā tu pātragam ।
tathā cāvidyamānaṃ yanmanasā vādya dhāraṇā ।।

pitṝṇāṃ tṛptaye hyevamiṣṭvā mantreśvaraṃ tataḥ ।
tatārā ?darbhalope taṃ pradadyāddehamodakam ।।

oṃ namo asmaptitṛgaṇāt prīto bhava jaganmaya ।
teṣāmastvidamakṣayyaṃ yat kṛtaṃ ca tvayā'tmasāt ।।

iti kartavyatā sā vai paitraṃ sthānātmanā nayet ।
mantreśaromakūpānāmāśayaṃ codayārkavat ।।

bahirhṛtkamaloddeśe smaret pitṛgaṇaṃ kramāt ।
athāntarmānaniṣṭhaṃ tu hyarghyādyaiḥ bhogasaṃcayaiḥ ।।

dravatpūrṇendudhavalaṃ marīcicayasaṃkulam ।
saṃviśantaṃ svaśaktyā vai dhyāyenmantrātmani sthite ।।

tejomaye pitṛvyūhe pitṛsaṃṅghaṃ hi tat punaḥ ।
madhyāhnārkāyutābhaṃ ca saṃsmaredvi sphuratprabham ।।

tadvayāpāre nivṛte atha romarandhre śanaiśśanaiḥ ।
mantrahṛtpuṣkarākāśamākrāntaṃ taiḥ smaredathā ।।

pīṭhasannihitaṃ mantrādādāyendudhiyā tataḥ ।
yāyādagnisamīpaṃ tu dhyāyettatroditaṃ prabhum ।।

santarpya vidhinā bhaktyā pūrṇāntaṃ mantrarāṭ tataḥ ।
tatrāpādya ścaruḥ prāgvat tathā piṇḍārthamodanam ।।

madhvājyatiladarbhāṇāṃ saṃpuṭe rajatānvite ।
abhimāntritamārādhyaistatastaistāḍanādibhiḥ ।।

nītvā nirdeṣatāṃ paścāt sthagayedambarādinā ।
athānusandhānapūrvaṃ sādhāraṃ tvāsanaṃ yajet ।।

kramāt kuśānāmūrdhve tu yathāsthānavibhāgaśaḥ ।
saṃsicya praṇavenātha satilena tu vāriṇā ।।

hemapūrvāṇi tatrāgre pātrāṇi kramaśo nyaset ।
pitrādyanukrameṇaiva tvādāvantye tadagrataḥ ।।

mantrapūrveṇa nāmnā taṃ sanamaskena nikṣipet ।
tilāstvambukuśāgrāṇi tvidaṃ ter'ghyaṃ paṭhan kramāt ।।

pratitāmahaparyantāmevaṃ kṛtvārdhyakalpanām ।
kāmo anyasmin śrāddhadāne hyevamanyeṣvapi dvija ।।

pūrvavannāmagotre tu hyardhyamāpādya pātragam ।
pṛthak pṛthagvā pātrāṇāmāsīnadvijasaṅkhayayā ।।

prakalpitamatha svaṃ svaṃ nītvā sārdhyaṃ tu bhojanam ।
pratitāmahaniṣṭhānāṃ pāṇau dadyāt kuśānvitam ।।

sāvaśeṣaṃ tathānyeṣāṃ haster'dhyaṃ pratipādya ca ।
kuryāt sārdhyodakānāṃ ca sumaryādāsu cāntare ।।

saṃsthānaṃ sarvapātrasya datte sārdhyodake sati ।
viprapāṇighṛtenātha tena cārdhyodakena tu ।।

visṛjya nayane sve vai pātre anyasmiṃstato dvija ।
kramādāhṛtya tattoyaṃ prayāyādagnisannidhim ।।

tatastadagre tatpātraṃ tilāmbuparipūritam ।
kṛtvā tasmin dhiyā dhyāyedviṣṭaraṃ parameśvaram ।।

saṃvibhajya pitṛvyūhaṃ tatroṅkāreṇa bhāvayet ।
vimalāmbarasaṃstha tu yathā nakṣatrasañcayam ।।

tathā kamalasaṃbhata tasmin pātrāntare sthite ।
apāvanyacyutākāśe hlādavṛttau vibhāvayet ।।

antaḥ sarveśvaraṃ devaṃ spandamānaṃ svatejasā ।
tator'dhyaiḥ kusumairgandhaiḥ kṛtvā teṣāṃ purārcanam ।।

madhulipte kuśākāṇḍe tatra dve salile nyaset ।
sthagayitvā pareṇaiva pātreṇa ca kajena tu ।।

dyāvāpṛthivyau te pātre boddhavye dvija pūrite ।
nidhāya cāryayitvā tu svottarottaramūlataḥ ।।

tāsu sūkṣmapitṛvyaktiṃ sāmānyacisvarūpaṃ tu tāraśabdaikatā gatam ।।

svavṛttimārgeṇāyātāṃ ruddhāṃ kuryāt kuśāsane ।
natroditakrameṇaiva prabhāvena vibhāvayet ।।

kvacicchabdaikavṛttau tu pūrvalakṣaṇalakṣitām ।
paṅktībhūtāṃ sthitiṃ paitrīmanumūrti prakāśitām ।।

tilodakena saṃpūrya ardhyapātrāt karāñjalim ।
dhārāṃ santānavaddadyāt kramāttadvai paṭhan dvija ।।

nāma praṇavaniṣṭhaṃ tu etatte pādyamastviti ।
tato anyapātramupādya prāgvadagnau samarpayet ।।

rajātalaṃkṛtenaiva sapavitreṇa pāṇinā ।
vyāpakaṃ citsvarūpaṃ tu dhātusaprakamūrtidhṛt ।।

brahmabhāvanayāntaṃ niścayīkṛtya cetasā ।
tīvānāmidamādhāramidamāpyāyanaṃ param ।।

saṃbhava ca layasthānaṃ paramāndalakṣaṇam ।
atastamādau pātrasthamardhyapuṣpānulepanaiḥ ।।

praṇavenārcanīyaṃ ca tenaivāpāgha vai tataḥ ।
paṭhaṃstameva manasā vartayedgolakākṛtim ।।

sarveśaktyātmakaṃ yasmāt santi
gṛhṇanti niyatā mūrtiṃ karmaṇāṃ pratipattaye ।।
sanābhīyānanugrahyānadhikṛtyākhilān pitṝn ।
yathār'dhyapūrvermantreśamiṣṭaṃ bhogaiḥ supuṣkalaiḥ ।।

tathānnamūrtimāpannāṃstānapi kramaśo yajet ।
alakādyaṃ hi vai bhāṇḍaṃ pūritaṃ gālitāmbhasā ।।

madhudarbhatilopetaṃ kṛtvānnaṃ tatra vai smaret ।
mantreśaṃ candrabimbasthamamūrtamamitadyutim ।।

bahiḥ svasminnullasantaṃ dhyāyettenāṃbhasā saha ।
kumbhādutkīryamāṇena nirmalaṃ śītaśīkaram ।।

ādāyātha karābhyāṃ tu prāktilaṃ madhusaṃplutam ।
āpūryāpūrya caikasya śraddhayā parayā dvija ।।

tilān stena bhāgavanāsahitena ca ।
pitṝṇāṃ kramaśo dadyāt tṛptayeṃbha stu mantritān ।।

atha prāṅmukhapūrvāṇāṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ samācaret ।
pūrvavat saviśeṣaṃ hi svaśrāddhe śraddhayānvitam ।।

sarvāṅgikaṃ kramādvipra āpādānmastakāvadhi ।
ardhyāmbumiśritaiḥ puṣpaiścandanādyairvilepanaiḥ ।।

tataḥ sa pakṣavyajanaisteṣāmudbodhya mārutam ।
nivedya vividhān paścādvastrān dhūpādhivasitān ।।

tatā alaṃkṛtya vai śaktyā kaṅkaṇādyairvibhūṣitaiḥ ।
upavītān sottarīyān dadyātteṣāmanantaram ।।

śiromālyāni śubhrāṇi tataḥ kaṇṭhastrajāni ca ।
divyagandhaṃ tataḥ kṣodaṃ mūrdhni karpūramiśritam ।।

tato nivedya vai teṣāṃ nayanāñjanamuttamam ।
darśayeddarpaṇaṃ paścāt purataḥ kusumān kṣipet ।।

sugandhadhūpapūtena tatastān dhūpayet kramāt ।
suprakāśena dīpena pūjanīyā mahāmate ।।

upānahau teṣāṃ chattrāṇi vividhāni ca ।
pādukāḥ pādapīṭhāni āsanāni ca tāni ca ।।

śayanāni vicitrāṇi śibikāśvādi caiva hi ।
kalpanīyāni sarveṣāṃ kṛtvā tadrajatadi ca ।।

tanmūlamathavā śaktyā sarveṣāṃ vinivedya ca ।
samavāyaśca sādhāraścetasaḥ parituṣṭaye ।।

punarardhyodakaṃ pāṇau datvā mantraṃ samuccaran ।
kuryāt saṃpūjanaṃ teṣāṃ bhagavadyāgavat kramāt ।।

madhuparkeṇa cānnena śraddhayā vividhena ca ।
bhakṣaiḥ saphalamūlaistu pāvanaiḥ pānakaistataḥ ।।

rasālābhiḥ sugandhābhiḥ śṛtena payasā saha ।
bhakṣitaścāgrataḥ sarvamalpakeṣu puṭeṣu vā ।।

prītaye akhilaviprāṇāṃ samaṃ kṛtvā nivedya ca ।
prāgvadardhyodakaṃ pāṇau dadyāt saṃprāśanāya ca ।।

saṃsmaran manasā mantraṃ pratipadya dvijāmbhasā ।
japan dhyāyaṃstathāstraṃ ca āste agre nānyamānasaḥ ।।

kalāṃ vai tuṣṭaye teṣāṃ sukhabodhamahāphalam ।
tapā dhikaṃ ?dharmaśāstraṃ mokṣaśāstramathottamam ।।

uddhoṣayan guṇāṃsta yasyopayujyate ।
nivedanīyaṃ tattasya atha tṛpte dvije ।।

pūrvavaccānusandhāne saṃpanne sati sarvadā ।
kuryādudakadānaṃ tu bhūyaḥ santarpayed dvija ।।

piṇḍadānāvaśiṣṭena annena saha vāriṇā ।
madhuparkatilakṣīrairājyasavyañjanena ca ।।

karāñjaliṃ ca saṃpūrya kṣipet piṇḍaṃ tato bahiḥ ।
dvijānāmagrataścāpi saha codakadhārayā ।।

kṣiped uttaradigbhāgān ninayed antakāspadam ।
pavitrakaṃ parityāgaṃ kṛtvātha pratiśāṭakam ।।

tadvāsaḥ parivartyātha ūrdhvaṃ vā saṃsmaran hṛdi ।
svamantreṇācamet paścād hṛnmantreṇāmalātmanā ।।

saṃpannamastu bhoḥ sarvaṃ codayed āsanasthitān ।
dvijān saṃpatacitāṃstu dadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ ।।

atha pūrvavad abdānām ācartavyaṃ yathākramam ।
prāṅmukhābhyāṃ vinā sarvair ācartavyam ataḥ sthitaiḥ ।।

dadyāt tābhyāṃ tadante atha sarvamuddhṛtya codanam ।
pātre saphalamūlaṃ ca madhvājyatilabhāvitam ।।

dvija nāṃ codanaṃ kuryād bhuktaśeṣasya sāṃpratam ।
ucyatāṃ viniyogaṃ bhoḥ prabrūyuste hyanākulāḥ ।।

uddhṛtaṃ tvasmadīyaṃ vai bhāṇḍasthaṃ vibhavecchayā ।
atha paitāmahīyaṃ yat pūjitaṃ cānnagolakam ।।

tasmin kiṃgehamānīyaṃ pṛthak kṛtya sphuliṅgavat ।
svadehāddrecakenaiva tvanusandhāya vai tataḥ ।।

dhyātvāamṛtapuṭāntastham amṛtāṃśusamaṃ hṛdā ।
kṛtvā dviṣaṭkajaptaṃ tu praṇatāyā dvijecchayā ।।

pratipādya svajāyāyāḥ śeṣaṃ brāhmaṇakāmyayā ।
viniyujyopasaṃhṛtya goṣvāpasvā dvijānale ।।

aṃṣaṭ bhojanapātrāṇāṃ kṛtvā prāgjvalanaṃ tataḥ ।
tatra vā bhagavatyagre satilaṃ codakāla kam ।।

sahiraṇyaṃ kramād dadyāt pitṛbhyaḥ prīṇanāya ca ।
rakṣayecca sṛgālebhyaḥ sāṃprataṃ kamalodbhava ।।

pitṛkarmaṇi mā tre asiman samyak sthāna kriyātmake ।
kriyānnaiḥ prāpaṇīpaiṇḍī nirvartyā bhojanād anu ।।

nākṣayyāṃ vācayet prītim uddiṣṭe apyudakakriyām ।
na pūrṇāhutidānaṃ ca na codak parivartanam ।।

paitryaṃ pātram athoddhāṭya svamantraṃ hṛtkuśeśayāt ।
virecya devāyānnena kalpāntārkānaladyuti ।।

tatpātraṃ gaganoddeśe tad dūre dviṣaḍaṅgulāt ।
dvādaśāntaṃ hi tatpitryaṃ pātrād aikyaṃ yathākramam ।।

saṃpaśyetāṃśca mantreśān dhyāyed dhyānadhiyā pitṝn ।
pātaṃ hi sāba laṃ tadvanniśi dīptānalācalaṃ ।।

evam ekatvam āpannāḥ saha mantreṇa tena te ।
śaśāṅkaśatasaṅkāśam atha mantreśvaraṃ harim ।।

nirastāvayavaṃ dhyātvā śaktayastatatra vaiṣṭarāḥ ।
pitṛvyūhavad ālīnaṃ kṛtvā tadanu mantrarāṭ ।।

ātmasāt pitṛmārgeṇa tatra tenodakena ca ।
visṛ jya nayane bhūyaḥ sapatnīko dṛśābjaja ।।

jalāyaiva ca nikṣipya prāgdattaṃ saha vāriṇā ।
kṣā ntānalagataṃ devaṃ samāsādyārcanālayam ।।

mantreśam arcayitvā ca pūrvavat prīṇayed dvija ।
tatastadupahāra kṛtvā bhojanam ācaret ।।

bāndhavaiḥ saha mantreśaṃ dhyāyan hṛtpuṣkarodare ।
yatavāg amṛtaprakhyairgrāsaiḥ tadanu pauṣkara ।।

nirucchiṣṭe tu bhūbhāge kṛte saṃkṣālane tataḥ ।
so danaṃ vyañjanīyaṃ yadduḥkhā ।।

tamāhṛtyāparasmin vai pātre darbhatilānvite ।
kṣiped dīpadvitīyaṃ tadbahirvai dakṣiṇena ca ।।

smaranmantraṃ śucau deśe datvā darbhāstaraṃ tataḥ ।
nayed dharmakathābhistu yogya ।।

ityevaṃ vidhināṃ śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vihitaṃ dvija ।
saṃsāraduḥkhaśamanam acirād apavargadam ।।

kṛtam ekaprakāraṃ ca śraddhayā cobhayātmakam ।
datvā jñānakriyānata ? yācopayujyate ।।

lokadharmasthitā sā saṃpūraṇe yāti vāsanām ।
tasmāccitraprasādaṃ vai jāyate yena karmaṇā ।।

ācartavyaṃ prayatnena mantrajairvitatāptaye ।
athamana[saḥ]saṃskāraṃ saṃpannānāṃ samācaret ।।

aurdhvadehikasaṃjñaṃ tu vyāpāraṃ samanantaram ।
pūrvoktaphalasiddhayarthaṃ tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।

taccāpi dviguṇaṃ viddhi dvividhaṃ kamalodbhava ।
sā dīkṣitānāṃ sarveṣāṃ muktānāmamṛtādikai ।।

vyaktādivṛttisthāneṣu hitaṃ nityaṃ tameva hi ।
prāgvad ārādhite mantre śraddhayā saṃpradattavat ।।

ātṛpteḥ bhagavatprītiparyantam amalekṣaṇa ।
dvitīyam amalāgre tu mantreśe sannidhīkṛte ।।

odanenātmakenaiva bhojanaṃ kriyayojjhitam ।
āhṛṣṭer alpasatvānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sarvadā hitam ।।

jvaladavyaktabījāntaṃ niviṣṭhaṃ vartate tataḥ ।
saumyavṛtti sasūkṣmaṃśca prāṇaśaktiparaṃśca san ।।

tad daśāṃśaṃ hi vai kālaṃ bāhyaṃ ca dinalakṣaṇam ।
samāśritya krameṇaiva kartā tadanukalpavān ।।

tatprāṇāṃśānuviddhā vyaktam indriyalakṣaṇam ।
āpādayati cāvyaktād annamūrticchalena tu ।।

śrotrendriyādikāścaiva upasthendriyapaścimāḥ ।
yamāśritya labhetāśu samatīte daśāhike ।।

ekādaśe ahni viprendra asmin śaktitvameva hi ।
trayāstriṃśāhikenaiva brahman vyaktareṇa tu ।।

vināḍi satyapūrveṇa tatprāṇāṃśena vai punaḥ ।
dviṣaṭkalakṣaṇenaiva śeṣaṃ tattvagaṇaṃ dvija ।।

buddhitatvāndhakāraṃ tu vyañjanīyaṃ yathākramam ।
prāk saṃvatsare buddhi dvitīyena tato dvija ।।

tatastvāśabdatanmātrāt pañcabhiḥ pañcakaṃ tu vai ।
tanmātrāṇāṃ vyañjanīyamākāśādyam ataḥ param ।।

māsānāṃ pañcakenaiva kṣmāntaṃ vai bhūtapañcakam ।
tataḥ sacele saṃpanne sthā bhuktojjhitaṃ tathā ।।

dantakāṣṭhe hṛdā pīte pañcagavyena te punaḥ ।
mantre tu vidhivat sthāne prāvṛte cāmbare tathā ।।

samācamya hṛdā nyasya mūlaṃ pāṇitale tataḥ ।
āmūrdhayātha tenaiva sakapalīkṛtya vigraham ।।

saṃkṣepeṇa niraṅgeṇa tato hṛnmantramantritāḥ ।
sagotravihitaṃ vipra pretānugrahakāmyayā ।।

toyāñjaliṃtrayaṃ dadyāt tannāmnā satilaṃ dvija ।
darbhā rājatasammiśram amunā tasya vai tataḥ ।।

śuddhaye śubhaśāntyarthaṃ japed aṣṭādhikaṃ śatam ।
svamantrād astramantraṃ vā sāmānyaṃ dvādaśākṣaram ।।

navātmabījasaṅghātam ekaṃ vā bhāvanāvaśāt ।
pravartetātha vidhivat pūrvoddiṣṭe tu karmaṇi ।।

tīrthoddeśe nadītare gṛhe bā'yatane śabhe ।
atīva śreyasaṃ dvābhyāṃ pretaśrāddhaṃ yate t dvija ।।

vighnavyūhatamorūpaṃ samāsādyā ?sphurādikam ।
vyavasāyavighātaṃ ca nyūnaṃ kuryācca karmaṇām ।।

tasmāt saṃrakṣaṇīyaṃ ca brahmamanbra balena tu ।
bhāsvareṇa tamorūpam āmūlād vai svakaṃ balam ।।

tiladarbhādikaṃ sarvaṃ mantreṇārādhya vai purā ।
etannirasyānyaḥ ?kā prāṅmukhaścotthitastataḥ ।।

sāṃprataṃ sarvasāmānyaṃ kuryāt sthānaparigraham ।
brahmabhāvanayā mūlamantraṃ sarvagataṃ smaret ।।

vasudhāgaganābhyāṃ tu aṣṭadikṣvantare smaret ।
prabhākaravad ābhāsā mūrtirddṛnmantramabjaja ।।

dhyāyedgaganamāntrātam akhilaṃ śirasā tataḥ ।
stambhabhūtaṃ śivaṃ madhye madhye saṃsāramārgavat ।।

brahmanāḍīsvarūpaṃ tu dhyātavyam amalaṃ mahat ।
kalpanālakṣaṇe bāhye vartma sadvastu vinyaset ।।

saṃśāntakarmabrahmabhyām anyonyasya tu vedane ।
gavākṣavat smaret tatra dvārabhūtaṃ tu locanam ।।

bhramad vahni sphulliṅgo sahastraparirājitam ।
rājahaṃsapadāntaṃ ca tato dhyāyet suvighnaham ।।

evam āyatanaṃ mantramūrtimantraṃ mayoditam ।
ādhārāsanapūrvāṇāṃ mantrāṇāṃ sarvakarmaṇām ।।

haṃsoparamaniṣṭhānāṃ siddhaye bhāvitātmanām ।
na tatrāntaṃ sthitiṃ ? kuryānmantranyāsaṃ yathāvidhi ।।

upaviśyāsane dārbhe praṇavavyāptibhāvite ।
mūlamantreṇa niṣpādya prāṇāyāmaṃ trilakṣaṇam ।।

dhāraṇādvitayenātha dehasaṃskāram ācaret ।
mantranyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt pūrvavat karadehayoḥ ।।

arghyaṃ pādyaṃ samāsādya prokṣayet ca tadambhasā ।
sarvamantreṇa santāya darbhakāṇḍagatena ca ।।

nirīkṣya proccarestatra dagdhaṃ tattejasā smaret ।
mūlena ravibhākāntim āpannam atha bhāvayet ।।

sānalāṃ sendhanāṃ cullīṃ prokṣayed astravāriṇā ।
jvālayen netramantreṇa tataścodbodhya varmaṇā ।।

prakṣālyāstrāmbhasā sthālīṃ tāḍayet tadanantaram ।
kṛtvāmbudarbhamūlena sthagayed atha varmaṇā ।।

taṇḍulān astramantreṇa kṣālayitvā punaḥ punaḥ ।
madhvājyatilagokṣīrayuktaṃ mūlena nikṣipet ।।

darvyārastramantranyastāyā śrapayed hṛdayena tu ।
siddham uttārayet paścānmūlamantreṇa mantravit ।।

prakṣālyālipya netreṇa śikhāmantreṇa vai tataḥ ।
dikṣūrdhvapuṇḍrīkṛtya prāk kavacenāvakuṇṭhya ca ।।

praṇavādhiṣṭhite kuryāt saṃsthitaṃ ca kuśāstare ।
sūpalipte tu bhūbhāge tilākṣatasamanvite ।।

pidhāya ca astramantreṇa tvevaṃ niṣpādya vai carum ।
taṃ susādhanakāle tu brahmāstaraṇakarmaṇām ।।

hṛnmantraṃ saṃprayoktavyaṃ mantramārge japan dhiyā ।
pretakāryaṃ tataḥ kuryāt ? vā tena laukikam ।।

tatra divye purā mantraṃ pūrvavat saṃprapūjya ca ।
vidhivat pretamuddiśya bhogaiḥ pūrvoktalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

puruṣāśanamātreṇa pātrasā cakrajaṃ hi yat ।
sarvānnena samāpūrya abhyaktādyena vai hṛdā ।।

dṛśāgninā tu saṃspṛśya kṛtvā savyañjanaṃ tu vai ।
vinivedya vibhoḥ proktaṃ tadanugrahakāmyayā ।।

svaśabdamūrtiṃ suvyaktāmoṅkāreṇāthavāmbarāt ।
pretaṃ svanāmnā tvāhṛtya kṛtvā hṛdvayomni taṃtu ?tat ।।

īṣan nirvāṇaśeṣāgnikaṇabhūtaṃ vicintya ca ।
kiñcitprāṇakalāyuktaṃ karmāṇir ca vaśīkṛtam ।।

viśeṣasattāmātraṃ ca śanaiścānalavartmanā ।
bahirnivedya svasthāne mantradṛk viṣaye sthite ।।

bhāvayet praṇavenātha tattvaśaktigaṇānvitam ।
annavīryāśritaṃ brahman prāṇākhyam avinaśvaram ।।

tatastadūṣmamārgeṇa hṛnmantreṇa tu saṃsmaran ।
pretaṃ śrotrendriyacchannaprāṇavattvād vinirgatam ।।

īṣadbhāvasvarūpaṃ tu viddhi jñānānurañjitam ।
pretena saha caikatvaṃ samāpannaṃ ca tattvataḥ ।।

cintayet tena taṃ vipra kiṃcid hṛdigataṃ kramāt ।
evaṃ śrotrendriyairvyaktaprāṇaikai katvamāgataiḥ ।।

sāṃprataṃ kamalodbhūta samūlamakhilaṃ hitam ।
līnamannotthite prāṇe smartavyaṃ vai yathānilam ।।

nighātavadamūrtaṃ tu prāṇaśaktyā dvijeritam ।
tadindriyamavadhyāyed hṛdā hṛnmantratāṃ gatam ।।

āsīnā māsane tvāṃ te pūrvavadvayāptibhāvite ।
yajenmantreśavat paścāt śaśvadarghyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

puṣpānulepanaiv dhūpair mātrāntaiḥ kamalodbhava ।
dadyāt tilodakaṃ paścānnāmnā gotreṇa vai hṛdā ।।

athānalāśrayāntasthaṃ hṛnmūrtiṃ tu tam indriyam ।
tarpayitvā yathānyāyaṃ pūrvoktena krameṇa tu ।।

samāhūya tataḥ pātraṃ pūrvoktaṃ bhagavanmayam ।
niveśya bhagavatyagre tvāsane pūrvavat smṛte ।।

nyastamantraṃ hṛdā kṛtvā tvarghyādyair arcayet tataḥ ।
yāyād ārādhanoddeśam upaviśya yathāsukham ।।

hṛdā tam indriye dhyāyet svaśaktyā mūrtatāṃ gatam ।
rasātmanānnaśaktau tu vibhāgena ca sthitam ।।

dhyātavyaṃ pūrvavat pretaṃ smartavyaṃ praṇavena tu ।
annādhiṣṭhātṛbhāvena nītvā ca pratipadya ca ।।

dvijendrasya ca mantrāntaṃ saha cārghyodakena tu ।
atha tatprāṇaśaktau tu hṛdā vaikātmatāṃ gatam ।।

naivedyaṃ ga ?narantastaṃ ? pretaṃ kamalasambhava ।
tatastad hṛdayākāśaṃ prāṇena saha vai kramāt ।।

vyaktaye śrautravṛttau tu prayātam anubhāvayet ।
evaṃ labdhātmakaṃ kṛtvā pretaṃ prāgvipravigrahe ।।

dadyāt tadodakaṃ pāṇau pūrvavat prāśanāya ca ।
saṃpravṛttasya vai tasya bhojane saṃśayasya ca ।।

dhyāyan dhiyāgratastiṣṭhed annavīryādbalena tu ।
hṛdā śrotrendriyāt tasya tathārthatvam upāgatam ।।

niṣpannabhojanasyaiva dvijendrasya dvijottama ।
svadehāt praṇavaṃ śabdaṃrecya dakṣiṇavartmanā ।।

vipra hṛtkamalākāśe pretam ākṛṣya tena vai ।
yathāmṛtena svahṛdā śrotre sattāsamanvitam ।।

apanīte tvathocchiṣṭe prīṇanaṃ pūrvavad vibhoḥ ।
vihitaṃ vipraśārdūla kartātha kṛtabhojanaḥ ।।

astraṃ vighnādiśāntyarthaṃ japed aṣṭādhikaṃ śatam ।
sāṅgam ārādhanasthānaṃ kuryānmantreśamā vān ।।

saṃhṛtya sārghyapuṣpādyaṃ svarāntam akhilaṃ hi yat ।
jalāśaye vinikṣitya kuryātsvāya ।।

tato mantrasamādhānaṃ sa japaṃ tu niśāgame ।
evaṃ cakṣū ?rasānāṃ ca ghrāṇasaṃjñaṃ catuṣṭayam ।।

catuṣkeṇa dinānāṃ tu vyañjanīyaṃ mahāmate ।
pañcakaṃ tvathā vāgādyaṃ krameṇa śirasā tataḥ ।।

pretaśreyāptaye kuryāt labdhasatta?dvijottama ।
ekādaśe atha divase saṃprāpte sādhayet yarum ।।

sabhakṣavyañnopetaṃ śraddhayā ca susaṃyutam ।
prakṣālitāṃghriṃ svācāntaṃ tāḍitaṃ cāvalokitam ।।

acchāmbupūtapraṇataṃ bhagavattattvabhāvitam ।
niveśyāsanavāre ca pūjite vyāptibhāvite ।।

samālabhya tato bhaktyā candanādyairvilepanaiḥ ।
sadvastraveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā yathāśaktyā vibhūṣayet ।।

hemakaṅkaṇapūrvaistu saratnairbhūṣaṇottamaiḥ ।
mālyairyajñopavītādyaiḥ śirovastraiḥ sapāvanaiḥ ।।

bhakṣyavyañjanahastaṃ tat kṛtvā mantreśam aryayet ।
śraddhayā parayā viprapretānugrahakāmyayā ।।

kṛtvā bhavanaparyantaṃ pūrvam ārādhanaṃ prabhoḥ ।
samācarettato mantranyāsaṃ vipravarasya ca ।।

ubhe haste tato mūlam aṅgulīṣu hṛdādayaḥ ।
netraṃ sarvanakhāgrāṇāṃ dehe tvāmastakāttataḥ ।।

nyastvā pādāvasāne ca svasthāneṣu hṛdādayaḥ ।
dhyātvā mantrasvarūpaṃ ca tadā tadabhimānayuk ।।

pitṛsaṃjñāsametena natinā praṇavena ca ।
pūjayitvārghyapuṣpādyaiḥ saviśeṣaistu pūrvavat ।।

pratipādyākhilaṃ tasya mṛ topakaraṇaṃ hi yat ।
gobhūhemāvasānaṃ ca toṣameti ca yena tat ।।

jāyate nirṛṇaṃ pretaṃ[samyukta]paraṃ padam ।
yathāvadbhojanenāthatarpaṇīyaṃ ca pūrvavat ।।

vyāpāraṃ hṛdayaṃ prāgvanmūlamantreṇa bhāvayet ।
kintvindriyagaṇāntasthaṃ samāyālakṣaṇaṃ hi tat ।।

praṇavaṃ mūlamantreṇa pretaṃ sarvatra saṃsmaret ।
evaṃ prāptāsmitaṃ samyagyuktam indriyaśaktibhiḥ ।।

buddhipūrvairdharāntaistu kṛtvaitam anurañjayet ।
budhyārtham ācaret tatra śikhāmantreṇa cālikhet ।।

vyaktaye manasaścaiva kavacaṃ vihitaṃ dvija ।
tanmātrāṇāṃ vyaktaye atha pañcānāmatha vai kramāt ।।

bhūtānām astrāmantraṃ tu vāditāṃ ? santataṃ hi nam ।
māsadvādaśakenaiva daśaikādaśakena tu ।।

pretam āpādya vai piṇḍaṃ prāpte māse trayodaśe ।
yojanā pitṛmārge tu kāryāsya bhagavanmaye ।।

yathā tathābjasaṃbhūta śṛṇu me gadataḥ sphaṭam ।
snānaṃ pūrve samākhyātaṃ paścāttadanu sādhayet ।।

śrāddhārthaṃ śraddhayānaṃ tu prabhūtaṃ ca susaṃskṛtam ।
svācāntānatha dhautāṅghrīn dvijendrān upaveśayet ।।

putrakān samayajñān vā sādhakānatha deśikān ।
gṛhasthān brahmacārīn vā vanasthānathavā yatīn ।।

sammukhān mantranāthasya catvāro vāpyudaṅmukhan ।
evaṃ pūrvānane dve tu viniveśya dvijottama ।।

tayorekasya cāstreṇa sakalīkaraṇaṃ hi yat ।
varmaṇātha dvitīyasya nyāsakarma vidhīyate ।।

udaṅmukhebhyastvādyasya nyāsakarmaṇi locanam ।
tasmāduparisaṃsthāsya śirasā vihitaṃ dvija ।।

hṛnmantreṇa dvitīyasya mūlamantreṇa vai tataḥ ।
ācartavyaṃ caturthasya hastanyāsādikaṃ hi yat ।।

ṣaṇṇām atha śikhāmantraṃ svā dyakhātapa vinyaset ।
tato agnibhavanāntaṃ tu kṛtvā bhagavadarcanam ।।

pūjayet saviśeṣaṃ tu kṛtvaivaṃ hi yathoditam ।
astranyastaṃ tato astreṇa pūjanīyaṃ dvijottama ।।

varmaṇā varmamūrtiṃ ca nāmagotradvayaṃ vinā ।
tataḥ svanāmnā gotreṇa kuryād anyeṣu cārcanam ।।

svena svena tu mantreṇa tatra pretaṃ dvijaṃ hi yat ।
netramantrakṛtanyāsaṃ tattenaiva samarcayet ।।

tasyoparyupaviṣṭaṃ tu saṃsthitaṃ pitṛlakṣaṇam ।
pūjane vihitaṃ tasya śiromantraṃ svakaṃ dvija ।।

vipra hṛnmantram abhyarcya yattadviddhi pitāmaham ।
pretaṃ tasyārcanaṃ kuryānnāmnā gotreṇa vai hṛdā ।।

mūlamantrakṛtanyāsaṃ tadviddhi pratitāmaham ।
mānanīyaṃ hi tenaiva nāmnā gotreṇa vai saha ।।

teṣāṃ vai hṛdgataṃ vipra pūjitānāṃ ca sāṃpratam ।
pretādipitṛkḷptasya kāryā cāntasthayojanā ।।

yathā tatpadmasaṃbhūta mattaḥ samavadhāraya ।
naivedyanāśaṃ kramaśaḥ prāgvadannarasātmanām ।।

svayaṃ devagaṇaṃ cintyaṃ samaṃ dhyāyed dhiyā tataḥ ।
ajahan svāśrayaṃ bhaktyā pūrṇendvā ?sakulyatām ।।

sāmā ?paitre annamātraṃ tu netramantraṃ vicintya ca ।
evameva śiromantramupayātaṃ dhiyā smaret ।।

saha locanaśaktyā tu pātre hṛnmantrabhāvite ।
dve śaktī netramūrdhvākhye samādāyātha hṛnmayīm ।।

śaktiṃ vai mūlamantrīyairnaivedyāntargatāṃ smaret ।
mantraśakticchalenaiva sānnena praṇavātmanā ।।

mantrabrahmaṇi caikatvaṃ kuryādvā tasya pauṣkara ।
pratipādyātha vai svasmin nītvā naivedyabhājanam ।।

dvijānām upaviṣṭānāṃ bhakṣyabhojyādikaiḥ saha ।
gokṣīramātraparyante dadyātpāṇau tato dakam ।।

bhojane saṃpravṛttānāṃ yasya yaccopayujyate ।
pṛṣṭvā pṛṣṭvā ca dadyādvai pitṝṇāṃ tṛptaye dvija ।।

svāhāntānāṃ tatasteṣāṃ tatra sthānaṃ samācaret ।
ekatvaṃ tviti śaktīnāṃ vidhinānena pauṣkara ।।

tattvaśaktiguṇopetaṃ pradīptamiva bhāskaran ।
sāṃprataṃ pūrvavatpretaṃ āhṛtya dvidvivigrahāt ।।

recya hṛtkamale mantratejasā tena tatpunaḥ ।
kuryādyuktataraṃ caiva tasmādākṛṣya vai hṛdi ।।

paitāmahe virecyātha hṛtpadmopari vṛddhaye ।
tasmāduddhṛtya saṃtṛptaṃ hṛdā kuryācca vai hṛdi ।।

pratitāmahahṛtpadmagocarau viniveśya ca ।
mantrabrahmakalādīptaṃ kṛtvā tatrānayet hṛdi ।।

vilāpya praṇavenātha śāntabhāvanayātmani ।
evaṃ kṛtvānusandhānaṃ tataḥ prabhṛti tasya vai ।।

pitṛtvaṃ vātsare śrāddhe kāla[diṣṭe]viśeṣataḥ ।
mṛtānāṃ ca vihitā vatsare gate ।।

nānyeṣāṃ dvijaśārdūla pitṝṇāṃ śrāddhakāṅkṣiṇām ।
pretatvamupaśānta vai jantorvāgrasthitasya ca ।।

pitṛtvaṃ labdha[ ?saṃskāraṃ]saṃsthitaṃ cottarottaram ।
evamuktaṃ hi sāṅgena mantreṇa kamalodbhava ।।

aurdhvadaihikasaṃjñaṃ tu vidhānaṃ bhāvināmatha ।
caturbhiścāturātmīyairmantraistadvinibodha me ।।

śrotrādyupasthaparyantam indriyāṇāṃ dvipañcakam ।
āpādya vāsudevākhyaṃ mantreṇa daśabhirdinaiḥ ।।

asmin vyaktimataḥ kuryāt sāṅkarṣaṇena pauṣkara ।
buddhitattve tṛtīyena vā vyañjayenmanasā saha ।।

kṣmāntam ākāśatanmātrād aniruddhena pauṣkara ।
pūrvavad vyañjanīyaṃ ca evaṃ saṃvatsare gate ।।

sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kuryād aniruddhāditaḥ kramāt ।
caturbhirvāsudevāntairmantrairmantravidāṃ vara ।।

evam icchennavātmajñaḥ samūrtinavakena yat ।
saṃvidhānaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha bāndhavānāṃ śubhāptaye ।।

tadidānīṃ samāsena ekāgram avadhāraya ।
śrotrādīnām indriyāṇāṃ tṛptaye kṣmādharaṃ smṛtam ।।

bhūgā dīnāṃ nṛsiṃhaṃ tu asmin śaktau khagāsane ।
vyaktaye brahmatattvaṃ tu buddhe samanasāṃ ?hitam ।।

tanmātrāṇāṃ sabhūtānāṃ mantrāṇāṃ dhāraṇātmakam ।
evaṃ tattvakalāyuktaṃ japaṃ kṛtvā mahāmate ।।

pañcabhistu varāhādyaiḥ tataḥ saṃvatsare gate ।
caturbhir aniruddhādyaiḥ pitṛbhāvanam ānayet ।।

pūrvoktena vidhānena jñānadhyānānvitena ca ।
divyenānaśvareṇaiva karmaṇānekasādhanam ।।

saṃvidhānaṃ dvitīyaṃ tatproktaṃ saṃsūcitaṃ mayā ।
tanme sphuṭataraṃ kṛsvā gadataścāvadhāraya ।।

sarvaṃ pūrvoditaṃ kṛtvā vidhānaṃ sādhane caroḥ ।
prajvālya pāvakaṃ kuryāt prāgvatsaṃskārasaṃskṛtam ।।

dhyātvā tadantarmantreśaṃ samidbhiktarpayet kramāt ।
tadagrato dakṣiṇāgrān kuśān āstīrya pūrvavat ।।

savāsam āsanaṃ dhyātvā tadūrdhve kamalāsanam ।
yuktam ādyādikaiḥ prāgvad vinyased annagolakam ।।

tasmin pūrvoditaṃ sarvam āpādya tadanantaram ।
pretanāmnā tadagre atha satilānudakāñjalīn ।।

dattvātha copasaṃhṛtya vinikṣapya jalāntare ।
kṛtvātha saha mantreṇa ātmasādasanaṃ dvija ।।

jale akhilaṃ samāhṛtya vinikṣipyānalaṃ vinā ।
daśāhamevaṃ niṣpādya prāgvadekādaśe ahani ।।

śrāddhaṃ kuryād vidhānajñaḥ piṇḍadānapurassaram ।
saṃvatsare atha niṣpanne pitṛtvāpādanāya ca ।।

dhyānaṃ samantraṃ pūrvoktaṃ[?tatpitṛ]tvādhikaṃ bhavet ।
bhāsvajjvalanasaṃkāśaṃ samarthaikatvamāgatam ।।

tadadhyakṣatvabhūtaṃ yanmantramadhyātmalakṣaṇam ।
adhibhūtam athāpannaṃ piṇḍaṃ nirgatya saṃsmaret ।।

tadūrdhvadeśe nabhasi vyāpāraṃ sannirīkṣayet ।
evam annātpṛthaṅnīte viprete kamalodbhava ।।

tanmantreṇa ca tatpiṇḍād adhibhūtamayād atha ।
samādāyannamuṣṭiṃ ca tatra tat khaṇḍitaṃ ca yat ।।

smaretpariṇataṃ samyam vyāpakatvena sāṃpratam ।
athādibhūtaṃ cādhyātmam adhidaivam athābjaja ।।

tadannaṃ pitṛpiṇḍe tu tadūrdhve atha sthitaṃ nayet ।
evam ekatvam āpanne prete citpratinā saha ।।

pretapiṇḍavad abjottha vācartavyaṃ hi cākhilam ।
vyāpāramatha tasyātha tasmātpaitāmahe tataḥ ।।

tasmāt tadapi tatprāgvatparatāṃ nayet ।
yathokte asmin dvijaśreṣṭha prājāpatye tu karmaṇi ।।

āde kādaśādyāvat pitṛtvāpādane dinam ।
tāvatpūrvoditaṃ śeṣaṃ yattatpūrvaṃ samācaret ।।

kintu bhojanabhūmau tu dvijaptairāsanasthitaiḥ ।
vacanīyaṃ hi cākṣayyaṃ tilamiśreṇa vāriṇā ।।

etāvatāsya tātparyaṃ yathāvatsaṃprakāśitam ।
aurdhvadaihikasaṃjñasya vyā sātvikam ।।

āsṛṣṭe sati rāgau ca?yathā spharati vai hṛdi ।
pratyayāvayavau caiva pauṣkara ।।

balyarthaṃ vihitaṃ teṣām annaṃ piṇḍaṃ tu sodakam ।
pretakriyāvidhau caiva svaṃ svaṃ kāla kulocitaṃ ।।

cāturmānaniṣedhaṃ ca vihitaṃ sūtakādike ।
pratiṣedhaṃ gṛhīturvai ābhūtād abjasaṃbhava ।।

dvijendrāṇāṃ tu sanyeṣāṃ cāturātmyaikayājinām ।
ārādhyānāṃ prabha vācca nāstīti dvijasattama ।।

ata evādhikāraṃ tu mṛtake sūtake tu vā ।
pratigrahe pradāne ca tatkālaṃ saṅkaraṃ vinā ।।

sahajā pratipattirvai ityeṣāmarayājinām ।
bhagavadyājināṃ caiva nissandigdhā parasparam ।।

mārgam icchati yastvevam anusartṛṃ hi cācyutam ।
āśaucaṃ samatītaṃ cettataḥ kuryād daśāhikam ।।

ityuktam abjasaṃbhūta sara[?hasyaṃ]yathā sthitam ।
saṃpradānādikaṃ śaśvat śrāddhāvaraṇam uttamam ।।

atha kāmya śrāddhavidhiḥ 

vidhyantaram atho bhūyaḥ prasaṅgād avadhāraya ।
svargāpavargaphaladaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

vyavahārapadasthaṃ yadvicchinnā śastra ? bandhubhiḥ ।
svayam icchati vaikastu dvādaśāhādvijākhilam ।।

tadidānīṃ samāsena yathāvatkathayāmyaham ।
purā saṃbhatasaṃbhāraḥ susahāyaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।।

manaḥ prasādajanakam evaṃ vā bahavo dvijāḥ ।
puraskṛtya dine śubhre pitṛpakṣāttu vai purā ।।

prāvṛṭkāle tu vācyatra śaratkāle tu mādhave ।
yāyād āyātanaṃ viṣṇoḥ puṣpadhūpajanākulam ।।

kūlaṃ nadanadīnāṃ vā sānvādyaṃ sodakaṃ gireḥ ।
nirātaṅkam asaṅkīrṇaṃ śvapākaśabarādikaiḥ ।।

tamāsādya tapaḥ kuryād yāgaṃ ca vidhipūrvakam ।
gaṇe ca nāgasthāne ca bhūtānāṃ ca vanaspateḥ ।।

kṣetravāsimukhenaiva yathāśaktyā sadakṣiṇām ।
apare ahani vai kuryāt svamantrārādhanaṃ tu vai ।।

[viṣṇorā]yatanasthaṃ ca mantram ajñātalakṣaṇam ।
vyaktaṃ vāpyarcanīyaṃ ca prārthayetta danantaram ।।

vibhoḥ praṇamate dhyakṣaṃ svacid bījānvitasya ca ।
vyaktāvyaktā[dya]saṃjñasya piṇḍam indriya[saṃjñitam] ।।

sthāpayāmi satattvāṃśaiḥ saṃdhayitvā yathāvidhi ।
bhedarūpam abhinnaṃ ca[kā]yātmāṃśucayasya ca ।।

sukṛtasya ca bhogārtham anyathā parameśvara ।
samutkrāntasya me dehāt sthitaṃ mārutalakṣaṇam ।।

saduḥkhāyā bhilāṣā ca dhanena ca samāvṛtā ।
jāyate saṃbhramopetā dīrghakālavadakṣayā ।।

niṣkriyā ca tathā jantorvaśā[?pyavaśā]sya ca ।
dehāntareṇa cāptena śaśvatkālāntareṇa vā ।।

sā sthitā dussahā ghora tattvato yāti saṃkṣayam ।
tvatprasādād ato nātha śīghram annaṃ jalena tu ।।

piṇḍam indriyasaṃjñaṃ yanniṣpādyaṃ tannirāmayam ।
niḥsantānastvasaṃdehaṃ nirāśaḥ karmajālagaḥ ।।

adhikṛtya tvamevādya karoti trāṇam ātmanā ।
patitānāṃ nirāśānāṃ nārakāṇāṃ parā gatiḥ ।।

tvameva luptapiṇḍānāṃ śaśvad uddharaṇakṣamaḥ ।
yatastvame tat śaśvad[nā]rabhya sanātana ।।

niṣpattidinaparyantaṃ vighnajālaṃ savāsanam ।
mama māyātu bhagavan karmasiddhirmamāstu vai ।।

evam abhyarthayitvājaṃ karamāpūrya vāriṇā ।
kuryāt tat śeṣapūrṇaṃ tu āsamāpti tu saṃyamam ।।

laukikaṃ vyavahāraṃ yaddharmakāmārthalakṣaṇam ।
nirasya pūrvavatsarvaṃ sāvadhānaṃ tato bhavet ।।

tato abhimatavṛttau tu kṛtvā devārcanaṃ tu vai ।
tadagrato dakṣiṇe vā calayiṣye śi ?tarpaṇam ।।

dvijendraṃ sanniveśyātha sarvaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi ।
nirviśaṅkena manasā tadvadeva dhiyā tataḥ ।।

svagṛhaṃ[ca]svacaitanyaṃ dhyāyet sānnidhyam āgatam ।
smared ekaṃ ca niṣpāpaṃ praṇavenāptakālavat ।।

gatāvasaṃ ?yatsaṃskāraṃ yathā śāstroditaṃ mahat ।
kṛtabhikṣastu vihitam uktadīkṣaṃ tu vā caret ।।

asthisañcayaṃ tu evaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi ।
samācaret tataḥ snānaṃ māntram abjaja tatra vai ।।

dvijendraiḥ kṛtadīkṣaistu ṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃgataiḥ ।
pradhānamantrairabliṅgairupasnāto bhaved atha ।।

dvādaśākṣarapūrvebhyo madhyātprāguktalakṣaṇam ।
japed ekatamaṃ mantraṃ dīkṣitasvekameva hi ।।

svamantrād astramantrairvā evaṃ snāne kṛte punaḥ ।
svamantraṃ dvādaśārṇaṃ vā dhyāyan hṛtkamalāntare ।।

taptakāñcanavarṇām amuktamūrtiṃ[ta]meva vā ।
muhūrtārdhaṃ muhūrtaṃ vā japannāste hyananyadhīḥ ।।

tena kalpāgnikaṃ vipra āśaucaṃ svakulodbhavam ।
kṣayametyabhisandhānān narāṇām adhikāriṇām ।।

tattvaṃ mānasam anyebhyaḥ saṃbhūtānāṃ yathākramam ।
na punaḥ sarvaśaktervai saṃbhūtānāṃ sukhānale ।।

taddhā nāṃ ca tajjñānāṃ dvijānām adhikāriṇām ।
evaṃ saṃśuddhadehastu annaṃ saṃsādya pūrvavat ।।

sabhakṣyaṃ vyañjanopetaṃ vibhoryāgārthameva ca ।
tarpaṇārthaṃ hi vai vahneḥ piṇḍanirvāpaṇāya ca ।।

yathāpivāhikaṃ dehaṃ dvitīyaṃ bhūtavigraham ।
karmaṇā nāśam abhyeti dīkṣādyena ca mokṣiṇām ।।

svayaṃ saṃprati datvaivam ādaśāhādikena yat ।
purastād upakārāya karmaṇāṃ dehameti tat ।।

[?dharmeṇānyacci]reṇaiva bhāvināṃ kamalodbhava ।
dīrghābhyāsena kālena saha karmacayaṃ mahat ।।

śamam āyāti vai nūnaṃ mantreśānāṃ prasādataḥ ।
pitṛtvāpādanaṃ tena karmaṇā vimalena ca ।।

asmādgurutaraṃ caiva svayaṃ saṃpāditaṃ tu vā ।
ādaśāhādikaṃ puṃsām upakārāya vai bhavet ।।

nityamante nivṛtte tu svārādhyaṃ saṃyajet tataḥ ।
abhisandhāya manasā svayaṃ gurumukhena vā ।।

karmādhāraṃ hi vai bhāvi dehaṃ śrāddhacchalena tu ।
sandhām īśvaratattvāṃgairdehabhāvāt pṛthaksthitaiḥ ।।

prāgvadiṣṭvātha mantreśaṃ bhogaiḥ saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇaiḥ ।
satilāñjalidānāntairvidhivat kamalodbhava ।।

pūrvoktena vidhānena bhaktyā saśraddhayā tataḥ ।
ekāhaṃ bahavo viprāḥ pañcakālaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

santarpya bhagavad yāgādyo hi vāñchati sampadam ।
tasmād uttaraṇe heturjīvitasya mṛtasya vā ।।

na paśyāmi ṛte yāgādetasmānmantrapūrvakāt ।
prabhavātyayatattvajñā vyāmiśrārādhanojjhitāḥ ।।

te atra pātrāstrayo ?nityaṃ jñānakarmaparāyaṇāḥ ।
mantrapratiparāsaktā itikartavyācyutiḥ ।।

bhaktiśraddhāsamopetā paramuttāraṇaplavaḥ ।
āstāṃ tāvad apāpānām upāyatvena pauṣkara ।।

yāgaṃ brahmamayaṃ śuddhaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ parairapi ।
patitatvāttu vai teṣāṃ piṇḍadānaṃ tilodakam ।।

nāmasaṃkīrtanaṃ caite prayānti paramāṃ gatim ।
ekamuktaṃ samutkṛṣṭam avyāpāraṃ parākramaḥ ।।

adhārādhanapūrvaṃ vā prājāpatyaṃ samācaret ।
sapiṇḍīkaraṇāntaṃ tu ādaśāhād dvijottama ।।

agnāvagre tadantasthe mantreśe tarpite sati ।
piṇḍanirvāpaṇaṃ kuryāt pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ ।।

viniveśyāsane vipram ekaṃ śaktyā bahūnapi ।
tarpaṇīyāni vidhivat tattvasandhānasiddhaye ।।

bhojane phalamūlaistu bhakṣyairuccāvacaistathā ।
pāvanairvividhaiḥ pānairlehyaiḥ peyaiśca coṣyakaiḥ ।।

dakṣiṇābhistu tāmbūlairvārikumbhasamanvitaiḥ ।
chatropānahayānaistu dānaiḥ kāmyairyathocitaiḥ ।।

dmītim abhyeti vai yena samūhaṃ bhagavanmayam ।
jñātvā vā vyavasāyaṃ yad deśakālabalābalam ।।

saha satpātralobhena śīghraṃ yatkartum icchati ।
śrāddhaṃ daśāhapūrvaṃ vā pitṛtvāpādanāntikam ।।

anekadivasotthaṃ tu siddhānnena vinā dvija ।
yathāvad arcanaṃ kṛtvā patrapuṣpādikairvibhaḥ ।।

vahnitarpaṇaniṣṭhaṃ tu svārtham uddiśya vai pitṝn ।
pātraṃ madhvājyasiktaistu saṃpūrṇaṃ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ ।।

upariṣṭādrasairmūrteḥ phalamūlairvibhūṣitam ।
sottarīyopavītāḍhyaṃ sarar ?yutam ।।

sasya ?ekasamopetaṃ vārikumbhasamanvitam ।
dhūpadīpādikairyuktaṃ pūjayitvā nivedya ca ।।

pitrarthaṃ tu dvijātmārthaṃ tato dadyāt tilodakam ।
ekamevaṃ hi cai[kāryaṃ vahyarthaṃ]bahavastu vā ।।

siddhānnaṃ sadvijendrāṇāṃ pūjita ।
pratipādya krameṇaiva pūjanīyaṃ hi vai vibhoḥ ।।

piṇḍaṃ madhvājyasiktairvā prāgvad āpādya taṇḍulaiḥ ।
agnigarbhagatasyāgre vibhordarbhasu ।।

ta yathoktaṃ tu sa ।

ti prāṇendriyāṇāṃ tu yathāvasaram atra ca ।।

gandhānāṃ pūrvavat kuryāt budhyā ca suviśuddhayā ।
pretoddiṣṭena vidhinā[yathāvadā]tmanātmanā ।।

vidhinā mantrapūrveṇa vatsaraṃ saṃprapūrya ca ।
pratisaṃvatsaraṃ śrāddhaṃ yāvajjīvaṃ samācaret ।।

nānādānasamopetaṃ bhāvaścāddhavibhūṣitam ।
yathoddiṣṭena mārgeṇa kintu gotrasamanvitāḥ ।।

mantrānte viniyoktavyāḥ samaśabdapurassarāḥ ।
svayaṃ jñānābhimānākhyaṃ mūrtiṃ dhyāyet svakaṃ dvija ।।

ataḥśuddhāṃ jvaladrūpāṃ kvacid ākṛtilakṣaṇām ।
kvacidgolakarūpāṃ ca madhyāhnādityasannibhāt ।।

kvacinmandatarābhāṃ ca tad vyāpāravaśena tu ।
evaṃ samāpya vidhivat bhagavadyāgapūrvakam ।।

vipratarpaṇaparyantam akhilaṃ pūrvacoditam ।
prā[go]dana[sya]piṇḍādyairvahnyante copasaṃhṛtaiḥ ।।

bandhubhiḥ saha cākṣīyād dattaśiṣṭaṃ dvijottama ।
prājāpatyaṃ tu vai divye aurdhvadaihipūrvake ।।

vyāpāre asmin samantre tu siddhirasti ?vidātmanām ।
svayamātmani kartṝṇāṃ bhāvānmantrāṃśca sā[dhitān] ।।

yena coparatasyāśu yathārthatvaṃ prayāti ca ।
tatra[śrāddhavidhiṃ]kuryānmantranyastena cākhilam ।।

āpaṅktisādhanātkāri ?tṛptyantam amalekṣaṇa ।
ācared vacasā sarvaṃ mantroccāraṇapūrvakam ।।

gṛhāṇānaya saṃyaccha tvevamādyaṃ hi yaddvija ।
manasā bhojanāntaṃ tu vyāpāram akhilaṃ smaret ।।

praṇavenārkacandrāgnisamūhadyutisannibham ।
saṃviśantaṃ svayaṃ mantramagnau tadrūpalakṣaṇe ।।

paramātmani vā bhinne cāturātmyaṃ tu viddhi tat ।
kadambakusumākāraṃ sarvaśaktimalepakam ।।

itīdam uktam abjākṣa jīvabhāvasthitasya ca ।
pāratrikaṃ vidhānaṃ tu mukhakalpasamaṃ mahat ।।

atra pūrvoditaṃ vipra uktānuktaṃ tu cākhilam ।
bhagavatprītiparyantaṃ vijñātavyaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।

vidhinānena yatkuryāt pitṛpretamayaṃ mahat ।
prītaye paratastasya śubhāṃ yacchanti santatim ।।

bhāvamantrakriyādravyairasaṃpūrṇastu yogavat ।
paṭhan vai śrāddhabhoktṝṇāṃ śrāddhādhyāyam idaṃ dvija ।।

samastaṃ hyagrato bhaktyā pitṝṇām anṛṇo bhavet ।
kiṃ punarbrahmasanmantraṃ mantrakarma mahāmate ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

va puvyena bhagavan brahma ।।

me mūrtaṃ atrāsti saṃśayaḥ ।।
śrībhagavānuvāca 

na teṣāṃ vrata[cayahiḥ]sūryabimbaṃ yathā vinā ।
tathā bhagavato viṣṇormūrtaṣāḍguvyavigrahān ।।

prakāśa ta pūrva ndarmāgrā ।
mā ।।

vyañjanti kamalodbhūta tvadanyenaiva sarvadā ।
bheda evaṃ hi ?vibhoścaturmūrteḥ parasya ca ।।

yattatpiṇḍār[thaṃ]kṛtānāṃ ca rasānāṃ bhinnarūpiṇām ।

paraspara dvayāpakatve sthitaṃ dvija ।।

vibhoḥ sarveśvarasyaiva sarvaḥ sarvāsu śaktiṣu ।
vartante ca yathā ।।

parupacaryate ।
viśvātmā bhagavān vipra vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।

ciddhanārutāḥ punaḥ samyagupakārāya karmaṇi ।

syarūpu vyañjayanti ca ।।

bhāvānāṃ bhāti saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇam ।
pūrṇātmani punaḥ sar vāḥ tathātvena ca saṃsthitāḥ ।।

kintu kurvanti tāḥ kṛtyāḥ kartā pa rā ।
prakāśaśaktyā yāṃ śakti sya ca ।।

svacitā raśmijālena yanmadhyādekam abjaja ।
prakaṭīkṛtam ātmanam āditattvena vai saha ।।

samādhisaṃvidhānaṃ ca lābhe vā dhyānakarmaṇi ।
paramātmā sasudbhūta vibhuḥ ।।

svaprakāśāṃśamātreṇa ata evānumīyate ।
evam āhlādaśaktervai lavamātraṃ hi candramāḥ ।।

jñātavyam aravindākṣa prītasya nidhi ? maṃ param ।

kti parijñeyā tadvadeva hi pāvakaḥ ।।

jagatyasmin hi ye bhāvā anye tad anukāriṇaḥ ।
jñānādayo api labhyante tena śaktija yāṃśajāḥ ।।

sarvatra bhagavānevaṃ sāmānyatvena vartate ।
nedaṃ māyātmakaṃ rūpaṃ jaḍaśaktiguṇairyutam ।।

bhagavatyabjasaṃbhūta tvantallīnaṃ hi vidyate ।
yato vicāryamāṇaṃ hi nityam acyutabhāvinām ।।

abhāvabhūmim āyāti svapnadṛṣṭam iveśvaram ।
mantrāḥ śrāddhe samā ye ca ye ca dīkṣādiṣūditāḥ ।।

vyāpāreṣvapi cānyeṣu te apyevaṃ mahimānvitam ।
budhyaivaṃ mantrapūrvaṃ ca sa pāraṃ śāstracoditam ।।

kṛtiṃ jñānātmanābhyeti hyacirādeva karmaṇām ।
śrotriyāṇāṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ tvadarthāśramavartinām ।।

yadvadbhuktāddha ?va śśūdrāt na doṣo jñānagauravāt ।
evaṃ svabhāvadīptānāṃ nirmalānāṃ sadaiva hi ।।

navairjātaṃ ?na malyaṃ bhavecchūdraparigrahāt ।
yathaitadeva śūdrāṇāṃ[na doṣo]jñānagauravāt ।।

avirodho asti sarvatra mantrāṇāṃ samayaiḥ saha ।

sarveṣāmata eva hi ।।

trayīmayānāṃmantrāṇāṃ pravṛttiphaladāyinām ।
asti ṣmāntadvijagraham ।।

anisargādvijaśreṣṭha brahmatejovibhāsitam ।

nāmavasthitam ।।

aniṣekaṃ ca saṃbuddhaṃ bodhyaṃ teṣāṃ sa vartate ।
apakāratvam evāsti parasparam ।।

dvijendrāṇāmṛgādīnāṃ mantrāṇāṃ kamalodbhava ।
ekanatarantaṃ tu viśrā kramāt kramāt ।।

saṃsthitaṃ ca caturthasya śūdrasaṃjñasya pauṣkara ।
prabhākaraṃ ca vāhaṃ ca ?taikṣya madhvavaśāttu vai ।।

nivartante tathā brahman tejovarṇatrayaṃ tathā ।
pratiṣiddhaṃ yadarthaṃ vai ।।

ādhārastadṛgādīnāṃ mantrāṇāṃ mana eva hi ।
pavitratā ca yā teṣāṃ viddhi sarveśvarī hi sā ।।

nivṛttacakra ?kāstu vai mantrāstannivṛttiphalapradāḥ ।
saṃśayāviṣkṛtānāṃ ca svāhā vauṣaḍvaṣaṭ tathā ।।

pratiṣiddhaṃ yadarthaṃ vai mayā te kathitaṃ purā ।
pūraṇairbhagavanmantrāḥ praṇava ।।

sarvajñapācakāste vai sāmānyā yadyapi dvija ।
mukhatvena ca tatrāpi vartanate masvakarmaṇi ।।

yena dīptikāratvaṃ ca nodvahanti mahāmate ।
ādidevena vibhunā ।।

trividhe śabdarāśau tu trividhā vikṛto janaḥ ।
ananyayājino viprā mantrasaṅghe añcalādikeḥ ? ।।

ṛgyajussāma vyāmiśrayājakāḥ ।
catvāro bījapiṇḍapadādike ।।

mantravyūhe suśuddhe ca rajomohānvayojjhite ।
rājasānāṃ hi mantrāṇāṃ tāmasānāṃ ।।

[vidhinā]dhikṛtāḥ sarve ātmalābhārthameva hi ।
suyantritena vai nityaṃ bhaktena ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

mantrajñena trayāṇāṃ ca bhāvyaṃ śūdreṇa sarvadā ।

gādbalādīnāṃ mantrāṇāṃ paramātmanām ।।

kāriṇāṃ phalakaivalyam abjaja ।
ṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃjñānāṃ prayuktānāṃ hi karmaṇi ।।

svarganiṣṭhaṃ hi cotkṛṣṭaṃ saphalaṃ sāṅgasāṃ ?tathā ।
siddhasarvajñamantrāṇām aṇimā ।।

saṃyuktam apavargeṇāprārthitaṃ sarvadaiva hi ।
ata eva hi sāmagrī niḥ śeṣārādhakasya ca ।।

apayujyati tatsidhyai phalaṃ yasyāṇimādayaḥ ।
bhāgena maha sāmaggryā pauṣkara ।।

sākṣātkaraṃ hi yattasya kaivalyaṃ śāśvataṃ phalam ।
rājasānāṃ hi mantrāṇāṃ tāmasānāṃ mahāmate ।।

īṣad dṛṣṭaphalopetam ātmasaṃskārameva hi ।
janmotkarṣasametaṃ ca cittotkarṣaphalapradam ।।

eṣāṃ pradhānabhūtaṃ yatphalam uktavyapekṣayā ।
sātvikānāṃ hi mantrāṇām ekadeśāśritaṃ hi yat ।।

pratyayārthaṃ hi mokṣasya siddhaye saṃprakīrtitam ।
maśanāmākaronmantrāḥ ?tatsiddhistatkriyāvaśāt ।।

kriyādhigamyate śāstrāt ।

saṃśuddhisantoṣabhaktipūrvāttu saṃyamāt ।।

bhavettatsādhusaṃparkāt bhot ? ।
sanmantrāṇāṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ śāśvatasya ca karmaṇaḥ ।।

kvacittrayasya saṃyoga phalam ।
kvacinmahattā mantrāṇāṃ phalaniṣṭhā kriyā dvija ।।

mukhasvarūpā ṇān sthitān ।
adhikāraṃ kvacitkartuṃ sthitaṃ mantravaśāt dvija ।।

janmotkarṣakriyā jāyante pratyayaiḥ saha ।
jātvaivaṃ yojanaṃ kāryaṃ bhaktānāṃ sarvadaiva hi ।।

mantravyūhe tu vividhe brahman bhogāpavargade ।
iti śrīpāñcarātre śrīpauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ śrāddhākhyāno nāma saptaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha aṣṭāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

- - śrī bhagavānuvāca 

na vedapāṭhasaktānāṃ na mokṣakratuyājinām ।
na tapo abhiratānāṃ ca dānadharmaikasevinām ।।

agnihotraparāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ caiva pauṣkara ।

mahata cāgnihotreṇa tvevamuktā garīyasī ।
tathā kathaṃ na saṃsāraduḥkhaśāntirbhavennṛṇām ।।

- 

śrī bhagavānuvāca 

svargamārgapradaṃ caiva tathātkṛṣṭaphalapradam ।
kevalaṃ cāgnihotraṃ tu viprāṇāṃ vedavādinām ।।

ye punastu tato brahman sthitā taddharmadharmiṇi ।
ta[pār]cane samādhau tu japakarmaṇi castu tau ? ।।

teṣāmunnatacittānāṃ bhagavatkarmavedinām ।
santapa[d]bhavanaṃ sacchāstrapariśodhinām ।।

guggulvādyādikairdravyaiḥ saṃpūrṇāhutibhiḥ saha ।
kṛtaṃ rahasyamantraistu bhavāduttārakaṃ bhavet ।।

dhiṣṇyā vaikaṅkatī vaistu sādhanaiḥ ।
dhanena dharmalabdhena bhaktyā ca śraddhayāpi ca ।।

yathāvadāhṛte vahnau nānāyonyudbhave tu vai ।
purā te vidhinā samyakkuṇḍaṃ saṃ[?sthāpya caiva tu] ।।

avatārya ca tanmadhye nānāyonyutthitaṃ tu tat ।

- -

pauṣkara uvāca 

yonayo bhagavaṃścāgneḥ jñāna[?tumicchāmi sāṃpratam ] ।

yathā tvatprasādādhitakāmyayā ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

yau niragnerdvidhā sauriprabhavā ratnalakṣaṇā ।
tatkarādarśasaṃyogād dvitīyā kamalodbhava ।।
vividhāraṇiyonistattai naikalakṣaṇā ।।
yā manthanakrameṇaiva jagatyasmin vyavasthitā ।
[vividhāraṇiyogād]vai parasparanidharṣaṇāt ।।
kadācit[sthāttadudbhūtiḥ]kaicakī yatjavarjitā ।।
triprakārāṃ tu pāṣāṇī tatraiṣā kevalābjaja ।
yā samagreśubhe ge vai parasparanigharṣaṇāt ।।

[dīptānāmana]lānāṃ tu prajvālayati parvatān ।
salohaghātakī caiva tarjanyā bhraṃśalakṣaṇā ।।

tṛtīyāvartayoḥ samyak tāmanaṃ ca parasparam ।
lohapāṣāṇayonīnāṃ[tāmanaṃ syāt ta]thaiva ca ।।
aṣṭama pi saṃkṣiptamekamanthānalakṣaṇam ।।
santāḍanaṃ ca nna paraṃ hi tam ।
yadratnata kutrāpi kamalodbhava ।।

prakṛṣṭamapi boddhavyaṃ kāla । jvālāgrāttu kacālācca tadbhūtimasta । āsāṃ pañcavidhaṃ sthānaṃ ntaṃ brāhmaṇākim ।

sadeva nānādevaistu vyaktiyuktā mahāmate ।
śaktirgaṇaśa raiḥ pūrṇā sāmānyavyāpa[kābhavetu] ।।

śaktibhāvena vai tasmādahartavyaṃ ca pāvakam ।
yathā gṛhī tathā[nṛbhyāṃ]virodhe nopapadyate ।।

tasmātsarvapadārthānāmādeśā śaktirabjaja ।
śa ṣaṇaṃ tu vai vahnervahnikārye hyupasthite ।।

catuṣprakārāgṣaiva gīyate saptadhā punaḥ ।
kathā kamalasaṃbhūta tavedānīṃ nigadyate ।।

yākṣī ca pārthivī saurī śaikhī bhrāṣṭrī tathaiva ca ।
kāpālī kamalodbhūta svatantrāgni śca taṃ vinā ।।

sthitirāsāṃ dvidhā vipra punareva nigadyate ।
nirbījākhyā sabījā ca nirbījā tāvaducyate ।।

bhavanī dviprakārā ca tatsthānākhyaca vai cakī ।
salo[hā]caiva pātrāṇi kevalāśmamayī tathā ।।

nirbījeyaṃ samākhyātā sabījā ca nigadyate ।
śaikhī bhrāṣṭrī ca kāpālī svatantrānalalakṣaṇā ।।

hotrā saṃyojanī caiva yaduktaṃ te mayābjaja ।
aviśeṣā susāmānyā sarveṣāṃ caiva sarvadā ।।

yadyapyabjasamudbheta tathāvaga[mitaṃ]śruṇu ।
[viśeṣayo]nīnāmāśramāṇāṃ sthitaṃ kramāt ।।

vihitā brahmacārīṇāṃ lohapāṣāṇalakṣaṇā ।
ādhānākhyā gṛhasthānāṃ kaicakī vanavāsinām ।।

sāvitrī ca yatīnāṃ vai tvārādhana[ratātmanām] ।
[yukta]ṣaṭkarmasaktānāṃ bākīmanyānalakṣaṇā ।।

vihitā nayane vahneraraṇīnāṃ parasya ca ।
nṛpasya tadanujñātā sāmānyānnābhasī dvidhā ।।

tad dvayaṃ tadanujñānaṃ tritaya ।
sīmanta vaiśyajāter vai trayametacca rā ।।

śūdrasya kramasiddhyarthaṃ viśeṣāttadanujñayā ।
dvijendrasya dvije ।।

daśāstu vai ।
dvitīyā caiva śūdrasya sa danyasya pauṣkara ।।

āpatkāle tu nānyasya yacchecchūdrasya vānya ।

।।

co virodhakṛt ।

tathāna metanmukhyamataḥ param ।।

tammukhya vyutkramaṃ cālpasiddhidam ।
phalabhedena sarveṣāṃ vihitā yonayo a khilāḥ ।।

ekādaśābjasaṃbhūta yathā tadavadhāraya ।
ratnajā bhūmikāmānāṃ kāṃsī tejo artbhināṃ tu vai ।।

gopa yacchatyaraṇilakṣaṇā ।
vijeyā kaicakī yoniḥ sukhasaubhāgyapuṣṭidā ।।

buddhivīryapradā bhūmiḥ khyā śatrunāśinī ।
kirtitā lohapāṣāṇaśobhinī yonirabjaja ।।

dharmā śaikhī bhrāṣṭrī bhūmipradā tu vai ।
saṃvedayoniḥ kāpālī sthānavṛddhikarābjaja ।।

rogopaśāntikāmānāṃ yonirbhūtakarī śubhā ।
caturṇāmāśramāṇāṃ ca manukalpe[pu roditā] ।।

aṇḍabhā ?nnavirodho asti tvanyonyaharaṇe sati ।
sarveṣāṃ yonayaḥ sarvā icchākāle hyupasthitau ।।

mantrārādhanasaktānāmaviruddhāḥ sadaiva hi ।
yāva vādhikaṃ kāle mābhūtaṃ yatpurā dvija ।।

pramādānupaśāntaśce dyoniranyāharet punaḥ ।
na balāduparodhācca saṃgrahasthasya nārcanāt ।।

saṃgṛhītasya vai bhuyaḥ prāyaścittaṃ samācaret ।
saviśeṣaṃ prakāśe tu hyaprakāśau tu cānyathā ।।

iti śrīpañcarātre pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ hutāśanayonivibhāgo nāma aṣṭāviṃśo adhyāyāḥ ।।

atha ekonatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

śrībhagavānuvāca 

prājāpatye daiśikīye śaiṣotthakarasaṃmite ।
kṣetraṃ kramān nayed vṛddhiṃ tāvad ekaikam aṅgulam ।।

yāvad aṣṭakaraṃ kṣetraṃ dhiṣṇyārtham upajāyate ।
evaṃ syānmānabhāvena tvekāśītyadhikaṃ śatam ।।

kuṇḍānāṃ sarva ।
jāyate aṣṭaguṇaṃ saṃkhyā tvaṣṭadiksaṃsthitā śubhā ।।

caturaśrādibhedotthā kāmyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ dvija ।

prakāreṇa kṣetrasāmyena vai sati ।।

sadratnamālāśrīvatsamukuṭāṅgadalakṣaṇāḥ ।
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaśārṅganānāśaropamāḥ ।।

sarve sapīṭhā vihitāścatustridvayekamekhalāḥ ।

nānāsvātavaśāt caiva sarveṣāṃ punareva hi ।।

aprakāśaprakāśākhyaṃ bhedaṃ tu vividhaṃ smṛtam ।
sadbhogalakṣaṇaṃ bandham anantaphalam arthinām ।।

vyāsasvātāḥ samā hi yā ।

prakāśilakṣaṇanyāye teṣāṃ svāto mahāmate ।

kṣayā ।।

ādvādaśāṅgulāḥ kuṇḍāḥ karānte ye trayodaśa ।

anukalpe tu vihitā jaṅgamā mantratarpaṇe ।

bhūmāvullikhya saṃpūrya dhānyairbījairmṛdā tu vā ।
sāmagrīvirahād vāpi śaśvatkarmasamāptaye ।।

anukalpānukalpe tu nityam evāvirodhakṛt ।
tvaganvitaiḥ samaiḥ pūrṇaiḥ sarasaiḥ saralaiḥ sthiraiḥ ।।

dalīkṛtaistu ।

kāṣṭaiḥ kāryātra vai purī ।।

dvādaśāṅgulapūrvāṇāṃ dhātūtthānām api dvija ।
vidheyā havyapūritve calānām evameva hi ।।

nākuṇḍaṃ havanaṃ yasmātsiddhikṛnmantrājinām ।
tasmātkuṇḍaṃ sadā kāryaṃ sautraṃ vā jaṅgamaṃ sthiram ।।

havyabhūmerviśeṣācca pīte tu dviguṇocchrite ।
tat tad dvicaturaśraṃ tu vyaṣṭāśraṃ parimaṇḍalam ।।

ṣaṣṭhāṃśadviṣaṭkāṃśena connatam ।
āpādya svātamānaṃ prāgyathābhimatam ucchritam ।।

iṣṭakābhiv apakvābhiḥ pakvābhirvā yathāruci ।

hitam anyadā ।।

kuryādvātha samāstulyā teṣvaṃśaṃ syataḥ kṣitaḥ ।
dvayaṅgulenādhikaṃ jātaṃ vāsād vāsāṃ yathā bhavet ।।

prāṅmekhalānanāt deśāt tattadvā pattadu ।

dupremā vaneḥ purā ।।

tribhāgonam athārdhaṃ ca nemimānasitātmanā ।
kuṇḍānāṃ tattvato mānād avasthānaṃ dvādaśānāṃ mahāmate ।।

dvādaśāṅgulaniṣṭhānāṃ dvādaśānāṃ kadācana ।
saṃvibhajya caturdhātra tridhā vāmalalocana ।।

tanmānam atha nemīnām ucchritā vistṛterapi ।
tatsamā sarvadā yone[ḥkār]yeṇa pṛṣṭataḥkṛteḥ ।।

kintu vdyaṅgulamānena pronnatā pṛṣṭhato avadheḥ ।
hlāsayed anupātena tvaṃtu nemya kramāt ।।

vistṛtā mekhalāmānāt pādonāt kamalodbhava ।।

vidheyātha tribhāgena tadagraṃ saṃprasārya ca ।

dya mekhalā ।।

bimbaprāṇapraṇālavat ।
taṃ yoniṃ vṛddhinirvāhaṃ koṣṭhāniṣṭhāvidhiṃ kramāt ।।

samāpādyānupātena samaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ gajoṣṭhavat ।
samāśritya svakaṃ ?mūrtiṃ vicitrāṃ guṇalakṣaṇām ।।

nirvahanti niśaṃ bodhapravāhenā nādinā ।
puṃsamudre tvagādhe tu sa kṣālanāśraye ।।

niśamya yoniṃ vyomni raja ।

yadamūrtaṃ paraṃ brahma tad viddhi nabhaso gatam ।।

caturātmānam avyaktaṃ tatra prāk paridheḥ svayam ।।

samaḥ saṃpūrṇamūrtīnāṃ mamāmokṣajam ।
guṇadvayadvayātmānam acyutādyaṃ kramāt trayam ।।

sā yoniḥ sarvakarmaṇām ।
yatpravāhāśritaṃ karma brahmaṇyekātmatāṃ vrajet ।।

kuṇḍanāmitimārī ?pūvravat ।।

palvastanagarbheṇa tamūrdhakṣaṇam āsapātayet ? ।।

kā vihitā vibhorviprānanasya ca ।

tatonnatiḥ ।
kamalālayagarbhaṃ tu tāmram āyasajaṃ tu vā ।।

tatrāgniṃ janayitvāvatārya ca ।

nakhilamantrestu saha mantrī ca saṃhitām ।
samuccaran dhiyā samyak svaśaktyā vā pṛthak pṛthak ।।

bhinnamantragaṇaṃ sarvam ājyadohairmudaṃ nayet ।
dhruvāccārcitayā ?ttu vai ।।

tallakṣaṇam atho vakṣye mānameyasamanvitam ।
prasiddhayajñavṛkṣotthaṃ na doṣairdṛḍhamavraṇa m ।।

suspaṣṭaṃ kāṣṭham ādāya davāgnitrāsavarjitam ।
nirasaṃjirakā ?paryuṣitaṃ śubham ।।

madhyamāṅ[gu]liparyantaṃ bāhnorāmaṇibandhataḥ ।
tamaṅguṣṭhodarairbhūyo naguṇya ca ।।

aṣṭāvaṣṭau tyajan yāyāt śeṣāstvekādhikāhi ।
ācāraste vai parijñeyā dhvajādya ṣṭau yathākramāt ।।

tatraivam avaśeṣaṃ yacchubhaṃ ca śubhanaḥ smṛtaḥ ।

catuṣṭaya sva vṛddhiṃ ca pañcakā vṛṣabhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
karaṣmakā ca śeṣācca gajā vai saptakāt tu vai ।।

ekākhyaḥ saptakāḥ śuddhestatrāmī śubhadāḥ smṛtāḥ ।

svaṃ svaṃ saṃveditaṃ kuryāt tena cāvedikaṃ śubham ।
kṣitimaṇḍalamadhyasthabhāgenādyena vai tataḥ ।।

kamalaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ kevalaṃ ṣoḍaśacchadam ।

tārāttā gaṇāḍhyaṃ vā ।

ataścāntānupātārtham aṣṭāṃśaṃ pakṣagaṃ punaḥ ।

antaraṃ vasudhābhyāṃ ṣṭāṃśasaṃmitam ।
kāryaṃ ṣaḍaṃśatulyaṃ vā vistṛtaiḥ śubhalakṣaṇam ।।

tad vistāraṃ dvidhā kṛtvā pañcadhā vā samaiḥ padaiḥ ।

madhyabhāgasya ।।

bhāgam abhāgaṃ ca pakṣayorvā dvayaṃ dvayam ।
agrataścānupātārthaṃ vibhajyaiva yathecchayā ।।

skandhāntaraṃ ca ।
matsyavallāṃñchana yathākramam ।।

pārśvābhyām antaraṃ bāhyāt śeṣaṃ kaṇṭhātmanā nayet ।
yathā syād gomukhe bhāsa kaṇṭhaṃ maharddhidam ।।

nirmuktavedikānāṃ tu śaṅkhādīnāṃ yadanta ।

paṭṭena yuktaṃ padmadvayena vā ।।

vedikāvāsudhāṃśā tvanupātena śātayet ।
skandhakaṇṭhāt samārabhyatrayo grīvā yathecchayā ।।

vidhāya bhāgaṃ prāgukta tam ।

kumbhabhāgatrayaṃ sadmadvayaṃ saṃśātayet kramāt ।
pṛthūdarasya śaṅkhasya pañcamāṃśena śātayet ।।

vartate mūlam āśritya dairdhyād bhāgatrayaṃ hi yat ।।

tanmadhyāt kaṇṭhadeśe prāgākṣipyāṅgaṃ yathoditam ।
śeṣaṃ tu daśadhā kṛtvā tataḥ saptāṅgasaṃmitam ।।

daṇḍaṃ kuryād gadākāraṃ kaṇṭhavistāravistṛtam ।
dviprakāraṃ yathoddiṣṭamatelavaṇānvitam ।।

aṃśakatritayenaiva tatra nirmāṇam ucyate ।
vedikopagataṃ kuryād ekabhāgasamāśritam ।।

svāstikaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ madhyataḥ kamalāṅkitam ।
karṇikā nicayaśścāntaṃ ?pratyaṃśaṃ racayet tataḥ ।।

aṅgaṇe petaiḥ susamair antarīkṛtaiḥ । 

dhārācanavidhānaivaṃ ?dviṣaṭkapariniṣṭhite ।
vartulaṃ caturaśraṃ tu cayamadhyagam ।।

karagrahavatīṃ muṣṭimarodayalakṣaṇām ।
īṣā mānādhikaṃ daṇḍaṃ bāhyam āpūrayet tathā ।।

śatapatram adhovaktraṃ pṛthulaṃ cordhvakarṇikam ।
muṣṭiniṣṭhāyudhau kuryāt bahuparṇaṃ sakesaram ।।

athavedikṣipet ?pīṭhalakṣaṇaṃ cāparaṃ śṛṇu ।
vihitaṃ cārdhakalpeyaṃ ?devapīṭhopamaṃ śubham ।।

uṣṇīvapadaparyantam ācāgreḥ sa ?vibhajya ca ।
sa bhāgaiḥ purātra syudvādadiṣṭamucyate ।।

padmaṃ cakrāravindaṃ vā lakṣaṇalakṣitam ।
kiṃtu mānaṃ vibhāgaṃ ca bhūyaḥ kṣetravaśāt śṛṇu ।।

brahmasthānāvadheḥ kṣetraṃ kṛtvā ṣaṅbhāgabhājitam ।
