dvau bhāgau bhūṣayenmadhye karṇikāpadasiddhaye ।।

paridhiścārdhabhāgena tvardhena kesarāvalim ।
sārdhena patranicayaṃ vyoma cārdhena tad bahiḥ ।।

pārthivaṃ puram aṃśena vicitraracanānvitam ।
sāntarāṇi samāsādya kṣetrāṇyetāni pauṣkara ।।

kiñcit kiñcit samādāya pro[nnate]ṣvavayaveṣu ca ।
ākhyātapari[to] brahman dalapādānikaṃ kramāt ।।

nimnatāṃ ca nayed īṣat kṣetrāt kṣetraṃ yathoditam ।
śeṣa eva sacakramya [pari]māryacānyathā ।।

khātātmakesarakṣetramānam atra yathoditam ।
dalajālaṃ samāpādya savyoma cāṃśakena tu ।।

sacakranemivṛttaṃ tu sārdhenāṃśena tad bahiḥ ।
bhāgakṣetraṃ kuryāt prāguktalakṣaṇam ।।

pṛṣṭhatasva kuryāt sapadmaṃ kaivalaṃ tu vā ।
kamalaṃ dalajālaṃ ca mukha ।।

etat pramāṇanirmāṇapari ।
tadā prameyam asyāṃ vai jñātavyaṃ karmasiddhaye ।।

śatapatrātmanānanto muṣṭistenantavātra ?dhṛk ।
antarbījātmabhāvena sthitvā cotthamukhaḥ punaḥ ।।

pataskandhaṃ yadaryātmabhūtaprāṇamarunmahat ।
preritaṃ brahmarandhreṇa tat tad icchāvaśāt punaḥ ।।

saptapātālanālaṃ ca tvagamakṣātmanāmbujam ? ।
yadāśritya svavāhe tu hyamṛtaṃ jalavat sthitam ।।

sacakraracanājāle sthitaste satramūrtidhṛk ।
śaṅkhavigrahadhṛgvāyurājyakośaṃ ca khaṃ tataḥ ।।

nirbījam ajam akṣobhyam ādyaṃ stragdevatasyādhidaivatam ? ।
satyabhūtam ameyaṃ ca prameyam idam acyutam ।।

saṃskārakāle tvāropya nityaṃ saṃmantrya tarpaṇe ।
dairghyam eva tam ujjhitya vedivistārameva ca ।।

yathoktāṃśaṃ ।

saṃhataṃ gadādaṇḍaṃ sukhiraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ tu vā ।।

nātisthūlaṃ nātikṛśaṃ yuktam ṛjugaṇena tu ।
evaṃ dravyamayaṃ kuryāt śubhadāramayaṃ ?tu vā ।।

stratukstruvānāṃ ca homārthaṃ tallakṣaṇam athocyate ।
āyaśuddhaṃ samādāya prāguktagaṇalakṣitam ।।

trayeṃśonaṃ strucā dairdhyād aṣṭadhā cocchritaṃ bhajet ।
tena bhāgapramāṇena tad vistāraṃ vidhīyate ।।

saṃvibhajya samāṃśaistat sūtraiḥ spaṣṭairyathākramam ।
kalaśaṃ kḷptayenmūlād aṣṭāṃśaṃ caturaśrakam ।।

varjayitvātha bāhulyaṃ vistārārdhena kalpya vai ।
kuryād ādhāraviśrāntaṃ kamalaṃ racitānvitam ।।

taṃ śaṃkhaṃ vitatāsyaṃ tu nandyāvartaṃ sulakṣaṇam ।
pārśvabhāgadvayaṃ tyaktavā caturaṃśa smṛtam ।।

pāśavadgrathitaṃ madhye suvibhaktaṃ ca vartulam ।
caturbhāgānanaṃ daṇḍaṃ nirgataṃ kalaśānanāt ।।

vitānaṃ śaṅkhavaktrād vā tritayasaṃyutam ।
dhārānāladvayaṃ kuryāt ṣṭāṅgasaṃmitān ।।

pīṭhavat kaṇṭhapīṭhaṃ tu caturaśraṃ samāpya ca ।
tasmin paṅkajam ullikhya cakravṛttāntarīkṛtam ।।

muktājālasamaṃ sūtraṃ śaṅkhakoṇacatuṣṭaye ।
ekāṃśenonnatā grīvā vistāravdyaṅgasaṃmitā ।।

īṣad vaktrā na sāṣṭāṃśād ūrdhve bhāgasamujjhitām ।
padmavaccottamāṅgaṃ ca grīvānālaṃ sakarṇikam ।।

anantakesaraprāntairāvṛtaṃ karṇikānanam ।
tad bahiḥ patrajālaṃ tu kesarocchrāyasaṃmitam ।।

avibhāga pṛṣṭhatastiryagānanam ।
kuryācca karrṇikāmadhye golakenaiva mudritam ।।

kaustubhenāṅkitaṃ caiva saurabhīyāśriṇāthavā ।
sārdhahomapramāṇena dravyajājyāhuteḥ kṣamam ।।

pramāṇope lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam ।
smṛtaṃ sadājyahomārthaṃ śeṣam anayannibodhatu ।।

sākṣād amṛtamūrtirvai varuṇaḥ kamalātmanā ।
nālātmanā tadastraṃ ca saṃsthitaṃ vighnabhītikṛtṛ ।।

jagadāpyāyakṛt candraḥ padmatcenāgradeśa ।
ānandākhyaṃ hi sāmarthyaṃ jñeyaṃ tat parameśvaram ।।

deśikastu tadānyāsasādhakaḥ saṃyatastu vā ।
daivīyam abhimānaṃ ca samāśritya te ।।

arcane sāgnikārye tu yathopakaraṇākhilāḥ ।
sannārya svakaraṇānāṃ tu hyekasmin svāśraye sthitāḥ ।।

sarva dehenānena tvardhyapātra ।

śaṅkhacakrādikairyutāḥ ।।

kāryā tvam abhimatāptaye ।
tasmād anadhikārye atha hyannadevaparastathā ।।

damaho saṃśrayet ।
niṣiddha dehāpaharaṇaṃ śubham ।।

saṃpādya padavīṃ yāti yo adhikārapade sthitaḥ ।
dadāti anujñājuṣṭānāṃ tvad bhaktānāṃ ca tatprati ।।

ājyasthālī bṛhad brahmalakṣaṇe ।
kuryāt kamalagarbhaṃ tu yāmyayātrātmato ?śubhāḥ ।।

gṛhītvātmāmṛtaḥ samyak saṃstutvaṃ labhate agninā ।।
dhruvaṃ pramāṇanālaṃ ca tanmūle śubhalakṣaṇam ।।
kuryād amalasāraṃ ca bjaja ।
tatsamarthaṃ ca tannālasaṃjñitāḥ śrīniṣevitāḥ ।।

saṃpādya nalinīṃ divyāṃ praphullair ardhapuṣpitaiḥ ।
tathā mukulitaiḥ padmaiḥ sapadmair antarīkṛtaiḥ ।।

dikpālitāścaiva dakṣiṇottarayostu vā ।
caturvistāravaktrāṃ ca phullapadmāntarāṇi tām ? ।।

cakravyomatribhāgena nimnā vātadalena tu ।
mūlayed galadeśa ḥsyād anyamanyaṃ samāpya vai ।।

uṣṇīṣaṃ cātpalopetaṃ saṃsiddhā surabhīravaiḥ ।
sanālā nalinī teṣāṃ tatpātraṃ pārameśvaram ।।

śayanāsanasaṃjñaṃ ca satataṃ cāmṛtārṇavam ।

dyāvāpṛthivyā ।।

straggaṃdhava teraste sapuṣpe copaladvaye ।
praṇītādīni pātrāṇi tūpayogyāni yānyapi ।।

tāni śaṅkhābjahetīśasaṃyuktānyakhilāni ca ।
vicitraṃ racanā dhātudārvamayāni vā ।।

yathābhimatamānāni kuryāt padmevatāni ?ca ।
mantrārādhanapūrvāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ kamalodbhava ।।

sarvaṃ salāñchanaṃ kuryāpadaṃtra ?kalaśādi ।

tvāsanādīni svātmopakaraṇāni ca ।।

muktāṅgulīyakaṃ caiva bhūṣakaṃ kaṭakādikam ।
uttamāṅgodvahaṃ sarvaṃ śiroṣṇīṣādīkaṃ tu vai ।।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ kuṇḍalakṣaṇaṃ nāma ekonatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha triṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pauṣkara uvāca 

saṃjāte bhagavan lope bhaktānāṃ mantrasevinām ।
jñānādiyoganiṣṭhasya sadvyāpārasya cācyuta ।।

pātatrāṇamupāyaṃ vai śrotumicchāmi sāṃpratam ।
kṛtena yena bhaktānāṃ jāyate kṛtakṛtyatā ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

kathaṃ saṃvatsarādvipra karmaṇābhimataṃ phalam ।
prāpnuyācca kriyāsaktaḥ pavitrārohaṇaṃ vinā ।।

yathāśvamedhaṃ viprāṇāṃ sarvecchāparipūrakam ।
rājasūyaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ tathā ।।

bhūṣaṇānāṃ yathā madhye kaustubhaṃ varabhūṣaṇam ।
jñeyaṃ pavitrakaṃ tadvadbhogajālasya cāntare ।।

yatpūrayati bhaktānāṃ vyāpāraṃ pārameśvaram ।
bhogamokṣāptaye śaśvadbhogastasmāstu ko adhikaḥ ।।

bhaktānāṃ satataṃ bhaktyā sālokyaṃ vidadhāti vai ।
sāmīpyaṃ sādhakānāṃ ca nānāsiddhisamanvitam ।।

sāyujyaṃ sādhakendrāṇāṃ svamantrātmani yacchati ।
taduttarāyaṇe atīte cāturmāsasya madhyataḥ ।।

ādāvante athavā kuryād dvādaśīṣvakhilāsu ca ।
saṃkrāntiṣu ca sarvāsu paurṇamāsiṣu cābjaja ।।

amāvāsyāsvaśeṣāsu tṛtīyāsu tathaiva ca ।
vaiṣṇaveṣvatha ṛkṣeṣu tatkṣaṇeṣvakhileṣu ca ।।

cāturmāsyasya kālasya tūtthāna dvādaśī tu yā ।
ṣaḍaśītimukhā divyā tasyāmāropayettu yaḥ ।।

pavitrakaṃ jagadyoneḥ sapavitrīkaroti ca ।
atītāṃ vartamānāṃ ca eṣyāṃ svakulasantātim ।।

tatra sannihitaḥ sākṣānnānānirmāṇavigrahaḥ ।
bhaktānāṃ bhagavān prītaḥ paramātmācyuto hariḥ ।।

yadyapyabjasamudbhūta bhaktānāṃ nityameva hi ।
nārāyaṇastu mantrātmā sthitaḥ sannihitaḥ svayam ।।

tathāpi balavattā vai tattithestatra karmaṇi ।
sannidhi bhajate yena mantriṇāṃ mantrarāṭ prabhuḥ ।।

grīṣmakālaṃ samāsādya yathārkastīkṣṇatā vrajet ।
svarūpamajahanneva sannidhānataraṃ vibhoḥ ।।

saptātradeśakālānām āsṛṣṭeḥ sthitaye tu vai ।
ataḥ pavitrakaṃ tasyāmanasyāṃ tadasaṃbhavāt ।।

kāryaṃ kriyāparairbhaktyā sākhaṇḍā yena jāyate ।
akhaṇḍakārī puruṣo jñānakarmaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

bhaktiśraddhātathotsāhayukto yogabalairyuktaḥ ।
brahmavyekātmatāṃ yāti acirādeva pauṣkara ।।

sarvabhāvena bhaktānāṃ yatpālayati sarvadā ।
manovākcittajaṃ kutsnaṃ vyāpāraṃ śubhalakṣaṇam ।।

parijñerāyatastasmāt svarūpaṃ tasya yādṛśam ।
phalameti ca vai yena bhaktānāṃ tatsamāpanāt ।।

yadacchinnaṃ jagadhoneranantaprasaraṃ sitam ।
vicchedamakṛtajñānāmeti nānātmanā svayam ।।

jagatsūtraṃ tu tadviddhi hemasūtrādinā tu vai ।
bāḍguvyamabhimānaṃ yaddhatte pratisarātmanā ।।

jñānarāgoparaktaṃ ca yuktaṃ kāryaistu vīryajeḥ ।
taijasairāvṛttaṃ mantrairbalenāvalitaṃ param ।।

aiśvaryamupacāre tu saṃprāpte śaktito avyayam ।
evaṃ pavitrakaṃ tāvatparijñātaṃ na tat prabhoḥ ।।

brahmavyadhipatau viṣṇau tadākāre pratiṣṭhite ।
bhaktyā ca vidhivaddattaṃ dadāti bhagavatpadam ।।

sthūlasya vyatiriktasya vyavahārapadasthitaiḥ ।
padārthaiḥ kalpanīyā ca yathā tadavadhārasya ।।

sūkṣmaṃ dṛḍhaṃ sitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ sūtraṃ brahmaprasūtayā ।
vinirmitaṃ kumāryā vā vṛddhayā vā vinītayā ।।

viśuddhayā vidhavayā saṃpāditamathāpi vā ।
yathālabdhaṃ tu cādāya kuryādastraviśodhitam ।।

avalokya smaranmūlaṃ viniṣpādya caturguṇam ।
cāturātmyavyapekṣāyāmathavāṣṭagūṇaṃ dvija ।।

bhagavanmūrtibhede tu bhedabhinnopalakṣitam ।
keśavādiṣvadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvena tricaturguṇam ।।

tantubhirviṣamaiviṣṇoḥ samasya parivarjayet ।
pavitrikī kriyā yasmādviṣamā sā na kasyacit ।।

pavitrakāṇi kāryāṇi tantubhistaiḥ sutānitaiḥ ।
mantrāstrakumbhayoḥ pūrvaṃ nānāmantrālayasya ca ।।

maṇḍalākhyapradhānasya tadgatastayākhilasya ca ।
karṇikāsthasya ca vibhoḥ kesaracchadagasya ca ।।

vibhavavyūharūpasya lāñchanā stradvayasya ca ।
mūrdhni kaṇṭhe asayoḥ puṣpapūjāyāmupari kṣitau ।।

pramāṇena jagannāthapratimāyāṃ catuṣṭayam ।
dvayaṃ hi kuṇḍānalayoḥ śāstrapīṭhasya ca dvayam ।।

lipervāktattvabhūtasya śabdatattvasya ca prabhoḥ ।
ghaṇṭākṣasūtrapūrvāṇāṃ kriyāṅgānāṃ mahātmānām ।।

jāyāyāṃ bhaktinamrāyāṃ raktāyāmarcane hareḥ ।
saṃbandhināṃ ca mitrāṇāṃ bhagavaddharmasevinām ।।

taduttarasahāyānāṃ cāturātmyābhilāṣiṇām ।
bhṛtyānāṃ svānukūlānāṃ puruṣottamayājinām ।।

vṛddhaye yoṣitā caiva pavitrīkaraṇāya ca ।
pavitrīkaraṇaṃ ramyaṃ racanīyaṃ yathākramam ।।

ṣaḍadhvapīṭhasaṃsthasya nānāprantrāspadasya ca ।
jñānādiguṇabhedasya catuḥsthānārcanāya ca ।।

mukhyamantrasya ca vibhoḥ śatenāṣṭādhikena ca ।
tantunā bhūṣaṇaṃ kuryādardhenāṃśena vābjaja ।।

japahomadikā saṃkhyā pūrṇā riktā tadātmanā ।
samīkaroti bhaktānāṃ mantrāṇāmata eva hi ।।

hemasadratnakarpūramālayakṣodakuṅkumaiḥ ।
sarvauṣadhisamopetaistvagelādivimiśritaiḥ ।।

pāvanairvividhairdravyairnirvyājapicunā saha ।
kuryāttadbharbharacanāṃ sūtrasaṃkhyopalakṣitām ।।

bījapūravadabjākṣa ārdrāmalakaśaṅkhavat ।
tadantarālāni punastvavicchinnena tu tantunā ।।

vibhāgapratipatyarthaṃ granthanīyānyadūrataḥ ।
yathecchayā tato anyeṣo yājyānāṃ parikalpya ca ।।

sūtrabhramasamopetairgabhairbhūṣaṇasaṃcayam ।
ārādhakasya ca guroḥ sagarbhaṃ bhūṣaṇadvayam ।।

vihitaṃ bhagavanmantranyāsāttādātmyabhāvanāt ।
ato anyeṣāmagarbhaṃca racanīyaṃ pavitrakam ।।

antarālagataṃ garbhaṃ kuryādbāhlīkarañjitam ।
alaṃkṛtyaṃ ca sauvarṇerūpariṣṭācca rūpakaiḥ ।।

patracchedasamatthaistu jātarūpamayaistu vā ।
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmamālāśrīvatsakaustubhaiḥ ।।

khageśatālamusalanandakajyāhalādikaiḥ ।
mandārakusumākāraiḥ pārijātadrumopamaiḥ ।।

śrīvṛkṣācalanāgendrasvastikaiścāmarairghaṭaiḥ ।
vedhānalārciṣāḍhyā ca vyañjanairātapatrakaiḥ ।।

saritsamudravṛṣabhabhaugajālaistu sārasaiḥ ।
ekasyaiva bahunāṃ vā yathāsthānānurūpataḥ ।।

dhātuje pittale bhāṇḍe vastracchanne nidhāya ca ।
dhādayedupariṣṭācca dhūpitenāhatena ca ।।

kṛtāhniko adhivāsārthaṃ daśabhyāṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ ।
deśikendradvitīyastu kartārdhyakusumodyataḥ ।।

saha sadbrahmaghoṣeṇa stutimaṅgalapāḍhakaiḥ ।
śaśāṅkodayavelāyāṃ kṛtvā dvāsthārcanaṃ viśan ।।

vairājabhuvanākāraṃ maṇḍapaṃ maṇḍanāṅkitam ।
upaviśya yathānyāyamanataryāgānatamārabhet ।।

nyāsapūrvamaśeṣaṃ tu ardhyāmbuparikalpanam ।
gaṇeśābhyarcanaṃ kṛtvā nirvighnaphalasiddhaye ।।

kalpayedbrahmakūrcaṃ tu śodhayedvasudhāṃ tataḥ ।
sthāpanaṃ toraṇādīnāmarcanaṃ kuṇḍasaṃskṛtiḥ ।।

mantrāstrakumbharacanā tayormantrāvatāraṇam ।
tadarcanādikaṃ sarvaṃ kuryāddīkṣāvidheḥ samam ।।

vyāpāramācareddivyaṃ kumbhakena smaran vibhum ।
nāniśaṃ yujyate yasmāttasmādeṣā pratikriyā ।।

vibhāvyā mantriṇā kaiṃbhī āstrī rakṣārthameva hi ।
tato avatārya bhagavān sthaṇḍile abhyarcya cāsanam ।।

japāntamakhilaṃ kṛtvā prayāyādbimbasannidhim ।
aṣṭāṅgena namaskṛtya yadyādardhyaṃ tu mūrdhani ।।

anulepanasaṃyuktaṃ tataḥ puṣpāñjaliṃ śubham ।
sāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ bhaktyā dhapūyet puruṣottamam ।।

puṣpapūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ madhyāhne yadvinirmitam ।
apāsyādāya śirasā abhivandya samarcya ca ।।

viṣvaksenasya cāstreṇa nirmalīkṛtya vāriṇā ।
sapīṭhaṃ bhagavadbiṃbaṃ prāsādaṃ śodhayettataḥ ।।

snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।
brahmakūrcādikaiḥ snānairmantrādānaprakalpitaiḥ ।।

padārthasaṃmitaiḥ śaktyā yathāvadadhivāsitaiḥ ।
phalai ratnādikopetaiḥ pūjayedvidhinā tataḥ ।।

bhaktyā kramopadiṣṭaistu bhogaiḥ kṛtsnairakṛtrimaiḥ ।
sarvaṃ kṛtvā praṇāmāntaṃ yāyādhomaniketanam ।।

tatrānalaṃ ca saṃskṛsya kuryādvai mantratarpaṇam ।
kalaśa sthārcabaimbīya saṃskṛtenātha vahninā ।।

caruṃ saṃśrapayecculyāṃ hṛdā kṣīrājyataṇḍulaiḥ ।
samuddhṛtyājyapūtaṃ taṃ vinivedya yathākramam ।।

kalaśasthalavṛttīnāmekāṃśaṃ juhuyāttataḥ ।
dadyātpūrṇāhutiṃ paścādbalibhiḥ sarvamantaram ।।

tarpayitvāmbusiktābhiḥ krameṇa juhuyāttataḥ ।
tadvadājyaṃ supūrṇaṃ taṃ mudrābandhādikaṃ tu vai ।।

kṛtvā praṇāmaparyantaṃ sthalastasyāgrato vibhoḥ ।
astramantreṇa saṃprokṣya kṛtsnadravyagaṇa tataḥ ।।

niveśya vāyudigbhāge sarvaṃ sūtrapuraḥsaram ।
sitavastrānvitenaiva tvakṣetenaiva varmaṇā ।।

arcayitvāstramantreṇa sthagayet kavacena caṃ ।
bahiḥ pakṣasamopetaṃ sarvamiṣvaṣṭakaṃ tataḥ ।।

digvidikṣvastrajaptaṃ tu dattvājyamanalālaye ।
pañcaraṅgeṇa sūtreṇa dṛḍheṇa susitena vā ।।

prādakṣiṇacatuṣkaṃ tu smaran varma samāpayet ।
grāsādasyāntarādbāhyādveṣṭayettadvadeva hi ।।

prāṅmukhastvāsanārūḍho gurupāṇiparicyutam ।
brahmakarcaṃ pibet paścāccaruśeṣaṃ tu bhakṣayet ।।

pibeddhṝdayasaṃjaptaṃ hemaratnakuśodakam ।
adyāttadanu tāmbūlaṃ dantakāṣṭhasamanvitam ।।

kutape kambalopete sthitvā ca sakuśāstare ।
japenmantravaraṃ sāṅgaṃ paṭhan stotravarān śubhān ।।

kathāṃ sarveśvarīṃ puṇyāṃ kurvanniṣpādha maṇḍalam ।
karmaśeṣaṃ tadāpādya bhūṣaṇānāṃ yathoditam ।।

ekādaśyāṃ prabhāte tu snānapūrvaṃ tu pūjanam ।
sampūrṇāhutidānāntaṃ hutvā samyagyathāvidhi ।।

āsādya kalaśoddeśaṃ vinivedanamācaret ।
tato viśeṣabhogānāṃ prabhorāmantraṇāya ca ।।

dantakāṣṭhaṃ satāmbūlaṃ mukhavāsāṃsi darpaṇam ।
candanādīni gandhāni jātipūgaphalāni ca ।।

viniveśya nidhāyāgre dakṣiṇe atha jaga tprabhoḥ ।
guggulaṃ mṛṣṭadhūpaṃ ca prakāśaṃ tāmrapātragatam ।।

dṛkprabhāmaṇḍanaṃ caiva hemasūtraṃ sakaṅkaṇam ।
madhvājyapūrite pātre taijase rocanāñjanam ।।

rasaṣaṭkaṃ mahāmūrternetravastre sitāruṇe ।
paścime atha vibhordadyāt puvyanadyudakaṃ tathā ।।

tīrthatoyānnābhogārthaṃ nagamṛt śrīphalādi yat ।
śāḍvalaṃ nīladarbhāṃśca tāmrapātre tu vāyase ।।

uttare atha vibhordadyāddevadevasya puṣkara ।
mālyānyoṣadhayaḥ sapta bījāni ca phalāni ca ।।

tilataṇḍulapātrāṇi kṣīraṃ dadhirasaṃ ghṛtam ।
gandhavṛndatvagelādyaṃ dhātavo gairikādayaḥ ।।

saphalaṃ nārikelaṃ ca vikārastvaikṣavo akhilaḥ ।
sarājate kāṃsyapātre saṃbhave sati padṛmaja ।।

yajñaparṇapuṭe vāpi vinivedyamasaṃbhave ।
sakuśodakamanyeṣāṃ tāmbūlaṃ dantadhāvanam ।।

sitāni sottarīyāṇi upavītāni candanam ।
kuṅkumāgurukarpūraśrīkhaṇḍairadhivāsitam ।।

catuḥ sthānāvatīrṇasya dadyādtrandhapavitrakam ।
tator'dhyapuṣpadhūpaṃ ca mudrābandhaṃ samācaret ।।

ādimadhyāvasāne tu samyāgacchidraśāntaye ।
japenmantravaraṃ sāṅgaṃ paścādvaddhāñjaliḥ paṭhet ।।

praṇavadavidyayādyaṃ tu strotramantraṃ nivedayet ।
sarvamantramayānanta nityasaṃnihitāvyaya ।।

guṇapradhāna yogeśa bhāvanābhogavigraha ।
nārāyaṇaṃ paraṃ brahma prāṇeśa caturākṛte ।।

sarvagācyuta sanmūrte sarvajña puraṣottama ।
asmātkālalavādyāvadvisarjanadināvadhi ।।

nānāmantragaṇopetaḥ sannidhiṃ bhaja me prabho ।
devabimbe tu tanmūrtau kalaśe maṇḍalakṣitau ।।

saṃkhyāsūtre akṣasūtre ca pāvake guruvigrahe ।
ghaṇṭāyāṃ śāstrapīṭhe ca yāgopakaraṇeṣu ca ।।

sruk-sruvādyeṣvaśeṣeṣu ekāntidvijamūrtiṣu ।
viṣṇu pāṣadabhedeṣu janmakarmarateṣu ca ।।

śraddhāpūteṣu dakṣeṣu tvadekaśaraṇeṣu ca ।
atīta vātsarīyāṇāṃ snānādīnāṃ hi karmaṇām ।।

naimittikānāṃ nityānāmapūrṇānāṃ hi śāntaye ।
tvatprītaye yathāśāstramadya nirvartayāmyaham ।।

pāvitrakaṃ vidhānaṃ ca sarvakarmaprapūraṇam ।
atoyaṃ mukhavāsādyamupacāraṃ hi carcitam ।।

homāntamadhivāsīyaṃ kuru sarvaṃ hi cātmasāt ।
tvāmarcayāmyahaṃ bhaktyā suptyatīte tu jāgare ।।

yathāvadbrahmasūtrāntaibhogairbhogāpavargada ।
vijñaptosīha bhagavan vetsi sarvaṃ hṛdi sthitam ।।

bhaktasya mama vātsalyāt prāptaḥ kāryastvanugrahaḥ ।
evaṃ nimantrayitvājamaṣṭāṅgena namet kṣitau ।।

catuḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya hṛdi mantramanusmaran ।
gītānṛttādikaiḥ stotrairvedapāṭhasamanvitaiḥ ।।

jayaśabdasametaistu jāgareṇa nayenniśām ।
snātvā brāhmamūhūrte atha kṛtakautukamaṅgalaḥ ।।

mahatā vibhavena prāk dvārayāgaṃ samācaret ।
yathāvadbhagavadyāgaṃ kuryāttadanu pauṣkara ।।

sāṃsparśikai rāsanādyairvividhairaupacārikaiḥ ।
hṛdayaṅgamasaṃjñaistu bahubhedavinirmitaiḥ ।।

bhakṣyairbhojyaistathā lehyaiścoṣyainānāvidhairapi ।
ṣaḍṛtuprabhavaiḥ sarvaiḥ śākairmūlaiḥ phalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

pāvanaiḥ pāvakasvinnairupadaṃśādikānvitaiḥ ।
gosaṃbhavaiḥ sthiraiḥ kāṃsyapātrairmadhvājyapūritaiḥ ।।

rasālakṣīrasaṃpūrṇairdiksthitaistu samudravat ।
mātrāvittaiḥ satāmbūlairantarmānairyathocitaiḥ ।।

varaśayyāsametaistu pāvanairātmavallabhaiḥ ।
svadeśaparadeśotthaiḥ krīḍābhogairakṛttimaiḥ ।।

jātarūpamayaiḥ pātrairgandhamālyādyalaṅkṛtaiḥ ।
japamudrāvasānāntamevaṃ maṇḍalasannidhau ।।

kṛtvā tu bhagavadyāgaṃ viśeṣāddevamandire ।
atha bhūṣaṇapātraṃ tu ādāyoddhāṭyapūjya ca ।।

pavitrakaṃ samādāya yāyātkalaśasaṃnidhim ।
ārādhanāṅganicayamavyaktaṃ tāttvikaṃ hi yat ।।

tṛtīyamubhayātmaṃ vai adhyātmaditrayaṃ tathā ।
anusandhāya vai tasmin saṃsmaran hṛdayāddhiyā ।।

tatrāṣṭāṣṭakasaṃkhyaṃ tu avyaktaṃ bhogasaṃgraham ।
mantramudrāsamūhaṃ tu tāttvikaṃ parikīrtitam ।।

svādhyāyagītavādyāni vratāni niyamāni ca ।
dānānyutsavapūrvāṇi nānānaimittikāni ca ।।

etānyubhayarūpāṇi puruṣārthapradāni ca ।
prītidāni jagadhānau mantramūrtau janārdane ।।

bhāsvaraṃ cinmayaṃ śuddhaṃ yadeṣāṃ rūpamakṣayam ।
tadbharbheṣvanusandheyaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tadanu pauṣkara ।।

sūryenduvahnisaṃkāśam iyattā parikalpitam ।
tadgranthigaṇadeśeṣu bhāvanīyaṃ mahāmate ।।

susthūlaṃ vyāvahāryaṃ ca tṛtīyaṃ sārvalaukikam ।
tattantunicayoddeśe bhāvanīyaṃ sadaiva hi ।।

evamādhyātmikī vyaptiṃ lakṣayitvā tu pauṣkara ।
cintayeddhidevākhyāṃ vyāptiṃ māntrīmmanaśvarīm ।।

caturṇāmavinābhāvi yadrūpamamṛtopamam ।
nānābhāsagaṇākīrṇaṃ mūrtāmūrtamanaśvaram ।।

kirīṭamālāśrīvatsakaustubhānāṃ mahāmate ।
sannidhiṃ bhāvayennityāmmadhidevātmanā trayam ।।

pṛkhyaptejo anilākāśapañcānāṃ samudāyiyat ।
ramaṇīyaṃ śubhaṃ rūpaṃ bhaktānāṃ paritoṣakṛt ।।

tadasya cādhibhūtatvaṃ mantavyaṃ yojanāvidhau ।
dhyātvaivaṃ mūlamantrānte samudīryābjasaṃbhava ।।

praṇavālaṃkṛtaṃ mantraṃ tamudyatakaraḥ paṭhet ।
tvatprāptisādhanaṃ deva jñānaṃ yadamalaṃ param ।।

bhaktiśraddhāsamopetā satkriyā svatprakāśikī ।
akhaṇḍasiddhaye tasyā hyupāyaḥ kathitastvaya ।।

jñānakarmaprasaktānāṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।
pavitrākhyaṃ yathāśaktyā tvatprasādānmayā kṛtam ।।

yathocitamidānīṃ tāṃ dhyāyasva parameśvarīm ।
tasmācchubhataraṃ karma vijñānamamalaṃ hi yat ।।

vidhyantaraṃ mantragaṇād dravyasaṅghastvameva hi ।
prāptiḥ pūrayitā pūrṇamapūrṇānāṃ hi karmaṇām ।।

taśyenānena bhagavan bhavabhaṅgārditasya ca ।
aśaṭhasya kriyākāṇḍamakhaṇḍaṃ sarvamastu te ।।

vijñapto asīha bhagavan arthitā me parā tvayi ।
vinā tvatparitoṣeṇa samyak jñānapradena ca ।।

āpatkāle tu saṃprāpte buddhipūrvaṃ mayācyuta ।
na santyājyaṃ kriyājñānaṃ tvaṃ sarvaṃ vetsi tattvataḥ ।।

yathākālaṃ yathāvacca bhogairdeva yathocitaiḥ ।
nārcito asi yathā samyak khedaścetasi tena me ।।

pūjanaṃ bhogasaṃbhogairājyadohaistu tarpaṇam ।
tvayyetatkṛtakṛtyānāṃ na kiñcidupayujyate ।।

sukṣetravāpitaṃ hyetadakhilārthasya mai'khilam ।
phaliṣyatyamṛtatvena jñātvaivaṃ hi purā mayā ।।

aṅgīkṛtaṃ gurumukhāt kintu sarveśvara prabho ।
parisphurati me buddhau na nirvyūḍhaṃ yathāsthitam ।।

manovākkāyakarmaistu āprabhātāmṛniśāvadhi ।
asvātantryādasāmarthyānmanasaścānavasthite ।।

śītoṣṇavātavarṣādyairantarāyairjvarādikaiḥ ।
asampatteḥ kriyāṅgānāṃ deva tvadunarūpiṇām ।।

āpravṛtteḥ parānandaprāptiniṣṭhaṃ yathāhnikam ।
yathoktamamarāṇāṃ tu yasmānna ghaṭate tvataḥ ।।

tasya saṃpūraṇārthaṃ tu pradhānataramarcanam ।
pavitrakākhyamādiṣṭaṃ vatsaraṃ prati yattvayā ।।

tanmayā kṛtamadhyakṣamarcitaṃ yadanirmalam ।
kriyāyogādasaṃpūrṇaṃ tanme nirmalatāṃ naya ।।

jñānato a jñānato vāpi yathoktaṃ na tu tanmayā ।
tatsarvaṃ pūrṇamevāstu sutṛpto bhava sarvadā ।।

omacyuta jagannātha mantramūrte sanātana ।
rakṣa māṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa kṣamasvāja prasīda om ।।

uktavaivaṃ mūlamantraṃ tu hṛdādyairlāñchanaiḥ saha ।
samuddiśya tato dadyānmūrdhni mantrātmano vibhoḥ ।।

sarvajñānakriyābhogaśubhasaṃkalpavigraham ।
maṇḍalāntargatasyaivaṃ prāsādāntaḥsthitasya ca ।।

vahnimadhyagatasyāpi samāropya mahāmate ।
arcanena puṭīkṛtya pāvanaṃ ca pavitrakam ।।

yāgopakaraṇānāṃ ca dattvā śāstrātmanastataḥ ।
deśikasya hṛdāropya pūjitasya ca devavat ।।

parituṣṭena tenātha tasya sarvārthasiddhaye ।
sāśiṣaṃ hi sadārabhya saṃsthitasyāgnisannidhau ।।

havanānter'canānte vā hyanyeṣāṃ kramaśastu vai ।
tataḥ prāvaraṇairdānairyathāsaṃpatti saṃbhṛtaiḥ ।।

sopavītottarīyaiśca chattropānatsamāyutaiḥ ।
vividhairbhojanairvipra dhūpaiścālabhanādikaiḥ ।।

pūjayedbrāhmaṇān sarvān susūpāyāṃstathā yatīn ।
trirātrādatha saptāhādupasaṃhṛtya pauṣkara ।।

mahadarcanapūrvaṃ tu kṛtvā pūrṇāvasānikam ।
kramaśaścopasaṃhṛtya svayaṃ gurvātmanāthavā ।।

ādāya pūjite pātre arcayitvā yathāvidhi ।
jānu nī bhūgate kṛtvā praṇipatya ca deśikam ।।

mānayitvārdhyapuṣpādyaiḥ praṇipatya svayaṃ purā ।
vinivedya ca tatpātraṃ prasādaḥ kriyātāṃ vibho ।।

sāśiṣaṃ bhagavatprītirvācyācāryeṇa tasya tu ।
yathāgamaṃ yathāśāstraṃ prasādāccaturātmanaḥ ।।

tvayi sāṃvatsaraṃ vipra susaṃpūrṇaṃ tadastu te ।
samutkīrtayatastasya āsanasthasya mūrdhani ।।

kalaśadvitayaṃ mantraṃ rakṣāsaubhāgyamokṣadam ।
visarjanaṃ vibhoḥ kuryāt pūjāpūrvaṃ yathākramam ।।

viṣvaksenaṃ yajet sāṅgaṃ tarpayettadanantaram ।
samāhṛtyākhilaṃ paścāt kṛte vai tadvisarjane ।।

prakalpya pūrvavatsomapānamacchidrasiddhaye ।
rukmarājatasadratnaghaṭite vā vibhūṣite ।।

cakrādhāre tu kalaśe vitate kamalodare ।
pāñcajanyavalīgrīve śatapatraśubhānane ।।

ūdhvārdhaḥ kaumudīmālāmaṇḍalālaṃkṛte abjaja ।
makarānanaśeṣābhiramṛtāmbupravāhake ।।

nadī samudraśrīvṛkṣamīnamālyaiḥ pariṣkṛte ।
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktā vibhorārādhanāya ca ।।

pādyārdhyācamanasnānadāne sāvatsarotsave ।
tathā sahasrakalaśairabhiṣekavidhāvapi ।।

ityuktamaravindākṣa pavitrāropaṇaṃ param ।
ūnātiriktādyadyati bhuvi bhaktajanaṃ sadā ।।

tasya nirvartanādmaktyā brāhmaṇo vedavidyavet ।
śrīmānatyugraśaśaktirvai kṣattiyo acchinnasantatiḥ ।।

dhanadhānyayuto vaiśyaḥ śudrastu sukhavān bhavet ।
gobhūsuvarṇadānānāmanantānāṃ hi yatphalam ।।

yāvajjīvaṃ pradatrānāṃ pratyahaṃ tu samāḥ śatam ।
paramāyuṣi saṃpūrṇe tatphalaṃ prāpanuyānnaraḥ ।।

prāptakālaḥ svabudhyā tu āsādyāyatanaṃ hareḥ ।
smaranmantreśvaraṃ samyak samyak sṛjati vigraham ।।

yānaiścandra pratīkāśairdivyastrījanasaṃyutaiḥ ।
vījyamāno divaṃ yāti pūjyamānastathāmaraiḥ ।।

bhuktvā bhogāṃstu vipulān sarvalokāntarodbhavān ।
kālena mahatā sādya mānuṣyaṃ punareva hi ।।

śubhe kāle śubhe deśe jāyate ca śubhe kule ।
nivṛtte bālyabhāve tu vyakte karaṇasaṃgrahe ।।

buddhitattve prabuddhe tu janmābhyāsavaśāttu vai ।
karmaṇā manasā vācā nārāyaṇaparo bhavet ।।

nityaṃ kriyāparo dhīmān brahmaṇyaḥ satyavikramaḥ ।
ananyathā viśuddhātmā duṣṭasaṅgavivarjitaḥ ।।

vyādhiśokavinirmuktaḥ putradārādikairyutaḥ ।
apamṛtyuvinirmukto jñānamāsādya nirmalam ।।

śvetadvīpaṃ samāyāti surāṇāṃ yatsudurlabham ।
jñānināmapi cānyeṣāṃ tatra dṛṣṭvā jagatpatim ।।

paraṃ brahmatvamāyāti tatkarmaparamaḥ pumān ।
paśyantyāropyamāṇaṃ ye brahmasūtraṃ jagatprabhoḥ ।।

tathānumodayantyanye yānti te apyamarāvatīm ।
śruṇvanti ye vidhānaṃ tu pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam ।।

prāpnuvanti ca te puvyamiṣṭāpūrtādikaṃ hi yat ।
nārīhyananyaśaraṇā patinā paricoditā ।।

tadbhaktā sā satī sādhvī karmaṇā manasā girā ।
nityaṃ bhartari cādrohā prayatā sāṅgatena vai ।।

pavittakaṃ jagadyonerāropayaticābjaja ।
sātulaṃ caiva saubhāgyaṃ prāpnuyādacireṇa tu ।।

dehānte devanārīṇāṃ devānāṃ yāti pūjyatām ।
sātvarundhatipūrvāṇāmavā k samabhivīkṣate ।।

jñānamāsādayatyante yena yāntya ttyutaṃ padam ।
prottārayati bandhūnāṃ duṣkṛtebhyo abjasaṃbhava ।।

pitṝṇāṃ janakādīnāṃ nāmnā snehapurastu yaḥ ।
dadāti bhūṣaṇaṃ vipra mantrī mantrātmano vibhoḥ ।।

durgateḥ sugatiṃ yāti dyusindhorasthirā naraḥ ।
yathā surāṇāmamṛtaṃ nṛṇāṃ gāṅgaṃ jalaṃ yathā ।।

svadhā yathā pitṝṇāṃ ca karmiṇāṃ tadvadabjaja ।
pavitrakaṃ kriyāḍhyānāṃ pāvanaṃ bhūtivardhanam ।।

sarvadoṣabhayaghnaṃ ca sarvopadravanāśanam ।
sarvasaukhyapradaṃ caiva sarvaguhyaprakāśakam ।।

yaḥ samyagbhagavadbhaktaḥ kṛtamantraparigrahaḥ ।
evamave pravṛttau vā janmābhyāsātsadārcane ।।

ananyatvena vai viṣṇoḥ parasya paramātmanaḥ ।
prayatnenārthanīyaṃ ca mahatānena deśikaḥ ।।

asannidhānāt svagurorabhāvāttasya cābjaja ।
pravartanīyamanyena guruṇābhyarthitena ca ।।

karmaṇā manasā vācā netarasyādhamasya ca ।
nānyadarśanasaṃsthastu madbhaktaistatparāyaṇaiḥ ।।

pavitrārohaṇādīnāmarthanīyo hi deśikaḥ ।
māmatipratipannaṃ ca antastho vetti yadyapi ।।

kṛtārthamatibhaktatvādamuṃ manye tadā gurum ।
prāptamuttārakaṃ śiṣyo manye bhaktivaśād gurum ।।

yatraiva cittavṛttīnāṃ sāmyamasti trayasya ca ।
śiṣyadeśikamantrāṇāṃ tantramokṣaśca siddhayaḥ ।।

jñātvaivaṃ yastu bhaktānāmabhaktaḥ saṃpravartate ।
mantradāne ca śiṣyāṇāṃ saṃ yāti narake adhamaḥ ।।

pratyakṣameti bhaktānāṃ bhaktiḥ prāgarjitā śanaiḥ ।
tatsamparkasamācārān mantradaivatanindanāt ।।

tasmādviṣayasaṃbhūtaṃ yasya yadviṣayaṃ sphuṭam ।
pareṣāmātmanaścāpi tasya tatsiddhidaṃ smṛtam ।।

yatrāsti deśikānāṃ ca bhaktiravyabhicāriṇī ।
tatraiva yadi śiṣyāṇāmabhilāṣo asti pūjane ।।

tadā mantravaraḥ prītaḥ sannidhiṃ kuruta'bjaja ।
siddhasya samabuddher vai niṣkriyasya tu yā kriyā ।।

ato anyasya kriyāṃ viddhi bhaktipūrvā tu sā smṛtā ।
yā ca tadviṣayā bhaktiḥ pativṛttisamocitā ।।

aṣṭāṅgalakṣaṇā pūrṇā śraddhāpūtā ca mokṣadā ।
ato anyā siddhidā siddhirvyabhicāraphalapradā ।।

sarvasyāhaṃ taṭastho ahamāśayaṃ vedmi tattvataḥ ।
bhaktirmā prati vai tābhyāṃ yadā hyavyabhicāriṇī ।।

mantrātmanānugṛhṇāmi śiṣya gurumukhena tu ।
nābhaktena tvato bhakto dīkṣaṇīyaḥ kadācana ।।

nābhaktastvatibhaktena yojanīyastvadarcane ।
guroraṃabhaktādbhaktānāṃ bhaktirabhyeti tāpanam ।।

śārīraṃ mānasaṃ duḥkhaṃ vardhate ca kṣaṇāt kṣaṇam ।
bhāvamāsuratāmeti yena yātyadhamāṃ gatim ।।

guroraananyaśaraṇādbhaktānāṃ kamalodbhava ।
dvividhaṃ trividhaṃ doṣamacirāt kṣayameti ca ।।

anugrāhyādabhaktācca sāvalepāt kriyojjhitāt ।
gurorakīrtiṃ mahatīṃ vidveṣaṃ sahate na vai ।।

sāṃmukhyaṃ duḥsahānāṃ ca doṣāṇāṃ dikṣitasya ca ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena adṛṣṭaphalasiddhaye ।।

vihitaṃ yacca tatkāryaṃ śiṣyeṇa guruṇāpi ca ।
nābhaktaḥ saṃvidāpnoti nābhakto dhyānamāpnuyāt ।।

lābhaktaḥ saṃtkriyāṃ vetti nābhaktaḥ śāstravidbhavet ।
nābhaktamarcāṃ yāgaṃ ca vahnimarcāpayettathā ।।

bandhāpayennamudrāṃ ca śrāvayetsamayānna hi ।
yo aparādhena vā lobhādabhaktānāṃ jagadgurau ।।

viparyayārthavetṝṇāmapahārasaratātmanām ।
abhigacchāpayenmohātsa yāti narakaṃ guruḥ ।।

prāyaścittaṃ hi pūrvoktaṃ tāpārto nācaredyadi ।
ityuktamaravindottha yattvayā paricoditam ।।

bhaktānāmupakārātha pavitrārohaṇaṃ śubham ।
prāvṛṭkāle pravṛtte tu trelīkyodaravartinām ।।

manuṣyāmarasiddhānāṃ vaktavyaṃ cānuvartinām ।
pravartanti hi vegena śraddhayā vatsaraṃ prati ।।

mahatyasmin mahābuddhe vyāpāre pārameśvare ।
vibhoḥ śayanasaṃsthasya kāle puṣphalākule ।।

gagane laṅghayamāne tu sabalākairvalāhakaiḥ ।
kumudotpalakahlārairbhūṣite vasudhātale ।।

vanopavanaudyāne haritaiḥ śādvalādikaiḥ ।
śālisasyādikairyukte palvalodakaśobhite ।।

pavitrakaṃ kṛtaṃ viṣṇorantaḥ sthasyātitu ṣṭidam ।
tasya prāgvihitā vipra satataṃ śayanakriyā ।।

athoktadivase tābhyāṃ brahmannirvartite sati ।
rakṣaṇīyamavaśyaṃ vai karmayāgaṃ kriyāparaiḥ ।।

iti śrīpāñcarātte mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ pavitrārohaṇaṃ nāma triṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha ekatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

śrībhagavānuvāca 

pavitrārohaṇaṃ kṛtvā cāturmāsyaṃ mahāmate ।
nirvahaṇīyaṃ niyamairvividhairlokapūjitaiḥ ।।

śayanaṃ devadevīyam arcayet tad vidhiṃ śṛṇu ।
hemādiratnaravacite sarvāṅgapariśobhite ।।

bhagavatyanurūpe ca śayane śaśivāsite ।
sitātapatracamarakiṅkiṇīvaramaṇḍite ।।

vaijayantīgaṇopete hemadaṇḍāṅghribhūṣite ।
vitānakena divyena kuṅkumādyairvibhūṣite ।।

śobhite copariṣṭāttu tiryagūrdhvapaṭāvṛte ।
jātīphalādikairlājasarvabījādipūrite ।।

vidik citrapaṭairyukte satpuṣpaprakarīkṛte ।
ratnadīpasamāyukta ityasmin śayane smaret ।।

śrīrodārṇavamadhyasthaṃ sahastraphaṇamaulinam ।
himakundendudhavalaṃ nāganāthaṃ mahāmate ।।

praṇavena svanāmnā ca varṇāntena sabindunā ।
dhyātvārcayitvā stutvā ca namaskṛtya prasādya ca ।।

niveśya tasmin karmārcāṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣitam ।
śrīkhaṇḍaśāśibāhlīkaviliptāṃ puṣpaveṣṭitām ।।

prāvṛtāṃ netravastreṇa mṛṣṭarūpaiḥ sudhūpitām ।
svabījaṃ mantravarṇaṃ tu oṃ lakṣmīpataye namaḥ ।।

samudīrya dhiyā cārdhyam aṅgopāṅgakrameṇa tu ।
dvādaśākṣaravarṇaistu svanāmapadasaṃyutaiḥ ।।

karmārcāyā abhāvāttu darbhamañjarijaṃ śubham ।
yathoktena vidhānena viṣṭare viniveśya ca ।।

tasmin mantravaraṃ nyasya svapadmagaganodarāt ।
nilīnākhila gaṇḍādiśaktipañjaramadhyagam ।।

vyaktīnāṃ mūrtidānena nītvā dhyānānvitena ca ।
devāṅgamahitaṃ vastram abhuktam amalātmakam ।।

kṣtvopari samabhyarcya puṣpadhūpavilepanaiḥ ।
sarvatatrvopasaṃhāraṃ citaḥ śaktiṃ tu vinyaset ।।

dakṣiṇe tvabhimānākhyāṃ mūrtiṃ tu camarodyatām ।
evaṃ jñānaniśāṃ vāme tālavṛntakarodyatām ।।

uttamāṃ bhāvayen nidrāṃ karasaṃvāhane ratām ।
pādāravindadeśasthāṃ lālayantīṃ karāmbujaiḥ ।।

ādāya caraṇe divye sākṣāchrīḥ sannidhisthitā ।
ānandaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ tasyai devādhidevatā ।।

tadantaḥ smaraṇānandajātavismayalocanāḥ ।
svanāmapadamantraistāḥ saṃpūjyāḥ praṇavādibhiḥ ।।

evaṃ hi devadevīyaṃ śayanaṃ kamalodbhava ।
yathoktaṃ saṃpratiṣṭhāpya cāturmāsyaparairnaraiḥ ।।

kāryātra pratyahaṃ pūjā mārjanaṃ copalepanam ।
mṛdā dhātuvikārairvā sugandhaiścandanādikaiḥ ।।

pradānaṃ dhūpadīpānāṃ vyajanenānilotthitaḥ ।
śaśicandanasaṃyuktaśītalodaka satkriyāḥ ।।

kadalīdalakahlāraiḥ padmotpalavimiśritaiḥ ।
svedaśāntiṃ samāpādya paunaḥpunyena pūjanam ।।

veṇuvīṇāsamopetāṃ gītiṃ ca madhurasvarām ।
evaṃ māsadvaye yāte jāte megharave ambarāt ।।

brahman bhādrapade māsi dvādaśyāṃ hi niśāmukhe ।
īṣat prabodham āśritya devadevo hyadhokṣajaḥ ।।

sthityartham amarāṇāṃ ca parivartanam ācaret ।
dakṣiṇenāṅgasaṅghena tyaktvā cottānaśāyikām ।।

yoganidrāṃ samāśritya prakurvan prabhavāpyayau ।
maruccakrākṣasaṃsthasya viśvabījasya pauṣkara ।।

mūlendumaṇḍalāccātha apāsyācchādanāmbaram ।
āste tvāśvayuje tveṣa dvādaśyāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।।

saṃtyajecchayanaṃ divyaṃ niśāyāṃ kārtikasya ca ।
utthāyāmaranāthaśca samākramya patatrirāṭ ।।

niḥśeṣabhuvanagrāmavīthīnāṃ doṣaśāntaye ।
vicaratyaprameyātmā nandayaṃstān surādikān ।।

āvīkṣayañjagatyasmin svakṛtaṃ dharmapaddhatim ।
evaṃ bhaktajanaiḥ kāryaṃ tasya tacceṣṭitaṃ maham ।।

vividhairutsavairdānajapajāgaraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।
nṛtragītasamopetairvilāsairhāsyasaṃyutaiḥ ।।

krīḍamānaiḥ sumanasaiḥ prayataiḥ praṇataiḥ prabhoḥ ।
ekadeśasthitairvipra ananyamānasaiḥ sadā ।।

māsaśeṣaṃ taponiṣṭhaiḥ samarthaiḥ punareva hi ।
svāśrame vāmarakṣetre rakṣaṇīyaṃ mahājanaiḥ ।।

brahman dvādaśarātreṇa ṣaḍrātreṇa śubhena ca ।
asāmarthyaṃ trirātreṇa ahorātreṇa vābjaja ।।

nayen naktāśanenātha catvāryete śubhavratāḥ ।
māsopavāsaniratairnaraiḥ paramavaiṣṇavaiḥ ।।

ante tridvayekarātraṃ vā kāryam acyutajāgaram ।
puṇyākhyānakathābhistu stotrapūrvaistu gītakaiḥ ।।

savādyairmadhurairnṛttairapahāsaiḥ tu irṣadaiḥ ।
jayaśabdairnamaskāraiḥ karatālasamanvitaiḥ ।।

samarcayecchrīnivāsaṃ juhvān dhyāyan japannapi ।
bhogaiḥ ṣaḍrasapūrvaistu sūpūrṇaiśaipacārikaiḥ ।।

ardhyairvilepanairmālyairmṛṣṭadhūpasamanvitaiḥ ।
brāhme muhūrte dvāśyāṃ mantramūrtiṃ yajeddharim ।।

śaṅkhadhvānasamopetairdundubhīpaṭahasvanaiḥ ।
vandivṛndotthitoccābhirnānāvāgbhirmahāmate ।।

mahājayajayārāvaiḥ punaḥpunarudīritaiḥ ।
prabodhalakṣaṇaistotrairutthāpya śayanāttataḥ ।।

mahatā vibhavenātha maṇḍalādau yajetkramāt ।
mahatsnapanapūrvaistu bhogaiḥ pūṇairyathoditaiḥ ।।

mahādīpaiḥ prabhūtaistu sāṅkuraiḥ pālikāgaṇaiḥ ।
phalaiḥ panasapūrvaistu madhvājyatilacarcitaiḥ ।।

puṣpārdhyacandanādyanatairbrahmasūtravibhūṣitaiḥ ।
mālatīmallikāpūrvasamutthairmañjarīgaṇaiḥ ।।

kadambacūtaśrīvṛkṣaṛjuśākhāsamanvitaiḥ ।
taraṇḍaiḥ sūtrasambadhaiḥ kuṅkumādyaiḥsupūjitaiḥ ।।

gobhūhemādikaidānaiścitraiḥ prāvaraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।
evamiṣṭvā tu homāntaṃ grāmaṃ vā nagaraṃ gṛham ।।

sapavitreṇa yānena sacakreṇa śubhena vā ।
mantrāstrakumbhayuktena tadbimbodarakeṇa vā ।।

brahmaghoṣasametena gītavādyānvitena ca ।
gaṇikābhagavadbhaktāḥ sahanāgarikairjanaiḥ ।।

parivrāḍbrahmacārībhirjapastutiparāyaṇaiḥ ।
mahatā ketuyuktena sitacchattrāvṛtena tu ।।

pradahan surabhiṃ dhūpaṃ pṛthak sāmyaṃ ca gugulum ।
yānamevaṃ paribhramya draviṇaṃ cārthiṣu kṣipet ।।

tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya caturdhāṃ praṇipatya ca ।
sarvāṅgairdaṇḍavad bhūmau bhaktyā tu puruṣotramam ।।

rathasthaṃ ālayasthaṃ tu cetasā saṃstuvan japan ।
prakṣipan cārdhyapuṣpe tu lājān siddhārthakān phalān ।।

dṛṣṭaṃ yadeva digdevaṃ bhāvayet sarvadik tathā ।
caṅkramedbhavanaṃ kṛtsnaṃ sthitiṃ badhnāti yena vai ।।

bhaktānāṃ bhagavān bhaktau dikkālādyair anāhataḥ ।
etatpradakṣiṇaṃ nāma sāmānyaṃ sarvadehinām ।।

samabhyastaṃ parijñātaṃ dadāti padamācyutam ।
jānubhyāṃ sahapāṇibhyāṃ jānubhyāṃ vā samācaret ।।

sakṛt saṃvatsarasyānte trisandhyādvādaśīṣu vā ।
ekameva tathejyānte śirasāvanatena tu ।।

samabhyarcya tato bhāvam acirād eva karmiṇām ।
phalaṃ yacchati dehānte kramāllokāstu vaibhavāḥ ।।

kṛtejyaḥ parayā bhaktayā praṇamyaivam adhokṣajam ।
pradakṣiṇair arcanīyaṃ praṇipātasamanvitaiḥ ।।

sarvakṣetrābhigamanāt sarvatīrthāṭanāt tu vai ।
phalaṃ dadāti bhagavān bhaktasya caraṇārcitam ।।

pradakṣiṇīkṛtā yena mūrtirmantrātmano hareḥ ।
doṣaiḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tyaktaḥ saṃbhavagairnareḥ ।।

bhagavat karmadīkṣāṇāṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।
prakṛṣṭam etad vyāpāraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ śubhavartmani ।।

jñānagolakatulyatvāt cakravad bhramaṇāt tu vai ।
pradadāti śubhaṃ nityaṃ kṣiṇoti kleśasaṃcayam ।।

bhagavat karmaniṣṭhānāṃ devāyatanavāsinām ।
bhaktānām api vānyeṣāṃ karmavāg indriyātmakam ।।

antargarbhagṛhe viṣṇorgarbhād vā ānanamaṇḍape ।
praṇipātagaṇaṃ kuryāt pradakṣiṇagaṇaṃ vinā ।।

vahnisthasya vibhoryasmāt pāṇipṛṣṭhasya darśanam ।
doṣakṛnmantramūrtīnām evaṃ deham asiddhikṛt ।।

jānupradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā antaḥ sannikaṭe vibhoḥ ।
viruddham aparaṃ vipra bhaktānāṃ caraṇabhramaḥ ।।

upānat pādukārūḍhacchatroṣṇīṣadharāstathā ।
yānāśvaśibikāsaṃsthaḥ tāmbūlādyaṃ hi carvayan ।।

krīḍāpakṣihilādaṇḍadarpaṇaṃ vyañjanaṃ vahan ।
prahasannathavāmodam ucchvasan pralapan bahu ।।

vilāsakelikrīḍāṃ ca kurvan kupitamānasaḥ ।
tvarāviṣṭaḥ śubhārthī yo labhen nātra bhraman phalam ।।

ananyabuddhinā tasmāt tagdatenāntarātmanā ।
kāryaṃ śubhepsunā nityaṃ gṛhāyatanayānage ।।

yasmād vai bhūriphaladam alpakleśaṃ mahāmate ।
ekaberam anantaṃ ca mahāmokṣakaraṃ param ।।

evaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kṛtvā puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ ।
avatārya rathānmāntraṃ cakrādhiṣṭhānapūrvakam ।।

pūjanīyaṃ punarapi mudrābaddhāñjaliṃ tataḥ ।
tarpaṇīyamathājyādyairdadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ śubhām ।।

ardhyadhūpapradānādyaiḥ kṣamayet puruṣottamam ।
yānapātraṃ tathā cchatraṃ pratipādya sadakṣiṇam ।।

śayanaṃ svagurorvipra dvijānāṃ tadasannidhau ।
kṛtvā jānudvayaṃ bhūmau baddhāñjaliridaṃ paṭhet ।।

deva sarveśvarānāde karmaṇānena cākhilām ।
śubhāṃ gatiṃ jano yātu prītiṃ tvaṃ paramāṃ bhaja ।।

bhojayed brāhmaṇān paścād vividhaiḥ pānabhojanaiḥ ।
śraddhayā dakṣiṇāntaiśca tṛptyarthaṃ pitṛsantateḥ ।।

anuyāgaṃ tataḥ kuryād bandhubhṛtyasamānvitaḥ ।
vibhave sati vābjottha kāryamevamanākulaiḥ ।।

draṣṭavyam amarairdevaṃ kṣetre brahmarathe sthitam ।
grāmīye nāgare sthāne vimāne vā sthitaṃ prabhum ।।

ityevamuktaṃ bhaktānāṃ vidhānaṃ kaumudīyakam ।
yasya sālokyatāpūrvaṃ phalaṃ bhāvavaśāt sthitam ।।

pavitrārohaṇādyaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।
yudaktamevam akhilaṃ yathākamalasaṃbhava ।।

asvātantrād asāmarthyād vittābhāvāttu vā dvija ।
dvādaśīṣvakhilāsvevaṃ kuryātsaṃvatsarāntare ।।

vārite api niśāyāṃ tu cāturmāsye tu saṃyame ।
bhaktairnirvahaṇīyaṃ ca tulābhāgāvasānikam ।।

prāk bhavetrulabho gastu ?dvādaśyāṃ vigataṃ yadi ।
niśāyām ācaret kṛtsnaṃ pāramyaṃ tat titheryataḥ ।।

kuryādvratavaraṃ caiva pañcāhamubhayorapi ।
ekādaśīpūrṇimānte tulādvai vṛścikāvadhi ।।

madhumāṃsaparityāgaṃ madirāstrīniṣevaṇam ।
māraṇaṃ mṛgajātīnāṃ drumavicchedanaṃ tathā ।।

vanadāhaṃ ca vasudhāsvātaṃ kuddālakādinā ।
tānaṃ gopaśūnāṃ ca vadhabandhādikaṃ nṛṇām ।।

niśāṭanam avarṇānāṃ vyavahāraṃ tu taiḥ saha ।
mṛṣṭodanaṃ tu sābhyaṅgaṃ sarvaṃ yatnād vivarjayet ।।

upasaṃhāradivasād apare ahani padmaja ।
bhaktānām āstikānāṃ ca vihitaṃ vatsaraṃ prati ।।

kartavyam abhiṣekaṃ ca svastiśāntiśubhāptaye ।
tasmād anugrahadhiyā kartācāryavareṇa tu ।।

jananyā janakenātha ṛtvigbhirvā vayo adhikaiḥ ।
gurorasannidhānācca sādhakaḥ sādhakaistu vā ।।

bhadrāsane samāropya sāmbuje svastikāṅkite ।
sūtrite navanābhe tu padme vāṣṭadale tataḥ ।।

kuṅkumādyairvilikhite kusumairvā supūrite ।
netravastraiḥ paricchanne yathoktarajasā kṛte ।।

ghaṇṭāvidhānapūrṇaistu prāksthitairvā naṣairyute ।
jātabījaśarāvaistu śubhapūrṇayavāṅkitaiḥ ।।

dadhidarpaṇasacchatrapuṣpaiḥ sanmāṅgalīyakaiḥ ।
sarvabījādikaitsarvaiḥ sugandhaiḥ śrīphalādikaiḥ ।।

maṅgalyagītibhirvādyairbrahmaghoṣasamānvitaiḥ ।
ācāryaiḥ pañcarātrajñairjapadhyānaparāyaṇaiḥ ।।

prabhavāpyayasadbrahmasadāgamamatasthitaiḥ ।
alābuvīṇājalajairvaṃśaghaṇṭāravaiḥ saha ।।

jvālāsumanasaḥ pūrṇakumbhasadvṛkṣamañjarīḥ ।
sākāravividhākanyālaṃkṛtaṃ yajñamandire ।।

dūrvādīnapi carvadbhirgovṛṣairbālavatsakaiḥ ।
paritaścāvṛte gobhirvandivṛndasamākule ।।

vṛddhaye tu parāṃ lakṣmī sarvaśaktisamanvitām ।
prāptaye tvācyutaṃ satyaṃ śāśvataṃ padamavyayam ।।

bhaktānāṃ vihitaṃ snānavidhinānena pauṣkara ।
pūrvoddiṣṭena vidhinā adhivāsya yathākramam ।।

hemādyaṃ ratnakhacitaṃ prāguktaracanānvitam ।
navakaṃ kalaśānāṃ tu nyastavyamudakodaram ।।

sarveṣāṃ varuṇaṃ tāvaddhayeyaṃ phaṇirathasthitam ।
varadābhayahastaṃ ca progdirantaṃ sudhārasam ।।

svādvākhyaṃ kṣīrasaṃjñaṃ ca ekabhāvatvam āgatam ।
vicitramakarārūḍhaṃ ratnapātrakarodyatam ।।

varapāṇiṃ samudraṃ ca dhyeyaṃ sarvatra cāmbuvat ।
nārāyaṇāṅghrisaṃbhūtāṃ pūrve janaghaṭodvahām ।।

āgneye kacchapārūḍhāṃ yamunāṃ devapūjitām ।
maṇḍūkāmbujasaṃsthāṃ ca dakṣiṇe tu sarasvatīm ।।

śanaiḥ pravāhasaṃjñāṃ ca pāśabandhavimokṣaṇīm ।
nairṛte vṛṣabhasthāṃ ca paścime siṃhavaktrakām ।।

airāvatīṃ tu vāyavye kalaśe tu gajasthitām ।
īśānapadmamadhye atra vitastāṃ mīnagāṃ ghaṭe ।।

narmadāṃ mahiṣārūḍhāṃ samāṅgāṃ devapūjitām ।
vṛ ṣadvatīṃ devikāṃ ca paroṣṇīṃ baḍabāhvayām ।।

sindhuḥ kakupsu sarvāsu aṣṭāsu paritaḥ kramāt ।
upakumbheṣu vābjasthāḥ sarvāstoyaghaṭodyatāḥ ।।

kusumaiḥstabakairyuktā jalamugdīryamānasāḥ ।
vāsudevādimūrtiśaiḥ śatāṣṭaparimantritaiḥ ।।

pūjitairabhiṣekaṃ ca dadyāt sarvaphalāptaye ।
dhyātvādhāre tu hemādye evaṃ cakragate ambuje ।।

nadīsamudravaruṇayathokte pūrvanirmite ।
utkṛṣṭamuktāratnādaye svastikādyairvibhūṣite ।।

dvādaśārāsu māsekeśavādyairadhiṣṭite ।
sarvāṅgadevatopete mantramanyaste pratiṣṭhite ।।

tadambunā tu vā kuryāt snānaṃ cāvabhṛthaṃ śubham ।
pratyahaṃ tajjalaṃ mūrdhni dhāraṇād abhivādanāt ।।

mucyate sarvadoṣebhyo maṅgalyaṃ vṛddhimeva ca ।
tīrthebhyastvāsamudrebhyo gaṅgādisarito gaṇāt ।।

snānotthaṃ phalamāpnoti bhāvitātmācyutāśrayī ।
kṛte cāvabhṛthasnāne parituṣṭo atha sādhakaḥ ।।

bhagavatpadasidyarthaṃ gurupādāmbunā svayam ।
dakṣiṇena kareṇaiva svamantraṃ manasā smaran ।।

mūrdhni saṃsicya śaṅkhākhyamudrayā cordhvavaktrayā ।
ambusikte ambare apāsya paridhāyāpare tataḥ ।।

prāgvaduṣṇīṣapūrvaistu puṣpairgandhaistu bhūṣaṇaiḥ ।
śarīram abhyalaṃkṛtya upaviśyāsane tataḥ ।।

yathoditaṃ purāstreṇa kuryānnirbhartsanaṃ tataḥ ।
abhinandya kṛtanyāso maṅgalārdhyapurassarān ।।

nṛpopakaraṇān sarvān chatracāmarapaścimān ।
deśikendrakarāt prāpya samutthāyāsanāt tataḥ ।।

namaskṛtya jagannāthaṃ parameśvaram acyutam ।
analālayam āsādya deśikendreṇa vai saha ।।

puṣpastraggandhadhūpaiśca phalairbījaistu vā ñjalim ।
pūrayitvārcanaṃ kṛtvā vibhorvahnigṛhāntare ।।

saṃsmaran hṛdi mantreśam upaviśyāgnisaṃmukham ।
tato mantrābhijaptena sāmbunā viṣṭareṇa tu ।।

prāgvadāmastakāt sarvaṃ spṛśeddhayānadhiyā śuci ।
kuryād vinyastadehaṃ tu dhyātvā mantraṃ karodare ।।

gandhapuṣpārdhyayuktaṃ tad dadyānmūrdhni śirohṛdi । sautraṃ vā kusumaṃ dārbhā 

sve ambare mekhalāsūtre upavīte atha kūrpare ।
kṛtvā samyam niviṣṭaṃ prāk dadyāt śiṣyakarāmbuje ।।

evam aikyaṃ samāpādya saguṇenānalena vai ।
āmokṣāt sarvasiddhīnāṃ tasya sāṃmukhyasiddhaye ।।

guruḥ samācareddhomaṃ pūrṇāntaṃ punareva hi ।
miśrībhūtaiḥ samiddravyaiḥ saptabhiḥ śarkarānvitaiḥ ।।

madhyasthaṃ mantramūrtervai sāṣṭakaṃ juhuyāt śatam ।
sahastraṃ vāyutaṃ vipra dadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ ।।

saviṣṭaram adhovaktraṃ strucām upari vinyaset ।
strucam abhyarcya puṣpādyairājyapūrṇāṃ strucaṃ tataḥ ।।

kuryāt pūjāṃ sugandhāktaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sārdhyairnirambubhiḥ ।
uktasaṃkhyaṃ tvatastvājyaṃ tadardham atha homayet ।।

pūjānte pātayet pūrṇāṃ punareva yathoditām ।
śatāt sahastrād ayutāllakṣād vāmalalocana ।।

jñānātmā pūrvamūrtīnāṃ caturthāṃśa pṛthak pṛthak ।
tatsamaṃ hṛdayādīnām athordhvam akhilāsu ca ।।

parameśvarakāntāsu tadardhena tu pauṣkara ।
lāñchanābharaṇādīni sarvāṇi juhuyāt kramāt ।।

sādhārāsanamantrāṇāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ kālātmarūpiṇām ।
gurvādīnāṃ ca vihitamardhaṃ lāñchanatarpaṇam ।।

sārastrāṇāṃ lokapālānāṃ dvārsthānāṃ kamalodbhava ।
gurupūrvakramād hutvā ardham ardhaṃ yathākramam ।।

kāryā caikādhikā saṃkhyā viṣamārdhasya cāhuteḥ ।
ājyahomasya viprendra tadvad eva ambujādiṣu ।।

brahmayajñadrumodbhūtāḥ pūjajñānadrumotthitāḥ ।
evaṃ kṣīratarubhyo vai samidhastrimadhuplutāḥ ।।

juhuyād vidhivanmantrī nayanmantragaṇaṃ kramāt ।
tṛptiṃ pūrṇapradānaistu aṃśāṃśahavanaiḥ kṛtaiḥ ।।

svabuddhisaṃkhyāhomena svāṅgaṃ vai viśvavighnajit ।
tarpaṇīyaśca pūrṇāntam evam ante analo dvija ।।

pūrṇāntena nayetrṛptiṃ mantravyūhe kṛte hṛdi ।
iti saṃpādite home dadyāt puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ ।।

tilakaṃ cordhvapuṇḍraṃ vā kuryād vai bhūtinā śiśoḥ ।
svasthāneṣu hṛdā varma śiromantreṇa ca kramāt ।।

hṛnmantreṇa prayoktavyaṃ sarvadā sarvakarmasu ।
tasya sarvāṇi karmāṇi sadā tena samācaret ।।

sarvamantrākhyabhūtasya vidhimevaṃ samācaret ।
kṛte cāstravaṇe vāribindavaḥ struṅmukhāt cyutāḥ ।।

dadyāt kareṇa śirasi praṇītābhājanāt tataḥ ।
homametanmumukṣorvai niṣkāmasya puroditam ।।

sakāmasya mumukṣorvai kuryāt sālaṃkṛtasya ca ।
kāṅkṣitaṃ nānujānāti sarvajño hṛdaye sthitaḥ ।।

aprārthito api svargaṃ tu bhaktānāṃ yo dadāti ca ।
kimadeyaṃ hi tasyāsti tasmād abhyarthanāṃ tyajet ।।

etāvadarthanīyaṃ ca parameśvaram acyutam ।
jantunā kṛtapūjena nityameva mahāmate ।।

mama yaccha parāṃ bhaktiṃ yayā tvaṃ me prasīdasi ।
tvayi prasanne deveśa kiṃ na prāptaṃ mayā bhuvi ।।

ityuktastvaravindākṣa ābhiṣecaniko vidhiḥ ।
samāpya bhagavat śāstraśravaṇe adhikṛto bhavet ।।

adhikārapadaṃ divyam āsādayati vaiṣṇavam ।
yenātibhaktaḥ saṃsārādutrārayati saṃkaṭāt ।।

kṛte kalaśadāne atha saktunā palalādinā ।
maṇḍalādbāhyato dadyāt prādakṣiṇyena pauṣkara ।।

sarvadigbhagavanbhūta ?baliṃ datrvā sahāmbunā ।
satilodakam adhvājyagandhapuṣpānvitena ca ।।

kāryā pitṛkriyā prāgvadodanenānalāgrataḥ ।
bahirmaṇḍalavat kuṇḍād balidāne kṛte sati ।।

ācamya pūjayitvājaṃ kumbhātkuṇḍācca maṇḍalāt ।
kṣāntyātha bhuktaṃ pūjārthaṃ mānanīyo yathāvidhi ।।

sāṅgaṃ saparivāraṃ ca dhūpayitvā yathākramam ।
tat kṣāntiprārthanāṃ kṛtvā nirambukusumādikaiḥ ।।

vahnipūjāṃ samāpādya namaskṛtya yathāvidhi ।
tacchaktim ātmasāt kṛtvā hṛdā saṃhāramudrayā ।।

visṛjya strukstruve kuryāt pariṣecanam ambunā ।
yajñabhūmeḥ svaśirasi praṇītottham athodakam ।।

atha dvābhyāṃ ca saṃhṛtya hṛdi tatsthitam acyutam ।
staropasaṃhṛtiṃ kṛtvā madhukṣīrāmbunā tataḥ ।।

saṃprāpya yarūvasudhāmānalīmapi padmaja ।
sarvam ambhasi nikṣipya samāhṛtyārdhyapūrvakam ।।

anugrahārthaṃ śiṣyasya anuyāgaṃ samācaret ।
bhagavadyāgavatkāryaṃ yāgaṃ tenāpi vai guroḥ ।।

dattvā śiṣyaṃ tato yāyād ātmayāge kṛte sati ।
yathāvad adyaprabhṛti mantrārādhanam ācaret ।।

mohālasyādikairdeṣairbuddhipūrveṇa cetasā ।
nācartavyaṃ vibhoḥ putra parityāgaṃ hi pūjane ।।

jape tathāgnibhavane snāne dāne yathodite ।
stutipāṭhe yathā śāstracintane śravaṇe api ca ।।

vyākhyāne bhavyabuddhīnāṃ nārāyaṇaratātmanām ।
śirasā dadhatām ājñāṃ kṛtvā pādābhivandanam ।।

prāṇayātrāṃ tataḥ kuryāt naivedyaprāśanādikām ।
kṛtopavāsā ye aśranti prāpaṇaṃ pārameśvaram ।।

saṃpradānāvaśiṣṭaṃ ca pūtadehā narāstu te ।
vandanīyā narāṇāṃ ca mānyā vai siddhisantateḥ ।।

anvātmatatrvaṃ vijñeyaṃ vihitaṃ tasya sarvadā ।
ātmanaivātmasiddhyarthaṃ yāgamannena tena ca ।।

sahayajñāvaśiṣṭena sāmbunā ca phalādinā ।
anuyāgaṃ ca taṃ viddhiṃ ātmanātmani yatkṛtam ।।

kurvanti bhojanāt pūrvaṃ pratyahaṃ prāśanaṃ tu ye ।
tacchakrigrahaṇaṃ prāṇe prayojanavaśāt tu vā ।।

bhāvabhaktisamāyuktāḥ sanmārgasthā dṛḍhavratāḥ ।
aprayatnena te yānti dehānte padamācyutam ।।

yeṣāṃ vratamidaṃ divyaṃ narāṇāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।
te sarvavratināṃ mūrdhni tiṣṭhanti makhayājinām ।।

mantrabrahmātmanoviṣṇoḥ samyagvidhiniveditam ।
śubhaṃ tasya parijñeyaṃ matvā vāpamidaṃ punaḥ ।।

idaṃ tadamṛtaṃ brahma idam āyuranaśvaram ।
idaṃ jñānamidaṃ vīryamidaṃ tejastu vaiṣṇavam ।।

idamindurakhaṇḍaṃ ca sthitam annātmanā svayam ।
parjanyadasya bhagavān vyañjanasthitasiddhaye ।।

hārdānalātmanā bhuṅkte adhyakṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।
tacchaktyānugṛhītatvāt so ahaṃ prakṛtigaḥ pumān ।।

evamannadamannādaṃ jñeyam annaṃ puraḥ sthitam ।
bāhyataḥ svāñyadānena saṃbodham upayāti ca ।।

yathā tathāmbunābhyeti dehastho hutabhuk prabhuḥ ।
kāraṇaṃ rasam annasya ṣaḍguṇaṃ ṣaḍvidhasya ca ।।

ātmabrahmā tataḥ tasmād īṣat kāraṇena tu ।
sāṃmukhyam ātmanāṃ nītvā tato annaṃ juhuyāt śanaiḥ ।।

prāntaparvaiścaturdhā prāk cāturātmyavyapekṣayā ।
turyāpekṣāvaśenaiva juhuyād vāhutitrayam ।।

sahṛdā mūlamantreṇa bhuñjīyāt kavalaistataḥ ।
prayatāsyakaraścānte pibenmantrābhimāntritam ।।

toyaṃ taddhyānapādābjaparistrutamathāpi vā ।
pratiṣṭitasya vā pūrvaṃ tadākṛtidharasya ca ।।

yataḥ tatsarvam āpannaṃ sarvadoṣakṣayaṅkaram ।
sarvopatāpaśamanaṃ sarvasaukhyapradaṃ sadā ।।

pāvanaṃ sarvatīrthebhyo mantrebhyaḥ padmasaṃbhava ।
atastu bhojanānte vai hārdāgnestarpaṇaṃ parā ।।

bhāvabhaktiparo nityaṃ kaṃ pibed ājyadohavat ।
brahmatīrthe tadā pāne dviḥ paṭhedvā catuḥ kramāt ।।

datraśiṣṭasya cānnasya prāpaṇākhyasya vai tadā ।
māhātmyam evam atulaṃ parijñeyaṃ yathoditam ।।

yāgāvasāne yogyānāṃ bhaktānāṃ parameśvare ।
pitṝṇāṃ tarpayen nityaṃ dayādvai prītaye vibhoḥ ।।

yo vettyevaṃ mahattāṃ ca naivedyasyācyutasya ca ।
vidhipūrvaṃ samaśrāti sayātyacyutasāmyatām ।।

vratajñena jagadyonerbhaktena ca viśeṣataḥ ।
prāṇavad rakṣaṇīyaśca prāṇebhyo nityameva hi ।।

annadānādinā samyagvidhinānena śaktitaḥ ।
parāṃ prītiṃ samabhyeti tasya vai parameśvaraḥ ।।

mūrtamannaṃ paraṃ brahma pūjitaṃ pradadāti yaḥ ।
bhagavat tatrvavetṝṇāṃ dattaṃ tenākhilaṃ bhavet ।।

vrataparyantakāle tu sthāneṣvāyatanādiṣu ।
puṇyeṣu sanmuddūrteṣu tithilagnāśriteṣu ca ।।

kṛtvākṣayaṃ bhagavato datram akṣayyam eti ca ।
satpātrāṇāṃ tadagre tu yena tuṣyatyadhokṣajaḥ ।।

apātrāṇām abhaktānāṃ nāstikānāṃ durātmanām ।
varjanīyaṃ prayatnena svānuṣṭhānapareṇa tu ।।

strīśūdrāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ ca bhṛktānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
sakāmo vātha niṣkāmo mantrajñaḥ sadvratasthitaḥ ।।

mantrapūtaṃ hi naivedyaṃ niṣiddhānāṃ dadāti yaḥ ।
siddho api yāti pātivyamārurukṣustu kiṃ punaḥ ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

jñātumicchāmi deveśa tattat saṃkṣepato yathā ।
laukikaṃ yatrvayoddiṣṭaṃ bhagavaddharmasaṃgraham ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

dhanena dharmalabdhena bhūriṇālpena vā punaḥ ।
adhikṛtyācyutaṃ devaṃ yadi vāpyaśubhaṃ śubham ।।

bhagavatprītaye tviṣṭaṃ sadasyaiḥ tanmayaiḥ saha ।
kratuvat svalphaladā svargadā yadyapi smṛtāḥ ।।

sakāmānāṃ hi tatrāpi tena tatphaladāstu vai ।
akāmānāṃ tu bhaktānāṃ nūnam acyutalokadāḥ ।।

kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni tapāṃsi vividhāni ca ।
kṛtāni bhagavatprītyai yathābhimatadāni ca ।।

yāvajjīvādhikāraṃ tu yadebhyo abhimataṃ hi yat ।
prītyarthaṃ parameśāya aṅgīkṛtam asvedadam ।।

tatphalatyācireṇaiva divyajñānātmanā tu vai ।
puṇyam āsādya vai kṣetraṃ tatra cāgatamavyayam ।।

sthale vā patrapuṣpādyairyor'cayatyaniśaṃ vratī ।
bhaktyā hyananyacittasatu dehānte tasya dehinaḥ ।।

prasādād devadevasya sthitiḥ syāt sārvalaukikī ।
pūjāṃ viṣṇuvad āpnoti yāvad jīvāvadhiṃ tu saḥ ।।

dehāvasānasamaye śvetadvīpaṃ prayāti ca ।
bhaktiśraddhāparo vidvān nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

tairvimānaiśca mārgeṇa hyacirādyān mahāmate ।
suprasiddhaiḥ sugandhaistu hṛdyaiḥ puṣphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

"arcirādyān mahāmate"ityantaṃ prathamo rāśiḥ ḥ paścāt "vibhavavyūha"ityupakramya"depādāmbupūrvaṃ tu tilasatphalacarvaṇam" ityantā ardhanyūnā ślokaviṃśatiḥ dvitīyo rāśiḥ atha ca "suprasiddhaiḥ"ityupastutya"tadbhūta darśite naiva mārgeṇa mahatā mune" ityantā ślokadvāviṃśatiḥ tṛtīyo rāśiḥ, ata ūrdhvaṃ"kṛtvā cāghrāya" ityupakramya ācādhyāyasamākṣi"caturtho rāśiḥ dvitīyakośavarge yathā prathama, dvitīya, tṛtīyarāśayaḥ yathāpūrva likhitāḥ caturthasya ārambhastu midyate yathā tṛtīyarāśeranantaraṃ punarapi dvitīyarāśim āntaṃ likhitvā tṛtīyarāśiṃ parityajya turīyarāśiranusyūtatayā samagrā likhitā vartate kośavargadvaye api dvitīyatṛtīyarāśayoḥ vyutkrameṇa lekhanameva viparyāse hetuḥ atraivaṃ samādhiḥdvitīyaturīyarāśyoranālakṣitasandhibandhatayā sthitiḥ granthasya paripāṭī anusīvyati, na viśleṣayati ca, yaḥ punarantarā patitaḥ tṛtīyo rāśiḥ sa tu turīyeṇa rāśinā sākaṃ kathaṃcidapi nānvetuṃ śaknoti । pratyuta prathamena rāśinā samaṃ sughaṭitasundhānaḥ prāptāvasaraśca saṃpadyate । asmāt paraṃ dvitīyarāśiḥ sādhūpakramaḥ granthānupūrvīṃ puṣṇāti । ataḥ darśitānusāreṇa granthaparipāṭī saṃniveśitā । paramataḥ sudhiyaḥ pramāṇam ।

yo'rcayatyacyutaṃ bhaktyā vane vā parvatāntare ।
bahavo abhimatān kāmān prāpnotyaprārthitāṃstu vai ।।

dehānte vāsavādīnāṃ saṃpūjyo bhagavāniva ।
vaiṣṇavāyatane divye saiddhe vā pauruṣe tu yat ।।

kuryāt karma dhiyā bhaktyā snānaṃ kṣīrādinā mahat ।
śrīkhaṇḍāgurukarpūrabāhlikenānulepanam ।।

sitapītāruṇairdivyairduttulairveṣṭhanaṃ ?tu vai ।
śubhena sottarīyeṇa upavītena tu dvija ।।

vibhave satyalaṃkāraiḥ sauvarṇai ratnarñjitaiḥ ।
maṇḍayet ca tataḥ puṣpaiḥ snagvaraiścaraṇāvadhi ।।

dhūpayed ājyasiktena guggulena śubhena ca ।
prabhūtaiśca mahādīpaistilatailājyapūritaiḥ ।।

abhuktāhatasuśvetarāñjitairvyativeṣṭanaiḥ ।
garbhīkṛtatvagelādyaiḥ pūjayet tadanantaram ।।

tato madhvājyayuktena dadhnābhyarcitam īśvaram ।
naivedyairvividhaiḥ pūtairbhakṣyaiḥ saphalamūlakaiḥ ।।

pānakaiḥ pāvanaiḥ svacchaiḥ śītalairmadhurādikaiḥ ।
tvagelādyanviptairdhṛṣṭairdhūpakarpūravāsitaiḥ ।।

nālikerodakopetaistarpaṇīyamanantaram ।
naivedyācamanārthaṃ tu gandhodakamanuttamam ।।

abhuktamahataṃ śuklamatha niṣpusanāmbaram ।
atha cūrṇitakarpūraghṛṣṭaśrīkhaṇḍabhāvitam ।।

sapūgaphalamutkṛṣṭaṃ tāmbūlaṃ vinivedya ca ।
śālayaḥ śimbadhānyāditilāḥ siddhārthakāni ca ।।

rocanā śrīphalaṃ puṣpaṃ dūrvā dhātrīphalaṃ dadhi ।
dukūlamahataṃ śvetaṃ dakṣiṇāvartam ambujam ।।

tamālādidalacchanne dhātūtthe vaidale api vā ।
pātre kṛtvārdhyapuṣpāḍhaye tatra madhye niveśya ca ।।

hemamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca svaśaktyā vātinirmalam ।
jānunī bhūgate kṛtvā śirasāvanatena tu ।।

ādāyottānapāṇibhyāṃ vinivedya jagatprabhoḥ ।
saṃpūraṇārthaṃ sarveṣāṃ bhogānāṃ dvijasattama ।।

yenāptiḥ sarvakāmānāṃ bhāvināṃ satphalārthinām ।
paramātmani saṃyojyam akāmānāṃ hi yena vai ।।

cāmakhyajanādīni bhogānyanyāni yāni ca ।
śayanāsananiṣṭhāni tantrīvādyāni yāni ca ।।

bhedīmṛdaṅgasatsaṅgaparyantāni mahānti ca ।
tat prekṣya svadhiyā samyam cittānandapradāni ca ।।

saṃbhave sati sarvāṇi manasā tadasaṃbhave ।
śraddhābhaktivaśāccaiva yo yajavyamarājitaiḥ ।।

svargādisatyaniṣṭhānāṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathecchayā ।
tataḥ kālāntareṇaiva devīyecchāvaśena tu ।।

tadbhūtadarśitenaiva mārgeva mahatā mune ।
vibhavavyūhalokānāmāste kalpaśatān bahūn ।।

jñānam āsādya tatraiva hyavatīryātha bhūtale ।
layaṃ ca sahasā yāti bhagavatyamitātmani ।।

śretrāyatanasattīrthavaśenācyutam arcanam ।
uktam uddeśataḥ kiñcit bhaktānāṃ bhavaśāntaye ।।

idānīṃ kā ma ?māśritya harerārādhanaṃ śṛṇu ।
bhaktānāṃ bhavanāśārthaṃ viṣṇvekaniratātmanām ।।

prabhūtaiḥ pāvanairbhogairnyāyopāyasamārjitaiḥ ।
yaṣṭavyaṃ śraddhayā bhaktyā puṇyeṣu divaseṣvatha ।।

naimittikeṣu kāleṣu nityameva nirākulaiḥ ।
divyāntarikṣabhaumākhyaśubhalagnakṣaṇeṣvapi ।।

dvādaśīṣu viśeṣeṇa pakṣayorubhayorapi ।
dineṣu deśarūḍheṣu vijñāteṣu āgamāntarāt ।।

satkriyeṣu aviruddheṣu devatāntarapūjanāt ।
payomūlaphalādyairvā parividdhādyavāsare ।।

koṣṭhasaṃkṣālanārthaṃ tu pañcagavyaṃ tataḥ pibet ।
bhagavadbimbapādāmbubhāvitaṃ parṇapātragam ।।

suvarṇadarbhasadratnakṣālitenāmbhasā saha ।
evaṃ kṛtopavāsaśca prāgvadārādhya keśavam ।।

hiraṇyānnāmbugobhūmidānaiḥ kṛṣṇājinādikaiḥ ।
niveditaiśca saṃtoṣya puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam ।।

tadājñāṃ śirasādāya yo yacchet tanmayasya ca ।
bhaktyā phalārthino nūnaṃ labhettu bhagavatpadam ।।

phalārthino asya ca punaḥ kalpakoṭiśatān bajūn ।
divyabhāvaphalatvena phalavyāśu mahāmate ।।

āyurārogyasadbhṛtyaputrapadārānvitasya ca ।
lāgnaṃ mauhūrtikaṃ karma taiyyaṃ yadapi vismṛtam ।।

saśeṣaṃ prāk samāpādya sāvadhānena cetasā ।
prāptāyāṃ puṇyavelāyāṃ karmaśeṣaṃ samāpayet ।।

pūrṇāntam ardhyapuṣpādyairdattairhemagavādikaiḥ ।
dvivāsaramaharvātra tridinaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ hi yat ।।

dvādaśāhaṃ dvipakṣaṃ yat kṣapayitvā yathāvidhi ।
vratāntavāsarātpūrvaṃ sahajāgaraṇādinā ।।

japahomārcacadhyāna praṇāmaiḥ sapradakṣiṇaiḥ ।
kathānakaistavaiḥ puṇyaiḥ kṣapaṇīyamatandritaiḥ ।।

tataḥ prabhātasamaye rātrau vā puṇyavāsare ।
prāṇāgnihavanāntaṃ ca snānapūrvaṃ samācaret ।।

sūryodayaṃ vinā rātrau viruddhamaniśaṃ dvija ।
siddhānnaṃ kalpayitvā tu dvijānām udakānvitam ।।

dadyācca bhagavatyagre susiddhaṃ haviṣā yutam ।
devapādāmbupūrvaṃ tu tilasatphalaṃcarvaṇam ।।

kṛtvā cāghrāya naivedyaṃ spṛśet punareva hi ।
bhojanāt prāk samaśrīyād aśubhadhvaṃsanāya vai ।।

vandanīyaṃ sadānandasukhasaubhāgyasiddhaye ।
eṣad dinodayaṃ hyevaṃ vratajñairbhagavanmayaiḥ ।।

vratādyadivasaṃ kāryamevaṃ vratadinasya ca ।
varjanīyaṃ prayatnena prajāsadgatikāṅkṣiṇā ।।

parapīḍadinaṃ śuddhamupādeyaṃ hi sarvadā ।
purovartidināṃśena yuktaṃ gurutaraṃ tu tat ।।

īṣadādyadinopetam upavāsadinaṃ yadi ।
loke labdhapratiṣṭhaṃ ca tathātvena tu sarvadā ।।

upavāsaparāṇāṃ tu na tad doṣapradaṃ bhavet ।
niṣkāmānāṃ hi bhaktānāṃ vrataṃ vrataparāyaṇaḥ ।।

phalārthināṃ tadbhavināṃ karmatantraratātmanām ।
pratiṣiddhaṃ ca siddhatvād upavāse aśane api ca ।।

tato aṅbhāvaṃ bhaktānāṃ natārthaṃ tatprayānti ca ।
manaso yena kāluṣyaṃ na bhavatyacyutārcane ।।

upavāsepyaśaktānāṃ karmabrahmaratātmanām ।
parapīḍasamaṃviddhi sadānaṃ sarvamācaret ।।

sopavāsavadavyasmin divase bhagavanmayaḥ ।
itikartavyatāśaktaḥ prāptādevaṃ guruṃ yajet ।।

santoṣpābhyarthyaṃ vai kṣāntiṃ vṛttyarthaṃ hi jagadguroḥ ।
divasārdhasamānena tadūnenādhikena vā ।।

yuktāmādyadinenaivaṃ purovartica vāsaram ।
kṛtvā naktāśanaṃ nityaṃ yadi saṃkalpamācaret ।।

phalaṃ sātiśayaṃ tasya upavāsāt tu jāyate ।
sarvadānāvasānāntam āpādya vratavāsare ।।

tasminnevātmayāgaṃ tu vidheyamupavāsinā ।
tadvāsarakṣayācchaśvad viśveśe pūjanādinā ।।

śiṣṭaṃ dine aparasmin vai kṛtaṃ tadabhavaṃ bhavet ।
virodhamanyathā si ddhi kṛtakṛtyasya dehinaḥ ।।

akṣīṇasya parityāgāt prabhāvādagrahasya ca ।
parapīḍatithiṣvevaṃ heyopādeyatāṃ purā ।।

jñātvā tithīśanāthātmā vāsudevo acyutaḥ prabhuḥ ।
pūjanīyo hi parvādau sopavāsaiḥ krameṇa tu ।।

pakṣayorubhayoścaiva sitapakṣe tu vecchayā ।
pitāmahātmā bhagavān tatrādya'hani padmaja ।।

vidhivatpūjanīyaśca bhaktiyuktena cetasā ।
evamabja dvipakṣeṇa ekapakṣārcane na vā ।।

kṣapayitvā yathānyāyaṃ dānairhaimaiḥ svaśaktitaḥ ।
vidhātrātmā dvitīyāyāṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ svayaṃ hariḥ ।।

tataḥ saṃyamanātmāhaṃ caturthe ha ni mānayet ।
pañcam amṛtātmānaṃ śaktiśaṃ ṣaṣṭhavāsare ।।

saptamyāṃ jñānamūrtiṃ vai viśvātmā tadanantaram ।
navamyām atha siddhātmā dharmātmā bhagavāṃsatataḥ ।।

īśānātmātha deveśaḥ sūryātmā dikprakāśakṛt ।
kāmātmātha trayodaśyāṃ kalātmātha mahāmate ।।

bhagavān pitṛsaṃjñātmā bhedāstvete jagatprabhoḥ ।
kāmyakarmādhikāreṇa nityaṃ cābhimatāptaye ।।

pūjanīyor'dhyapuṣpādyairupahāraiḥ kriyānvitaiḥ ।
pūjārtham ādyadivase brāhma ṇaṃ vatsaraṃ yajet ।।

evaṃ hi vāgvibhūtyarthī devaṃ dhātāramavyayam ।
mokṣavighnavināśārthaṃ hariṃ tatsiddhaye api ca ।।

adharmaśāntaye caiva yamaṃ saṃyamatāṃ tataḥ ।
āyurārogyavṛddhyarthaṃ pañcamyām amṛteśvaram ।।

yajecchakriprabhāvārthaṃ ṣaṣṭhyāṃ śaktīśam acyutam ।
svasaṃvidāptaye samyak taddineśamathārcayet ।।

prabhūtaye tu viśvātmā trividhāsvatha siddhiṣu ।
prāptyathraṃ navamīnāthaṃ sadharmāvāptikṛttataḥ ।।

daśamyāmarcanīyaṃ ca taddineśaṃ mahāmate ।
ekādeśe ahni vidyārthī vidyānāthamaheśvaram ।।

mahattejaḥ prabhāvārthaṃ tadīśaṃ dvādaśe ahani ।
nānāstrīratnalābhārthaṃ trayodaśyāṃ ca tatpatim ।।

kālātmā kālamṛtyūnāṃ vijaye atha yajetsadā ।
śāntaye trividhasyātha ṛṇasya parameśvaram ।।

evaṃ pañcadaśāheśo mānanīyaḥ sa sarvadā ।
yadyapyuktaṃ tithīśānāmarcanaṃ tithiṣu dvija ।।

naikāntināṃ tadvihitaṃ dvijānāmaphalārthinām ।
ekādaśyāṃ hi vai teṣāṃ pakṣayorubhayorapi ।।

parapīḍaṃ ca vihitaṃ tānniṣṭaṃ vā parāvṛtam ।
tithīśvaradvayenaiva yadyapyuktaṃ tithidvayam ।।

ekādaśyādikaṃ caivaṃ tathāpi dvijasattama ।
gauṇam etanna mukhyaṃ ca mukhyatvena tadācyutam ।।

na kevalaṃ hi tadyāvad vastujālaṃ hi cāparamṛ ।
manavaścopadeṣṭāraḥ prapañcāsyāsya pauṣkara ।।

evaṃ pravartitaṃ sarvaṃ bhaktānugrahakāmyayā ।
pūrṇabhāveśvarapadāt supūrṇamaya mudīritam ।।

vratārtham upavāsānāṃ yena saṃvatsarasya ca ।
saṃkalpamudakakṣepapūrvaṃ kṛtam akṛtrimam ।।

tasya dvādaśame māse anuyāgāvasānikam ।
dvādaśyāṃ vihitaṃ sarvam anayathā vātsaraṃ phalam ।।

viphalaṃ nūnamāyāti trayodaśyāṃ samarcanāt ।
icchayābhimatāyāṃ vai ekādaśyāṃ samācaret ।।

trivargaphalasiddhyarthaṃ bhaktyā tāvatphalaṃ vinā ।
ekarātrādikaṃ vipra vrataṃ vrataparāyaṇaḥ ।।

sarvabhāveṣvasaktatvānnadoṣastasya jāyate ।
yajane cātmayāge ca trayodaśyāṃ vinodayāt ।।

pūrvapraharaparyantakālād vā dharmamiśritam ।
ūnādhikaṃ tu praharaṃ dvādaśākhyaṃ yadā dvija ।।

aṅgabhāvaṃ trayodaśyām upayātaṃ mahāmate ।
anudyamenecchayā tu parihṛtya viśeṣataḥ ।।

svabudhyā ca trayodaśyām itikartavyatāṃ caret ।
pratyavāyo mahāṃstasya vihitaṃ vaiṣṇavasya ca ।।

amantrajñasya devānām adhikaṃ dvijatarpaṇam ।
mantrajñasyārcanaṃ homaṃ japadāne svaśaktitaḥ ।।

prītaḥ samācaredyatnaṃ vratavāṃśca kriyā paraḥ ।
saṃpadyate akhilo yena mukhyakalpavidhiḥ sadā ।।

bhaktyā saṃpratipannānāṃ vinā śāṭhyena māyayā ।
vratināṃ mukhyataḥ samyaganukalayaṃ samaṃ smṛtam ।।

sarvasya hṛdayastho vai devaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ ।
satyārthaṃ vetti vai bhāvaṃ phalaṃ yacchati tatsamam ।।

suvarṇaṃ ratnamudakaṃ ṣaḍrasāni tilāni ca ।
ājyopavītātapatramupānadvastragomahīḥ ।।

straggandhadīpadhānayaṃ ca satphalaṃ kāmikāstvamī ।
pradāya samudāyena kāmadāste bhavanti ca ।।

kāmadhenughaṭaistasmād budhaśravaṇavāsare ।
dvādaśyāṃ prīṇanīyaśca nimnasāgararakṣitau ।।

sarvakāmāpraye devaḥ sarvasatvahitāya ca ।
sarvadvandvavināśārthī pitṝṇāṃ tṛpataye ghaṭam ।।

kāmadhenvākhyadānena anena parameśvaraḥ ।
prayoti paramāṃ prītiṃ jagaduddharaṇodyataḥ ।।

avekṣya deśakālādīn gṛhe vāyatane acyutam ।
śraddhayābhyarcitaṃ taṃ tu pradattaṃ syād yathāvidhi ।।

na cet kintvaṅgabhāvaṃ tu bhāvaśaktivaśāt tu vai ।
dvijalaṃ yatra vā tīrthaṃ gaṅgāyamunasaṅgame ।।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasuhitāyāṃ

lokadharmo nāma ekatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

।।

atha dvātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa nṛṇāṃ san mantrayājinām ।
tadarcana parikhyāgād buddhipūrvāt tu kiṃ bhavet ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

mantrapūrvaṃ hi saṃkalpaṃ kṛtvā mantrasamarcane ।
anirvedānmahābuddhe yāvadāyuṣa meva ca ।।

saṃdiṣṭadevatānāṃ ca karmaṇā manasā girā ।
yatnāt nirvahaṇīyaṃ tat śaktyāsvavibhavena ca ।।

asvātantryād asāmarthyāt jāte vai sūtakādike ।
vidhivat prārthanāpūrvaṃ gurum arcāpayet tadā ।।

saṃyataṃ guruputraṃ vā bhrātaraṃ sahadīkṣitam ।
kaniṣṭham athavā jyeṣṭham anyathā kamalodbhava ।।

prāyaścittaṃ bhaved ghoraṃ prāksaṃkalpaparīkṣayā ।
tadarbham itareṣāṃ vai mantramudrādikaṃ svakam ।।

nākhyeyamatyaye prāpte samyaksiddhiparairnaraiḥ ।
prakāśayati yo mohānmantramudrādikaṃ svakam ।।

itareṣāmabhaktānāṃ tantra mantreśvaro dvija ।
sahasiddhagaṇenaiva samabhyeti parāṅmukham ।।

dattvā caiva mahāduḥkhaṃ tasmāt yatnena yājakaiḥ ।
svamantraṃ gopanīyaṃ ca itikartavyatānvitam ।।

muktvā guruṃ sutaṃ jāyāṃ tatśiṣyaṃ cāpyakṛtrimam ।
nānyeṣāṃ sannidhau kuryān mantrasantarpaṇārcane ।।

tatrāti kamalodbhūta itikartavyatāparaṃ ।
proccarenmanasā mantraṃ mantradhyānaṃ tu gopayet ।।

nmudrākṣasūtraṃ ca yathā vai siddhibhāga bhavat ।
evameva hi vai yena vinā mantraparigrahāt ।।

devārcāṃ svagṛhe bhaktyā saṃskṛtya viniveśitām ।
tasyārcane niyoktavyaḥ svasāmarthyādike sati ।।

dvijendraḥ paṃcakālajñaḥ ṣaṭkarmaniratastu vā ।
saṃbhave sati caitasya vṛttiṃ kuryāt ca śāśvatīm ।।

śāśvataṃ bhavato yena aihikāmuṣmikaṃ phalam ।
anyathā parodhena na bhayena na māyayā ।।

devam arcāpayet prājño nitye apyākasmike api vā ।
susaṃpūrṇaphalaprāpteḥ sadvṛttyamlekṣaṇa ।।

tadarthamarcanaṃ yena nityamaṅgīkṛtaṃ purā ।
pratyavāyaṃ hi tallopāt tasya tat phalabhāga bhavet ।।

nā vaktavyamatastasmād vṛttilopaṃ śubhepsunā ।
kādācitketu vā nitye niyuktānāṃ hi vārcane ।।

bahiḥ pratiṣṭhitānāṃ ca sthāpitānāṃ tu vā gṛhe ।
vṛttiṃ bhuṅkte tu yāṃ yasya yannimittaṃ mahāmate ।।

tannimitāt phalaṃ tasya saphalpādeva cākhilam ।
tasmān na lopayed vṛttim ārādhanaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

manasā mantramūrter vai arthināṃ gṛhamedhinām ।
jñātvā hṛdayasadbhāva dvābhyāṃ vai devatā dvija ।।

vidadhāti phalaṃ samyak pratyavāyaṃ karoti vā ।
evaṃ jñātvā prayatnena śāstrasadbhāvam abjaja ।।

nopekṣyā buddhipūrvā ca sāvalepena cetasā ।
yā kācit cāturātmīyā mūrtirvā vaibhavī vibhoḥ ।।

sā arcā tu śailakāṣṭhotthā paṭe kuḍaye ca citritā ।
ātmaśaktyanusāreṇa sūtakādau sadārcane ।।

lopaḥ sarakṣaṇīyaśca jñātvā kālaṃ kulotthi tam ।
kṛtvā svasvanivṛttiṃ ca śraddhāpūtena cetasā ।।

tāvad arcāpayet yāvat - kālam abhyeti nirmalam ।
kṣāntyartham arcanaṃ bhūyaḥ snānapūrvaṃ samācaret ।।

hutvāgniṃ vidhivat bhaktyā gurvādīnāṃ ca dakṣiṇā ।
prāyaścito anyathā viprabhaved ārādhakasya vai ।।

anarcanāt tu devānāṃ kalitānāṃ gṛhāntare ।
yasmād vyaktigatānāṃ ca devānām arcanaṃ nṛṇām ।।

śubhapradaṃ hyevameva kiṃ punaḥ kamalodbhava ।
vidhipūrvaṃ tu niḥśeṣaṃ sāmagrībhiḥ samanvitam ।।

saha vai bhogasaṃpatyā bhaktyā saśraddhayā dvija ।
nīti mārgagatenaiva buddhyā tu suviśuddhayā ।।

mantra - mudrāsana - dhyānair devatānāṃ yadarcanam ।
tadartha - siddhikṛt śaśvad yājakānāṃ yathāsthitaiḥ ।।

evaṃ jñātvā nāvalepaḥ kāryaḥ saṃsāra - bhīruṇā ।
anarcane tu devānāṃ kāmye naimittike abjaja ।।

pratyahaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa tava vighnaṃ yathā bhavet ।
viprādīnāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ viprayogā dikāt tu vai ।।

divyapitryocitaṃ snānaṃ kṛtvā tadanu pauṣkara ।
prāṇāyāmaṃ japāntaṃ ca prādhānyenābhivartinām ।।

mantrāṇāṃ ca mahat teṣāṃ siddhāntākhyāgamasya ca ।
prāpyate tadanuṣṭhānāt sarvotkṛṣṭhataraṃ phalam ।।

tathā ca kamalodbhūta jagatyasmin hi dṛśyate ।
devāsura - manuṣyāṇāṃ vyavahāraṃ svabhāvajam ।।

jātyuktaiḥ svapraṇair yuktā varṇādyāśramiṇo akhilāḥ ।
purāṇa - smṛtipārajñā veda vedānta vedinaḥ ।।

svakarmadharmaniratā munayo api mahāmate ।
na yānti paramāṃ siddhiṃ vinā mantra piragrahāt ।।

saidhdāntikād anuṣṭhānāt tadvidhānāṃ ca sevanāt ।
kiṃ punar lobha mohārthaṃ mānavā mandabuddhayaḥ ।।

jñātvaiva yatnamātiṣṭhen mantrārādhana karmaṇi ।
prasādane gurūṇāṃ ca siddhāntādyavagāhane ।।

tanniṣṭhānāṃ yataḥ samyak kaivalyam amalekṣaṇa ।
aparokṣam ato anyeṣāṃ śuṣkatarkaratātmanām ।।

jñāna - karmaratānāṃ ca siddhayo vividhāstviha ।
sarvathā yānti kaivalyaṃ śaśvad dehaparīkṣayā ।।

pauṣkara uvāca

nāthar jñānānuviddhasya jñātumicchāmi sāṃpratam ।
karmaṇo ahaṃ svarūpaṃ ca mantriṇāṃ yanmaharddhidam ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca

vācakāntāniviṣṭaṃ tu mantrakṛvyādikaṃ hi yat ।
prayāti cāṅgabhāvaṃ tu bhogajāle hi mantriṇām ।।

tat tadādau parijñeyaṃ nityamārādhakena tu ।
śuddha - saṃvit - svarūpaṃ ca prasphurantaṃ svatejasā ।।

viṣayendriyabhūtākhye nānā karaṇaśaktibhiḥ ।
susaṃpūrṇaṃ prabuddhābhidnyagbhūtābhiḥ parasparam ।।

yaccābhimānike rūpe bhoge vyaktiṃ vrajanti ca ।
tat punar bhogakaivalya siddhaye svayameva hi ।।

prasiddhaṃ lakṣaṇenaiva vapuṣā mantrayājinām ।
samāyātyaṅgabhāvaṃ ca evaṃ nityaṃ sthitā sthitiḥ ।।

sāṃprataṃ ca prabuddhaistu sā padmadalalocana ।
kṣeptavyā bhāvanāpekṣo vastu taccāsato na hi ।।

satvaṃ syād bhāva mantreṇa sadbhāvaṃ kintu sādhanam ।
āptavākya pradhānānām āgamaika ratātmanām ।।

samyagacyuta bhaktyā vai nirmalīkṛta cetasām ।
yathā jalatvaṃ vai vahner yuktibhir nopapadyate ।।

evaṃ jalasya vahnitvaṃ na kadācit prajāyate ।
yatra vā mantriṇā tābhyāṃ viparyāso abhidṛśyate ।।

tadindrajālaṃ vai māntraṃ bhaktānāṃ śubhavartmani ।
prerakaṃ kamalodbhūta nānā pratyayalakṣaṇam ।।

jñānamūrtistu bhagavān bhaktānugrahakāmyayā ।
bhuktvā bhogātmanāṃśena bhunakti svayameva hi ।।

muktye yājakānāṃ tu dvividhaṃ vastusaṃgraham ।
dvividhena tu bhedena tasmān nityaṃ samabhyaset ।।

jñānayuktaṃ hi vai kartṛ karmaivaṃ suvilakṣaṇam ।
yat prāptam āptavaktrt tu āgamānniścayīkṛtam ।।

abhyarthanādinā mantraṃ yatkramāt samupāgatam ।
mudrānvitaṃ mahābuddhe hyastitvenāpyalaṅkṛtam ।।

tat pramādād abuddhānām anyakarmaratātmanām ।
varṇādyaiḥ vyatyayībhūtaṃ viluptaṃ vā svarādinā ।।

adhikaṃ vābjasaṃbhūta tat karotyāśubhaṃ sadā ।
mantriṇām acirādeva tatrāpi kamalodbhava ।।

atibhaktiprabhāvena vācasyānekarūpaṇiḥ ।
saṃmukhīkaraṇādīnāṃ karmaṇā saṃprayojitam ।।

tadanugrahasāmarthyāt vāñchitaṃ saṃprayacchati ।
yasmāt sadbhakti bhūtānāṃ prapannānāṃ kramaṃ vinā ।।

prasādameti mantreśastvacirād bhāvitātmanām ।
kiṃ punar vai kriyā jñānasaṃpūrṇānāṃ tu pauṣkara ।।

bhaktiśraddhāparāṇāṃ ca bodhitānāṃ ca deśikaiḥ ।
vinā garvoktibhiḥ caiva vākyaiścittānurañjakaiḥ ।।

samudrāṇāṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ upāyaṃ prāgyato mahat ।
paraṃparāgataṃ caiva śāśvataṃ hi gurukramam ।।

tataḥ sadāstikatvaṃ ca tat parigrāhiṇo dvija ।
saṃyamaṃ bhaktipūrvaṃ tu sakriyaṃ tadanantaram ।।

tataścaivāgamārthaṃ tu paścāt saṃvedanaṃ svakam ।
buddhvaiva bhaktipūrvaṃ tu hyupāyair vividhaiḥ punaḥ ।।

āptaḥ sadāgamajñaśca sevanīyaḥ sadaiva hi ।
nityaṃ mantrapareṇaiva dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa phalārthinā ।।

saṃbhave sati samyak ca pratyahaṃ tasya pauṣkara ।
yogakṣemādikaṃ sarvaṃ cintanīyaṃ svaśaktitaḥ ।।

yasmād asmin hi saṃsāre gurutvena pravartitam ।
īśvarecchāvaśāt caivam acyutaṃ parameśvaram ।।

tanmukhena mahābuddhe yaḥ prasarpitum icchati ।
svamantraṃ bhaktimatyarthaṃ tadādau tasya[pauṣkara] ।।

tat putrasya athavā bhaktyā anuyāgavidhau sadā ।
nivedanīyaṃ pākāgraṃ parituṣṭhena cetasā ।।

āstāṃ tāvan mahābuddhe svaguruṃ tatsutaṃ tuvā ।
kramaviccāgamajño anya ekāntī vā trayīmayaḥ ।।

kṛtāhnikaḥ susaṃtuṣṭaḥ śāntacinto hyanākulaḥ ।
abhyarthito atibhakto vai cirakālaṃ mahāmate ।।

svamantrasādhanākhyaṃ vā dvi ṣaḍaṣṭaṣaḍakṣaram ।
jitantasaṃjñaṃ praṇavam ādyaṃ cāntaṃ sabījakam ।।

evam ekatra saṃyojyam ūrdhvam aṅgārakṭavat ।
sāṅgaṃ pāṇitale nyasya tadvijñānādināṃ tanau ।।

tad ahaṅkāram ālambya yasya sānugrahaṃ gṛhe ।
bhunakti tad anantaṃ vai jāyete tasya tatkṣaṇāt ।।

maṇḍalādau tu mantreśo bhogair iṣṭastathākhilaiḥ ।
tarpitaścāvnimadhye tu ājyādyairna tathābjaja ।।

samabhyeti parāṃ prītiṃ yathācāryaśarīragam ।
tasmān nimittam āśritya pratipakṣasya cāntare ।।

tathā māsasya cābdasya māsaṣaṭkasya vā abjaja ।
madhye abhyarcyaṃ viśeṣeṇa svamantraṃ gurusannidhau ।।

pitṝṇāṃ prītaye paścād bhūtaye api hi cātmanaḥ ।
prapūjya deśikendraṃtu kālaṃ rātrikṣayāvadhi ।।

pādasaṃvāhanāntaistu bhogaiḥ pādyārdhya - pūrvakaiḥ ।
prasādya ca yathāśaktyā mātravittaṃ nivedya ca ।।

anuvrajya mahābuddhe vrajantaṃ svagṛhādikam ।
evaṃ saṃpratipannā ye mantrārādhana - karmaṇi ।।

varṇā dvijendrapūrvāstu brahnacāri - puraḥsarā ।
bhaikṣukāntāstu vai sarve siddhiṃ samupayānti ca ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

purā yasyajagannātha mantramūrtir gṛhāntare ।
ekā vā nekaṃ bhedotthā vidyate bimbalakṣaṇā ।।

bhaktyā parigṛhītā prāk svayaṃ vā pūrvajair dvija ।
niveśitā mantrapūrvaṃ nikṣiptā vā pareṇa tu ।।

dhanenāptāthavānyasmād ayogyāt taskarādikāna ।
sāṃprataṃ svaguror labdhā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa prasiddhaye ।।

cittaprasāda janako mantraḥ saṃsāraduḥkhahṛt ।
sa ca tadviniyuktastu sāṅgaḥ saparivārakaḥ ।।

ārādhakasya bhagavan vihitaṃ vā navādiśā ।

śrībhagavānuvāca

svayaṃ vyaktaṃ hi yad vipra tathā maragaṇair dvija ।
sthāpitaṃ mantrasiddhestu ākāraṃ bhagavanmayaiḥ ।।

tadadhiṣṭhita - mantrāṇāṃ saha tasya ca yojanā ।
vihitā kamalodbhūta nṛṇāṃ sannidhisiddhaye ।।

evaṃ saparivāraṃ ca na svamantraḥ sadā gṛhe ।
mantrākṛtau tu cānyasmin yojanīyaḥ padādiṣapha ।।

pūjanīyaṃ svamantreṇa lāñchanāṅgānvitena ca ।
bimbasaṃruddha - mantraṃ ca tadvimuktamapi dvija ।।

sarvā caiva svayaṃvyaktapūrṇānāṃ hi mahāmate ।
niveśanaṃ hi mantrāṇām anyonyānāṃ guṇāvaham ।।

nityaṃ yo yatacittastu mantrārādhana - karmaṇi ।
dehasthaṃ kṣapayet śeṣaṃ karmabandham aśāśvatam ।।

samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu mantreṣu ca viśeṣataḥ ।
niṣiddhaṃ tadvinā nyeṣāṃ svamantrasya niyojanam ।।

kasyacit kutracit samyak yasmān manyākṛtau dvija ।
prasīdati svamātmānaṃ śudhdajñānodayaṃ vinā ।।

na niṣiddhaṃ svamantreṇa kvacid anyatra pūjanam ।
prādhānyena svamārgā cca gṛhe vā nyatra maṇḍale ।।

samāhṛtāṃ ca pūjārthaṃ mantratantrārcane sati ।
svamantreṇa na doṣo asti tadvad āyataneṣu ca ।।

mantreṇa bhinnamārgā cca pratimā maṇḍalaṃ tu vā ।
adhiṣṭhitaṃ yadā tatra vihitaṃ darśanaṃ tu vai ।।

puṣpadānaṃ svamantreṇa vyāpakena malātmanā ।
cinmātratā - svarūpeṇa mantrāṇāṃ hi yato abjaja ।।

aviśeṣaṃ hi sāmānyaṃ śabdabrahmamayaṃ vapuḥ ।
dhyāna - nyāsādikaiḥ teṣo viśeṣastu parasparam ।।

jāyate śabalaṃ bhīmam abhicāraphalapradam ।
anugrahaparaṃ mantraṃ śabdabrahmamayaṃ svakam ।।

yājya - yājakabhāvena samabhpeti tathābjaja ।
saṃruddham api yat tūtra vyaktiśakti - dhiyā vinā ।।

śabdabrahmātmanā tvāste tadaikyāt ca balaṃ kutaḥ ।
paṭavyakti - dvayenaiva vinā aikyaṃ namaso yathā ।।

dvābhyāṃ śabdasvarūpābhyām evam aikyam anugrahāt ।
sujanma caivaṃ kṣobhasya viśeṣayajanaṃ vinā ।।

svagṛhe maṇḍale yāge divyādyāyatane api ca ।

pauṣkara uvāca

paraṃ mārgaṃ na paśyāmi jagatyasmin jaganmaya ।
vāsudevātmakaṃ yasmāt sarvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca

satyam etanmahābuddhe yathā saṃyoditaṃ tvayā ।
kintu kriyāpravṛttasya jantor bhaktiparasya ca ।।

hṛdayāvarjako yatra viśrāmaḥ paramārthataḥ ।
tat sanmārgo yāñakasya vaiṣṇavaḥ sa hi sātvikaḥ ।।

svayameva pravṛttasya lokānugrahakāmyayā ।
vibhavavyūhabhāvena svacchasat ṣaṅguṇātmanā ।।

tasyopacaryate yena āgamenātha karmaṇā ।
sanmārgaṃ viddhi taṃ vipra śaśvad brahma vibhūtidam ।।

vibhurvibhavabhāvastha icchayā vitanoti yat ।।
prākṛtaṃ kṣetramāśritya tadguṇaṃ devatātmakam ।।
tanmāyīyaṃ ca niḥśeṣajñānādyaiśchuritaṃ guṇaiḥ ।
guṇātmakaṃ tu taṃ viddhi śabalaṃ nātinirmalam ।।

tad vyañjakaṃ hi yat śāstram itikartavyatā ca vai ।
asanmārgaṃ tu taṃ vipra viddhi pūrvavyapekṣayā ।।

tasmāt parapadaprāpteḥ kāraṇaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam ।
vibhavavyūhasaṃjñaṃ tu śāśvataṃ rūpam ācyutam ।।

kṣiprameva prapannānāṃ jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā ।
dadāti satpadaprāptiṃ kartiṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

kāmyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ prāptau hi acireṇaiva padmaja ।
upāyaṃ nāparaṃ manye nityaṃ bhogābhilāṣiṇām ।।

susūkṣma - nyūhavibhavaṃ muktvā sadbrahna - yājinām ।
sāṃsārikaṃ phalaṃ heyaṃ svargādi - prāptilakṣaṇam ।।

prārthyamānaṃ hi yajñādyaiḥ śaśvat tasmān na cāvyate ।
ataeva hi māyīye nārādhyo devatāgaṇaḥ ।।

samyam saṃpratipannaistu sanmārge paricodite ।
tasmāt kamalasaṃbhūta prayatnena sadaiva hi ।।

kuryād ārādhanaṃ bhaktyā mantrāṇāṃ hi yathākṣaṇam ।
eṣām anugrahād duḥkhaṃ trividhaṃ kṣayameti ca ।।

adhibhautikam ādhyātmam adhidevīyam abjaja ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

ārādhakānāṃ bhagavan mantrāṇāṃ śaśvad arcane ।
sarvadā patrapuṣpādyaiḥ bhogaiḥ kiṃ phalamarcanāt ।।

vistareṇārcanāt teṣāṃ bahubhiḥ kusumādikaiḥ ।
kiṃ phalaṃ yājakānāṃ tu atra me saṃśayo mahān ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

phalasāmyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha bhāvabhaktivaśāt sthitam ।
daridrāṇāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ phalapuṣpādinā vinā ।।

yatphalaṃ tad dvijāḍhyānāṃ nirannānāṃ tu cārcanāt ।
sadāḍhyānāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ homādyair arcanāt phalam ।।

yat tad viddhi daridraṇāṃ bhaktānāṃ kusumādikaiḥ ।
kṣaṇasya ca samaṃ jñeyaṃ sadā horātralakṣaṇam ।।

nṛpāṇāṃ ca daridrāṇāṃ kālaṃ yat tat kriyaśritam ।
tatrāpi kamalodbhūta bhūtārtham avadhāraya ।।

yathālabdhena śuddhena bhogajālena vai saha ।
kartavyā dhāraṇā dhyānaṃ mantrāṇāṃ yatra pauṣkara ।।

samudrāṇāṃ ca yogasya vistarāt nityameva hi ।
tad yājakānāṃ yajanam acirād bhuktimuktidam ।।

saṃkṣiptaṃ dhāraṇādyair yat tat kṛtam cāpyabhogadam ।
saṃbhogair dhāraṇādyair yat saṃkaṭaṃ tat cireṇa tu ।।

vidadhāti ca bhaktānāṃ bhogahīnaṃ paraṃ padam ।
tasmāt śreyo arthināṃ nityaṃ bhuktimukti - phalāptaye ।।

nirvyākudhilayā bhaktyā kālāṃśam avalabmya vai ।
vimuktamanyair vyāpārair vidhivad ghaṭate yathā ।।

susaṃpūrṇaṃ tu yajanaṃ dhāraṇādyaiḥ suvistṛtaiḥ ।
bhogair yadyapi saṃpūrṇaiḥ saṃpattiḥ saha vai nṛṇām ।।

tathāpi karmaniṣṭhānāṃ ādhikyaṃ cāsti pauṣkara ।
bhogāpavargahṛt śāṭhyāt tannirāsāt kṛte sphuṭe ।।

jāyete yājakānāṃ tu nāto tsāhaṃ parityajet ।
dravyasaṃpadvinā nityaṃ mantrārādhana - karmaṇi ।।

paraṃ hi yasya vā bhāvo bhogavṛndasya pauṣkara ।
bhogāpti phalaniṣṭhasya prathamaṃ cākṛtātmanaḥ ।।

na punarmokṣaniṣṭhasya karmaṇaḥ śāśvatasya ca ।
puruṣārthapradasyāśu khaṇḍanaṃ sadvivekinām ।।

pauṣkara uvāca

saṃsāriṇāṃ hi bhaktānāṃ nānākarmaratātmanām ।
putradārādibharaṇe nityaṃ vyākulacetasām ।।

vistareṇārcane teṣāṃ kathaṃ saṃpadyate acyuta ।
anarcanāt tvayoddiṣṭa - phalaṃ vaikalyam uttamam ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

kramayuktaṃ hi yat karma tacca śreyaskaraṃ nṛṇām ।
tasmāt tat na parityājyaṃ saṃkṣiptamatha vistṛtam ।।

mukhyakalpaṃ hi vistāram anukalpam ataḥ param ।
samatva ghaṭate kena hetunā kamalodbhava ।।

tatrāpi cā śaṭhānāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।
vihitaṃ patrapuṣpādyaiḥ sabhogaiḥ vāgbhir arcanam ।।

karmaṇām anusaṃdhānaṃ vinā kālāntareṇa tu ।
kṣmā - jalānalavāyvākhyaṃ nābhasīyaṃ mahāmate ।।

dhāraṇāpañcakāt caiva saṃkṣiptaṃ vihitaṃ dvayam ।
dahanāpyāyanākhyaṃ yad ādehāt sarvaśuddhaye ।।

parāpara - svarūpāt ca dhyānāt ekaṃ paraṃ mahat ।
hṛnmantraṃ sarvamantrayāṇām upacārakriyāvidhau ।।

karmaṇā samanaskaṃ ca praṇavādyaṃ mahāmate ।
ekā hi ārādhyamudrā vai yogamantrasya sā smṛtā ।।

smaraṇānnetrayormadhye svoccāraṃ niṣkalasya tu ।
nati - praṇavagarbhābhiḥ svasaṃjñābhiryadarcanam ।।

vidhivan mantramūrtīnāṃ tatparaṃ kṣiprasaṃjñitam ।
bījair viśeṣitābhiḥ tad dvitīyaṃ sūkṣmalakṣaṇam ।।

yallakṣaṇāmṛtaiḥ piṇḍaiḥ saha saṃjñābhir abjaja ।
japāntam akhilaṃ karma mantrāṇāṃ tad bṛhat smṛtam ।।

kṣipramādyāt ca kaivalyaṃ kiṃcit kālāntareṇa tu ।
dvitīyād abjasaṃbhūta buddhipūrvakrameṇa tu ।।

jñānādi guṇaṣaṭkaṃ ce ihaivādyaṃ prayacchati ।
aṇimādi aṣṭakaṃ caiva dvitīyam amalekṣaṇa ।।

samastabhuvanaiśvaryaṃ tṛtīyam acirāt tu vai ।
sāmyaṃ niḥśreyasāvāpteḥ sarveṣāṃ kintu pauṣkara ।।

kṣipraṃ lakṣaṇapūrveṇa kālena trividhena tu ।
mahattaiva hi mantrasya svasaṃjñākhyasya yadyapi ।।

tathāpi kamalodbhūta kṣiprapūrvādiker'cane ।
bījaṃ vā piṇḍamantraṃ ca praṇavād anusaṃsmaret ।।

ārādhyaṃ mantranāthasya hṛdādīnāṃ tathaiva ca ।
anyeṣām antaraṅgākhyaṃ mantrāṇāṃ kamalodbhava ।।

pradhānalakṣaṇānāṃ ca kamalāsanavartinām ।
na virodhasti ataḥ anyeṣāṃ bījaiḥ piṇḍairvinā abjaja ।।

vajraḷāñchana lokeśatadastrādhārartinām ।
tathāsanākhya vighneśa pūrvāṇāṃ dvāravāsināma ।।

brahmacāri - gṛhasthasya svatantrasya yaterapi ।
kiṃ punastu gṛhasthasya vyāpāraniratasya cā ।।

etad vai naiṣṭhikānāṃ tu taccittaniratātmanām ।
sādhakānāṃ savittānāṃ hitam ekāntavāsinām ।।

bhaktiśraddhāparaḥ samyaggṛhītvā yaḥ samācaret ।
dadāti tatra manyātmā pūrvoktaṃ dvividhaṃ phalam ।।
saha sādhakasiddhībhira nirvighnena mahāmate ।।
iti śrīpāñcarātre sahopaniṣadi pauṣkara -
saṃhitāyām ārādhanalopavicāraḥ nāma
dvātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha trayastriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pauṣkara uvāca 

navamūrteḥ parijñātaṃ pūrvaṃm ārādhanaṃ mayā ।
nānātvenāpavargārthaṃ na jñātaṃ caturātmanaḥ ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

anujjhitasvarūpasya devasya caturātmanaḥ ।
kevalasyārcanāt mokṣaṃ bhavete tad dvidhārcanāt ।।

nānāphalāptaye brahmannānārūpadharasya ca ।
nānātvenārcanaṃ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu samyagyathāsthitam ।।

vyāpakaṃ paramātmānam ādidevam adhokṣajam ।
prāg arcanīyaṃ sarvatra pūjānte cāpi madhyataḥ ।।

tataḥ prabhavayogena prākpatrādi samarcayet ।
catuṣkaṃ saṃkarṣaṇādyaṃ kramānnārāyaṇāntima m ।।

punarapyayayogena vandhyādhīrāpadāvadhi ? ।
nārāyaṇādyaṃ yaṣṭavyaṃ saṃkarṣaṇāntameva hi ।।

evam āgneyapadme tu pradyumnādyaṃ catuṣṭayam ।
śabdabrahmādidevāntam arcanīyaṃ sadaiva hi ।।

dakṣiṇe tu aniruddhādyaṃ garuḍāsanapaścimam ।
vihitaṃ caiva vinyāsaṃ prabhavāpyayalakṣaṇam ।।

nārāyaṇanṛsiṃhāntaṃ rakṣaḥpadmer'cayet tataḥ ।
pratyag diksaṃsthite padme brahmādyaṃ kṣmādharāntimam ।।

saṃkarṣaṇāvasānāntaṃ viṣṇvādyaṃ mārute ambuje
nṛkesariṃ varāhaṃ ca jñānādyodakṛdyudak ? ।।
trayaṃ saṃkaṣaṇādyaṃ yat īśāne kṣmādharādikam ।
prabhavenāpi ayenaiva mānanīyam ataḥ kramāt ।।

navasaṃkhyam idaṃ vipra prathamaṃ yatprakīrtitam ।
tadīyaṃ jāyate tasya prabhāvaṃ tat kamārcanāt ।।

navamūrtimayaṃ mahat ।
cāturātmyacaturvargaphaladaṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

nānāphalāpitara ācirāt jāyate ca phalārthinām ।
svātantryeṇārcanāt nityam eteṣāṃ caturātmanām ।।

yasya yasya caturmūrteḥ prathamaṃ yat prakīrtitam ।
tadīyaṃ jāyate tasya prabhāvaṃ tatkramārcamāt ।।

etāvad uktaṃ hi phalaṃ sanniveśavaśāt tu vai ।
yataḥ pratihataṃ vīryam aiśvaryaṃ prabhavāpyaye ।।

taṃ vipraṃ mantramūrtīnāṃ mantram apratimaprabham ।
anantaṃ svaprakāśatvam anaupamyaṃ jagatprabhoḥ ।।

parameśvaramūrtīnāṃ parijñānavaśāt sati ।
anādinidhano anantaḥ karmiṇāṃ pratipattaye ।।

taduttāraṇasidhyarthaṃ vyūhatām āgataḥ svayam ।
prāṇecchāśabdakālakhyacaturātmatayā nava ।।

aviśeṣasvarūpasya devasyaiva mahātmanaḥ ।
nityasannihitāśeṣaśakternityoditasya ca ।।

śabdavitsaṃbhavānandaviśeṣairgamitasya ca ।
idaṃ uktaṃ mayā yogaṃ bhavināṃ bhavaśāntaye ।।

aheyam api abhinnaṃ ca prapañcaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।
satyarūpasya vai samyak kṣobhaṃ niśreyasapradam ।।

yasya sāṃsārikī māyācakramicchāvaśāt punaḥ ।
nirgatā yatra muhyanti ṛṣayaḥ sāmarā narāḥ ।।

yāvannānugṛhītā vai deśikavyaktigena ca ।
ṣāḍguṇyamūrtinānena pareṇa caturātmanā ।।

asyārādhanakāle tu bahirvā hṛdayāmbare ।
kadambapuṣpavad vyaktiṃ saṃsmaret ṣaḍguṇojjvalām ।।

bahvātmanā cārcakena caturvarṇamayena ca ।
svareṇa vākṣareṇaiva kevalena sabindunā ।।

bāhyopacāranāmnā tu suprasiddhena kenacit ।
mukhyenābhimatenaiva manasaḥ tuṣṭidena ca ।।

nyasyāṅgāni svakānyasya prāk saṃpūrṇaguṇāni ca ।
svamantrairarcanenaiva sthānabhedaṃ vinābjaja ।।

tasmin kadambakusumasadṛśe mantragolake ।
dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa tvabhinnena tu sāṃpratam ।।

vyaktim āpādya vai tasyāṃ punarvarṇakrameṇa tu ।
aṅgopāṅgasthitiṃ kuryāt sthāneṣu hṛdayādiṣu ।।

hṛdi mūrdhni śikhāyāṃ ca skandhyoḥ karamadhyataḥ ।
netrayoḥ udare pṛṣṭhe deśe bāhudvaye tataḥ ।।

urubhyāṃ jānuyugme ca pādayoḥtadanantaram ।
tatra praṇavapūrvaṃ tu ṣaḍvarṇāstvāḍgikā matāḥ ।।

ṣaḍupāṅgābhidhāstvanye eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu ।
yat supratiṣṭhitaṃ śuddhaṃ sāmānyaṃ yad anāvṛtam ।।

prabuddhaṃ bhāsvaraṃ nityaṃ jñānaṃ sākṣāt tad ācyutam ।
svasya śaktisamūhasya balādyasyākhilasya ca ।।

udayasthitisaṃhārakāraṇe aṅgātmanā punaḥ ।
viśeṣatāṃ samāyāti svarūpam api cātyajan ।।

mantreśāmāntraśaktīnām anantānāṃ tu tadvija ।
nānāsāmarthyavargānāṃ hṛdayaṃ ratnadīpavat ।।

ātmaprakāśakaṃ caiva balādīnāṃ tathā ca tat ।
sarvātiśāyi caiśvaryaṃ yadguṇaṃ pārameśvaram ।।

tacchiraḥ sarvamantrāṇāṃ śrīmad bhogāpavargadam ।
yā bhūriśaktibhiḥ pūrṇā śaktirvai pārameśvarī ।।

ūrdhvatejovahā śuddhā viddhi māntrī śikhā tu sā ।
dhairyaṃ yannāparaṃ prāṇād ācyutaṃ dhṛtilakṣaṇāt ।।

tad eva kavacaṃ viddhi mantrāṇāṃ hi balātmakam ।
yad apratihataṃ vīryam aiśvaryaṃ prabhavāpyayam ।।

tad vipra mantramūrtīnām astram apratimaprabham ।
yadanantaprakāśatvam anaupamyaṃ jagatprabhoḥ ।।

tannetraṃ tatparijñānāt dhāma cālakṣyate param ।
hṛdā saha pralīnaṃ ca tatkeṣāṃcinmahāmate ।।

svakaṃ ujjhitya vai kṣetraṃ jñānam uddīpayed sthitam ।
mantrāṇāṃ netramantraṃ tu īśvarecchāvaśād dvija ।।

kvacid aṅgacatuṣkasya antasthā janavatprabhā ।
vartate mūrdhapūrvasya ratneṣviva upāśrayam ।।

vācakena vinā tasmāt tadīyājñāmayaprabhā ।
bhagavatkarmakuśalaiḥ parijñeyārcanā tāḥ ।।

ityāṅgikī sthitistāvat sarvatra nyāsakarmaṇi ।
prakāśitābjasaṃbhūta tvaupāṅgaṃ niścayaṃ śṛṇu ।।

kroḍīkaroti vai yena jñānadharmeṇa sarvadā ।
vahirvā viṣayaṃ svalpam upāṅgam udaram ca tat ।।

saṃsiddham upacarād vai anye apyevaṃ mahāmate ।
upāyadharmavad yastu siddhimokṣavaśāt punaḥ ।।

pṛṣṭhataḥ sarvadāne ca aiśvaryasya phalātmanaḥ ।
pṛṣṭhasaṃjñām upāṅgaṃ tad dvitīyam amalekṣaṇa ।।

dvyātmakaṃ hi yad ullāsaṃ vibhoḥ śaktyātmano dvija ।
sutīkṣṇam atisaumyaṃ ca tad upāṅgaṃ bhujābhidham ।।

vibhūtiśaktervyaktasya nānābījasya yanmahat ।
rasaṃ vīryamayaṃ kṣetram ūrusaṃjñaṃ tadātmakam ।।

yatsarvajñasya śaktervai vidyāvidyātmakaṃ vapuḥ ।
jānvākhyaṃ tad upāṅgaṃ vai pañcamaṃ parikīrtitam ।।

ācyutasthitiśaktiryat svaguṇaṃ hi vilakṣaṇam ।
saṃdhārakatvam abjākṣa tat pādāhvam udāhṛnam ।।

sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāranyāse svātmani vā prabhoḥ ।
dvādaśākṣarapūrvāṇāṃ pūrvāṅgopāṅgakalpanā ।।

sā punaḥ svalpavarṇānām adhikākṣaravartinām ।
hīnātiriktarūpāpi tad aṅgāḥ parameśvara ।।

evaṃ bhajanti māṃ nityaṃ prakriyārthaṃ tu vai punaḥ ।
svakṣetreṣu arcayen nāmnā natinā praṇavena tu ।।

varṇādhikānāṃ mantrāṇām upāṅgeṣvidamācaret ।
saha dvādaśamānaiva varṇena samudīraṇā ।।

sāmānyaśabdabhāvena syād eva hṛnmayī sthitā ।
akārādisvareṇaiva kādinā vā sabindunā ।।

svakhyañjanamiśreṇa piṇḍībhūtena pāṇinā ।
yatra dvijendra vihitaṃ vyaktidānaṃ purāṇiṣu ।।

aṅgopāṅgamayī vyāptiḥ smartavyā vānyalakṣaṇā ।
jñānāṅgopāṅganirmuktā mantrajñānaprabhātmikā ।।

yā parā prakṛtirvāṇī cidrūpā nirmalāṃ parā ।
pūritādhyakṣabhāvena niṣkalena mahātmanā ।।

śarīram iva jīvena sthūlasūkṣmād vilakṣaṇam ।
sthūlaṃ bhūtamatha tatra sūkṣmaṃ puryaṣṭakābhidham ।।

dehastham ātmatattvaṃ tu bhogaṃ viṣayajaṃ yathā ।
bhunakti tadvad ādatte pūrṇavyaktigataḥ prabhuḥ ।।

sarvathā tu svamantreṇa mantreśaṃ mūrtisaṃsthitam ।
bhogairjapaiḥ tathā stotrairvividhairvahnitarpaṇaiḥ ।।

dānairviśeṣayāgaistu pitṛtarpaṇapaścimaiḥ ।
netavyam atulāṃ prītiṃ prayogaiḥ prativācakaiḥ ।।

mantreśasyārcanaṃ kuryāt kramāttadanu pauṣkara ।
tanmūrtivācakādīnāṃ mantreśānāṃ hi mānanām ।।

antaraṅgāṅgayuktānāṃ lāñchanānāmapi dvija ।
bhogabhūmau tu tanmūrtau kintu bhogāvanestu te ।।

yathoktalakṣaṇāḥ sarve dhyātavyāstu yathākramam ।
mantramūrtau sadehe ca prasphuratkiraṇojjvalāḥ ।।
