yā parā prakṛtirmāntrī vaiśvarūpyāttu sā punaḥ ।
nānānāmākṣaratvena nānāmūrtitvam eva ca ।।

ato na vihitaṃ vitra mūrtidānaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।
mūlamantravad anyeṣāṃ mantrāṇāṃ pṛthag akṣaraiḥ ।।

kāraṇānirgatāḥ kecidvacaktiśaktiguṇairyutāḥ ।
pṛthak vyaktimayāḥ cānye mantranāthāstadicchayā ।।

ekaḥ sarveśvaro ananto jīvānām anukaṃpayā ।
nānāmantrasvarūpeṇa saṃsthitiṃ svecchayā yathā ।।

prakṛtyekā tathā bahvī hyādheyānāṃ mahātmanām ।
lokanāthecchayā vipra bahudhā saṃvyavasthitā ।।

yā parā prakṛtirmāntrī vāsudevākhyalakṣaṇā ।
ṣāḍguṇyavigrahā sarvaśaktitattvaguṇānvitā ।।

kośabhūtatvam āpannā svayam ānandalakṣaṇā ।
prakāśaikasvabhāve tu sūkṣme sve mantravigrahe ।।

japāt saṃsmaraṇād yasya svavyaktisthasya pūjanāt ।
tad abhinnaṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ param āpnoti tad vratī ।।

evam ekatvam āpannaṃ yor'cayati acyutaṃ vibhum ।
nityākṛtadha rastasya bhogamokṣau karasthitau ।।

śuddhasaṃvitsvabhāvānāṃ jñānādiguṇināṃ tu vai ।
svamantraśaktivyūhānāṃ vyaktaye parameśvaraḥ ।।

svecchayā śabdaśaktiṃ svām anabhivyaktalakṣaṇām ।
prakāśya cābjasaṃbhūta yasyāṃ mantramayaṃ vapuḥ ।।

te sarvajñaguṇaiścātha mantraiḥ saṃproktalakṣaṇāḥ ।
anugrahārthaṃ bhavināṃ nibadhnanti sthitiṃ sthirām ।।

lipivyūhe tu vividhairbīja piṇḍavad ātmike ।
kevale api ca saṃmiśre bhūrisaṃkhye japātmike ।।

jñaśuddhiḥ cid adhiṣṭhātṛvaśād amarapūjitā ।
yasyopacāramantratvam āmūlād upayānti ca ।।

śabdadehāḥ punaḥ tu ete mantrā mananadharmiṇaḥ ।
aparicyutarūpāśca nānātvam upayānti ca ।।

nānākāravaśāccaiva nānāsattvavaśād api ।
śraddhābhaktivaśānnānā nānāphalavaśāt punaḥ ।।

nānājātivaśāccāpi nānādeśavaśāt punaḥ ।
nānākālavaśād brahman nānāsādhanasaṃbhramaiḥ ।।

mokṣaikaniratānāṃ ca narāṇām ātmasiddhaye ।
viṣayākṣiptacittānāṃ bhūtaye bhavinām api ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

tvayoktaṃ bhagavad yāgaṃ śuddhasattvasya karmiṇaḥ ।
jitondriyasya bhaktasya mantrasiddhasya cācyuta ।।

yogaṃ tattvajayārthaṃ vai jñātum icchāmi ahaṃ punaḥ ।
vidhivad yat parijñānaṃ mantrajño labhate sthitam ।
nivātācaladīpābhe samādhau pārameśvare ।।

śrībhagavān uvāca 

pradhānayogam uktaṃ te karmayogād anantaram ।
tad gārhasthasya ca munervihitaṃ nānyayājinaḥ ।।

tathā paramahaṃsasya lokabāhyasthitasya ca ।
tattvayogaṃ ato vakṣye bhūmikābhinnalakṣaṇam ।।

śuddhaye akhilatattvānāṃ kṛtadīkṣasya pauṣkara ।
śaśvat sākṣtāt tu karaṇe nānāsiddhivyapekṣayā ।।

apavargāptaye caiva jñānāvaraṇaśāntaye ।
śuddhasaṃvit svabhāvena paramātmani tiṣṭhati ।।

citprakāśasvarūpeṇa mantrātmani mahāmate ।
vibhavavyūhayogena karmaṇācchādya saṃsthitaḥ ।।

vyāptaḥ pareṇa vibhunā sarvaśaktyātmakena tu ।
yam ācchādya sthitaḥ samyag bodhyaṃ taṃ sarvadābjaja ।।

asaṅkīrṇam asaṃkhyaṃ ca vāsanāśatavāsitam ।
guruṇā anugṛhītasya mantraikaniratasya ca ।।

samagraṃ tattvajālaṃ tad vinivartati nānyathā ।
atastu labdhalakṣeṇa karmatantraratena ca ।।

nityaṃ tattvajayaṃ kāryaṃ svarūpaprāptaye tu vai ।
vyāpakaḥ sarvaśaktyātmā samārādhya vibhāvya ca ।।

tattvādhiṣṭhātṛbhāvena āpādān mastakāvadhi ।
jñātavyaṃ sthānabhedena dīkṣāyāṃ kathitaṃ yathā ।।

kadalīpuṭhavaccātha tato modakavad dvija ।
tajjāyārtha samabhyasya yogam evam tridhā amalam ।।

kintu cābhyā samānasya ?moham āyā ti sāṃpratam ।
nidrālasyaśramaśvāsaśūnyadṛṣṭitvam abjaja ।।

ṣaṭkośalakṣaṇaṃ viddhi savighnaṃ te tadātmanā ।
niścayāt tad jayed etad astradhyānād japād api ।।

prāṇādīnāṃ tu vāyūnāṃ kṛtvā tu vijayaṃ purā ।
sukhāsanopaviṣṭastu gurvaṅghriṃ vandayed dhiyā ।।

vyāpakatvena cārādhya nyastvākāraśarīragam ।
tataḥ tādātmyam ālambya cittaṃ bāhyastham ācaret ।।

hṛtpuṇḍarīkamadhye tu tridhāma bhuvanodare ।
praṇavenāparaṃ brahma sarvaśaktimayaṃ dvija ।।

abhyasyābhyāsayogena prathamaṃ bhāvayet tataḥ ।
kuryāt tattvajayābhyāsaṃ vidhinānena vai dvijaḥ ।।

praṇavādyantaruddhena hṛdā saṃjñāpareṇa vā ।
sahasraraśmiṃ dhyāyed vai tattvajālaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

japād vilayam āyāti tattvajñānaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।
ādhāraṃ praṇavaṃ śabdaṃ hṛnmantraḥ tanmaye tataḥ ।।

tattvato bhavahṛt śabdaṃ tatsaṃjñaṃ praṇavodare ।
svātmānaṃ praṇavaṃ śabdam ātmānandamaye harau ।।

evaṃ krameṇa kṣmādīnāṃ tanmantrāṇāṃ jayaṃ dvija ।
kuryāt svakaraṇānāṃ ca indriyāṇāṃ parājayam ।।

iti tridaśakaṃ jitvā tattvānāṃ cāvyayena tu ।
tato manaḥ tu ahaṃkāraṃ buddhiṃ guṇagaṇaṃ kramāt ।।

tamo rajaḥ sattvasaṃjñaṃ dhyātvā japtvā parityajet ।
sūkṣmaṃ saṃdhātasaṃjñaṃ tu svaguṇebhyo vilakṣaṇam ।।

sākṣātkṛtvātha saṃtyajya avyaktaṃ ca jayet tataḥ ।
kāraṇaṃ yat prapañcasya asyoktasyāparasya ca ।।

nānāmatiniviṣṭasya svavikalpotthitasya ca ।
kālatattvam ataḥ cintyaṃ bhūtabhavyabhavātmakam ।।

suddhikṛd yad anantasya sadasad-lakṣaṇasya ca ।
prapañcasya mahābuddhe dhyātvā evaṃ tritayaṃ tyajet ।।

upāyalakṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ catuḥ saṃkhyaṃ hi lakṣaṇam ।
jñānakriyecchātrāṇākhyaśaktisaṃjñaṃ hi śāśvatam ।।

sākṣāt kuryād japād dhyānād yogābhyāsād athordhvataḥ ।
upādeyam ato brahman samūhaṃ vyāpakaṃ dhruvam ।।

saptasaṃjñaṃ padaṃ divyaṃ dhyātavyaṃ karmaśāntaye ।
śabdabrahmāvasānaṃ ca jñātavyaṃ ca sadoditam ।।

śabdabrahmasvarūpasya parasya paramātmanaḥ ।
amūrtasya ca tanmūrteḥ sthitiḥ sā ṣaḍguṇātmikā ।।

śabdabrahmana samabhyasya guṇaṣaṭkād anantaram ।
anuccāryaṃm avarṇaṃ taṃ nirāvaraṇam asvaram ।।

sadbrahmavācakaṃ tad vai vāṅmayātītam acyutam ।
svakhyañjanarūpāśca sarveṣāṃ mūrtivācakāḥ ।।

svaviśeṣācca bahavo daśūlakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ ।
akṣarasvaravarṇākhyaghoṣa rāgasvarātmakāḥ ।।

dhvaniḥ kūṭastathā sphoṭavisargāntā mahāmate ।
ebhyaḥ saṃkīrṇarūpābhyo yatne vākyatarātmanā ।।

āmokṣāt sarvasiddhīnāṃ pradātā siddhibhāg bhavet ।
dhyātā tasmin hi niṣṇātaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati ।।

samyagvetti tadābhyāsāt svārādhyenānurañjanāt ।
vilakṣaṇaṃ ca tad dhyānaṃ dhyānādhyātmakam abjaja ।।

prakāśānandarūpe ca nānābhūtaṃ hi yad bahiḥ ।
te dve sacchabdanāthasya ūrmiḥ sūkṣmatamā amalā ।।

yathā saha samaṃ yāti tattvajñastu avyaye pade ।
ātmalābham ataḥ prāpya parasmāt parameśvarāt ।।

jñānakarmaratānāṃ ca śraddhāsaṃyamasevinām ।
āstikānāṃ jitākṣāṇāṃ sadbhaktānāṃ sadā bhavet ।।

na etad vācyaṃ abhaktāya nāstikāya kadācana ।
na kutarkaṃ atiṣṭhāya karmabrahmojjhitāya ca ।।

ā prabhātāt niśāntaṃ ca vyāpāraṃ pārameśvaram ।
lokātītāstu ye viprāḥ teṣāṃ tad hṛdayaṃgamam ।।

laukikavyavahārasthā bahavo anye ca neśvarāḥ ।
śūnyabrahmaikaniṣṭhāya vākprapañcadhiyānvitāḥ ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

tattvagrāmasya bhedaiśca heyopādeyalakṣaṇam ।
jñātum icchāmi vidhivat tan mamā cakṣva śāśvata ।।

śrī bhagavān uvāca 

yathā kṣīrasya vai snehaṃ bhedena na tu vartate ।
evaṃ hi viddhi sarveṣāṃ tattvānāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।।

ekatvena pṛthaktvena samādhau proktam abhyaset ।
kevalaṃ hi yathāpūrvam udviṣṭaṃ ca tadāptaye ।।

ākṣiteḥ karaṇagrāmam indriyākhyagaṇānvitam ।
uttamavyaktaparyantaṃ prapañcaṃ tad anaśvaram ।।

nānāmūrtisamākhyaṃ ca bhogakṣetraṃ hi karmiṇām ।
sukhaduḥkhaguṇopetaṃ mohamāyāmayaṃ dṛḍham ।।

ajñānaṃ tu tadāsaktervardhane tu kṣaṇāt kṣaṇam ।
jñānād vilayam āyāti tasmāt nityaṃ hi tad dvija ।।

heyabhāvanayā cintyam upāyaṃ yadyapi sphuṭam ।
siddhīnām ātmalābhe tu tatrāpyasthiram eva tat ।।

sāram ādāya vai tasmātsādhanaṃ yogasiddhaye ।
manobuddhirahaṅkāraḥ sattvaṃ sattvavatāṃ vara ।।

catuṣkam udaṃ avyaktaṃ brahmaprāptyā nivartate ।
athopakaraṇaṃ divyaṃ pañcaśaktyopalakṣitam ।।

kālajñānakriyākhyecchāprāṇasaṃjñaṃ mahāmate ।
aheyam aparaṃ nityaṃ karmaṇyānāṃ ca siddhikṛt ।।

tattvavṛndasya vijaye guṇaṣaṭkopalabdhaye ।
cāturātmyaparijñāne śabdabrahmāptaye tu vai ।।

prakāśānandalābhe tu nirvikalpapadāptaye ।
navaprakāreṇānena prākprāptena gurormukhāt ।।

prākṛtenācyutīyena sādhyasādhanavastunā ।
tad nāsti yad na ca āpnoti sākṣātkārāttu sādhakaḥ ।।

siddhadhyāna jayāt svaṃ svaṃ phalaṃ yacchati vai sadā ।
etasmāt kāraṇāt sādhyaṃ sādhyasyānyasya sādhanam ।।

tacca jñānādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ brahmatattvavilakṣaṇam ।
aṇimādyaṣṭakaṃ caivam ato anyaṃ rocate hi yat ।।

prabhavaḥ pralayaśvaiva aiśvaryaṃ sarvatomukham ।
ādhyātmam ādhidaivatyam ādhibhūtātmanā dvija ।।

tattvābhyāsasamādhau tu jñātavyaṃ tattvacintakaiḥ ।
śabdabrahmapadād eva kṣityante tattvasaṃgrahe ।।

adhyātmaṃ paramaṃ brahma sāmānyaṃ viddhi sarvadā ।
jñātavyam adhidaivaṃ ca seśvaraṃ praṇavaṃ tathā ।।

svaṃ svaṃ svabhāvaṃ sarvasya sthūlasūkṣmaparātmakam ।
vijñeyam adhibhūtatvaṃ sākṣātkamalalocana ।।

sāmānyam etat sarvatra dhyeyam adhyātmapūrvakam ।
saviśeṣam ayo vakṣye śruṇuṣvaikāgramānasaḥ ।।

nistaraṅgaṃ paraṃ brahma śabdabrahmaṇi akṛtrime ।
adhyātmaṃ dvija boddhavyaṃ mantrakoṭyā hyanekaśaḥ ।।

adhidaivatyabhāvena tasminneva sadā sthitāḥ ।
adhibhūtaṃ tu boddhavyaṃ tad vāktttvacayaṃ tu yat ।।

adhyātmaguṇaṣaṭkākhyaṃ śabdabrahma yathoditam ।
cāturātmyaṃ parijñeyam adhidaivam anākṛti ।।

śaktivyūham asaṃkhyaṃ yad guṇebhyaḥ pravadanti tu ।
tadviśeṣasvarūpaṃ ca ādhibhūtaṃ tu viddhi tat ।।

prāṇaśaktestu cādhyātmaṃ ṣāḍguṇyam akhilaṃ hi yat ।
adhidaivatam abjākṣo vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।

adhibhūtam apānādyā vāyavo viśvadhārakāḥ ।
icchāśakteḥ paratvena sthitaṃ jñānabaladvayam ।।

jñeyaṃ tad adhidaivaṃ ca paraḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।
sāmarthyam adhibhūtaṃ ca sarvatattvāśritaṃ hi yat ।।

dvayam aiśvaryavīryākhyam adhyātmaṃ viddhi pauṣkara ।
kriyāśaktestu daivatyaṃ pradyumnaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।

mahatprakāśaprasaram adhibhūtaṃ sadoditam ।
tejaḥ śaktirdvijādhyātmam avyaktam amalekṣaṇa ।।

arkenduvahnitritayaṃ daivataṃ parikīrtitam ।
guṇatrayam asaṅkīrṇam adhibhūtaṃ mahāmate ।।

guṇatrayasya cādhyātmaṃ saṅghātakaraṇaṃ svakam ।
sattvasya daivataṃ vahnī rajasaḥ tvaṃ amṛtātpa dam ।।

tamasastapano viṣṇuḥ satva [jñānā]dhibhūtatā ।
rajasyarāgo vijñeyam adhibhūtaṃ mahāmate ।।

mahāmohaṃ hi tamasastvadhibhūtaṃ prakīrtitam ।
adhyātmaṃ cetano buddherdharmaṃ sadadhidevatā ।।

sa vai rāgaṃ ?dvijaiśvaryam adhibhūtaṃ tadātmakam ।
ahaṅkārākhyatattvasya buddhiḥ adhyātmam abjaja ।।

adhidaivaṃ parijñeyaṃ kālavaiśvānaro mahān ।
mahattvam adhibhūtaṃ ca manaso atha nirucyate ।।

adhyātmaṃ tu ahaṅkāro nṛvarāhaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
vijñeyam adhidaivaṃ ca saṃkalpaṃm adhibhūtatā ।।

pañcānām indriyāṇāṃ tu adhyātmaṃ ca manaḥ smṛtam ।
kālātmadaivataṃ viddhi adhibhūtaṃ sukhādikam ।।

vāgādīnāṃ dvijādhyātmaṃ vyūhaṃm indriyakaṃ tu yat ।
adhidaivaṃ tu boddhavyaṃ viśvarūpākhyam acyutam ।।

vyāpāram adhibhūtaṃ ca aṣṭayonyātmakaṃ hi yat ।
tanmātrāṇāṃ sabhūtānāṃm adhyātmam amalekṣaṇa ।।

sūsūkṣmaṃ karaṇavyūham adhidaivaṃ nibodhatu ।
vaibhavaṃ bhagavadvyūhaṃ vicitraṃ viddhi padmaja ।।

boddhavyaṃm adhibhūtaṃ ca tattvabhūmijayaiṣiṇām ।
uktam adhyātmapūrvaṃ yat tritayaṃ yogasiddhaye ।।

prabhāvena krameṇaiva tatpunaḥ caturānana ।
āpyayena krameṇaiva abhyastaiḥ sarvayoginām ।।

ā sarvaśaktyātmā padaparyantaṃ ācyutam ।
tattvabuddhanirāsārthaṃ yogābhyāsaṃm idaṃ smṛtam ।।

bhavet tattvajayād bhinnaṃ phalaṃ tattvaṃ phalarthinām ।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi

pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ tattvasamākhyānaṃ nāma

trayastriṃ'dhyāyaḥ ।।

atha catustriṃśodhyāyaḥ

śrībhagavānuvāca 

kṣetre vāyatane divye tīrthoddeśena saṃkutne ।
kṣudradmāṇivimukte ca vane tūpavane śubhe ।।

bhūgṛhe vā gireḥ śṛṅge gupte devagṛhāntare ।
svāsthyaṃ matvaikadeśe vā goṣṭhe dvijaparigrahe ।।

ardharātrād atikrānte kāle kamattrasaṃbhava ।
khamantrasyāgratastveva tattvābhyāsaṃ samācaret ।।

tatra śrramajaye ttrabdhe dattvārdhyaṃ mantramūrdhani ।
ghaṇṭāśabdasamopetaṃ dhūpaṃ dattvā mahāmate ।।

stutvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śucisthāne tu sāstare ।
kṛṣṇājinapraticchanne kutape kambale tu vā ।।

nidrāṃ santyajya vai brahman pāvane śayane sthitaḥ ।
brāhme muhūrte cotthāya pañcāṅgaṃ snānam ācaret ।।

plavane vāpsu madhye vā sandhyāṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi ।
tasyāgrataścopaviśya nirmalaṃ darpaṇaṃ dvija ।।

darśayitvopasaṃhṛtya mantraṃ hṛtkamalodare ।
pratiṣṭhitaṃ nitya mantraṃ vinā sthala jalātmakān ।।

mantrān kriyāṅgasaṃruddhān saṃhṛtya tadanantaram ।
śeṣamardhyādikaṃ sarvaṃ bhuktapūrveṇa vai saha ।।

pāṇinā toyapūrṇena viṣvaksenāya cārpya ca ।
prāgvad abhyasi nikṣipya samāhṛtya tadākhilam ।।

svadehādupasaṃhāramantrāṇāmapi cācaret ।
manasātmani viprendra kuryād bhogārjanaṃ tataḥ ।।

bhagavadyāgasidhyarthaṃ śuddhena draviṇena ca ।
yācayitvā ca pātrebhyo vaiṣṇavebhyo hi nānyathā ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

atyarthena jagannātha bhūyobhūyaḥ praśaṃsasi ।
bhogebhyo dhūpadānaṃ ca ghaṇṭādhvanisamanvitam ।।

mahattāṃ jñātumicchāmi pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tathā ।
yathāvad dhūpaghaṇṭābhyāṃ dhūpāgnerdhārakasya ca ।।

svarūpaṃ dhūpadhūmasya lakṣaṇaṃ pratyudīryatām ।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

śabdabrahmaikadehāyāḥ lakṣaṇaṃ kamalodbhava ।
pramāṇamatiśuddhaṃ ca saprameyaṃ nibodhatu ।।

samamardhasamaṃ jyeṣṭham āyāma m atha madhyamam ।
tattribhāgasamaṃ viddhi caturthāśaṃ tu kanyasam ।।

tribhāgena taducchrāyād dvā daśāṃśānvitena tu ।
pramāṇena tu vistāraṃ trividhaṃ tu vidhīyate ।।

kṛtvā sūtraparicchinnaṃ prākpratyagdakṣiṇottaram ।
caturaśrāyataṃ kṣetram evamāpādya vai purā ।।

tiryagūrdhvagataissūtrai bhaṅktvā saṃpūryate ?tataḥ ।
tatra pañcordhvasūtrāṇi dadyād ekādaśāni ca ।।

bhujākhyāni ca vai yāni vibhāgam atha me śṛṇu ।
sārdhaistu pañcabhirbhāgaiḥ śabdakṣetraṃ vidhīyate ।।

tatra cakraṃ ca kamalaṃ sarvadaśyaṃ prakalpya ca ।
śaṅkhaṃ kamalasaṃbhūtaṃ muktāhārādikaṃ kramāt ।।

valayatritayāntasthaṃ muktāhāraṃ suvartulam ।
bhāgārdhenāgrataḥ kuryāt tyaktvārdhār dhaṃ tadūrdhvataḥ ।।

śiṣṭenāṃśena mahatā bhāgārdhena tadūrdhvataḥ ।
nābhikṣetrānvitaṃ cakraṃ dvādaśāraṃ vidhīyate ।।

kevalaṃ kartarībhirvā miśraṃ kṣmāmiśritairvaśāt ।
ṣoḍaśāraṃ tu vā vipra śataśṛṅgaṃ manoharam ।।

sāṃśenāthordhvabhāgena karṇikākesarānvitam ।
caturviṃśaddalaṃ padmam āpādya kamalodbhava ।।

cakranābherdalāgrāṇāṃ varjayitvāntaraṃ dhiyā ।
yathābhimatamānaṃ ca suślakṣṇaracanojjhitam ।।

dalamadhyaniviṣṭaṃ va kiñjalkanicayaṃ śubham ।
kuryād vā karṇikālagnam ucchritaṃ ca susaṃhatam ।।

ūrdhve mārgadvayenātha bhāgena śubhalakṣaṇam ।
karṇikāvaniviśrāntam ardhadvaśyaṃ ca śaṅkharāṭ ।।

bhuvanāvattriyogena valībhūtena bhūṣitam ।
oṅkārāvartarūpeṇa kumbhaṃ tasyāṃśasaṃmitam ।।

kumbhoparyatha cārdhena bhāgena tu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।
kalaśaṃ ku śatāṃ ?nītvā cchidradeśāvadheḥ kramāt ।।

śaṅkhakumbhāvadhervipra śātanīyaṃ ca digdvayāt ।
matsyavallāñchanaṃ caiva ardham ardhaṃ padadvayāt ।।

caturaṃśārdhavistīrṇā prathamā bhuvanāvalī ।
dvitīyā viratā cānyā tṛtīyā bhāgasaṃmitā ।।

ā agrāt svadhiyā tvīṣadūrdhvāntaṃ kamalodbhava ।
anupātavaśānmadhyaṃ kṣāmaṃ kṣetraṃ vidhīyate ।।

śaṅkhopari yathā kāryaṃ tathā tadavadhāraya ।
sārdhabhāgacatuṣkeṇa taducchrāya mahāmate ।।

vistāraṃ sārdhabhāgena gadāyāṃ vihitaṃ tu vai ।
muṣṭisaṃjñaṃ tu yatpīṭhaṃ kuryād bhāgonnataṃ dvija ।।

caturaśraṃ tu vā ślakṣaṇaṃ citrakarmavibhūṣitam ।
vṛttāyāṃ caturaśraṃ tu turyāśraṃ vartule smṛtam ।।

tulyarūpaṃ hi vā brahman karagrāhaṃ ca tatra yat ।
tattvaṣṭāgraṃ tu vā vṛttaṃ sāmānyaṃ sarvataḥ smṛtam ।।

muṣṭerūrdhvagataṃ kuryād gadāstambhaṃ ca pūrvavat ।
viddhi taṃ saptaparvaṃ tu granthikā śuktibhiryutam ।।

muktāvaligaṇopetaṃ tīkṣṇāśraṃ caturaśrakam ।
valayākṛtirūpeṇa yuktaṃ tārāgaṇena ca ।।

śuktivṛndasametena vartulaṃ vā samāpya ca ।
racanārahitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ kevalaṃ caturaśrakam ।।

aṣṭāśraṃ ca suvṛttaṃ vā svapramāṇena lakṣitam ।
kuryād evaṃ gadāstambham atha tanmastakopari ।।

bhāgadvayonnataṃ kuryād dvibhujaṃ vā caturbhujam ।
prāguktaṃ pravibhaktāṅgaṃ pakṣamaṇḍalamaṇḍitam ।।

tatpakṣavistṛtaṃ kuryāccaturbhāgasamaṃ dvija ।
tribhāgavitataṃ cātha pucchapakṣadvayaṃ hi tat ।।

tatsamaṃ vitataṃ caiva mukhyapāṇiyugaṃ tu vai ।
vidheyaṃ kamattrodbhūta tasya saṃpuṭavadyathā ।।

pakṣavatprasṛtaṃ svasthaṃ vedādhyayanacihnitam ।
mantrajātarataṃ caiva vidheyaṃ vā savistaram ।।

prastāryaṃ vidhinānena svayaṃ kṣititattre tataḥ ।
śilpinaścaiva draṣṭavyaṃ pramāṇenākṛtaiḥ saha ।।

nyūnatvam atiriktaṃ vā ato hetostadagrataḥ ।
pūrayedghṛdayenaiva svadhiyā karmaṇā svayam ।।

calantaṃ garbhamānena tīkṣṇalohena nirmitam ।
bhāgārdhenādhikaṃ kṣetrāt śabdavyañjakamabjaja ।।

etāvad ādyaṃ vihitaṃ nirmāṇaṃ taijasaṃ mahat ।
vyaktaṃ yatrāśritaṃ kāttraṃ nābhisthaṃ kamalodbhava ।।

tatra cākramarāvṛndaṃ svakaṃ dvādaśakaṃ smṛtam ।
tadeva ṣoḍaśāraṃ ca varṇaiḥ saha napuṃsakaiḥ ।।

varṇānāṃ trividhaṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣāṃ kamalodbhava ।
saṃsthitaṃ vaikharīniṣṭhaṃ paśyantī pūrvamabjaja ।।

arāśritadviṣaṭkāre vāksvarūpaṃ paraṃ hi yat ।
tatraiva ṣoḍaśāre ca tatrevākartarīṣu ca ।।

madhyamākhyasvarūpeṇa nityameva hi vartate ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ caturviṃśatsaṃkhyaṃ varṇaguṇaṃ hi yat ।।

dalajālaṃ hi yatpadmaṃ parijñeyaṃ mahāmate ।
makārasaṃjñaṃ yadvarṇaṃ viddhi sā padmakarṇikā ।।

śaṅkhaṃ yakāravarṇaṃ samuṣṭīke gadāgrahe ।
rādayaḥsapta ye varṇā hāntāḥ parvagadātmakāḥ ।।

kṣāntaṃ patatrirāṅviddhi evaṃ kamalasaṃbhava ।
śabdabrahmasvarūpaṃ ca ghaṇṭāvigrahalakṣaṇā ।।

vijñeyā bhagavacchaktiḥ ṣāṅguṇyāntargatā hi sā ।
tejogaṇasamopetā tejastad dravyarūpadhṛk ।।

ghaṇṭākhyameta dvai viddhi adhyakṣīyaṃ guṇadvayam ।
śabdabrahmatvaheyaṃ yad hṛdayākāśamadhyagam ।।

nityoditamanaupamyaṃ manasā dagocaram ।
upadeṣṭum ato anyeṣām abhaktānāṃ na yujyate ।।

parasvarūpamantrāṇām etallakṣaṇam abjaja ।
daśaprakāre yacchabde visargānte a kṣarādike ।।

nānāmantrasvarūpe ca vartate varṇavigrahe ।
bhogamokṣaprade mantre ya āptaḥ sadgurormukhāt ।।

pañcasthānagataṃ jñeyaṃ bhaktairdivyakriyāparaiḥ ।
bahisthaṃ pratimādau tu jihvāgre hṛtkuśeśaye ।।

dhūpadhūmaśikhāyāṃ ca ghaṇṭāśabde sulakṣaṇe ।
svarūpaṃ jyotireṣāṃ tat bhāsayatsaṃsthitaṃ hṛdi ।।

madhyamena svarūpeṇa abhyucchinnaṃ mahāmate ।
dhūpadhūmāśritaṃ viddhi vaikharīvigrahaṃ punaḥ ।।

ghaṇṭāyāṃ cālyamānāyām acchinnam anubhūtaye ।
asyām āśritya ye saṃsthā jñātavyāstu sadaiva hi ।।

nityam arcanakāle tu sādhakaiḥ siddhilālasaiḥ ।
kālavaikhānaropetam anantaṃ śabdacodake ।।

muktāhārāśritaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ghaṇṭāyā vadane sthitam ।
saṃsthitaṃ ca mahābuddhe tadūrdhve gaganāśritam ।।

cakraṃ yasminnaroddeśe dvādaśātmā sthito raviḥ ।
māsātmanā punaḥ saiva kartarīṣvavatiṣṭhati ।।

ṣoḍaśātmakalātmā vai kalādehastu candramāḥ ।
sarveṣu vṛttakṣetreṣu varuṇaḥ svayameva hi ।।

tattvasaṃvalitāvyaktapadmapatrāśritastu vai ।
jīvaḥ kamalakiñjalke karṇikāśrita īśvaraḥ ।।

śaṅkhāhitaśca praṇavo vidyāṃ viddhi gadāśritam ।
prāṇādhidaivaṃ garuḍam ityevaṃ devatāgaṇam ।।

dhyātvābhyarcya purārdhyāyaiḥ dhūpayitvā yathāvidhi ।
pīṭhapratiṣṭhitāṃ kṛtvā kāleṣu kamalodbhava ।।

saṃcālanīyā vaidheṣu tāni me gadataḥ gṛṇu ।
gaṇeśapīṭhamadhyasthadevānām arcane tataḥ ।।

āhutīkālamantrāṇāṃ dhūpadāne viśeṣataḥ ।
japastutyavasānābhyāṃ pravṛtte cāgnitarpaṇe ।।

pūrṇāhutipradāne ca mantrāṇāṃ ca visarjane ।
viṣvakasenārcanākāle tatpūjāpratipādane ।।

nāto anyathā syāt vihitaṃ cālanaṃ siddhimicchatā ।
pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ saprameyaṃ sadaivatam ।।

yathāvad aravindottha mukhyam ityudinaṃ sphuṭam ।
mukhyābhāsāni cānyāni rūpāṇyasya nibodhame ।।

yathoktaṃ trividhaṃ mānaṃ vistārāyām asaṃjñitam ।
cakrādigarūḍāntena pañcasaṃkhyoditenatu ।।

saṃcālyābhimatenaiva yogyasthānāśritena ca ।
pādanīracanāṃ vipra sarvāsāṃ ca vidhīyate ।।

padmaṃ kuryāt tadūrdhve tu praphullaṃ cordhvakarṇikam ।
vitataṃ dīrghapatraṃ tu kiñjalkanicayānvitam ।।

tatkarṇikāśritaṃ kuryāt śaṅkhādyaṃ tritayaṃ hi yat ।
vaktrasūtrasamīpe tu cakraṃ vā kevalaṃ dvija ।।

kṛtvā padmānvitaṃ paścāt śakhaṃ pūrvaṃ hi tat trayam ।
yathoditaṃ ca saṃpādya sarvaṃ garuḍapaścimam ।।

vimuktacakrapadmasya kṣetrasyopari padmaja ।
śaṅkhaṃ gadāṃ khagendraṃ ca saṃpādya caturānana ।।

kavāṭopari padmaṃ tu dīrghacchadam adhomukham ।
śaṅkhacihna vinirmuktaṃ gadanālakhagānvitam ।।

samānena sabhūmervai śaṅkhaṃ kṛtvā yathoditam ।
gadā kāryā tadūrdhve tu pannāgārisamanvitā ।।

kuryād vā garuḍoddeśe ūrdhvavaktraṃ ca hetikam ।
kamalaṃ vā khavaktraṃ tu taduddeśe vidhīyate ।।

śaṅkhaṃ ca dakṣiṇāvartaṃ valitritayabhūṣitam ।
ekaikam evam āpādya śaṅkhacakrāmbujojjhite ।।

suślakṣṇavartule kṣetre muktātāragaṇānane ।
nirmuktalāñchanā ghaṇṭā vighnānām āśrayā bhavet ।।

lāñchitenānvitā vipra vighnavidrāviṇī hi sā ।
ataḥ salāñchanā kāryā nūnaṃ bhartṛphalāptaye ।।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ dhūpaghaṇṭālakṣaṇaṃ nāma catustriṃśodhyāyaḥ ।।

atha pañcatriṃśodhyāyaḥ

śrībhagavānuvāca 

ityuktaṃ dhūpaghaṇṭāyā lakṣaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam ।
yasyāṃ sañcālyamānāyāṃ dhūpadānāvadhau dvija ।।

sannidhiṃ bhajate śaśvanmantra ārādhakasya ca ।
athāṅgulaiḥ svakaiḥ kuryād adhvamānamayaistu vā ।।

caturviśatibhirbrahman dhūpaṃ dāhakam uttamam ।
āyāmenātha śilpīyairāyaśuddhaistu pūrvavat ।।

svacaturthāṃśamānena tadvaktram analāśtreyam ।
caturaśraṃ samāpādya vṛttaṃ vāṣṭāśram abjaja ।।

asyāṣṭāśrasya vai madhye kuryāccakraṃ tu sāmbujam ।
kamalaṃ vā sahetīśaṃ svastikaṃ vā nalagṛham ।।

yuktamuṣṇīṣapaṭṭena niṣṭhoddeśāttu kambunā ।
caturaśrasya vṛttasya taccakrasyātha me śṛṇu ।।

lakṣaṇaṃ hi yathāvasthaṃ saviśeṣaṃ mahāmate ।
caturatraṃ samāpādya kṣetraṃ vā vartulaṃ samam ।।

tadantare abjam abjotthanalinīnālarājitam ।
kevalaṃ tu sacakraṃ vā vidhivad bhogabhājitam ।।

āmadhyād aṣṭadhā taṃ vai kṛtvā vai susamaiḥ purā ।
bhramaṃ dadyāt ṣaḍaṃśena karṇikākoṭarāt tataḥ ।।

bhramantaṃ karṇikākhātaṃ nimnatāṃ ca nayed dvija ।
tanmānaṃ golakārdhena jānīyānmudritaṃ yathā ।।

tṛtīyāṃśena ṣaḍbhāgāt paritaḥ karṇikocchritiḥ ।
kiñjalkaistu susaṃvītaṃ tanmānenopalakṣitaiḥ ।।

saptamāṃśāttu yacchiṣṭaṃ bahiḥ kesarasantateḥ ।
bhāgadvayaṃ tu vai yena dalajālaṃ samāpya ca ।।

yathābhimatasaṃkhyaṃ ca evaṃ bhāgena tadbahiḥ ।
muktājālasamopetaṃ cakramāpādya pūrvavat ।।

aṣṭamāṃśāccaturthāṃśaṃ bhāgam ādāya vai dvija ।
kṣetrasya coktamānasya vedyartham anuyojya ca ।।

vedyāḥ koṇacatuṣke tu kuryācchaṅkhacatuṣṭayam ।
caturaśrasya yā proktā vedikā śaṅkhabhūṣitā ।।

sthitirnaiṣā ca vihitā vṛttakṣetrasya padmaja ।
padmapṛṣṭhād viniṣkrāntaṃ yathābhimatavartulam ।।

vedikāvaniparyantaṃ cakranemyavadhiṃ tu vā ।
vaktrākāraṃ suvṛttaṃ vā taduddeśāt tu taṃ punaḥ ।।

vedisaṃdhāraṇārthaṃ tu procchritaṃ paṅkajadvayam ।
tanmadhye lakṣaṇopetaṃ sthitaṃ padmāsanādinā ।।

kuryād āgneyam ākāraṃ tatpādayugalaṃ tu vai ।
prasāritaṃ khavaktraṃ ca procchritaṃ śrotredaśagam ।।

nālāvasāne saṃpādya karṇikākamale dvija ।
ardhaprakullai racitaiḥ padmapatraistathāgataiḥ ।।

tanmūle sādhikā kuryāt tadvistārāṃ mahāmate ।
kṣmākṣetraṃ svastikopetaṃ suṣiraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ tu vā ।।

pṛṣṭhadeśe atha padmasya marutkṣetraṃ sabindukam ।
kuryād ādhārabhūtaṃ ca kṣmākṣetrasyonnateḥ samam ।।

sārdhaṃ kṣmāvyāsavistāraṃ tatsamaṃ dviguṇaṃ tu vā ।
cakranemyāśritaṃ caiva pralīnaṃ tacca susvanam ।।

ādyaṃ vā kiṅkiṇījālaṃ vighnavidrāvaṇaṃ param ।
ityevaṃ saviśeṣaṃ hi lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam ।।

māntrasya dhūpamātrasya sāmānyam atha me śṛṇu ।
vṛttasyābhyantare padmaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam ।।

aṣṭapatraṃ samāpādya vyomaktṛvibhūṣitam ।
muktāsūtrānvitaṃ vātha evameva savedikam ।।

antarā dvādaśāreṇa sāmbujenātha vā[hitam] ।
vicitrapatravitataṃ kuryāt pṛṣṭhāvadhestataḥ ।।

praphullapatrasthāne tu uṣṇīṣāṃśukabhūṣitam ।
vaktraviśrāmabhūtaṃ ca ādhāravalayānvitam ।।

śuddhaṃ suślakṣṇanālaṃ ca nalinīracanojjhitam ।
evam abhyūhyamākāraṃ mānenābhimatena tu ।।

sarvalohaiḥ svaśaktyā tu kṛtaṃ yacchati vai sukham ।
mantriṇāṃ sūgahasthānāṃ bhaktānāṃ kamalodbhava ।।

vakṣye samudgarākhyasya lakṣaṇaṃ taṃ nibodhatu ।
vistāroddiṣṭamānena suṣiraṃ vṛttasaṃpuṭam ।।

susamaṃ prāksamāpādya samudgakamivābjaja ।
sanālaṃ ca tayorekam upariṣṭācca madhyataḥ ।।

prakullakamalenaiva adhovaktreṇa padmaja ।
dvitīyam ūrdhvavaktreṇa sthagitaṃ paṅkajena tu ।।

sacchidraṃ bījasaṅghena yuktam ūrdhvasthitaṃ hi yata ।
nālam āpādya mūlādvai vinatena gajāṅghriṇā ।।

nāladeśagalād dvābhyāṃ sthityarthaṃ viniyojya ca ।
evaṃ praphullarūpāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam ।।

protthitānām idānīṃ vai lakṣma śṛṇu yathāgatam ।
prāgāyāmāccaturthāṃśaṃ vaitatyena mahāmate ।।

caturaśrāyataṃ kṣetraṃ nikṣipya vasudhātale ।
aṣṭadhātha tamāyāmaṃ susamaṃ saṃvibhajya ca ।।

caturdhā vistṛteścaiva kuryāttadanu padmaja ।
aṣṭabhāgonnataṃ pīṭhaṃ prāguktaracanānvitam ।।

pādādyuṣṇīṣaparyantaṃ yathāvistāravistṛtam ।
pīṭhārdhena ucchritaṃ caiva vistārāt tryaṃśasaṃmitam ।।

kamalaṃ pīṭhamadhye tu kuryād dvitayakarṇikam ।
aṣṭapatraṃ sakiñjalkaṃ vyomavṛttavibhūṣitam ।।

vistārāccārdhabhāgena pṛthulaṃ connateḥ punaḥ ।
sārdhabhāgacatuṣkena aṣṭāśraṃ vā suvartulam ।।

catusśraṃ tu vā ramyaṃ tadeva racanānvitam ।
stambham āpādyam evaṃ hi yathābhimatam abjaja ।।

yebhyo yadvartulaṃ tadvai vicitraracanānvitam ।
stambhamarutakaviśrāntaṃ bāhulyenāṃśasaṃmitam ।।

pīṭhatulyaṃ tu vistārāddvādaśāravibhūṣitam ।
nābhinemiprathīyuktaṃ muktāhārādyalaṃkṛtam ।।

prāgvat sakiṅkiṇīkaṃ ca cakram āpādya padmaja ।
tadakṣamadhyasaṃrūḍhaṃ sārdhāṃśenonnataṃ tu vai ।।

agrāt pīṭhasamaṃ caiva bāhulyāccakrasaṃmitam ।
vistārād ardhabhāgena aṣṭoddeśācca saṃkaṭam ।।

kramaśaścānupātena tadvistāraṃ vidhīyate ।
mukham evaṃ samāpādya sadhūmasya analasya ca ।।

sadāśravaṃ sadākālaṃ vibhorarcanakarmaṇi ।
jalajaiḥ sthalajaiścaiva prāṇibhir nākajaistataiḥ ।।

patravallīvitānaiśca saśaṅkhaiḥ svastikaiḥ kajaiḥ ।
kusumastabakaiḥ svacchaiḥ siddhavidyādharādikaiḥ ।।

devāṅganāsametaiśca dikṣu veśo bhavedbahiḥ ।
etat prāsādayuktasya vṛttapīṭhānanasya ca ।।

yathāvad upadekṣyāmi sanniveśamatobjaja ।
valitritayasaṃyuktaṃ śaṅkhānanamivāsanam ।।

padmamānonnotaṃ kuryād āsanopari padmaja ।
stambhādhāraṃ vicitraṃ ca dvivyam āmalasārakam ।।

racanāracitaṃ stambhaṃ raktapūrvam athocchritam ।
valayāvalitulyaṃ vā stambhanālasya tūpari ।।

cakravat kamalaṃ kurcāt sakiñjalkaṃ dviṣaṭpadam ।
vistīrṇakarṇikaṃ vipra prāgvad vaktraṃ tadūrdhvagam ।।

yathoktaracanopetaṃ paritaḥ kintu vartulam ।
muktāsūtrānvitaṃ caiva kiṅkiṇījālalāmbitam ।।

ebhyaścoktam athaikaṃ vai savidhānaṃ tadabjaja ।
jalajasthalajā yātmyaracanā racitā mayā ।।

samabhyūhya ca sā kāryā sarveṣāṃ sarvadābjaja ।
sphuṭāvasya ?yasmin vai kṛtāṅge ?tyantarājate ।।

idamuktaṃ samāsena lakṣaṇaṃ ca savistṛtam ।
dhūpadāhakriyāṅgasya nānākṛtidharasya ca ।।

saṃpādyaivaṃ ca saṃskṛtya nītvā satyantatā ?punaḥ ।
svamantrādhiṣṭhitaṃ kṛtvā pūjyam ādhārasaṃsthitam ।।

mūlataḥ svastikāsthāne kṣmātattvaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam ।
salilaṃ kamalaṃ viddhi cakram agniṃ mahatprabham ।।

kiṅkiṇījālamanilam ākāśaṃ karṇikodare ।
ityevaṃ sādhibhūtādhidaivatānugataṃ hi vai ।।

prāk proktaṃ bhāvanīyaṃ ca siddhaye akhilakarmaṇām ।
cakrasya sakalaṃ rūpaṃ nābhyarānemisapradhi ।।

niṣkalaṃ hi suvṛttaṃ yat vyomavṛtteti gīyate ।
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ dhūpapātraṃ samarcayet ।।

saṃskṛtya ca yathānyāyaṃ svavaṃśasya ca kīrtayet ।
svanāmacihnitaṃ kṛtvā pratipādya mahāmate ।।

harerāyatane divye surasiddhaniṣevite ।
trekālyaṃ balidānena dhūpadhūmena vai saha ।।

vādayet susvanāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ bherīśabdādikairyutām ।
stotreḥ pradakṣiṇīkuryād bahudhā divyam ālayam ।।

siddhasaṃghaṃ ca tatrasthaṃ śabdabrahmaikam āsanam ।
śrutvā ghaṇṭāravaṃ bāhyāt paritoṣaṃ mahāmate ।।

kasyedam acirādyāti amivyaktim anāhatam ।
bhavyānām upadeśārthaṃ yenedaṃ vyañjitaṃ bahiḥ ।।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi

pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ dhūpādhāralakṣaṇo nāma

pañcatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

oṃ

atha ṣaṭtriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

bhagavan jñātum icchāmi tvayā yat samudīritam ।
mahātmano anuvidhdaṃ ca lakṣaṇenopalakṣitam ।।

yad yad āyatanaṃ divyaṃ sidhdāyatanam eva ca ।
nṛṇām upāyabhūtaṃ yad ajñānāṃ jñāninām api ।।

yatrārādhanapūrvaṃ hi māntram abhyeti mantriṇām ।
śaśvat prasannatā deva tathā tattvajayo mahān ।।

nirvighnena bhavatyāśu snātakabrahmacāriṇām ।
yatīnāṃ muktasaṅgānāṃ viratānāṃ gṛhāśramāt ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

ākṣiter bhedabhinnaṃ vai māyāmayam idaṃ jagat ।
kṣetrāravyair bhagavattattvaiḥ kṣetranāthasamanvitaiḥ ।।

nānāvibhavarūpaistu vyāptavyūhātmapūrvakaiḥ ।
nityanirmalaṣāḍguṇyavigrahaistaiḥ svayaṃ punaḥ ।।

anugrahārthaṃ bhavinām akṛtajñālpamedhasām ।
bhaktānām apyabhaktānāṃ nāstikānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।

bhūcakrākṣaṃ gate dvīpe hyanādiprathitaṃ hi yat ।
kṣetraṃ svakarmaphaladaṃ puṇyaṃ parimitaṃ tu vai ।।

nṛṇām anugrahārthaṃ tu sthānabhedair adhiṣṭhitam ।
amūrtestu svasaṃjñābhiḥ kāruṇyāt kṣetrasattamaiḥ ।।

tathā kṣetrādhipaiḥ kintu mūrtair yuktā navābjaja ? ।
bījabhāvena bhūmau vā sthitiṃ kṛtvā sthitāṃ tataḥ ।।

jñānādyair vāṇimādyaiḥ tu avyaktaiḥ kṣmānalādikaiḥ ।
tattvabījakalārūpair brahmasattāsamanvitaiḥ ।।

sahāvatīrya cāsṛṣṭeḥ prāg vyaktiṃ yānti vai tataḥ ।
svayam evātmabhāvena sarvānugrahakāmyayā ।।

kṣmāmaṇḍalopasaṃhārakālaṃ kṣetravaraiḥ saha ।
vaśitvāvaradehāṃstu pradhānamunivigrahān ।।

svāsmin svasmin hi yugapat kṣetre kṣemagatiprade ।
svakāmanaikabhūtāṃ ca mūrtiṃ caivābhimānikīm ।।

kṛtvā vai vyaktibhāvaṃ ca pramāṇair uttamādikaiḥ ।
yathākālānurūpaiśca vāsudhenopalātmanā ।।

ataḥ tadrūpanāmnā vai khyātā kṣetreśvarā bhuvi ।
prakhyātāḥ tulyanāmnānye devāḥ sāyatanāstu vai ।।

evaṃ kṣetreśvaraiḥ kṣetraiḥ karmabhūmir adhiṣṭhitā ।
kṣetrair amūrtaiścidrūpair mūrtaiḥ kṣaitrādhipaiḥ tathā ।।

iti yuktyāvatīrṇā ye kṣetrāṇāṃ kṣaitranāyakāḥ ।
te api kālāntareṇaiva svayaṃ doṣaṃ śilāmayam ।।

budhvāntardhānam āyānti deśabhaṃgādikair dvija ।
vicāraiḥ pracuraiḥ bhūyaḥ prāgvad vyaktiṃ vrajanti ca ।।

svayaṃvāvanimadhyāt tu svasāmarthyena codayet ।
kurvannanambunidher yadvad ambudaugham acoditam ।।

iti matpratipannānāṃ svapne pratyakṣato api vā ।
vadanti yogakṣemādyaṃ svayaṃ vā tanmayātmanām ।।

tattattvato atibhaktanāṃ satyārthaṃ sarvadā bhavet ।
asatyārthamato anyeṣāṃ kintu puṣkarasaṃbhava ।।

ityutkarṣaṃ bhavatyeṣām astitvena samanvitam ।
nirāsārtham abhaktānām nāstikatvena vāsatā ।।

tuṣṭaye hyāstikānāṃ tu tīrthādīnāṃ hi siddhaye ।
kṣetreśā vāsudevāste sthitāścopalakukṣiṣu ।।

kvacit sākṣāt tathā cakraśaṃkhapadmagadātmanā ।
viśeṣeṇa trikūṭe tu girau raivatake tu vai ।।

sālagrāme tu sahayādrau tathā viṣṇupade dvija ।
vyāvarte caiva kṛṣṇāśve kukṣau tu tuhinācale ।।

mahendre malaye vindhye pāriyātre athavārbude ।
satyavratasthe hastyadrau vikaṭe parvatottame ।।

siṃhācale mama kṣetre puṇye vā sumanohare ।
evaṃ kamalasaṃbhūta vāsudevair adhiṣṭhite ।।

anekākṛtibhedasthair anekaikena kena cit ।
ayatnāt kalpite kṣetre svanudhyā tu vrajanti ye ।।

āśritya kṣetranāthaṃ tu vipadyante ca tatra ye ।
avasāne tu vā cā cānye dharāṃśe madhyame tu vā ।।

ādye vā devadṛg dṛṣṭe te prayānti krameṇa tu ।
tasya vai kṣetratāthasya satyattvakṣmāgatasya ca ।।

tat sālokyaṃ tu sāmīpyaṃ sāyujyam amalekṣaṇa ।
parigrahavihīnaṃ ca vivekarāhitaṃ janam ।।

śaraṇāgatabhūtaṃ tu api cennāstikaṃ purā ।
tathāntikaṃ śraddhadhānaṃ niśceṣṭaṃ cāpi pauṣkara ।।

visaṃjñaṃ bandhubhir nītaṃ kārūṇyāt kamalodbhava ।
trāhityuktvā jagannāthaṃ kṣiptvā strībālapūrvakaiḥ ।।

jñātvā vimuktadehaṃ taṃ saha puryaṣṭakena tu ।
mahatā tūryaghoṣeṇa kṛtvā rathavare tu vai ।।

jitvāntakabhaṭān raudrān balāt kṣetreśakiṃkaraiḥ ।
nṛsiṃhakapilakroḍavāmanāśvaśiromukhaiḥ ।।

sasaumyavadanaiḥ padmaśaṃkhacakragadādharaiḥ ।
sīranandakadhṛga vajrapāśāṅkuśa dhanurdharaiḥ ।।

musalāditathādaṇḍahastaiśca garūḍānanai ।
ānīya kṣetranāthasya tvabhigacchāpayanti ca ।।

devakṣetre tvadīye asya vimuktaṃ pāñcabhautikam ।
śarīram adyānāthasya kurūśaśvad yathocitam ।।

kṣaitranāthastu tad vākyaṃ samākarṇyāñca gaṇeritam ।
karūṇānugatenaiva taṃ nirīkṣya tu cakṣuṣā ।।

kṛtaṃ vigatapāpaṃ tu tasminnāyatane purā ।
saṃprāptasya svake sthāne doṣaśeṣaṃ hi vai punaḥ ।।

saṃsargeṇa layaṃ nītvā kramāt kālāntareṇa vai ।
dvābhyām evaṃ prakāreṇa yad anyaccātmasāt kṛtam ।।

tatsthaṃ liṅgavaśātkṛṣya svaśaktyā ca svavigrahāt ।
saṃskārayogyatāṃ jñātvā samyajjñānāptaye tu vai ।।

dadāti karmabhūmau tu janma satkarmiṇāṃ kule ।
sava kṣetrai vā parakṣetre tatra sālokanaṃ hi yat ।।

kālāt prāptādhikāraśca kṛtvā vyāptāṃ samāsataḥ ।
yathocitam anuṣṭhānaṃ trayodaśavi[dhaṃ] śubham ।।

tat tena kṛtakṛtyaṃ syāt tadardhena tu cāparam ।
tṛtīyaṃm abjasaṃbhūta samyajjñānena yujyate ।।

jñā tamātraṃ hi vai kālād indriyavyaktilakṣa ṇāt ।
svayaṃ cīrṇavrataṃ prāgvat tat kṣetre budhdipūrvakam ।।

tīvrabhāvena vai paścāddehatyāgaṃ vratādinā ।
kuryāt kṣetrādhipasyāgre tad vattaṃ gatakalmaṣam ।।

pṛthagdehāraṇīṃ kṛtvā jñānaṃ yada malaṃ śubham ।
sa tasyopadaudiśatyājyaṃ ? tatrai va kamalekṣaṇa ।।

yatprāpya paramaṃ dhāma vāsudevākhyam eva ca ।
yogināṃ tīrthapuṇyāni brahmannāpatitāni ca ।।

sadāvyādhārabhāvena hayaṃgabhāvaṃ vrajanti vai ।
yogotkṛṣṭaprakṛṣṭaṃ ca prāpyanti jñānino api ye ।।

śaśvajjñānasamākīrṇaṃ nirvighnenāpnuvanti ca ।
evamāyā tanād brahmannupāyaṃ bhavināṃ param ।।

yato asti ca ato hetoḥ sevanīyaṃ sadaiva hi ।
abhijātasya bījasya yathāmalamarīcayaḥ ।।

prārohajananīṃ śaktiṃ santāpān dhvaṃsayanti ca ।
vinā svarūpahāner vai sāṃ hyevameva hi ।।

svaprabhāvena vai samyak svaśaktikiraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।
prakṣīṇakalpamaṣaṃ kṛtvā kṣetre vai kṣetravāsinām ।।

kurvantyanugrahaṃ paścāt kṣīṇapāpasya tasya ca ।
mṛdambuhutabhug vātapātair gaganalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

prasiddhayaṃtritaṃ hyatra asidhdaṃ tadvayaṃ śruṇu ।
yad annāmbu parityāgādvātaṃ tad vāta saṃjñitam ।।

sarvadvāroparodhena yad annābhāsamuttamam ।
kālaṃ vā deha pātīyaṃ sanyag jñātvātra pauṣkara ।।

kāryam ārādane yatnāt tatra bhaktyā śubhaiṣiṇā ।
yadi na prāpnuyāt caiva janmābhyāsādavāpyate ।।

vilayaṃ yānti vai yena trāhi janmani janmani ।
kṛtabudhder manuṣyasya pāpenātibalīyasā ।।

na sañjātā ca tat prāptir yadyapyabjasamudbhava ।
na śāsanasya ghorasya cāntakasya sa bhājanam ।।

mānyo yamabhaṭānāṃ ca yajñayājī yathā pumān ।
āstāṃ hi tāvanmanujā niyamādyair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।।

bhāvabhaktiviśeṣāḍhyāḥ prāṇino anyepi tatra ye ।
prāksaṃskāravaśājjātāḥ te api jātyantaraṃ punaḥ ।।

nāpnuvanti mṛtā vipra sadvivekavivarjitāḥ ।
mama bhaktāya nāṃ ca ityeṣāṃ yastu vindati ।।

nṛṇāṃ madhye sa dhanyo vai duṣkṛtair nātibādhyate ।
karmaṇāṃ vai hyabhuktānāṃ na nāśosti ca yadyapi ।।

tānavaṃ kṣetramāhātmyaprabhāvāt saṃprayānti te ।
janmābhyāsavaśenaiva nūnaṃ karmakṣayo bhavet ।।

sāmarthyāt kṣetranāthānāṃ sakṣetrāṇāṃ mahāmate ।
kṣetreṣvevaṃ prakāreṣu dānaṃ yacchanti ye arthinām ।।

vibhorārādhanārthaṃ tu bhaktyā kurvanti vā tapaḥ ।
sādhayanti ca mantreśaṃ tarpayanti tilādibhiḥ ।।

yajanti makhair devān labhante te akhilaṃ phalam ।
dvādaśākṣarapūrveḥ tu prasidhdaiḥ kamalodbhava ।।

mantrair jitantā matrāntaiḥ prāptairvātha guror mukhāt ।
svakena mantremukhyena vidhivat parameśvaram ।।

ārādhyāyatanasthaṃ ca yat yatkiñcid adhikāriṇām ।
dvijendra dvijamukhyānāṃ dīyate pāñcakālinām ।।

tad akṣayaṃ parijñeyaṃ bhavabhogābhilāṣiṇām ।
dānānnivṛttarāgāṇāṃ tat punar mokṣasiddhaye ।।

grāma maṇḍaladeśāntarmaryādāyatanavāsinām ।
dattam ātmasamaiḥ ? bhūtyai bahubhir nirūjo aśnute ।।

saṃpūrṇāsu svaśaktyā ca nityaṃ janmani janmani ।
anantabhavikaṃ vidhdi tat divyāyatanāt punaḥ ।।

ajñeyaṃ lakṣabhavikaṃ tat sidhdāyatanāt tu vai ।
sahasrabhavikaṃ vipra viprapravarakalpitāt ।।

daśāṅgabhavikaṃ tadvai kṛtaṃ yat kṣatriyena tu ।
tadardhabhavikaṃ viddhi sadvaiśyaparikalpitāt ।।

satśūdra kalpite vipra dattam āyatane tu vai ।
dviṣaṭak bhavanaṃ tadvai dānaṃ jñeyaṃ dvijottama ।।

ananyaśaraṇebhyo vai varṇebhyaḥ parikalpite ।
dvijendrāyatane dattaṃ phalaṃ tat punareva hi ? ।।

vyāmiśrayājibhir varṇair nirmitāyatanāstu ye ।
pūrvoktebhyaḥ prayacchanti tadardhabhavikaṃ kramāt ।।

phalakāmaphale psūnāṃ niṣkāmānāṃ hi pauṣkara ।
sarvāyatanago devaḥ sarvamūrtiṣvavasthitaḥ ।।

mūrtyantaragataścāpi prādurbhāvagatastvapi ।
prādurbhāvānta yā ? vṛttiṃ dadāti paramaṃ padam ।।

ācartavyam ataḥ tasmādyatnena mahatā dvija ।
mantrārādhanapūrveṇa karmaṇā cidvilakṣaṇam ।।

tasmādvimuktarāgāṇāṃ nṛṇām acyutayājinām ।
vyajyate svātmavṛttisthaṃ vāsudevam ajaṃ vibhum ।।

tadadhiṣṭhitacittastu yatra yatra yajet bahiḥ ।
tatra tatra tadā teṣāṃ vyajyate brahma śāśvatam ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

devāyatanajātānāṃ nṛṇām aśubhakāriṇām ।
mṛtānāṃ tatra vāhya tra jñātum icchāmyahaṃ gatim ।।

śrībhagavān uvāca 

kenacit prāktanenaiva karmaṇāvimalena ca ।
ācarantyabjasaṃbhūta matervai duṣkṛtaṃ punaḥ ।।

jñātvāpi kṣetramāhātmyaṃ vivaśāt tu balāt tu vai ।
taṃ mriyantaṃ ca tatrāsthe janmābhyāsavaśena tu ।।

kṣetre ca pāpataḥ teṣāṃ saṃkṣipatyantakasya ca ।
śaśvadduṣkṛta śānyarthaṃ upāyair nātiśāsanaiḥ ।।

tvam eva teṣāṃ kurūṣe bhuktaśeṣaṃ hi kalmaṣam ।
śamayatyacirādeva ācaranti yathāśubham ।।

bhūyaḥ prāptena dehe na asmadīye parigrahe ।
sa cājñāṃ śirasā tāṃ vai kṛtvā caiva mahāmate ।।

karūṇānugatenaiva saṃśodhayati cetasā ।
evaṃ vigatadoṣāḥ te yānti kālāntareṇa tu ।।

sā[hacaryāc]ca sākalyāt satsaṃparkādviśeṣataḥ ।
prakṣīṇakalmaṣā nūnaṃ punarāyānti vaidikīm ।।

samācaranti tadvastu sāyujyaṃ yānti yena vai ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

tadutpannā vipadyanti pāpiṣṭhā hyatra vai yadi ।
kā gatir bhavate teṣāṃ narāṇām atipāpinām ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

śodhayatyantakaḥ teṣāṃ duṣkṛtiṃ nātiśāsanaiḥ ।
gatadoṣāḥ samāyānti mānuṣyaṃ hi tadā punaḥ ।।

matir dehavipattyarthā tīvreṇa manasābjaja ।
prayāti pūrvavacchuddhiṃ yathā duṣkṛtino narāḥ ।।

tatra jātāśca nirdeṣā ye anyatra vilayaṃ gatāḥ ।
prayānti sāṃprataṃ te vai vimānair antakāspadam ।।

saṃpūjayatyasau teṣāṃ brūyādbaddhāñjalistataḥ ।
sthānam āyatanaṃ[yeṣāṃ] bhagavantaṃ vrajantu vai ।।

sālokyasaṃjñaṃ vimalaṃ bhavabandhakṣayaṃkaram ।
madīyadarśitenaiva mārgeṇānena sādhunā ।।

bhavatāṃ saṃprayātānāṃ śubhaṃ tatra bhaviṣyati ।
tadvāsināṃ yathānyeṣāṃ bhagavat tattvavedinām ।।

evaṃ abjasamudbhūta phalam āyatanāt bhavet ।
narāṇāṃ nirvivekānāṃ tadanyeṣāṃ tu kiṃ punaḥ ।।

kṣitiḥ pādau ca khaṃ nābhirdyaiḥ śiraḥ śaśibhāskarau ।
netre lokā mahatpūrvā vibhoryasya śirorūhāḥ ।।

diśaḥ śrotre bhujāścaiva vidiśaḥ sarva eva hi ।
ādhāraśaktiparyantaṃ yasya pātālasaṃtatiḥ ।।

sthitiḥ pādataloddeśe nityākṛtidharasya ca ।
vibhor vai rājamānyasya sarvagasya mahātmanaḥ ।।

sarvaṃ padātmakaṃ yasmād bhaktānām ata eva hi ।
nahyanāyatanaṃ deśam āstikānāṃ dvijāsti vai ।।

carācaram idaṃ sarvaṃ nāstikānāṃ tamomayam ।
suprasiddhaṃ tu vai sthānamāstāṃ tāvanmahāmate ।।

bhaktyāvasthāpitā yatra sthāne vipravarādikaiḥ ।
acalā vā calā ramyā citramṛtkāṣṭhaśailajā ।।

hemādidhātulohotthā yā kācit pratimā hareḥ ।
nṛṇāṃ tatra vipannānāṃ tanmāhātmyavaśāt tu vai ।।

sthitiḥ triviṣṭape teṣām anatyutkṛṣṭalakṣaṇā ।
ante paricyute janma yeṣām āyataneṣu ca ।।

yathākramaṃ mahābuddhe parijñeyaṃ hi matparaiḥ ।
sākṣādvṛttir dvijendrīyā kṣetrakṣetreṣu jāyate ।।

kṣatriyāyatanādvi ddhi janmāmaravinirmite ।
sadvaiśyakalitoddeśe janma puṣkarasaṃbhava ।।

munibhir nirmitasthāne acyutāyatane abjaja ।
mā janma maudgalīyācca prāpnotyārādhanānnaraḥ ।।

kalpitaṃ mantrasiddhena nareṇāyatanam mahat ।
bhogotkarṣaṃ hi vai nṝṇāṃ tathā kālāntareṇa ca ।।

mantrajñaiḥ kalpitāntaṃ ca yāvad āyatanam dvija ।
śaśvat pāpakṣayaṃ cānyat kṣatriyaṃ tadanantaram ।।

krameṇa savitānaṃ ca nātidīrdheṇa pauṣkara ।
kālāntareṇa vai teṣāṃ doṣāṇāṃ tu parikṣayam ।।

avatīrya kṣitiṃ paścād bhuktaśeṣaṃ hi padmaja ।
kṣapayatyāśu tatraiva niyamaiḥ pūrvaduṣkṛtam ।।

prāgvat smṛtāḥ krameṇeva te yānti paramaṃ padam ।
pātā ye vihitāścātra dehatyāgavighau śubhe ।।

vivekināṃ na vihitāḥ prāyaścittasthameva hi ।
ājanma sañcitānāṃ ca duṣkṛtānāṃ kṣayāya vai ।।

labhante taistu nirdagdhair dehānte padam ācyutam ।
tasmāt kṣetraṃ samāsādya prāyaścittaṃ samācaret ।।

svayaṃ pāpaphalaṃ jñātvā sattvam āśritya śāśvatam ।
virūddhacittabuddhistu yena yāti śubhāṃ sthitim ।।

balavā nya dapi kṣetraṃ nṝṇāṃ śubhagatipradam ।
tadvivekaṃ dvitīyaṃ vai svasāmarthyaṃ tu nojjñati ।।

mano buddhīndriyagaṇaṃ karaṇagrāmasaṃyutam ।
āmlādyasya saṃśuddhamante vā tapasā mahat ।।

kurvantyanugrahaṃ tasya śaśvadāyatanādayaḥ ।
jīva bhāvasthito jantuḥ paralokaṃ gatastu vā ।।

bhūguṇā api cādeyāḥ sarvatra vidhigauravāt ।
yathā mahānubhāvānām purūṣāṇāṃ tu yācakāḥ ।।

saṃhṛṣṭam annapānārthaṃ guṇajñam aguṇaṃ tu vai ।
tyajantyaguṇatāṃścaiva saguṇaṃ vāpi cānyathā ।।

jñātvaivaṃ kṣetramāhātmyaṃ tapodhyānajapādikaiḥ ।
karmavākcittasaṃtoṣādupaśobhāṃ nayet parām ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

caturbhir vāsudevādyair mūrtibhiḥ prāgudīritaiḥ ।
keśavādyair dvādaśabhir matsyādyair daśabhiḥ tataḥ ।।
kṣmāntaṃ ṣaḍviṃśasaṃkhyaṃ yat tattvavṛndaṃ puroditam vyāptam īśvarapūrvaṃ vai dvādaśānām saha sthitam ।।
susthūlenānurūpeṇa daśakaṃ tena cāvṛtam ।
tattvaṃ tattvaṃ samāsādya vāsudevādinā saha ।।

sthitir evaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ bhavaśāntaye ।
guṇaṣaṭkasamopetaṃ vaiśvarūpyaṃ mahāmate ।।

svavyāpāravaśenaiva vyañjayanti sadaiva hi ।
anugrahavaśenaiva vibhoricchāvaśena tu ।।

sarvaiḥ kṣititalaṃ vyāptaṃ nānākāradharaiḥ sadā ।
ekaikā vaibhave mūrtir anantenātmatāṃ yathā ।।

yānti nānātmanām evaṃ vāhanāyudhalāñchanaiḥ ।
ataścellokanārthāyaicchātaḥ prābhavena tu ।।

sthitir nānāprakārā vai sarveṣāṃ ca svabhūtiṣu ।
niyataḥ sāyudhānāṃ ca lāñchanānāṃ ca yadyapi ।।

tathāpi sarvamūtīnāṃ sarve sādhāraṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
yadyapyevaṃ hi vai vipra tatrāpi vinibodha me ।।

na ca anyabhrāntiśāntyarthaṃ viśeṣaṃ lāñchanair dhvajaiḥ ।
prādurbhāvāḥ tu vijñeyāḥ svavyāpāravaśāttu vai ।।

prādurbhāvāntarāstadvadaṃśasya tu vaśādapi ।
ādyakā rakṣakādhārāḥ ? kecit tu dhvajalāñchanaiḥ ।।

tulyam evaṃ trayāṇāṃ tu prādurbhāvagaṇaṃ param ।
apare keśavādīnāṃ tulyam udvahati dvija ।।

ākārair lāchanaiḥ sārdhaṃ tad viśeṣeṇa vai saha ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

śrotum icchāmi bhagavan sarveṣāṃ lāñchanādikam ।
viśeṣo yaḥ layoddiṣṭo bhavināṃ bhavaśāntaye ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

śṛṇu lāñchanavinyāsam ādidevāditaḥ kramāt ।
matto nigadataḥ samyak yathāvad amalekṣaṇa ।।

ādyaḥ pāṇiḥ caturṇā vai dakṣiṇe tvabhayapradaḥ ।
varaprado vā bhaktānāṃ dhātavyamamalekṣaṇa ।।

vāmo śaṅkhodvahaṃ viddhi nānāsthityā caturṣvapi ।
ādyasya paścimābhyāṃ tu vāmadakṣiṇayoḥ punaḥ ।।

kālacakraṃ gadāṃ gurvīm acyutasyāvadhāraya ।
lāṅgalaṃ musalopetaṃ vāmahaste sadakṣiṇe ।।

paścime bhujayugme asya saṃhate ca dhanuḥ śare ।
kheṭakaṃ nandakopetam anirūddhasya pauṣkara ।।

dvābhyāṃ paścimapāṇibhyāṃ madhyahastāditaḥ tu vai ।
ityevaṃ hi caturmūrter etanmūrtyantareṣu ca ।।

śaṃkhacakragadāpadmalāṃchanānāṃ sthitiṃ śruṇu ।
ādidevīyadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ tāvaducyate ।।

vāme paścimage cakraṃ viddhi śaṅkhaṃ tu dakṣiṇe ।
dakṣiṇe mukhyahaste abjaṃ gadā tadapare tu vai ।।

evaṃ hi bhagavān dhatte keśavaḥ kamalādikam ।
savyāpasavya hastābhyāṃ mukhyābhyāṃ tu gadāmbuje ।।

vāmādau śaṅkhacakrau tu sa dhatte paścimadvaye ।
nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavān mādhavākhyo nibodhatu ।।

mukhye savyāpasavpaye tu śaṅkhaṃ dhatte gadāṃ prabhuḥ ।
paścime padmacakre tu sarvapūrve bhujadvaye ।।

mūrtitrayam idaṃ divyaṃ kundendusphaṭikaprabham ।
bhagavadvāsudevena sahāsya caturātmanā ।।

tritayasya parijñeyā mokṣadā bhavabhogadā ।
kāmapālīyadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ kamalodbhava ।।

padmaṃ mukhyakare vāme gadānyasmin hi dakṣiṇe ।
vibhorgovindasaṃjñasya ityevaṃ samudāhṛtam ।।

vinyāsaṃ lāñchanānāṃ ca viṣṇoratha nibodhatu ।
vāmadakṣiṇapāṇibhyām agrataḥ śaṃkha paṅkaje ।।

evaṃ paścimahastābhyāṃ cakraṃ kaumodakīdvayam ।
madhusūdanasaṃjñasya saṃniveśam ataḥ śṛṇu ।।

padmaṃ mukhyakare vāme pāñcajanyaṃ tu dakṣiṇe ।
gadā paścimataḥ savye cakraṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pare ।।

trayam evaṃ hi devānāṃ saha vai jñānamūrtinām ।
cāturātmyād dvitīyāṃ tu padmarāgojjvaladyutim ।।

atha pradyumnadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ krama ucyate ।
varṇabhedena saha vai lāñchanagrahaṇaṃ śṛṇu ।।

agrato vāmapāṇau ca cakram anyakare gadā ।
vāme tu paścime śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ tadapare smṛtam ।।

vibhoḥ trivikramākhyasya vāmanasyāvadhāraya ।
gadāgravāmahaste tu cakraṃ mukhye tu dakṣiṇe ।।

vāme tu paścime padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ tat dakṣiṇe kare ।
śrīdharasya gadā vāme mukhyahaste prakīrtitā ।।

cakram agre apasavyākhye śaṅkhaṃ vāme tu paścime ।
tadānyasmin pare padmaṃ cakraṃ koṭisamaprabham ।।

mūrtitritayam ete vai saha ca svāminā dvija ।
hemadhāmaprabhaṃ jñeyaṃ cāturātmyatayā sthitam ।।

ato anirūddhamūrtīnāṃ tritayaṃ cāvadhāraya ।
lāñchanodvahanaṃ caiva varṇabhedena vai saha ।।

padmaṃ agrakare vāme tat dvitīye tu hetirāṭ ।
savyāpasavyahastābhyāṃ paścimābhyāṃ krameṇa tu ।।

padmakośaṃ gadāṃ gurvīṃ padmanābhe nibodhatu ।
agrage cakrarākhyapadmaṃ muḍvāmekare pare ।।

vāme gadāṃ paścimage tadanyasmiṃśca śaṅkharāṭ ।
dhatte dāmodaro vāme gadāṃ cāgrasthite śubhām ।।

apasavye agrage śaṅkhaṃ vāme cakraṃ tu paścime ।
paścime tvapasavye tu kamalaṃ sūryavarcasam ।।

atasīpuṣpasaṅkāśam idaṃ mūrtigaṇaṃ smṛtam ।
sahānirūddhadevena asyāpi caturātmatā ।।

viśveśvarasya vai viṣṇoḥ sthitaye asmin jagattraye ।
amūrtānāṃ ca mūrtānām āyudhānāṃ sthitiṃ śṛṇu ।।

pāṇidvayena cākrāntau pārśvadvaye pṛthak sthitau ।
tanmukhaṃ ca nirīkṣantau gadācakrau mahāmate ।।

śaṅkhapāṇiṃ ca śaṅkheśaṃ yugmam anyena hetinā ।
dvayādikaṃ karajālaṃ yat tannānābhisamanvitam ।।

pāṃśāṃṅkuśāsipadmādyair yuktaṃ cānyair varāyudhaiḥ ।
mūrtyantarāṇāṃ mūrtīnāṃ ṣoḍaśānām ataḥ śṛṇu ।।

mukhyahaste caturṇāṃ tu pāñcajanyaṃ nirākṛtim ।
sarvadehaṃ hi sañcintya gadācakre dvijottama ।।

hastadvayena cākrāntau sākāraṃ ca vibhor mukham ।
pibantam iva mṛtpātre ? smartavyaṃ tatparāyaṇaiḥ ।।

amūrtamantrasaṃsthānam idānīm avadhāraya ।
tam icchayā ca smartavyaṃ śobhālīlāvaśād api ।।

nānādeśajanasthityā āsṛṣṭeḥ saṃsthitaṃ yathā ।
āmūrteḥ sahamūrtānāṃ saṃdhāraṇam athocyate ।।

paścimābhyāṃ bhujābhyāṃ tu yasya yadvihitaṃ dvayam ।
mūrdhadeśāt samākrāntaṃ nirīkṣantaṃ vibhor mukham ।।

ājñāpratīkṣakaṃ caiva haste taṃ vyajanādikam ।
kakṣāntar gatahastaṃ vā atha vismayamudrayā ।।

yuktaṃ sampuṭasaṃjñākhyaṃ mudrayā vābjasaṃbhava ।
caturvadanapādā vai dhāna rūpaṃ tu saṃsthitiḥ ।।

sarveṣāṃ vihitā vipra prayojanavaśena tu ।
sādhakecchāvaśāccaiva tathā kālavaśāt tu vai ।।

prārthinaścopaviṃṣṭāstu bhogaśayyāgatāstvatha ।
cakrāmburūhapīṭhasthā hṛhi dhāmatrayānvitam ।।

dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu vācakaiḥ prāgudīritaiḥ ।
sāmānyair dvijamantrair vā ṣaḍbhiḥṣāḍguṇyalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

yor'cayet bhaktipūrvaṃ tu svaśaktyā vibhavena vā ।
sa muktadoṣa abhyeti tat tat padam anāmayam ।।

vyaktaṃ kṣetravaśe yasmin svayaṃ bāhaye avatāritam ।
siddher viśeṣanāmnā ca tatra sidhyanti sādhakāḥ ।।

svamantrajapino bhaktā nityaśuddhāḥ kriyāparāḥ ।
atha mūrtyantarāṇāṃ ca devānāṃ kamalo dbhava ।।

dhvajādyaṃ ya cca saṃketaṃ tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।
trayaṃ vadāmi devīyaṃ keśavādyaṃ prakīrtitam ।।

bhūṣitaṃ prapatākena mahad garūḍaketunā ।
mahatā tālavṛkṣeṇa lāṅgalīyena pauṣkara ।।

govindādyaṃ trayaṃ yadvai vijñeyam upaśobhitam ।
dhvajena makarākhyena pradyumnaṃ yena ca dvija ।।

trivikramādyaṃ tritayaṃ nityam eva vibhūṣitam ।
kuraṅgalāchanenaiva anirūddhena lāñchitam ।।

trayaṃ dāmodarāntaṃ ca hṛṣīkeśādikam hi yat ।
viśveśvarasya ca vibhor icchārūpadharasya ca ।।

vihitāḥ sarva evaite rūpaiśvaryeṇa vai saha ।
varāhanārasiṃhādyair devaistribhuvaneśvaraiḥ ।।

prādurbhāvāntaropetaiḥ[devaiḥ] sarvaguṇojvalaiḥ ।
yathocitaiścāturātmyaiḥ keśavādyaistato abjaja ।।

haṃsamatsyahayaiḥ kūrmasiṃhasūkarasaṃjñakaiḥ ।
yathoktalakṣaṇair brahman śaktitaḥ pratipattijaiḥ ।।

vṛttitvena jagatyasmin arcanādhyānakarmaṇi ।
yatīnāṃ muktasaṅgānāṃ siddhānāṃ kṣetravāsinām ।।

evaṃ yathoktavadanair nṛśarīrair mahābhujaiḥ ।
nṛvarāhanṛsiṃhākhyair nṛvājivadanābhidhaiḥ ।।

anugṛhadhiyā vyāptaṃ bhūbhāgam amalekṣaṇa ।
tathā vāmananāthena kharvamūtidhareṇa ca ।।

snātakabrahmacārī ca lāñchanair bhūṣitena ca ।
tasya rūpāntareṇaiva sukhānāṃ sukhadena ca ।।

trivikramākhyasaṃjñena trailokyākrāntamūrtinā ।
rāmasaṃjñena vibhunā jvalat paraśupāṇinā ।।

bhārāvataraṇaṃ yena pṛthivyāṃ bahuśaḥ kṛtam ।
etair anyair dvijaśreṣṭha vakṣyamāṇasamanvitaiḥ ।।

sabāhayābhyaṃtaraṃ vyāptaṃ brahmāṇḍanicayaṃ hi yat ।
prādurmāvāntaraiḥ sārdhaṃ prādurbhāvair dvijākhilaiḥ ।।

apyayaiḥ prabhavākhyaistu gauṇamukhyaiḥ sureśvaraiḥ ।
svabhāvam ajahacchaśvad ākārāntaram ākṛteḥ ।।

yat tattvam aṃśasaṃbhūtaṃ prādurbhāvāntaraṃ tu tat ।
prādurbhāvāntaropetaṃ prādurbhāvagaṇaṃ param ।।

śṛṇu me gadataḥ samyak yair vyāptam akhilaṃ jagat ।
rāmo aparaḥ kṣatrajanmā bhrātrā bhedaiḥ stribhiḥ saha ।।

nihantā rākṣasānāṃ yo manuṣyo aham iti smaran ।
kṛtakṛtyastu yo vettā svabhāvaṃ divyam uttamam ।।

aparaḥ sīrapāṇir vai rāmaḥ kṛṣṇātmanā saha ।
śiśubhāvaṃ samāśritya yo mahaddivyakarmakṛt ।।

kālkiśca viṣṇur bhagavān naṣṭadharmāvatārakṛt ।
urvyāṃ mleṃchagaṇaṃ hatvā viddhi tam yat kalau yuge ।।

dharmātmā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ prādurbhāvaṃ ca śāśvatam ।
prādurbhūtaṃ hi vai yasmānnarādyaṃ kṛṣṇapaścimam ।।

sapañcakālaṣaṭkarmama svadharmaiḥ samanvitam ।
japadhyānasamopetam evaṃ yaḥ pāti sarvadā ।।

caturmūrtimayaṃ vipra naro nārāyaṇo hariḥ ।
kṛṣṇasaṃjñaśca bhagavān prādurbhāvottaram vibhoḥ ।।

prakāśitaṃ caturdhā te ato anyam avadhāraya ।
viśvarūpaḥ sa bhagavāna bahuvigrahalakṣaṇam ।।

tatraikam antarākhyaṃ hi kṛṣṇanāthasya pauṣkara ।
mānuṣyatve avatīrṇasya trayam ādyam anaśvaram ।।

sahasravadanaḥ śrīmān sahasrāṅghrikarastathā ।
mūrtāmūrtaṃ ca yo dhatte gotreṣvamarasaṃgraham ।।

jalāravindanābhaśca prādurbhāveśvaro mahān ।
prabhavāpyayakṛdyogair bahubhedairūpāsitaiḥ ।।

madhukaiṭabhamāthī ca prādurbhāveśvarasya ca ।
prādurbhāvāntaraṃ viddhi padmanābhasya tadvibhoḥ ।।

mandarotpātakṛddeva vastvatvamṛtāharaṇa stathā ।
sudhākalaśadhṛk caiva vanitākṛtivigrahaḥ ।।

bhūyo rūpāntaraṃ tasya rāhościccheda mastakam ।
evaṃ caturdhā bhagavāneṣa eva mahāmate ।।

prādurbhāvāntaropetaṃ prādurbhāvottamottamam ।
samastasaubhāgyanidhir lakṣmīnāthaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ ।।

na dvitīyaḥ prasannātmā nṛṇāṃ bhogāpavargadaḥ ।
lakṣmīrūpāntarair yuktaḥ caturbhir garūḍāsanaḥ ।।

punaḥ tadāsanaṃ cānyad adaṣṭabhedaiḥśriyānvitaḥ ।
devādīnāṃ manovṛttipūrako bhogapūrvakam ।।

bhogavān kālanemighnaḥ pakṣīndravaravāhanaḥ ।
sahasrārakaraḥśrīmān śrīvatsāṃṅkitalakṣaṇaḥ ।।

kālavaiśvānaraḥ śālinātha pāthonivāsinaḥ ? ।
ādhāraśaktijñaṃsya ā mūrtasya ca vai vibhoḥ ।।

abhimānatanuryo vai nānābhedaiśca vartate ।
gajendragrāhamokṣī ca saṃsārādrasalakṣaṇāt ।।

jñānopadeṣṭā bhagavān kapilākṣastvadhokṣajaḥ ।
vidyāmūrtiścaturvaktro brahmā vai lokapūjitaḥ ।।

tamaṃśabhūtaṃ vai samyak viśvavyañjanalakṣaṇam ।
yugāvasāne saṃhāraṃ yaḥ karoti ca sarvadā ।।

śaṅkarākhyo mahārūdraḥ prādurbhāvāntaraṃ hi tat ।
devasyānalaśāler vai sarvādhaḥ saṃsthitasya ca ।।

lokeśvaraḥ śāntatanurbaudhdaṃ yasmāparaṃ viduḥ ।
nirya ntā buddhidharmāṇāṃ hiṃsādoṣasya dūṣakaḥ ।।

agnīṣomātmasaṃjñasya devasya paramātmanaḥ ।
sūryācandramasau viddhi sākārau locaneśvarau ।।

tadvaktraṃ daivataṃ cānyaddhutabhuk parameśvaraḥ ।
mantrapūtaṃ sadādāya hutamājyapurassaram ।।

brahmāṇḍabhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ santarpayati sarvadā ।
viśveśaprāṇaśakter vai vāyvākhyam adhidaivatam ।।

jagatsandhārakaṃ caiva nānāskandhātmanā tu vai ।
ete bhagavadākārāstiṣṭhantyasmijagattraye ।।

nānāveśasvarūpaiśca nānāsaṃsthānalakṣaṇaiḥ ।
nānākāryavaśenaiva nānākāravaśena tu ।।

evaṃ kṛtakaśabdādyair bhagavāṃstatkṣaṇena ca ।
ārādhyākṛtitulyena tajjapadhyānasevinām ।।

yathābhimatarūpeṇa guṇaṣaṭkānvitena ca ।
jñasvabhāvena nityena svarūpeṇāmalātmanā ।।

viśvamāpūritaṃ sarvaṃ sarvānugrahakāmyayā ।
sarvatra yāsti sarveṣāṃ yathoktānāṃ mahāmate ।।

vāsudevādimūrtīnāṃ vaiśvarūpyam anaśvaram ।
yogaiśvaryaprabhāvena acyutecchāvaśādapi ।।

jñātvaivam abjasaṃbhūta na kāryo hṛdi vismayaḥ ।
sphuṭe[śvabhrasva]rūpeṇa nānānāmānvitena vai ।।

dṛṣṭo bhagavadākāre svayaṃ vyaktādikena ca ।
kṣitimadhye avatīrṇe ca pūrvoddiṣṭena vartmanā ।।

tīrthoddeśeṣu sarveṣu kṣetreṣu vividheṣu ca ।
giriśṛṅgeṣu ramyeṣu tanmadhyeṣu guhāsu ca ।।

vaneṣūpavanāḍhayeṣu pātālatalabhūmiṣu ।
lokontareṣūrdhvageṣu devair gandharvasattamaiḥ ।।

nāstikā bhinnamaryādā mohamāyāmalānvitāḥ ।
vikalpadoṣairāviṣṭāḥ bhrāntabuddhijaḍīkṛtāḥ ।।

caraṇāmbujanālaṃ tu parāmṛśyanti ye adhamā ।
majjanti narake ghore pitṛbhiḥsahitāścirāt ।।

sadāyatanadevānāṃ mūlaṃ ye cānviṣanti vai ।
mūrdhnaśchedo bhavetteṣāṃ bhāvopahatacetasām ।।

dhṛtiśaktimayaṃ mūlaṃ devānāmapi durdṛśam ।
tatkathaṃ lakṣyate mūḍhairyanmūrtadravyatāṃ gatam ।।

mānameyaiḥsvatantraṃ ca yathā tatparama[dbhu]tama ।
yairetanmadhyaṣaṭkaṃ tu kṣetreśāṅghrikajaissthitaiḥ ।।

guṇairdivyayaguṇopetairūrjitaiḥ prākṛtairguṇaiḥ ।
svayamevaṃ jayannāthair avatīrya ca yā sthitiḥ ।।

gṛhītā susthirā caiva susiddhaiścāpi kalpitā ।
doṣaisadigvibhāgādyair anyadātvena yānti ca ।।

nityasannidhimāhātmyāt kālaṃ kalpakṣayāvadhi ।
uttarottaratā caiva jagatyasmin hi vartate ।।

duṣṭopaśāntidā śaktyā siddhidā yā ca vai saha ।
paurūṣāyatanānāṃ ca siddhākhyānāṃ mahāmate ।।

svayamevāvatīrṇānāṃ tattveśānāmapi kṣitau ।
ataḥsaṃsārabhītaiśca bhaktaiḥsarveśvarasya ca ।।

gamyaiśca ter'canīyāśca kālaṃ vai jīvitāvādhi ।
nityaṃ tūpāsitavyāśca tatrasthairāśramānvitaiḥ ।।

prāptādhikārair dīkṣāntasamayajñādikairnaraiḥ ।
yadaiva kṛtadīkṣāṇām adhikārasamanvitam ।।

acyutārādhanārthaṃ tu niḥśreyasapadāptaye ।
tadaiva pratiṣiddhaṃ ca devatāntarapūjanam ।।

parametaddhi samayam aprameyaratātmanām ।
sā prasiddhā tu vai vyaktād ākārāt parameśvarāt ।।

vyūhād vā vibhavākhyācca ṛte nānyat puroditāt ।
samarcanīyam ākāraṃ na budhairvasudhāgatam ।।

kvacidbhagavadaṃśaistu prādurbhāvair adhiṣṭhitāḥ ।
dṛśyante pārthivā liṅgāḥ śrūyante ca dvijottama ।।

yadyapyevaṃ mahābuddhe vaiṣṇavānāṃ tathāpi hi ।
viruddhatvād anarcyāste nopādhir vaiṣṇavī hi sā ।।

svayaṃmuvāpi ye kecit surasiddhāvatāritāḥ ।
skandarudramahendrādyāḥ pratiṣiddhāstu ter'cane ।।

antaryāmī ca sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ puruṣottamaḥ ।
yadyapyavyaktarūpe ca vyaktau siddhiḥsvakā svakā ।।

bhāvabhaktivaśād vipra svakri yādhigamādapi ।
jñātvaivaṃ bhaktisāṃkaryaṃ na kuryādevameva hi ।।

varjanīyaṃ prayatnena ya icched uttamāṃ gatim ।
viprā ekāyanākhyā ye te bhaktāstattvato acyute ।।

ekāntinaḥsutattvasthā dehāntānnānyānyayājinaḥ ।
kartavyatvena ye viṣṇuṃ saṃyajanti phalaṃ vinā ।।

prāpnuvanti ca dehānte vāsudevatvam abjaja ।
vyāmiśrayājinaścānye bhaktābhāsāḥ tu te smṛtāḥ ।।

parijñeyāḥ tu te viprā nānāmārgagaṇārcanāt ।
tasmāt saṃsiddhadehastu dīkṣākhyena tu karmaṇā ।।

yāvajjapādhikāraṃ tu nārāyaṇaparo bhavet ।
japahomakriyāsaktaḥ samāste stutitatparaḥ ।।

dehānte vaiṣṇavaṃ lokaṃ prāpnuyāt punareva hi ।
janma cāsādya cotkṛṣṭam ābālyād dvijasattama ।।

bhagavatkarmaniṣṇātaḥ tatparastanmayo bhavet ।
nābhisandhāya ca phalam āpatkālagato api vai ।।

tyaktvā dehaṃ punarjanma nāpnuyādiha pauṣkara ।

pauṣkara ucāca 

bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa kṣetraiḥ kṣetravaraissaha ।
pāramyena ca yairvyāptaṃ kṣityantaṃ tattvasaṃgraham ।।

vāsudevākhyasadbrahmatatvād ārabhya vai kramāt ।
vaktumarhasi me śaśvat sarvānugrahakāmyayā ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

ṣāḍguṇyadehasaṃjñena svasthena caturātmanā ।
svargāntaṃ svapadā vyāptam adhidevātmanā dvija ।।

yā vai sarveśvarī śaktir īśvarākhyā viśāmanī ।
jñānādibhedabhinnena ādyena caturātmanā ।।

vyāptā cāvyaktaliṅgena bhārūpeṇa mahātmanā ।
yā parā prakṛtirdaivī satvaikaguṇalakṣaṇā ।।

pūrṇā śaktisamūhena vaibhavīyena padmaja ।
saha mūrtyantareṇaiva prādurbhāvāntarastathā ।।

prādurbhāvamayairbījaiḥ samūhe caturātmanā ।
jīvakṣetrajñakātmanāmadheyam anaśvaram ।।

vartate vai samāsādya nityaṃ saiveśvarecchayā ।
traiguṇyasāmyam ādhāram avyaktākhyaṃ ca śāśvatam ।।

tatrastham abhimānākhyarūpeṇa parameśvara m ।
sphuṭam avyaktabhedaṃ ca cāturātmyaṃ jagatprabhum ।।

dvibhujaṃ purūṣākārayuktam ādityasannibhaiḥ ।
dhvajair ābharaṇaiścihnaiḥśaṅkhacakrādisaṃjñitaiḥ ।।

avyakte buddhitattve ca sthitaṃ vyaktataraṃ vibhum ।
caturmūrtiṃ caturvaktraṃ caturbāhuṃ caturgatim ।।

lāñchanair dhvajaparyantair vyaktairyuktamanaśvaraiḥ ।
ahaṅkāraṃ samāśritya avyaktaṃ kamalodbhava ।।

sthitā mūrtyantarāḥsarve keśavādyāstu vai smṛtāḥ ।
haṃsādyāḥṣaṇmayoktā ye yathāsaṃsiddhilakṣaṇāḥ ।।

manastattvaṃ samāsādya samyak jñānaguṇānvitāḥ ।
buddhīndriyaguṇaṃ vipra ṣaḍete punaranyathā ।।

paurūṣaṃ dehamāsādya saṃsthitāḥ parameśvarāḥ ।
kalkiniṣṭhā ṣaḍbhujāśca vāmanādyā dvijeśvarāḥ ।।

karmendriyasamūhaṃ tu tiṣṭhantyāśritya sarvadā ।
dharmādyā viśvarūpāntā ye ca sarvaguṇairyutāḥ ।।

tanmātrāpañcakaṃ khādyaṃ samāśritya ca saṃsthitāḥ ।
ākāśādyaṃ samūhaṃ yadbhūtānāmabjasaṃbhava ।।

saṃsthitā vai samāśritya prāguktā vibudhottamāḥ ।
uktaśeṣair mahābuddhe prādurbhāvāntaraiḥ saha ।।

uparāgaṃ yathāsādya lokatrayasamanvitam ।
ekadeśaṃ samāyāti tīrthasaṃṅgaṃ kurūkṣitau ।।

anugrahadhiyā caiva parayā kṛpayā dvija ।
antakāle tu buddhānāṃ devairvyāptam anusmaran ।।

adhyakṣo daivataṃ kṣmāntaṃ vigrahaṃ tattvasaṃgraham ।
vācyavācakayuktāstu te api yānti parāṃ gatim ।।

yasmādvai bhagavacchaktyā tvanukampākhyayā dvija ।
āviśya bāndhavaiḥsnigdhaṃ jantoḥ saṅgatisiddhaye ।।

tattasyānena vidhinā āpādayati vai śubham ।
tīrthe vāyatane kṣetre visaṃjñasya mahāmate ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

kṣetraiḥ kṣaitreśvaropetair bhūtānām iha yatprabho ।
anugrahārtham ākrāntaṃ tamādiśatu sāmpratam ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

karmabhūmau manuṣyāṇāṃ bhavyāḥ kṣetrāḥ tathā hi ye ।
agamyāḥ tvapi teṣāṃ ye surasiddhagaṇaṃ vinā ।।

sāmprataṃ me ca te śaśvadekāgram avadhāraya ।
āryāvarte tu bhūbhāge pṛthivyāṃ puṇyasaṃjñake ।।

madhyadeśasamopete caturdikpariniṣṭhite ।
sāmudrajalalekhāyāṃ tatparyante mahāntare ।।

āsṛṣṭeravatīrṇā yeḥ svādhiṣṭhānaiḥsahākhilāḥ ।
ādidevādayo devā vyaktivigrahalakṣaṇāḥ ।।

yatra yatra ca bhūbhāge yo yassārveśvaraṃ vapuḥ ।
yasmādyasmāttu vai tasmād āsṛṣṭeretya saṃsthitāḥ ।।

kṣetraśenānvitāścaiva tīrtheśena tathaiva hi ।
yasmāddevālayodeśāt dhmātasya jalajasya ca ।।

bhavecchabdāttavedhaśca tāvat kṣetraṃ taducyate ।
divyādyāyatanādīnām antaraṃ yadanaśvaram ।।

krośādhikasamaṃ nyūnaṃ mānenānena yena tu ।
antarvedī ca sā jñeyā nārāyaṇaratātmanām ।।

yajane śrāddhakaraṇe dāne votkramaṇer'cane ।
japadhyāne tapoyajñe agnisantarpaṇena ca ।।

sthitaṃ yadekadeśe tu dīpāloko dvijottama ।
ābhāsayati bhūbhāgaṃ paratastadvadeva hi ।।

svakṣetraṃ kṣetranāthaṃ ca samāsādya ca vartate ।
aihikāmuṣmikī caiva siddhir bhavati dehinām ।।

tatra tāvaccaturmūrter mūrtyantaragaṇasya ca ।
sanniveśaṃ pṛthivyāṃ vai sāmprataṃ tvavadhāraya ।।

puṣkaraṃ kṣetramāśritya puṇḍarīkākṣasaṃjñayā ।
vāsudevastu bhagavānnityasannihitaḥsthitaḥ ।।

evaṃ kṣetravaraiḥ sarvametya viśveśvaraḥsvayam ।
caturmūrtidvijādyaṃ vai āsṛṣṭeḥsaṃsthitiṃ kratau ।।

caturṇāṃ mūrtibhedaṃ yad dviṣaṭkaparisaṃkhyayā ।
kṣetraiḥ tīrthānvitaisteṣāṃ saṃsthānam avadhāraya ।।

keśavaḥ kleśahā loke vai rūpyeṇa kṣitau sthitaḥ ।
abhivyaktena rūpeṇa govindaḥ purūṣottamaḥ ।।
bhūbhāgapadamāśritya saṃsthito nagasāhṛye ।।
sthāne vṛndāvanākhye api dvidhaiva kamalodbhava ।
viṣṇurlo[kāgha] he vipra sthito viṣṇupadena ca ।।

mandarākhyagiriṃ caiva āsādya madhusūdanaḥ ।
bhūtānām anukampārtham avatīrya ca saṃsthitaḥ ।।

yāmunaṃ jalamāśritya devadevastrivikramaḥ ।
sthitaḥ kamalasaṃbhūta nṛṇāṃ ca sugatipradaḥ ।।

mūrtyantaraṃ vāmanākhyaṃ sahayādrau kamalodbhava ।
svatattvādetya viśrāntaṃ bhavināṃ śokaśāntaye ।।

narmadākhyaṃ hi cākramya jalaṃ pāpakṣayaṅkaram ।
śrīdharaḥ saṃsthito devaḥ kauṇḍale ca śriyā saha ।।

hṛṣīkeśastu bhagavān saṃsthito apyātmanā bhuvi ।
dharādhare dhvajākhye tu kṣetre kubjāmrake abjaja ।।

padmanābhastu mādhyeśastvavatīrya ca saṃsthitaḥ ।
dākṣiṇāṃ diśam āśritya samīpe jaladhikṣitau ।।

girau revatake vipra svatattvādetya vartate ।
dāmodarastu bhagavān hitārthaṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

ebhir mūrtyantaraiḥ sārdhaṃ mūrtibhiḥ viśvamandiram ।
samāsādya dvijaśreṣṭha ato anyeṣāṃ ca saṃsthitim ।।

nibodhatu mahābuddhe sāvadhānena cetasā ।
siddhāmarārcitaṃ viddhi śvetadvīpe tu haṃsarāṭ ।।

matsyātmā bhagavānapsu aśvātmā baḍabāmukhe ।
rasātale tu kūrmātmā vindhyāraṇye tu pauṣkara ।।

vijñātavyo mṛgendrātmā pāpahā sarvadehinām ।
saukarīyena rūpeṇa kṣetre tatsaṃjñake tu vai ।।

gāṅge śubhajale kūle surasiddhaniṣevite ।
hemottamāṅgadṛgdevo hemaśailamahāntare ।।

naubandhanagirāveva mīnavaktraḥ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ ।
kṛṣṇāśve aśvaśiro devo kṣitikṣetre kṣamārcite ।।

lavaṇodadhiparyante bhūbhāge siddhasevite ।
kūrmavaktraśca bhagavān saṃsthitaḥ śaṅkhacakradhṛk ।।

nṛhariḥ kṛtaśauce tu ujjayinyām api dvija ।
viśākhamūlasaṃjñe tu sthāne tvevaṃ sthitastridhā ।।

kokāmukhe varāhastu vārāhe tu nagottame ।
kandamāle vivai taste kulakukṣau himācale ।।

vāmanaṃ kharvamūrtiṃ ca vaiśvarūpyeṇa saṃsthitam ? ।
madhyadeśe tu gaṅgāyāḥ kurūkṣetre tu pauṣkara ।।

yāmunaṃ kulamāsādya prādurbhāvāntaraṃ mahat ।
sthitaṃ trivikramākhyaṃ yastrailokyākrāntāvigrahaḥ ।।

nagottame mahendrākhye paraśvathakaro dvija ।
rāmasaṃjñaśca bhagavān saṃsthitaḥ kṣatriyāntakaḥ ।।

dharādhare citrakūṭe rakṣaḥkṣayakaro mahān ।
saṃsthitaścāparo rāmaḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇaḥ ।।

rāmo anyaḥsīrapāṇir vai yāmunaṃ bhrāmayañjalam ।
saṃsthito mānuṣīyeṣu bhūbhāgeṣu śubheṣu ca ।।

sāmudre api tato dvīpe dvārakākhye amarārcite ।
vartate bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ ।।

kalkī viṣṇuśca bhagavān stūyamāno dvijaiḥ sthitaḥ ।
samāsādya vipāśāṃ ca nadīṃ niyatamānasaḥ ।।

dharmamūrtir mahātmā vai dharmāraṇye surārcite ।
anugrahaparastvāste lokānāṃ lokapūjitaḥ ।।

narasaṃjñaṃ jagannāthaṃ siddhaiḥ saṃpūjiteṣu ca ।
bhūbhāgeṣu ca ramyeṣu nityasannihitaḥ sthitaḥ ।।

girau govardhanākhye tu devaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ ।
saṃsthitaḥ pūjite sthāne gavāṃ niṣkramaṇeṣu ca ।।

sāligrāme ca bhagavān rājendrākhye vane dvija ।
tathaiva vasudhāṃśena sthito devavratābhidhe ।।

kṛṣṇo aparaścaturmūrtir avatīrya dharātale ।
sthitaḥpiṇḍārake vipra mocayanduṣkṛtājjanān ।।

śvetadvīpe kurūkṣetre himavantācale abjaja ।
vedikāyāmapi nare viśvarūpaḥsthitaḥ prabhuḥ ।।

kṣīrodadhau padmanābhaḥśeṣāhiśayanopari ।
sthito nābhyabjasaṃbhūto yasmāccaiva pitāmahaḥ ।।

caturdhā rūpamāśritya viśve asmin saiva vartate ? ।
hitāya sarvalokānāṃ yathāvad avadhāraya ।।

āsādya śayanaṃ brahman pātālatalasaṃsthitaḥ ।
[rūpa]mādāya cāgneyaṃ yo ante saṃharate jagat ।।

vaṭamūlaṃ samāśritya prayāge surapūjite ।
jagadekārṇavaṃ kṛtvā divyam āsādya pādapam ।।

santiṣṭhate sa bhagavāṃstasmiṃstīre kṣitau dvija ।
nyagrodhaśāyinaṃ caiva dhyoyeddivyagatipradam ।।

himācalaikadeśe tu tuṅge vai bhṛgusaṃjñake ।
madhukaiṭabhamāthī ca saṃsthitaḥ so avanītale ।।

kṣīrodakakṣitikṣetre surāsuraniṣevite ।
mandrarādrikaro devo vartate devapūjitaḥ ।।

tatraivāmṛtajiddevaḥ saṃsthitaḥ siddhasevitaḥ ।
kāntārūpadharaścaiva sudhākalaśadhṛk tathā ।।

siddhānāṃ ca munīnāṃ ca devānāṃ mṛtyujit sthitaḥ ।
dvidhā kartā gaṇopetaṃ devaṃ garūḍavāhanam ।।

sālavṛkṣabhujoddeśe sāligrāme sthito vibhuḥ ।
trikūṭagiripṛṣṭhe tu gamye gaganacāriṇām ।।

gajoddhṛticchalenaiva aprameyākhyayā sthitaḥ ।
śvetadvīpapatir deva avatīrya ca saṃsthitaḥ ।।

gaṃgāsamudrasaṃyoge kṣityudeśe manorame ।
yajñabhug bhagavān devo naimiśe siddhapūjite ।।

saindhavāraṇyam āśritya ananto bhagavāṃssthitaḥ ।
śārṅgapāṇistu deveśo daṇḍakāraṇyasaṃjñake ।।

rakṣogaṇakulaṃ caiva saṃsthitaḥ tajjayaiṣiṇām ।
utpalāvartake deśe śaurisaṃjño acyutaḥsa ca ।।

kṣitau samudrasindhvorabdheḥ saṅgame siddhasevite ।
jñānopadeṣṭā bhagavān saṃsthito duḥkhaśāntaye ।।

āsādya sūkarakṣetraṃ devo garūḍavāhanaḥ ।
saṃsthito garūḍārūḍhaḥ pārijātakarāṅkitaḥ ।।

siddhaiḥ suragaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ gagane cāpi pauṣkara ।
devadeveśanāmnātha hastiparvatamastake ।।

ekadeśaṃ samāsādya sarvasya varadaḥ sthitaḥ ।
mālyodapāṇir vaikuṣṭho magadhāyāṃ mahāmate ।।

oḍḍīnye puṇyabhūbhāge saṃsthitaḥ purūṣottamaḥ ।
acintyātmātha bhagavān parvate gandhamādane ।।

śipiviṣṭākhyayā devaḥ śipiviṣṭavrate sthitaḥ ।
prāksamudrāpayāne tu bhūbhāge śubhalakṣaṇe ।।

kāpilaṃ mūrtim āsādya vāsudevaḥ sthita prabhuḥ ।
avatīrya svatattvācca brahmasaṃjñaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।

maṇibandhaṃ samāsādya nityaṃ sannihitaḥ sthitaḥ ।
magadhāmaṇḍale vipra mahābodhadharāśritaḥ ।।

saṃsthito lokanāthātmā devadevo janārdanaḥ ।
devadakṣiṇagākṣṇor vai yo abhimānatanur dvijaḥ ।।

sūryasaṃjñastu bhagavān hemaśailopari sthitaḥ ।
acyuto vāmanetre tu yo abhimānatanur vibhuḥ ।।

bhagavān somasaṃjñaḥ tu somatīrthāśrame api ca ।
agnisvarūpamajitaṃ saṃsthitaṃ baḍabānale ।।

vasvātmā gagane vipra bhāsate tvasurāntakṛt ।
viṣṇunāmnā punar devaḥ tvanekāyudhamaṇḍitaḥ ।।

jayākhyayojjayinyāṃ vai sthitaḥ pāpajaye nṛṇām ।
kāśmīramaṇḍale puṇye kṣetre cakradharābhidhe ।।

cakrapāṇistu bhagavān bhaktānāṃ mokṣadaḥ sthitaḥ ।
surottamābhidhānaśca gadāpāṇistu pauṣkara ।।

sadā sannihitaṃ viddhi gaṅgādvāre suraiḥ saha ।
caturbhujaścaturmūrtiścaturvaktraścaturgatiḥ ।।

sthitaḥ piṇḍārake devo viṣvaksenaḥ sanātanaḥ ।
śubham āsādya bhūbhāgaṃ prāgjyotiṣapure tathā ।।

devaṃ viśveśvarākhyaṃ ca sthitametya svagocarāt ।
sātatranābhidhakṣetre siddhavidyādharānvite ।।

svāmisaṃjño jagannāthaḥ sthito mandākinītaṭe ।
bhallātake mahāyoge dhyāyinām apavargadaḥ ।।

rasātale nṛsiṃhākhye devikāyā stataṭāśrite ।
ripukṣayākhyayā vipra devaḥ sarveśvaraḥ sthitaḥ ।।

śaṅkarākhye tu bhūbhāge sarvadevaniṣevite ।
jñānamūrtir jagannāthaḥ saṃsthitaḥśubhakṛnnṛṇām ।।

pṛthivyāṃ tu pitṛkṣetre mocayantānṛṇatrayāt ।
janārdanākhyayā brahman viśvātmā bhagavān sthitaḥ ।।

ete avatārāḥ kathitā leśataḥ kamalodbhava ।
ebhiḥ kṣititalaṃ vyāptaṃ paunaḥpunyena ca svayam ।।

saṃsāriṇāṃ janānāṃ tu anugrahadhiyābjaja ।
saṅkīrtanam agamyānāṃ trisandhyaṃ nityam ācaret ।।

matiṃ cakre gamyānāṃ sevane darśane api ca ।
mlecchānāṃ teṣu deśeṣu kṣitau kṣetrādayo hi ye ।।

sāṅkaryaparihāreṇa draṣṭavyāste sadaiva hi ।
ṛṣibhiḥ sāmaraiḥ siddhaiḥ svāśrameṣu mahatsu ca ।।

jalāśayeṣu puṇyeṣu pṛthivyāṃ vividheṣu ca ।
sarve bhagavādākārā vibhavavyūhalakṣaṇāḥ ।।

u ktā gatāśca ye cānye samutprekṣya dhiyāsvayam ।
pratiṣṭhitāśca vidhivat samantrāḥ satyavikramāḥ ।।

sthityā nānāprakārā ye bhūtabhavyādikākhyayā ।
saumyāgneyobhayākhyena sanniveśavaśena vai ।।

līlārūcimayenaiva cittasaukhyapradena ca ।
bhujādyāyudhasandhānaketubhedena vai saha ।।

alaṃkṛtaśca bhūbhāgo manujaistvevameva hi ।
bhaktair anugrahītaiśca siddhādyaiśca yathoditam ।।

ādidevādayaścaite tattveśāḥ samudīritāḥ ।
parasmin bhagavattatve tattvabhedena vyavasthitāḥ ।।

sūryasya raśmayo yadvadvahnercirgaṇaṃ yathā ।
jaladherūrmayo yadvat tadvadevābjasaṃbhava ।।

citsāmānyāni tyaśuddhā vyāpakāḥ parameśvarāḥ ।
tattvasattāṃ samāśritya jñānādyaiḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ ।।

aṇimādyaṣṭakopetāḥ saṃsthitāḥ svātmanā tu vai ।
adhvāvaniṣu sarvāsu nityaṃ kurvanti sannidhim ।।

muktaye sarvabhūtānāṃ viśeṣeṇa tu vai bhuvi ।
āviśvaprabhavāt kālādārabhya pralayāvadhi ।।

kṣetreṣu tīrthatīreṣu śabdabrahmayātmanā ।
sāmānyenāpi mantreṇa tadvivartena bhātmanā ।।

tato vyaktetaraṃ rūpam āśrayanti ca pārthivam ।
hitārthaṃ sarvalokānām avatīrṇam anaśvaram ।।

jagatyāyatanākhyāyām atra sidhyanti yoginaḥ ।
kālāntareṇa vyaktīnāṃ majjanaṃ jāyate yadi ।।

sannidhiṃ śaktibhāvena nityaṃ kurvanti tatra ca ।
yogeśvarāmarāḥ siddhāḥ smṛtvākāraṃ tadātmakam ।।

śailamuddārūdhātūtthāṃ vyaktiṃ saṃsthāpayanti ca ।
yatrānuvedhaṃ kurūr te mantraśaktidharā stu ye ।।

yenācyutīyanāmnā vai yadyatsvānāntaraṃ smṛtam ।
sannidhisthasya vai rūpaṃ śabdamūrtidharasya ca ।।

bhinnātmanāṃ svayaṃvyaktirūpeṣvavyaktakeṣu ca ।
sannirūddheṣu mantreṣu icchāvṛttigateṣu ca ।।

ākārāḥ saṃnniveśācca pārameśvaram anyathā ।
anyathā vai jagatyasmin khyātākhyātaṃ ca śāśvatam ।।

evam āyatanānāṃ ca nityatvaṃ saṃprakāśitam ।
anāditvam asaṃkhyaṃ ca mahattvam api pauṣkara ।।

jātā ye māṃ prasiddhir vai sati vyaktivaśād dvija ।
vinā vyaktisvarūpeṇa śabdenāpyakṣayātmanā ।।

vdyātmanāpi hi cānyatra śabdavyāktimayātmanā ।
anye munivarā vipra dṛṣṭvā sthānaṃ manoramam ।।

nirdeṣaṃ salilaṃ śuddhaṃ pādapauṣadhisaṃkulam ।
sthitiṃ kṛtvā sthirāṃ tatra karmaṇā manasā tataḥ ।।

sulakṣaṇaṃ tu pāṣāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā cānyatra vāhṛtam ।
viśvakarmakulodbhūtaṃ samājñāpya tu śilpinam ।।

upale asmijjagadyonerviṣṇoḥ sarveśvarasya ca ।
pādāravindamudrāṃ ca sampādya ca manoharām ।।

evam anye tu munayaḥ svasthāneṣu mahāmate ।
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmapūrvā ye harilāñchanāḥ ।।

niveśaṃ tatra kṛtvā vai bhaktipūtena karmaṇā ।
apare tu dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaktibṛṃhitamānasāḥ ।।

kurvanti sanniveśaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।
pūvokteṣu ca deśeṣu siddhādyai raciteṣu ca ।।

mudriteṣu sahasrārapūrvamudrāgaṇeṣu ca ।
pāṣāṇairvā mahābuddherāsṛṣṭeḥ pūjaneṣu ca ।।

kṛtvā saṃskārarūpaṃ tu nyāsaṃ yatrocitaṃ hi yat ।
kurvanti vidhipūrvaṃ tu nityaṃ traikālyam arcanam ।।

ṛksāmapūrvaiḥ sanmantrairdviṣaṭkārṇasamanvitaiḥ ।
bhagavatpadasidhyarthaṃ śiṣyādīnāṃ śubhāptaye ।।

evaṃ puṣkarasaṃbhūta grāmāśca viṣayākhilāḥ ।
nagarāḥsapurā rājñāṃ prakhyātā ye kṣitau śubhāḥ ।।

ṛṣibhir manujaiḥśuddhaiḥ svayaṃ sarveśvareṇa tu ।
bhaktānāṃ anukampārthaṃ nītāḥ puṇyapadātmatām ।।

vibhavavyūhabhedena sthitā cānugrahecchayā ।
taskarādyupaghāte tu antarbhāvagate dvija ।।

pūrvamantrādayo mantrāḥ tatra ye prāṅnirodhitāḥ ।
bimbam ujjhitya tiṣṭhanti tadbrahmavivarāmbare ।।

saṃskāraṃ na kṛtaṃ yāvat pūrvaṃ tat sthāvaroditam ।
vardhate ca mahādoṣo dinārdhaṃ dinam anyathā ।।

taddeśajānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sādhakānāṃ nṛpasya ca ।
dvijendrādyair atasmād vaṇigbhirvā kuṭugbibhiḥ ।।

deśikair naranāthena kāryaṃ ca bhayanārānam ।
sarveṣāṃ pāpaśamane kṛtamantragaṇaṃ hi yat ।।

prātimaṃ vigrahaṃ śaśvatsarveṣāṃ śreyase tu vai ।
nirjanāyatanānāṃ tu dharmārthaṃ yaḥ samācaret ।।

doṣopaśamanaṃ tasya sarvaduḥkhakṣayo bhavet ।
bhavinām āptapūrṇānāṃ mahāmohakṣaya ca ।।

brahmaṇyadhipatitvena ākāraṃ cācyutaṃ hi yat ।
saviśeṣaiḥ samopetaṃ vibhūtyaṃśaiḥ samanvitam ।।

prajāpatiḥ tam āsādya saṃkrāntaṃ buddhidarpaṇe ।
tena karṇapathaṃ nītaṃ śilpinaḥ svātmajasya ca ।।

saṃpannasya ca homādyair deśikaiḥ saṃskṛtasya ca ।
saṃkrāman hyacirāttatra gauṇam ākāramaiśvaram ।।

saha vinyāsakāle tu vācakena mahātmanā ।
evamevam anāditvaṃ dravyajāsvākṛtīṣu ca ।।

saṃsiddhabhūtidṛṣṭir vai tulyakālaṃ tu bhūtale ।
viśvavadvismṛtiṃ naiti śilpibuddhisamāśritam ।।

sa hi yacchati bhaktānāṃ kṛtvākāraṃ sulakṣaṇam ।
yasya cābhimatastādṛk bhāvabhaktivaśāt tu vai ।।

dṛṣṭā svayaṃvyaktimato bhuvi bimbaṃ tu vai budhaḥ ।
brahmarudraikasūryākhyam ācyutaṃ viddhi tanmahat ।।

yad uktaṃ vyūhabhedasthaṃ mūrtibhedaiḥ samanvitam ।
tathaiva hi samārādhyaṃ budhyā kamalalocana ।।

ārādhane samādhau vā upaviṣṭāstu cotthitāḥ ।
saṃsthitāḥsthānakaiścānye tamo mūrtiṣvanuṣṭhitaiḥ ।।

dhārayatyadbhūtaṃ caiva lācchanadvayam icchayā ।
dvayaṃ karadvayenaiva lambamānacatuṣṭayāt ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmapūrvādyāyudhasaṃgrahāt ।
yathoddiṣṭakrameṇeva lokeśādiṣu vai purā ।।

jyādayaścecchayā cānye karaistiryak prasāritaiḥ ।
sūcayantyatibhaktānām udbhujatvena saṃpadam ।।

mandabhaktibharāṇāṃ tu tiryak saṃsthānasaṃsthitaiḥ ।
mahadātmapadaṃ divyaṃ yad [antasthaṃ hi saṃpadāt] ।।

yeṣāmantaritā bhaktirnṝṇāṃ vyābhiśrayājinām ।
prāptistriviṣṭape teṣāṃ bhujavṛndādayo mukhāt ।।

samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu brahman yadyapyahaṃ sadā ।
upadekṣyāmi yuktyā vai madbhaktā yānti saṃpadam ।।

aparair aṣṭabhedasthair varṇair vā brāhmaṇādikaiḥ ।
prasthāpitāśca vidhivat pratimā yā nṛpottamaiḥ ।।

pratibimbamayīṃ vyaktiṃ svayamevācyutena vā ।
jīrṇadoṣaṃ vinā caiva cālanaṃ yad aśāntikam ।।

kṣatam utpātapūrvaistu doṣaistu nṛpanāśakṛt ।
tadastamitamantrāṇāṃ bhūyaḥ saṃsthāpane kṛte ।।

udayaṃ jāyate śaśvacchāntaye kintu pauṣkara ।
deśikendrair yathādhyātāḥ sūryendvanalasaṃnibhāḥ ।।

praviśanti ca mantreśāḥ praṇavadhvanisādhitāḥ ।
karṣayanti vibhūtiṃ svāṃ kiñcitkālāntareṇa tu ।।

kṛtā vai dhvastadoṣāśca nirvidhnaṃ nirmalāḥ punaḥ ।
niveśitāḥ susiddhādyaistīrthaiḥ kṣetravaneṣu ca ।।

nivārayanti ye mohād vibhavavyūhamūrtiṣu ।
saṃsthānamānam ākāraṃ doṣaṃ kālāntare sthitam ।।

te cāntakāle majjanti ghore tamasi duḥsahe ।
svalpavittair ataḥ tasmād alpabodhasamanvitaiḥ ।।

varjanīyaṃ vinānena devaṃ śreyo abhivāñchitaiḥ ।
svayam eva jagannāthastvavatīrya yathāsthitaḥ ।।

gṛhītaḥsusthirastvevam asiddhaiścāpi kalpitaḥ ।
doṣaiḥ sadigvibhaṅgādyair anyathātvaṃ na yāti ca ।।

nityasannidhimāhātmyāt kālaṃ kalpakṣayāvadhi ।
uttarottaratāṃ caiva jagatyasmin hi vartate ।।

bhūtyā kāntyā ca kīrtyā ca kriyayā cāprameyayā ।
duṣṭopaśāntidā śaktyā siddhidā yā ca vai saha ।।

pauruṣāyatanānāṃ ca siddhākhyānāṃ mahāmate ।
svayamevāvatīrṇānāṃ tattveśānām iha kṣitau ।।

evaṃ kṣetreśvarāṇāṃ tu sakṣetrāṇāṃ mayābjaja ।
prakāśitaṃ rahasyaṃ ca muktaye bhavināṃ mayā ।।

phalārthināṃ ca bhavināṃ kṣetre kṣetreśasevinām ।
yathābhimatasaṃprāptim ihaivāyāntyanaśvarīm ।।

atha bhūmitale jātā pralayākhye mahānti te ।
kṣetre kṣetreśvarāṇāṃ tu rahasyam avadhāraya ।।

jñānādyaiḥ sāṇimādyaistu avyaktaiḥ kṣmāvasānikaiḥ ।
tattvabījair upādeyair brahmasattāsamanvitaiḥ ।।

sahāvatīrya vā sṛṣṭeḥ prāgvyaktiṃ yānti vai tataḥ ।
svayamevārthabhāvena sarvānugrahakāmyayā ।।

kṣmāmaṇḍalopasaṃhārakālaṃ kṣetradharaiḥ saha ।
sthitim īśvaratattve tu kurvanti ca tadicchayā ।।

saviśvavyaktisamaye prāgvyaktiṃ pravadanti ca ।
jātijanmatathādeśaduḥkhair dehotthitaiḥ saha ।।

ādhivyādhiprapūrvaistu mānasair duḥsahaistathā ।
ityevamādibhirdeṣair mucyate [tvāpṛte] katham ।।

samyagjñānaṃ vijānanto kṣetrīyānugraheṇa vā ।
āviṣkṛtā bhaved bhaktistīvrabhaktādyanugrahāt ।।

jāyate ca matirnṝṇām ante kṣetre dvijācyute ।
necchanti savikalpāsu abhaktā nāstikottamāḥ ।।

vivekaḥ puruṣādīnām āyātaṃ ca phalādvibhoḥ ।
puruṣārthaparityāgaṃ na kāryaṃ bodhitena vai ।।

jīvanaṃ ca jagatyasmin viprakarmasamanvitam ।
īśvarastannirāse tu śakto bahuvidhair makhaiḥ ।।

tadastitvaṃ gurumukhāt tatsaṃvedanasaṃyutam ।
śraddadhānāśca bhaktāśca labhante ca narottamāḥ ।।

jñātavyam ātmanātmānaṃ tataḥ sarvajñam īśvaram ।
abhimānam anādyaṃ yat prākṛtaṃ satvajaṃ tvatha ।।

asmitālakṣaṇaṃ ghoraṃ sarvadāvāñchitapradam ।
vijñeyam ātmanātmānaṃ tāvad yāvannibodhitam ।।

bījānāṃ hi yathākālaṃ vyā ptānāṃ phalam alpadā ।
evaṃ vyāpānā nācca kṣetreṣvāyataneṣu ca ।।

janmābhyāsavaśāccāpi nūnaṃ karmakṣayo bhavet ।
iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ āyatanavicāro nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pauṣkara uvāca 

pādamudrāṅkitānāṃ ca upalānāṃ jagatprabho ।
cakrapadmāṅkitānāṃ ca nyāsaṃ saṃskārapūrvakam ।।

ādhārāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ jñātum icchāmi sāṃpratam ।
evaṃ cānādisiddhānāṃ pāṣāṇānāṃ jagatpate ।।

śaṅkhādyair aṅkitānāṃ ca lāñchanaiḥ pārameśvaraiḥ ।
prāptaiḥ saṃpūjanārthaṃ tu gṛhasthairvā vanasthitaiḥ ।।

anyeṣāṃ caivamādīnāṃ yāganiṣpattaye tu vai ।
calānām acalānāṃ ca saṃvidhānaṃ mamādiśa ।।

śrībhagavān uvāca 

āpāditaṃ purā dravyaṃ śilpinā ca yatātmanā ।
kṛtvā saṃskārasaṃśuddhaṃ dravyaiḥ prāṅ mantraprabhāvitaiḥ ।।

yatra yatrānurūpaṃ ca tatra tannyāsam ācaret ।
tadānugrahaśaktyantam ākṣiteḥ kamalodbhava ।।

mantrāṇāṃ sannidhiḥ kāryaścalapīṭhe tu kevale ।
tātkālikaṃ tu vihitaṃ nirodhaṃ tatra cārcanam ।।

ādhāraśakter ārabhya mantragrāmasya pauṣkara ।
susthire sannirodhaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ vihitaṃ sadā ।।

tatrāvāhya yajen mantram iṣṭvā cotthāpayet punaḥ ।
na hitaṃ pūjyamantrasya pūjākālaṃ vinābjaja ।।

sādhanāt sannimittatvāt jñānenātra nirodhanam ।
puṣpādyāharaṇe kāle pratyahaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।।

anugrahaparastvāste sa tatraiva khaśabdavat ।
calabimbena saha vai ekībhāvagatasya vā ।।

pīṭhasya mantravinyāsaṃ vihitaṃ calapīṭhavat ।
susthirasyaikayonervā viyoge susthirasya ca ।।

mantrāṇāṃ vihitaṃ nyāsaṃ sthirapīṭhoditaṃ tu vai ।
āpādād brahmarandhrāntaṃ calabimbasya pauṣkara ।।

prākṛtānāṃ tu tattvānāṃ kuryād vai sanniveśanam ।
kṣityādikānāṃ pādāntam avyaktād vā dharāntimam ।।

sarvatattvamayaṃ mantraṃ tasya vā kevalaṃ hṛdi ।
prādhānikaṃ yojanīyam abhinnaṃ tattvakāraṇam ।।

athejyāvasare prāpte mantratantre niyojayet ।
jaḍatvavinivṛtyartham tattvamantragaṇasya ca ।।

jīvabhūtaṃ tu taṃ vipra nityaṃ śuddhaṃ sadoditam ।
sāṅgam āvāhya mantraṃ ca lāñchanādyaiḥ pariṣkṛtam ।।

upasaṃhṛtya tatrasthaṃ niṣpanne vārcane sati ।
vinyāsam upasaṃhāraṃ māntraṃ yatsamudīritam ।।

tīrthakṣetradharāṇāṃ ca vihitaṃ tatpravāsanam ।
nityapratiṣṭhite bimbe prāsāde svagṛhe api vā ।।

anyatra vāṅkaṇādau tu tasya kuryāt nirodhanam ।
ādhārapīṭhamantraistu lāñchanīyaiḥ svakaiḥ saha ।।

asthirāṇāṃ pratiṣṭhānāṃ viśeṣam idam ācaret ।
yathodite tu saṃpanne sthāpite parameśvare ।।

kuryāt tato anuvedhaṃ ca ādhārācca śikhā vi dhi ।
sāmarthyaśaktasūtreṇa īśvareṇākṣayena ca ।।

sati yena viluptasya vimbādyair anvitasya ca ।
na jahāti mantraughastasya kālāntareṇa ca ।।

aprabuddhaḥ prabuddho vā tasminnāyatane pumān ।
niveśayati yo bimbam aparaṃ dravyajaṃ tu vā ।।

tadvijñānānuviddhaṃ ca jāyate samanantaram ।
evaṃvidhasya jñānasya trailokye asmin hi padmaja ।।

pratītyāyatanatvena bhavatyācandratārakī ।
sanniveśaṃ jagaddhātur yatra yatsiddhasevitam ।।

tad asiddhairna netavyam anyathātvaṃ malīmase ।
[ṭa yastajjñastattvavid bhaktaḥ śraddadhānaḥ sadāstikaḥ ।।

budhvāvaniviparyāsamekaṃ kālāntarodbhavam ।
prayatnaiḥ sucikitsyaṃ yat tad aṃtardhānaśaṅkayā ।।

prasannādyaiḥ samādāya tadājñāṃ vratapūrvikām ।
praṇavena mahāyogaṃ pūrvaṃ pūrṇāntam arcanam ।।

samāpādya sadānaṃ ca sanniveśyāsane apare ।
parameśvaram anyathā jāyate tasmin sade ।।

vyādhitaskaradurbhikṣaṃrāṣṭrabhaṅgapuraḥsaram ।
āgāmi vartamānaṃ ca deśaṅgādyupaplavaiḥ ।।

cālanaṃ vidhipūrvaṃ tu tu kṛtaṃ nāniṣṭadaṃ bhavet ।
punaranyatra vā tasmin sthāne kuryācca yojanam ।।

yathāśāstroktavidhinā samyagutsavapūrvakam ।
kintu prabodhayenmantraṃ tantraṃ yatsakriyāṃ vinā ।।

sthitaṃ śāntasamānau tu āśraye cākṣaye sati ।
cālanād vidhinirmuktād doṣaḥ saṃcālakasya yat ।।

taddhomārcanadāne tu sthāpanāt prāk samaṃ nayet ।
susthiraṃ vācalaṃ bimbaṃ tatra kṛtvā niveśya ca ।।

gobhūsuvarṇadānaṃ ca yathāśaktyā samācaret ।
dhātumṛcchailadārūtthaṃ vastrādiṣvatāritam ।।

akasmād bhagavad bimbaṃ dhatte vai mlānatāṃ yadi ।
vyatyayāt tatkriyālopād akālaparipūjanāt ।।

mahadbhayaṃ sarāṣṭrasya pūjakasya janasya ca ।
tasmānmantravaraṃ sāṅgaṃ tantrasaṃśodhitaṃ ca yat ।।

kalaśe maṇḍale agnau tu saptāhaṃ tarpayet kramāt ।
hemantaśaiśire kāle daivīm arcām tu śailajām ।।

snāpayitvārcayitvā ca vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।
suvastraveṣṭitāṃ kṛtvā gavyena haviṣā tataḥ ।।

āpīṭhāt piṇḍatāṃ nītvā rañjayeccandanādinā ।
patracchedamayaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sitādyair api nirmitaiḥ ।।

nānādeśodbhavaiścānyaiḥ sitaiḥ pītādikaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।
chāyāmārutasaṃśuṣkaiḥ haritairbhedasaṃyutaiḥ ।।

pūjāṃ yathoditāṃ kṛtvā bhūṣaṇairvividhaiḥ saha ।
vāsasā sthūlaśuklena kārpāsenāvakuṇṭhya ca ।।

kuṅkumenāmaleṃnaiva kambalenāvikena vā ।
sitena sughanenaiva abhuktenāhatena ca ।।

śītakāle hyatīte tu apanīyājyakambalam ।
pāvanārthaṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

bhaktānāṃ nāgarādīnāṃ yacchet saṃprārthitaṃ kramāt ।
bhūtaye aśubhaśāntyarthaṃ rakṣārthaṃ prārthanaṃ kramāt ।।

vijayenāpamṛtyūnāṃ vyādhīnām upaśāntaye ।
prāpte nidāghakāle tu pratyahaṃ śītavāriṇā ।।

yathoktena vidhānena kuryāt snānam adhikramāt ।
masūramāṣacūrṇena rajanīśālijena ca ।।

samudvartya ca saṃkṣāṣya haviṣābhyañjanādinā ।
vāsasā nirmalaṃ kṛtvāṃ candanena sitena ca ।।

śītakenodakenātha kṣālanīyaṃ tadālayam ।
saṃmārjya gomayenaiva kṛtvā bāhyopalepanam ।।

vikīrya patrapuṣpāṇi kumudotpalapaṅkajān ।
jalārdraistālavṛntaistu vījayet bimbam ācyutam ।।

stutvā ca vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ svareṇoccatareṇa tu ।
tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya dvicatuḥsaṃkhyayābjaja ।।

naikaṃ tripañcasaṃkhyaṃ ca gaṇanāviṣamaṃ ca yat ।
yataḥ samo hi bhagavān devaḥ sarvasya vai hariḥ ।।

saṃnyāsī daṇḍavatkuryāt praṇipātaṃ ca sarvadik ।
pradakṣiṇasamopetaṃ bahudhotthāya cāgrataḥ ।।

vihitaṃ snātakādīnām anyeṣām evam eva hi ।
sahāntaḥkaraṇenaiva bhaktiyuktena cetasā ।।

natapṛṣṭhaśirojānulalāṭataṭahṛtkaraḥ ।
gṛhastha ācarennityaṃ praṇāmaṃ sapradakṣiṇam ।।

smarannaṣṭākṣaraṃ buddhyā asakṛt vitate kṣitau ।
saṅkaṭe sati bhūbhāge bhagavatyagrataḥ sthitaḥ ।।

yathā tu bhaktitaḥ kuryāt baddhvā tu karasaṃpuṭam ।
hṛddeśe mūrdhni kampaistu saha sarveśvaraṃ smaret ।।

kṛtenānena vidhinā svaśaktyā valitena vā ।
yatheṣṭaṃ phalam āpnoti pumān bhaktikriyāparaḥ ।।

niṣkāmaḥ śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ prāpnuyāt surapūjitam ।
bhaktaiḥ saṃpūjitaṃ bhaktyā ye paśyanti jagatprabhum ।।

śraddhayā cānumodante te api tatphalabhāginaḥ ।
saṃsārakṣayam akṣayyaṃ karmir ṇāṃ kṣayam eti ca ।।

dvividhena hyupāyena nānyathā tu kathañcana ।
samantrācca kriyākāṇḍāt saṃpūrṇāt pañcalakṣaṇāt ।।

samyagbodhaparijñānāt bhagavad bhaktirañjanāt ।
karmaṇā manasā vācā yo nityaṃ bhagavanmayaḥ ।।

śāsane tvadhikārīṇām avatiṣṭhettu tattvataḥ ।
pāramyaṃ vetti śāstrasya mokṣadasyācyutasya ca ।।

so acirācchuddhim āpnoti duṣkṛtāt pūrvasañcitām ।
iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ āyatanavicāro nāma saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha aṣṭātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pauṣkara uvāca 

ākārāṇām anantānāṃ kṣitau kṣetreṣu vartinām ।
kālenāntarhitānāṃ ca teṣāṃ bhūyo niveśanam ।।

kurvanti vibudhāḥ siddhāḥ smṛtvā smṛtvā tadākṛtim ।
asatyair martyadharmasthaiḥ kathaṃ kāryaṃ niveśanam ।।

svakuloddharaṇārthaṃ ca kīrtyarthamapi cātmanaḥ ।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

sāṅgenārādhya mantreṇa jñānadhyānānvitena ca ।
bhavanārcanayuktena sajapena tu pauṣkara ।।

niveśanaṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ dravyajāsvākṛtīṣu yat ।
vihitā sā pratiṣṭhā vai mantriṇām āptalakṣaṇā ।।

mantrasiddhipradaṃ śaśvadante mantraṃ padaṃ dvija ।
mantrajñānām asāmarthyāt mṛtānām atha pauṣkara ।।

anugrahadhiyā cāryapreritaistatsutādibhiḥ ।
yathoditena vidhinā tanmantreṇa mahāmate ।।

saha ṛksāmasaṃjñaistu mantraiḥ svavyāptisaṃyutaiḥ ।
cetasā sāvadhānena vyavahārayutena ca ।।

kriyate madhyamā sā vai pratiṣṭhā svalpabhogadā ।
padamātraṃ ca dehānte saṃyacchatyamalaṃ śubham ।।

kevalaiḥ śrutimantraistu yathāvasaralakṣaṇaiḥ ।
dhāraṇā bhagavaddhyānamantranyāsena vai saha ।।

deśikendreṇa vai kāryā bhaktānāṃ parameśvare ।
sāmānyā tu parijñeyā yajñavat svargabhogadā ।।

aihikāmuṣmikaṃ māntraṃ phalaṃ yatkamalodbhava ।
vijñeyaṃ deśikādhīnaṃ loke asmin lokapūjita ।।

tasmād yastattvavijñānī śāstrajñaḥ satkriyāparaḥ ।
ṣaḍadhvavid asaṃkīrṇaḥ sarvabhāvena pauṣkara ।।

tena pratiṣṭhito devaścalo vā susthiro bṛhat ।
tatra saṃrodhito mantraḥ samyag abjadalekṣaṇa ।।

calastharavibhāgena bhavet sannihitaḥ tadā ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

deva kālāntareṇaiva dravyam eti kṣayātmatām ।
apratyakṣo hi mantrātmā lokānāṃ lokapūjita ।।

pratīkṣyate kiṃ tattvajñair atra me saṃśayo mahān ।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

karmabandhāt pṛthakkṛtya devo deśikamūrtikaḥ ।
nānābhaktiprapannānāṃ tathā nānāphalārthinām ।।

karmiṇāṃ kīrtiśaktiryā viśvamandirapūrakī ।
nirastadoṣā mahatī tām ākramya mahāmate ।।

divyamantrasvarūpeṇa vṛttidravyamayeṣu ca ।
upāyeṣvanuviddhā sudhṛtyā śaktimarīcibhiḥ ।।

tiṣṭhatyanugrahārthaṃ ca sā pratiṣṭheti kīrtitā ।
evaṃ dravyamayo yatra sanniveśo abjasaṃbhava ।।

ubhayānugrahaṃ nityaṃ karuṇābhaktilakṣaṇam ।
pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ hi tatkarma śuktimuktiphalapradam ।।

tacca sad brahmaniṣṭhānāṃ dvijānām ātmasiddhaye ।
kartavyatvena vai nityaṃ niṣiddham amalekṣaṇa ।।

tad doṣācca yatasteṣāṃ nistāro hi na vidyate ।
dehāpātād ṛte nānyastatpātastvatidoṣakṛt ।।

ādāveva hi tat tasmānnācartavyaṃ kṛtātmabhiḥ ।
tatkarmapratipannānāṃ caturṇām api taiḥ sadā ।।

kāryaṃ samyak pratiṣṭhānām anugrahadhiyā sadā ।
noparodhasvabhāvena na lobhena na mānataḥ ।।

prāpte tvākasmike doṣe hyaṅgabhaṅgādike abjaja ।
