bhaktānām anukampārthaṃ divyairmantrairbalādikaiḥ ।।

dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu mokṣaikaphalalakṣaṇaiḥ ।
saṃpūjitaiḥ hutaiḥ japtaiḥ kurute niṣkṛtiṃ sadā ।।

tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kartavye asmin dvijottama ।
traividyaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiḥ śūrdrairvā bhagavanmayaiḥ ।।

sakāmair atha niṣkāmaiḥ mantrārādhanatatparaiḥ ।
snātakaiḥ bhagavadbimbasthāpanārthaṃ sadaiva hi ।।

purā prasādanīyaṃ prārthanāpūrvakaṃ tu vai ।
adhikārapadasthaṃ dvijendraḥ pāñcarātrikaḥ ।।

vettā yo vyūhapūrvasya vyaktasya paramātmanaḥ ।
so anyeṣāṃ bhagavadbimbasthāpane adhikṛtaḥ sadā ।।

anugrahapratiṣṭhā cāpyadhikāranirūpaṇā ।
ananyair upapannānāṃ bhaktānāṃ kāryamucyate ।।

ananyāḥ pañcakālajñāḥ vyatiriktā na ye purā ।
prāksṛṣṭestanmukhodbhūtā dviṣaṭkādhyātmacintakāḥ ।।

caturvyūhaparatvena yeṣāṃ vai prabhavāpyaye ।
karmaṇām api saṃnyāsaṃ kurvantyadhyakṣataḥ kramāt ।।

ato anyo durlabhataraḥ pāramyaṃ yasya taṃ prati ।
prameyaniṣṭhā śuddhā ca sphuṭā tatkarmaṇi sthitiḥ ।।

paratvam anyamārgasthā necchanti ca parasparam ।
ya icchanti vibhosteṣāṃ sthitirnāsti tadākṛteḥ ।।

muktādhikāriṇaṃ taṃ vai labdhalakṣyam akṛtrimam ।
pañcakālarataṃ śuddhaṃ tantrasiddhāntapāragam ।।

tena vai śrutimantrāṇāṃ trayāṇām api codanā ।
pratikarmaṇi vai kāryā yathāvasaralakṣaṇā ।।

yasmāt abjasamudbhūta maṇḍalādiṣu vṛttiṣu ।
svārthato vā parārthena sadārādhanakarmaṇi ।।

nityasiddhe tadākāre tatparatve api pauṣkara ।
yasyāsti sattā hṛdaye tasyāsau sannidhiṃ bhajet ।।

mantrarūpī jagannāthaḥ paramātmācyutaḥ prabhuḥ ।
atyautsukyaṃ vinā vipra manasaḥ prītaye tvapi ।।

kāmāptaye tā kīrtyarthaṃ tasya tadvihitaṃ dvija ।
sādhanena pratiṣṭhānāṃ prāsāde svagṛhe tu vā ।।

iti samyak samākhyātaṃ mukhyakalpam ataḥ param ।
anukalpaṃ yadatrānyat tatsamāsānnibodhatu ।।

prākprāptadīkṣaiḥ vidhivat trayīdharmasthitair dvijaiḥ ।
nityārādhanasaktaistu bhaktair bhāgavatair vibhoḥ ।।

dhāraṇādhyānapūrvaistu labdhalakṣyaistu karmaṇām ।
mantramaṇḍalakuṇḍāstramudrādīnāṃ kṛtaśramaiḥ ।।

ṣaḍadhvavyāptiniṣṭhaistu tyāgaśīlair amatsaraiḥ ।
anujjhitakramair dakṣaiḥ svakarmaparipālakaiḥ ।।

satkīrtiprathitaiḥ loke tathākīrtibahiṣkṛtaiḥ ।
pratiṣṭhāṃ labhate kartā taiḥ pratiṣṭhāpane kṛte ।।

niṣidvam aravindākṣa ato anyeṣāṃ hi sarvadā ।
mahāmahaṃ pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ tathānyaṃ miśrayājinām ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

deva vyāmiśrayājitvaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ punaḥpunaḥ ।
prāguktānāṃ ca yāgānāṃ draṣṭum aṅgīkṛtaṃ ca yat ।।

tanmātrasaṃśayaṃ jātaṃ chettum arhasi sāṃpratam ।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

satyametanmahābuddhe yathā saṃcoditaṃ tvayā ।
kintu kriyāntare prāpte na doṣastvadhikāriṇām ।।

yasmātsarvaparatvaṃ hi teṣām astyacyutaṃ prati ।
tadāśritatvād devānām anyeṣāṃ pūjanāt tu vai ।।

na doṣo hi yathā loke bhrātṛbhṛtyagaṇasya ca ।
mānanād dharmapatnīnāṃ samakṣādvā parokṣataḥ ।।

ye punarlokadharmasthāḥ samabuddhipadojjhitāḥ ।
bhagavatyaviśeṣajñā nityaṃ kāryavaśena tu ।।

vāṅmātreṇa paratvaṃ vai sarveṣāṃ pravadanti hi ।
adhikāraṃ vinā ye atra preritā devatārcane ।।

evaṃ mārgasthiterlobhāt parijñāya tadāśayam ।
vyāmiśrayājinaste vai pātityapadasaṃsthitāḥ ।।

nayanti narakaṃ nūnam evam eva pravartinaḥ ।
na tu sadbhaktipūtānāṃ vāsudevaratātmanām ।।

kadācit tatkṛtaṃ doṣaṃ vidadhāti ca khaṇḍanām ।
āstāṃ tāvanmahābuddhe kartavyaṃ bhaktipūrvakam ।।

bhaktyā vai mantraniṣṭhānāṃ tanmantro japakarmaṇi ।
varṇavyatyayam āpanno luptastena svareṇa vā ।।

svarādinādhikaṃ caiva mantraikārthapradaḥ sadā ।
acirāt tatprayoktṝṇāṃ tathāpi kamalodbhava ।।

atibhaktiprabhāvācca vāñchitaṃ saṃprayacchati ।
yasmāt sadbhaktipūtānāṃ prapannānāṃ kramaṃ vinā ।।

prasādam eti mantreśastvacirād bhāvitātmanām ।
kiṃ punarvai kriyājñānasaṃpūrṇānāṃ tu pauṣkara ।।

śraddhābhaktiparāṇāṃ ca bodhitānāṃ ca deśikaiḥ ।
tasmāt samyak prasannānāṃ śāsane asmin mahāmate ।।

kāryaṃ dīkṣādikaṃ sarvaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhaktavatsalaiḥ ।
mām asaṃpratipanno yo matprāptyarthaṃ karoti ca ।।

mandamadhyamabhaktānāṃ kāmabhogaratātmanām ।
bhavināṃ māmakī dīkṣā mohād vā sthāpanādikam ।।

sa nayatyacirāt tasya bhaktibījena vai saha ।
svakarma karmatantraṃ ca siddhayaśca parāṅmukhāḥ ।।

ihaiva śīghram abjākṣa dehānte gatasadgatiḥ ।
ghoraṃ prayāti narakaṃ bhuktvaivaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ mahat ।।

bhagavanmantramāhātmyāt tadvyāpāravaśāt tu vai ।
saṃsargottham aghaṃ yāti prāksaṃskāravaśāt punaḥ ।।

cīrṇaduścarito bhūyaḥ prāpnuyānmānuṣīṃ tanum ।
prayatnam ācarecchubhraṃ yena śāntim avāpnuyāt ।।

sāhaṅkāraṃ tam ācāryam abhaktaṃ nādhikāriṇam ।
prāpnoti nūnaṃ sa labhet sakāmaṃ nārakīṃ sthitim ।।

sarvagastvapi mantrātmā sarvānugrahakṛ [dṭa dvija ।
yadyapyevaṃ hi tatrāpi na bhajet tatra sannidhim ।।

pratimām arcya dehāntaṃ nūnaṃ māṃ na viśatyuta ।
tatkṣaṇād bhūtavetālāḥ kurvantyarthādikakṣayam ।।

anyadarśanasaṃsthā ye nānugrāhyā ato abjaja ।
nāpāsyo hi tathā'cāryaḥ saṃsārabhayabhīruṇā ।।

samyagbhaktipareṇaiva ḍambharāgojjhitena ca ।
ata eva mahābuddhe pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ makhottamam ।।

nirvartanīyam āmūlāt vaiṣṇavānāṃ hi vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

caturṇāṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ bhagavadbhāvināṃ vibho ।
hitārthaṃ jñātum icchāmi bimbāpādanameva ca ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

devārthaṃ vanayātrārthaṃ kuryād rakṣādike śubhe ।
prāpte vanabhuvo deśe kṛte tad devatārcane ।।

śāśvataṃ vanaparyante pāṣāṇaṃ vā hareddrumam ।
cetasā suviśuddhena bhagavadyāgapūrvakam ।।

saha tatpañcarātrajñaistathā ṛksāmapūrvakaiḥ ।
bhaktaiḥ kriyāparaiḥ svacchairvinītaiḥ śilpibhiḥ saha ।।

saṃyatair dīkṣitaiścāpi vṛkṣādyaṃ prāk samāharet ।
pāṣāṇaṃ dhātavo mṛdvā mṛdu garbhāṃstu secayet ।।

vanabhūmivanotthānāṃ dhātūnāṃ mṛtsvarūpiṇām ।
saṃgrahaṃ vihitaṃ svalpaṃ melanīyaṃ ca tad dvije ।।

pratimāpādanārthaṃ ca mahāmṛtsaṃcaye śubhe ।
dhātudravyamayānāṃ ca mṛdgarbhāṇāṃ hṛdā saha ।।

tārahāṭakatāmrotthareṇūnāṃ kamalodbhava ।
vihitā yojanā nityaṃ mantramṛddāhaśāntaye ।।

aṅgārakāṣṭhaparyantaṃ vanāntād upayujyate ।
tatsarvaṃ vidhipūrvaṃ tu siddhikṛt syāt samāhṛtam ।।

evam ādāya tu purā vṛkṣapūrvaṃ vanāvaneḥ ।
tatra vā svagṛhoddeśe bimbāpādanam ācaret ।।

vidhivat karmaśālāyām ājñaptaṃ guruṇā yajet ।
śilpisvāmisvakaṃ paścāt svotthitena krameṇa tu ।।

buddhimān yajamāno vā ārambhādeva santyajet ।
sarvottame asmin vyāpāre bhāvaṃ rājasatāmasam ।।

nūnaṃ kaluṣabuddhīnāṃ na tatsaṃpadyate abjaja ।
yadyeva paripūrṇaṃ vā vighnadoṣaśatākulam ।।

karmaṇā prāktanenaiva sāttvikasyāpi padmaja ।
ghaṭamāne aṅgavaikalyaṃ jāyate daurmanasyakṛt ।।

atha tatra vidhānaṃ yad vihitaṃ tannibodha me ।
varṇakaiścitrabimbasya gālitenāmbhasādinā ।।

vihitāvayavānāṃ ca yojanā gandhabhāvitaiḥ ।
sitaraktādikai rāgaiḥ pāvanair astramantritaiḥ ।।

mṛdā mṛnmayabimbānāṃ madhvājyakṣīramiśrayā ।
kauśayacūrṇayutayā suvarṇodakasiktayā ।।

dārujasya tu saṃjāte bhede bhaṅge tu vābjaja ।
yojanā vastrāśastrabhyāṃ vihitā śāntipūrvikā ।।

sarvadā vihitaṃ tyāgam aśmajānāṃ bṛhatkṣate ।
kṣate hīṣatkṣate jāte sati ratnaśalākayā ।।

sahemayā ca vihitaṃ ghṛṣṭaśāṇasya gharṣaṇam ।
kṣatasāmye kṛte caiva pratimā syād guṇāvahā ।।

sthāpanaṃ sakṣatānāṃ ca karoti maraṇaṃ dhruvam ।
gurośca yajamānasya śilpiśreṣṭhasya deśinām ।।

kṣatam indriyacakrasthaṃ karturbhavati doṣadam ।
ākarṇān nābhiparyantam agrasthaṃ putramṛtyakṛt ।।

paścāddvaye tu jāyāyāḥ praṣṭhāṅgaṃ bhrātṛhānidam ।
ākaṭeḥ pāyuparyantaṃ bhaginīnāṃ kṣayo bhavet ।।

ūrumūlācca jānvantaṃ yatra yatra bhavet kṣatam ।
dhanadhānyapaśūnāṃ ca kṣayakṛccācireṇa tu ।।

jānoḥ pādatalāntaṃ ca bhṛtyavargasya doṣadam ।
sarveṣām anukampārtham ātmanaścāpi kīrtayet ।।

kartā kamalasaṃbhūta kṣatam akṣatatāṃ nayet ।
kriyamāṇasya bimbasya madhūcchiṣṭojjhitasya ca ।।

jāte avayavavaikalye hyanukalpam idaṃ śṛṇu ।
vigrahārambhe kṣatadoṣaḥ bhagavatpratipattau tu jātāyāṃ sati tatra ca ।
tattyāgaṃ ca vināśaṃ ca viruddhaṃ hyuttarottaram ।।

bṛhad bimbādyapekṣāyāṃ dravyatyāgaṃ hi nocitam ।
hemādīnāṃ tu dhātūnām utkṛṣṭānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

jāte avayavavaikalye śāntyarthaṃ yāgam ācaret ।
bhūyaḥ saṃpūrya tasyāṅgaṃ viśeṣavidhinābjaja ।।

kevalaṃ hema haimasya yathālābhaṃ kṣate kṣipet ।
sarvaṃ ratnamayaṃ cūrṇaṃ dvādaśākṣaramantritam ।।

etatpūrvaṃ tathā cānyadhātūtthānāṃ mahāmate ।
īṣatsuvarṇamiśreṇa pūrayetsvena dhātunā ।।

yadi vai vidhinānena kriyamāṇena pauṣkara ।
na bhaveccittanairmalyam ācartavyaṃ kriyāntaram ।।

saṃmatena guruṇāṃ ca prāgvad arcanapūrvakam ।
āvīkṣayanti vai sākṣāt nayeccāmūrtatāṃ punaḥ ।।

āpādyam aparaṃ tena bimbadravyeṇa cākṣatam ।
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ manohāri vilakṣaṇam ।।

saṃbhave sati tacchaśvad vinā kālāntareṇa tu ।
yasmāt kamalasaṃbhūta saṃkalpād eva śāśvatam ।।

sthānam āsādayantyāhustasya pūrvapitāmahāḥ ।
prapitāmahapūrvāstu vivadanti parasparam ।।

prāyaśo muktadoṣāstu santānena kṛtā vayam ।
yāsyāmo vāsudevatvaṃ yadi cecchati tatpunaḥ ।।

tataḥ śīghrataraṃ kāryaṃ pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ makhaṃ mahat ।
prītaye cāturātmyānām anūnāṃ tattvavedinām ।।

ṛṣīṇāṃ vibudhānāṃ ca pitṛṇāṃ padmasaṃbhava ।
mānavānāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ trailokyodaravartinām ।।

bhinnāgamotthitād bhagnabimbād dhātumayād dvija ।
kṛtabimbāntaraṃ kuryād evam āmuṣmikādikam ।।

atastadeva vihitaṃ tad bhedaṃ vā tad anvayāt ।
lokadvayodbhavaṃ yena kartāpnoti śubhaṃ mahat ।।

saṃsthitānāṃ svadeśe ca vihitānāṃ dhanādinā ।
dravyapramāṇaṃ kartavyaṃ pūrvair bhedair vibhājitam ।।

yor'the vai bāndhavādīnāṃ kuryādvai pratimāṃ vibhoḥ ।
sarvadoṣavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।

svayaṃvyaktaṃ tathā saiddhaṃ vibudhaiśca pratiṣṭhitam ।
ṛte viprādikairvipra devabimbaṃ niveśitam ।।

vinyastaṃ tatra yanmantram aṅgamantraiḥ salāñchanaiḥ ।
saha prayāti svaṃ sthānaṃ bimbaṃ tyaktvā kriyāṃ vinā ।।

śaptvācāryaṃ tathā kartrā yadarthaṃ ca pratiṣṭhitam ।
piśācabhūtavetālāḥ sayakṣāścaiva rākṣasāḥ ।।

sthānaṃ ca pīṭhaṃ bimbaṃ ca dhvajāntaṃ saṃśrayanti ca ।
evaṃ jñātvā mahābuddhe tathā kāryaṃ śubhepsunā ।।

pratiṣṭhitasya bimbasya yathā saṃpadyate śubham ।
pūjāhomapradānaiśca vāditraiḥ saha gītakaiḥ ।।

svagṛhe calabimbasya puṣpadhūpādikīṃ sthitim ।
sarvakālaṃ yathāśaktyā bhaktaiḥ kāryā śubhāptaye ।।

yāvajjīvāvadhiḥ kālaṃ tattvamantrair adhiṣṭhite ।
traikālyaṃ calabimbe tu mantraṃ mantrī svakaṃ yajet ।।

dvādaśākṣarapūrvaṃ vā sāmānyaṃ guruṇāṃ purā ।
nyastaṃ saṃpratipannānāṃ bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।

saṃhṛtyaivaṃ yathāśāstraṃ bhaktyā bhogaphalāptaye ।
nivedya mātrāsahitaṃ svagurorbhavaśāntaye ।।

tadaṅghrigau karau kṛtvā vijñāpya natamastakaḥ ।
tvayā dehaparityāgakāle yogyasya vā mama ।।

nyastavyaṃ vaiṣṇavaiḥ pūrṇaṃ madanugrahakāmyayā ।
dehasaṃnyāsakāle tu svaśiṣyasyānukampayā ।।

evaṃ hi guruṇā kāryā yogyasyānyasya codanā ।
tenāpyanyasya dehānte saṃyatasya mahāmate ।।

satkriyasya ca bhaktasya tad abhāvānmahāmate ।
sthitirvāyatane vipra vidheyā gṛhamedhinā ।।

asaṃpattestu bhogānām annādyaṃ saṃparityajet ।
vibhorārādhanārthāya śuciḥ snātaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।।

mūrdhni dattvāmbunārghyaṃ prāk sapuṣpaṃ kevalaṃ tu vā ।
ambupūjeyamādyā vai bhogānāṃ mūlameva hi ।।

yato rasamayāḥ sarve tadrasaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।
nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavāṃstadarghyaṃ cottamaṃ smṛtam ।।

pādayostatpunardadyāt bhogajālaṃ yato akhilam ।
svakāraṇapuṭāntastham ānantyam upayāti ca ।।

acirād eva bhaktānāṃ mantriṇāṃ mantrayājinām ।
kṣmānalāmbaravāyavyavibhavenāpi yadyapi ।।

puṣpadhūpādayo bhogā mantrāntāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
tatrāpi rasamūlā vai vyaktisteṣāṃ tadātmikā ।।

sthitamānandabhāvena khādīnāṃ caiva tadrasam ।
sarvaḥ sarvatra vai yena rasiko dṛśyate abjaja ।।

ityevaṃ mānavīyānām arcanāṃ kamalodbhava ।
calānām acalānāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ samudāhṛtam ।।

muktvā dvijendrakarmārcām anyāṃ vai vaiṣṇavīṃ calām ।
nārkarudrendrasaṃsthānāṃ saṃsthānaṃ bhagavadgṛhe ।।

vihitaṃ pratimānāṃ ca pramādajanakaṃ ca tat ।
na mūrtyantaradevānāṃ mūrtayo vyūhalakṣaṇāḥ ।।

bhuvanāntargatāḥ kāryā vidhinā susthireṇa tu ।
prādurbhāvāntarāṇāṃ ca prādurbhāvāstathaiva ca ।।

niṣiddhaṃ bhittigeheṣu uccastheṣu niveśanam ।
devānāṃ bhavanādvāme ucchrāyā[?yā]masamaṃ vinā ।।

yathoktaṃ mukhyakalpād vai hetvapekṣāvaśād bhuvaḥ ।
vyatyayaṃ kartumicchedyaḥ śraddhābhaktipuraḥsaram ।।

pūjāhavanapūrvaṃ ca ājñām ādāya daiśikīm ।
tathaiva ca samūhotthāṃ bhuvanāntaravartinām ।।

surāṇām arcitānāṃ ca kadācinna virodhakṛt ।
anyathā kṣmāmarāṇāṃ ca bhaktibhāgānuvartinām ।।

ādṛṣṭavigrahāṇāṃ ca pīṭhānām aśubhaṃ bhavet ।
evam āyatanasthānāṃ gṛhītāntaravartinām ।।

vibhavavyūhamūrtīnāṃ mantramūrter'cane sati ।
vihitaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca viprādīnām upārjanam ।।

ārādhanārtham ādau tu mantrāntam akhilaṃ tu vai ।
mukhyatvenānukalpe hi yadanyasthaṇḍilādikaiḥ ।।

ūnam aṣṭāṣṭakāccāpi bhogajālād asaṃbhave ।
sarveṣām eva bhogānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kamalo adbhava ।।

ūnādhikaviśālārthā bhagavadyāgalakṣaṇā ।
vidheyā paramā śāntiḥ satataṃ ca śubhārthinā ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

sarvadoṣapraśamanī yathā kāryātha deśikaiḥ ।
śāntirmāntrī parā devī tām ādiśa jagatpate ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

sarvadoṣapraśamanaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।
hitaṃ pūrvoditaṃ cakraṃ paṅkajaṃ veśmavarjitam ।।

yasmādvā sthāpya pīṭhaṃ ca viṣvaksenāntam arcanam ।
nopuyajyati vai tatra ṛte sarveśvarārcanāt ।।

vyatiriktā nirāśānām ambarasthāmbareṣu ca ।
vidhijñena sthitiḥ kāryā ṛgvidarcāpayet tataḥ ।।

pīṭham aśrānvitaṃ kṛtvā puraṃ tvācaraṇānvitam ।
tatra pūrvoditanyāsaṃ kuryād ādhārapūrvakam ।।

svadehavat tamālakṣya smṛtvādhyakṣaprakāśitam ।
tad vācakena mūrtestu citsāmānyena sāṃpratam ।।

yatheha ca savedyādi smṛtvā yuktasvavigrahe ।
na hi sāṃkaryadoṣo asti adhyakṣādhiṣṭhite sati ।।

tathaivādhāraśaktyādi viṣvaksenāntam arcanam ।
nirdeṣaṃ maṇḍale kintu bhagavacchabdapūrvakam ।।

sarvasya nāma coccārya tadante tvātmane namaḥ ।
evam āsanadevānāṃ dharmādīnāṃ samarcanam ।।

sthānabhedasthitānāṃ ca kṛtvā tadanu pauṣkara ।
maṇḍale mantramūrtīnām āhūtānāṃ samarcanam ।।

saṃpūrṇaṃ śāntaye tatsyād asaṃpūrṇam aśāntaye ।
ataḥ svaśaktyā śāntyarthe sadānaṃ vahnitarpaṇam ।।

bhagavadyāgapūrvaṃ tu sarvatra vihitaṃ sadā ।
tacca jñānānuviddhena karmaṇārghyādikaiḥ saha ।।

samyaktato da yīṃ jñātvā sadravyaṃ saṃsthitaṃ śubham ।
yathā bījāṅkurābhyāṃ tu ananyatvamanādimat ।।

phalāptaye phalepsūnāṃ jagatyasmiṃstathābjaja ।
anyonyānugatatvaṃ hi saṃsthitaṃ jñānakarmaṇoḥ ।।

jñātavyam avivekācca budhyā tu suviśuddhayā ।
bhagavadvāsudevākhyaparasya paramātmanaḥ ।।

anugrahārtham ullāsaṃ jñānakarmasamanvitam ।
mantramudrāsametaṃ ca karmiṇām anukampayā ।।

tattvaśaktisamopetaṃ jñānādyairanvitaṃ guṇaiḥ ।
aṇimādyaṣṭakenāpi siddhibījena vai saha ।।

śāntaye sarvadoṣāṇāṃ śaśvat parapadāptaye ।
parameśvarollāsaḥ pārameśvaram ullāsam ityabhinnaṃ dvijottama ।
parijñeyaṃ yathā vahnernirdhūmasyārciṣaḥ śubhāḥ ।।

samudrasyormayo yadvad raśmayo bhāskarasya ca ।
saṃkalpād bhaktipūrvāt tu sūryavaddhṛdayāmbuje ।।

karoti nityam udayaṃ bhavyabuddheḥ mahāmahe ।
saṃkalpalakṣaṇair bhogair makhairiṣṭvā tu pūrvavat ।।

bahiḥ śubhataraiḥ paścāt bhogair ājyādikaistataḥ ।
tarpitaścānalādhāre yathoktavidhinābjaja ।।

deśikadvijamūrtiśca sānnapānadhanādinā ।
paritoṣaṃ paraṃ nītaṃ śāntiṃ yacchati vai para m ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

karmaṇāṃ śāntikādīnām ādhāre maṇḍalādike ।
dhyātam asya jagaddhātur jñātum icchāmyahaṃ prabho ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

vyaktiḥ saṃpūjyate yā yā jñānādyaiḥ sā guṇair yutā ।
jñātavyā kamalodbhūta nityā sarvātmanā vibhoḥ ।।

saṃsāraduḥkhaśāntyarthaṃ tajjā vā sā suśāntaye ।
saṃyajed gocarīkṛtya bhaktyā suśraddhayā tu vai ।।

vācakair dvādaśārṇādyaiḥ śaśvaccābhimatāptaye ।
vicitrākṛtir astrāṅgavastrasragbhūṣaṇādikaiḥ ।।

śaktipūtaiḥ susaṃpūrṇā tathānyaiḥ sādhanaiḥ svakaiḥ ।
śuddhasaṃvinmayaṃ tvevaṃ vyaktavigraham ācyutam ।।

pauruṣeṇa tu rūpeṇa smartavyaṃ satpadāptaye ।
vapuṣā sundareṇaiva divyenāvikṛtena ca ।।

muñcantam aniśaṃ dehād ālokaṃ jñānalakṣaṇam ।
prayatnena vinā jñānaṃ nyāsakṛd dhyāyināṃ mahat ।।

sragvastrābharaṇair yuktaṃ svānurūpair anūpamaiḥ ।
cinmayaiḥ svaprakāśaistu anyonyarucirañjitaiḥ ।।

pūrvakarmānalārtānāṃdhyāyināṃ svedaśāntaye ।
svadattenducayotthena hlādeyad gogaṇena tu ।।

vidyākalābhidhe śaktī saṃdhatte śaṅkhacakravat ।
jñānakriyātmake viddhi icchāsaṃvalite abjaja ।।

anantaśaktir bhagavāṃstam anantaguṇaṃ smṛtam ।
dṛśyadṛṣṭāntasūryenduvahnitattvair vilakṣaṇam ।।

svabodhapratyayenaiva iyattāsya vidhīyate ।
sarvam evaiṣa bhagavān kimu sarvam ataḥ param ।।

dhyeyam asya yadā bhāti sā vidyā svātmani sthitā ।
bhaktyā yathocitadhyānād etasmād eva śāntaye ।।

evam asya paraṃ rūpaṃ paramaṃ vinibodhatu ।
dhyāyināṃ bhavyabuddhīnāṃ paramānandadaṃ hi yat ।।

dhanukuñcitanīlāliga litāñjanasannibhaiḥ ।
karpūradhūsarairdivyaiḥ puṣpasaṃvalitāntaraiḥ ।।

kirīṭamakuṭākrāntaiḥ śobhitaṃ suśiroruhaiḥ ।
sthalābjakāśasaṃkāśapadmarāgaruciprabhaiḥ ।।

pāṇipādatalai raktairvadanair adharādikaiḥ ।
nāsāśravaṇarandhrāntair muktābhāsādikair dvijaiḥ ।।

īṣadāraktagokṣīraśuddhanīlābjalocanaiḥ ।
evaṃ hṛtpuṇḍarīke prāk puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam ।।

nānāmantraprabhākāntidhyānam icchāpradaṃ bhavet ।
bahirvai maṇḍale dhyānaṃ bhavaduḥkhaṃ nayet kṣayam ।।

parasmād bhagavattattvād ananyatvena vartate ।
atra sthitaṃ bahirjñeyaṃ mantravyūhaṃ sadoditam ।।

nānāvyaktisvarūpeṇa bhavināṃ mokṣadaṃ hi yat ।
tatra tāvat parijñeyā kramaśo vai puroditāḥ ।।

nirdiṣṭalakṣaṇā brahman varāhādyāstu śaktayaḥ ।
tāsāṃ vyaktaṃ kramād dhyānaṃ yathāvat prāk prakāśitam ।।

parasya brahmaṇastvevaṃ nityā vā vyāpakāmalā ।
mūrtirvai vāsudevākhyā tvabhedena sthitābjaja ।।

jvālā jyotstnā prabhā yadvat vahner indor vivasvataḥ ।
svecchayā yo abhimānākhyarūpaṃ dhatte yathoditam ।।

anugrahārtham evaṃ vai bhagavanmantraśaktayaḥ ।
vyayañjayanti svakaṃ rūpam ābhimānikam uttamam ।।

yamālambyācireṇaiva japād dhyānāt samarcanāt ।
sarvam āpnoti mantrajñaḥ tava bhaktipradaḥ sthitaḥ ।।

sāhajaṃ prākṛtaṃ karmabandhaṃ karmātmajaṃ hi yat ।
saṃsthitaṃ hi yathā tāmraṃ dhātorabjaja kālikam ।।

bhūtvā sarvajñaśaktiḥ sā svayaṃ mantratarātmanā ।
kramāt karmātmatattvānām anuvedhaṃ karoti ca ।।

bhaktiyuktam asaṃbādhaṃ śaśvad ye cāpnuvanti te ।
pibanti paramaṃ brahma īśaṃ mantrātmanāptaye ।।

labdhādhikārāḥ kramaśaḥ saṃprāpya sveśvare pade ।
prayānti mantrasāmarthyād yasmānnāyānti te punaḥ ।।

jñātvaivaṃ kamalodbhūta dhyeyāḥ pūjyāstathaiva hi ।
ye pradhānatarā mantrā mūrtayo api jagatprabhoḥ ।।

ārādhanājjapād dhyānāt parijñānācca te śubham ।
yacchanti padam ātmīyaṃ tat tad akṣayam ācyutam ।।

dahanti vahnivat karmajālaṃ karmātmanāṃ mahat ।
evaṃ jñātvābjasaṃbhūta suprasiddhaistu vācakaiḥ ।।

dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu ṣaḍaṣṭākṣarapaścimaiḥ ।
svasaṃjñākhyaiḥ svabījairvā saṃprāptair deśikānanāt ।।

smartavyā vāsudevākhyā dvibhedāḥ parameśvarāḥ ।
catvāraścāniruddhāntāścaturvyūhavyavasthayā ।।

evam anye varāhādyāścaturvyūhena vai saha ।
tathaiva keśavādyā ye dvādaśāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ ।।

anujjhitasvarūpasya nānāmūrtiyutasya ca ।
nānāvyatyayasaṃsthasya yajanaṃ caturātmanaḥ ।।

yat tu nānārthasiddhyarthaṃ tathā ruciguṇāptaye ।
samyag jñātvā tu ṣāḍguṇyaṃ mahimā śāntatā parā ।।

prāptum icchati yacchīghraṃ dhīmatā tena pauṣkara ।
pūjanīyaṃ yathāvastham adhyakṣāntaṃ hi kevalam ।।

prāgvadvibhavamūrtīnāṃ pañca vyūhādyapekṣayā ।
aiśvaryapūrvaṣāḍguṇyaṃ cāturātmyādyam icchati ।।

sapradyumnācyutādhyakṣavāsudevādyam arcayet ।
yaḥ punarmūrtipūrvaṃ tu icched guṇagaṇaṃ mahat ।।

saṃkalpasiddhayaḥ sarvā vividhāścāṇimādayaḥ ।
sarveśvaro anugantavya adhyakṣāntaṃ tu sācyutam ।।

pradyumnāntaṃ tu satataṃ samādhāvarcane hitam ।
mukhyatvena tu vai yasya calādyaṃ guṇasaṃgraham ।।

pratibhāti gurorvaktraṃ dhīraṃ tasyārcane punaḥ ।
vāsudevācyutādhyakṣakramaṃ pradyumnapaścimam ।।

ṣaṭkaṃ tu vīryapūrvaṃ vai icchatyārādhanāttu yaḥ ।
apradyumnaṃ tam adhyakṣamacyutaṃ saṃyajettadā ।।

tejaḥpūrvaṃ tu ṣāḍguṇyaṃ yor'canād abhivāñchati ।
tasyārcane tu vihitaṃ bhūyo adhyakṣādikaṃ trayam ।।

prāgarcanāttu mūrtīnāṃ kevalād arcanāt tu vā ।
kaivalyaṃ bhagavattattvaṃ mantrajñaḥ samavāpnuyāt ।।

mūrtitrayaṃ tadante yat sarvagaṃ yadyapi sthitam ।
tathāpi viśvavibhavaṃ yatsatyaṃ tvātmanā prabhuḥ ।।

jñātvaivam arcanīyaṃ tu tameva samanantaram ।
jāgrad īśvaram adhyakṣaṃ tvayā nāthātmanā saha ।।

trayāṇām acyutādīnāṃ prāthamyena tu pūjanāt ।
tatpadeṣvādidevasya kramād ārādhayet trayam ।।

cāturātmīyayogena guṇānām evam arcanam ।
kuryād vai vidhivanmantrī yathā tadavadhāraya ।।

jñānaṃ balamathaiśvaryaṃ vīryaṃ ca tadanantaram ।
catuṣṭayam idaṃ bhinnaṃ yajanāt siddhikṛt sakṛt ।।

balam aiśvaryavīrye ca tejoniṣṭhaṃ catuṣṭayam ।
yaṃ ya icchatyabhimataṃ parijñānād avāpnuyāt ।।

tejaḥ śaktistathā jñānaṃ balaṃ vīryāntam eva hi ।
iṣṭaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ dadyāt mantriṇām idam abjaja ।।

jñānātmane samuccārya praṇavādyaṃ padaṃ śubham ।
yathā jñānaguṇasyoktaṃ sarveṣām evameva hi ।।

anujjhitakrameṇaiva vyatyayenoditena ca ।
mokṣabhogāptaye tvevam arcanaṃ vividhaṃ smṛtam ।।

bhedabhinnaṃ jagadyoner abhedena yajet punaḥ ।
dvādaśāre mahācakre tathāsaṃkhyacchadodare ।।

guṇātītastu bhagavān pūrvavat kaṇikāntare ।
dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa patragaṃ hi tadakṣaraiḥ ।।

namaḥ praṇavasaṃruddhaiḥ prādakṣiṇyena prāk padāt ।
prāptaye guṇabhūtānāṃ ṣaṭkayuktaṃ hi yacca te ।।

divyānāṃ cāturātmyānāṃ trayaṃ saṃcaritaṃ hi yat ।
trayaṃ guṇamayaṃ cānyat cākārāṇāṃ kramād yajet ।।

upāyaistaiḥ phalaprāptyai tasmād yaṣṭavyam icchayā ।
bhaktiśraddhāsametena jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā ।।

svavarṇāśramadharmeṇa saha samyak samādhinā ।
ā anugrahakālācca yāvajjīvāvadhi dvija ।।

tīvraprabhāvaśāntācca jñānam ārādhanena ca ।
dehenānena tenaiva hyanenānyatareṇa vā ।।

mandamandavaśād bhāvavaśād amarapūjitaḥ ।
evaṃ yad adhikāreṇa kuryād ārādhanaṃ hi yaḥ ।।

bhogairyathoditaiḥ śuddhaiḥ kriyābhirvividhaistataḥ ।
niṣpattau tu kriyāṅgānāṃ hṛdāstrārghyaṃ svamantrarāṭ ।।

nānarcitaṃ vibhorbhogaṃ kalpitaṃ vinivedya ca ।
praṇavādyantakenaiva sanamaskapadena tu ।।

kalpayāmīti nāmnā tad bhogānāṃ vidhyupārjanam ।
dhiyā nivedanaṃ teṣāṃ śirasāvanatena yat ।।

samarpaṇe yad vijñeyaṃ vācakena hṛdeśvarāt ।
pūrakeṇa hṛtānāṃ prāk bahiḥsthānāṃ krameṇa tu ।।

hṛdayaṅgamasaṃjñaṃ yat pañcakaṃ tvarhaṇādikam ।
kṛtam añjalimudrāyāṃ śraddhāpūtena cetasā ।।

nivedanīyaṃ bahudhā yathāsaṃbhavameva vā ।
paramāśritya vai yattu indriyaiḥ saṃyataiḥ saha ।।

vadanaṃ nāsikārandhre sthagayitvāmbareṇa tu ।
svaśvāsopahataṃ caiva na bhavet tad yathābjaja ।।

subharjitānāṃ bījānāṃ prasavaṃ na punaryathā ।
kriyāphalānāṃ ca tathā prathamaṃ cācyutārcanāt ।।

āstāṃ tāvanmahābuddhe karmasaṃjñaṃ hitāccayutam ।
phalahīnaṃ hi cāmūlād bhavakṣayakaraṃ param ।।

aśvamedhādayo yajñā nūnaṃ karmaphalapradāḥ ।
te api sanmantrabhaktānāṃ na yacchanti phalaṃ svakam ।।

jñasvabhāvāstu vai yajñāḥ samyagbudhvā parāśayam ।
yachanti paramāṃ śāntiṃ bhagavattattvavedinām ।।

svargādyaṃ phalamanyeṣāṃ martyabhogaṃ tu vepsitam ।
phalam āmuṣmikaṃ caiva aihikaṃ vābjasaṃbhava ।।

kṛtvā buddhiniviṣṭaṃ tu japādīn śraddhayā caret ।
bhaktipūtena viprendra tātparyeṇa tu vai saha ।।

sāṅgaṃ saparivāraṃ ca iṣṭvaivam ajam avyayam ।
śaktivyaktivibhedena ādimūrtikramāttu vai ।।

ṛṅmayenātha yajuṣā pūjanīyaṃ tameva hi ।
acirākhye pade mantre tantrair abhimatāptaye ।।

paraṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma pavitraṃ paramaiśvaram ।
sāmarthyād acyutaṃ netrā nāmnā yatsamudāhṛtam ।।

vyaktam asya parabrahma kvacinnayanalakṣaṇam ।
antarnigūḍhamantrāṇāṃ vartate anyatra vai bahiḥ ।।

ata eva ṣaḍaṅgāni pañcāṅgāni mahāmate ।
vācakāni tu vācyāni yuktānyārādhanāttu vai ।।

netrākhyaṃ bhagavattattvaṃ yadaṅgebhyo atiricyate ।
śiro ambare tu mantrāṇāṃ pradhānetaravartinām ।।

svabījaṃ viniyoktavyaṃ sthityarthaṃ prāk prabhātmakam ।
parāvarasvarūpeṇa smaret tatsthaṃ digīśvaram ।।

audayena tu yogena mantrāṇi ca parāt padāt ।
yathākramasthānyāhūya arcanāvasaraṃ prati ।।

niveśya ca yathāśāstram astrāvaraṇapaścimam ।
saṃpanne vidhivad yāge punaḥ sarveśvare harau ।।

kramāt pravilayaṃ kuryāt sādhakaḥ siddhim icchatām ।
evaṃ niyantṛśaktir vai netrākhyā pārameśvarī ।।

prabhā vatvena mantrāṇām apyayatvena vartate ।
bahirvā kamale hārde smartavyā sāmalāntare ।।

niṣedhākhyena bījena sānusvāreṇa svenaṃ ca ।
sahasrānalasūryenduvarāhāyutabhāsvarā ।।

vācyavācakayogena mānanīyaṃ sadaiva hi ।
sahasṛṣṭisvareṇaiva sṛṣṭau sarvaṃ yad īpsitam ।।

bhogabījam akhaṇḍaṃ ca pratīpaṃ mantriṇāṃ punaḥ ।
śaśvad ajñānānusiddhaṃ ca saṃprayacchati pūjanāt ।।

nityamantropasaṃhāravelāyām udaye api ca ।
yathāvad ādau boddhavyaṃ kramān mantraṃ yathāsthitam ।।

bījaṃ piṇḍaṃ padākhyaṃ ca tathā mantraṃ salakṣaṇam ।
bhedam etaddhi mantrāṇāṃ phalaṃ bhedena cānvitam ।।

nānāvācyasvarūpeṇa yataḥ sarveśvaraḥ sthitaḥ ।
catuṣprakārair amalairvācakair upacaryate ।।

vācakānāṃ hi vācyānām evamasti parasparam ।
āpekṣikaṃ vaiśvarūpyaṃ saṃsiddhe niyame sati ।।

vinā piṇḍākṣarairbrahman saṃjñākhyaiḥ padalakṣaṇaiḥ ।
svakairbījākṣaraiḥ kuryād vācyasya parikalpanam ।।

sopāṅgānāṃ tu cāṅgānāṃ dvādaśānāṃ svasaṃjñayā ।
kevalānāṃ tu ṣaṇṇāṃ vai pañcānām api cecchayā ।।

te anusvārayutāḥ sarve kāryāḥ praṇavamadhyagāḥ ।
nyāsātmavān manomūrteḥ sāmānyārādhane param ।।

karmānurūpamante tu namaskārādikaṃ nyaset ।
tathā phalābhisandhāne namaskāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

saṃprāptau tvaṇimādīnāṃ svāhākāram udīrayet ।
āpyāyane tu vai vauṣaṭ sarvatra kamalodbhava ।।

vaśyārthe cāpi vidveṣe duṣṭoccāṭanakarmaṇi ।
huṃphaṭkāraṃ ca vihitam anyonyaprītaye vaṣaṭ ।।

tṛptyarthe balidāne ca tejaso hyabhivṛddhaye ।
ṛte sapraṇavād vipra namaskārapadāt tu vai ।।

mantrāṇāṃ karmasaṃnyāsakartṝṇāṃ jātayo aparāḥ ।
niṣiddhāstatphalopetāstathā siddhāntināṃ nṛṇām ।।

mantrasiddhāntavetṝṇāṃ mantrajñānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
tathā tantrāntarajñānāṃ mantriṇāṃ kamalodbhava ।।

saha jātigaṇenaiva vidhinā mantrasiddhayaḥ ।
phalārthinām anujñātāḥ kāmabhogaratātmanām ।।

prakṛtipratyayādhīnā mālāmantrādikāstu ye ।
śrutimantraiḥ samopetāstutimantrāśca ye smṛtāḥ ।।

āvarjayanti tajjñānāṃ satataṃ cittam abjaja ।
natinaḥ praṇavādyā ye tyāgapiṇḍaṃ tathābjaja ।।

mantrāṇāṃ vividhārthānāṃ teṣāṃ vai pārameśvarī ।
śaktirnityoditā sūkṣmā sattākhyā jñānalakṣaṇā ।।

āviśvasādhanaṃ kāryā teṣām icchā kriyābjaja ।
vikāsayati sad vipra pradāne muktaye api ca ।।

bhaktikriyāparāṇāṃ ca hitārthaṃ nityasevinām ।
vidvān yathoktanītyā tu oṣadhyo mūlam ūrdhvagāḥ ।।

dagdhāgnināpi kurvanti samyagjñātakriye bhuvi ।
kiṃ punastvāgamajñaistu bhaktyā tu vidhipūrvakam ।।

upadeṣṭā prabuddhānāṃ kurvanti ca manohitam ।
teṣāṃ gantā rahaḥ sarvaṃ baddhādyaṃ śabdaḍambaram ।।

hitaṃ yat padamantrāṇāṃ samāśrityānupūrvakam ।

pauṣkara uvāca 

jñātum icchāmi bhagavan kālabhedena vai saha ।
svarūpaṃ mantrasiddhānām āgamānāṃ yathāsthitam ।।

kālabhedaḥ 

śrībhagavānuvāca 

kālam ekaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha tad vyāpāravaśāt punaḥ ।
bhinnamābhāti kartṝṇāṃ bhagavadbhāvināṃ tu vai ।।

nāḍikākalitaṃ yad vai ahorātraṃ tu ṣaḍṛtu ।
pañcadhā viṣamāṃśaistad āprabhātād vibhajya ca ।।

brāhmaṃ muhūrtam āsādya mantrajñaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ ।
śodhayitvā svakaṃ deham āyāmādyair yathoditaiḥ ।।

mantravinyastadehotthaṃ kuryān mantrārcanaṃ tataḥ ।
japastotrāvasānaṃ ca yāvad ādityadarśanam ।।

kuryād bhogārcanaṃ paścāt puṣpamūlaphalādikam ।
gate dināṣṭame bhāge snānapūrvaṃ samācaret ।।

prāgvadārādhanaṃ mantraṃ tṛtīyapraharāvadhi ।
tataścaturthaprahare śāstrādhyayanam ācaret ।।

cintanaṃ śravaṇopetaṃ vyākhyānaṃ svadhiyecchayā ।
astaṃgate dinakare āsādyārādhanālayam ।।

kuryānmantrārcanaṃ samyagjapadhyānasamanvitam ।
āsādya śayanaṃ paścāt smarenmantreśvaraṃ hṛdi ।।

kṣapayitvā niśāṃśaṃ tu utthāya śayanāt tataḥ ।
yogaṃ yuñjīta vai māntraṃ prāgvaddhṛtkamalodare ।।

talpam āsādya vai bhūyaḥ prabuddhaḥ kamalodbhava ।
utthāya śayanaṃ tyaktvā tataḥ pūrvoktam ācaret ।।

kālabhedam imaṃ viddhi śāstrabhedam athocyate ।
kartavyatvena vai yatra cāturātmyam upāsyate ।।

kramāgataiḥ svasaṃjñābhibrāhmaṇair āgamaṃ tu tat ।
viddhi siddhāntasaṃjñaṃ ca tatpūrvam atha pauṣkara ।।

nānāvyūhasametaṃ ca mūrtidvādaśakaṃ hi yat ।
tathā mūrtyantarayutaṃ prādurbhāvagaṇaṃ tu vai ।।

prādurbhāvāntarayutaṃ dhṛ taṃ hṛtpadmapūrvakam ।
lakṣmyādiśaṅkhacakrākhyagārutmyasadigīśvaraiḥ ।।

sagaṇair astraniṣṭhaistu taṃ viddhi kamalodbhava ।
mantrasiddhāntasaṃjñaṃ ca śāstraṃ sarvaphalapradam ।।

vinā mūrticatuṣkeṇa yatrānyad upacaryate ।
mantreṇa bhagavad rūpaṃ kevalaṃ yāgasaṃyutam ।।

yuktaṃ śriyādikenaiva kāntāvyūhena pauṣkara ।
bhinnair ābharaṇair astrair āvṛtaṃ ca savigrahaiḥ ।।

tantrasiddhāntasaṃjñaṃ tacchāstraṃ bhogāpavargadam ।
mukhyānuvṛttibhedena yatra siṃhādayastu vai ।।

catustridvayādikenaiva yogenābhyarcite tu vai ।
saṃvṛtāḥ parivāreṇa svena svenānvitāstu vā ।।

yacchaktyārādhitaṃ sarvaṃ viddhi tantrāntaraṃ tu tat ।
evaṃ nānāgamānāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ viddhi sarvadā ।।

nāmadvayaṃ ca siddhāntaṃ pañcarātreti pauṣkara ।
ekaikaṃ bahubhirbhedair āmūlādeva saṃsthitam ।।

nānāśayavaśenaiva siddhādyaiḥ prakaṭīkṛtam ।
saṃkṣiptaṃ saprapañcaṃ ca tṛtīyam ubhayātmakam ।।

setihāsapurāṇaistu vedair vedāntasaṃyutaiḥ ।
ye janmakoṭibhiḥ siddhāsteṣām anto atra vai smṛtaḥ ।।

tasmāt samyak paraṃ brahma vāsudevākhyam avyayam ।
etasmāt prāpyate śāstrād jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā ।।

siddhāntasaṃjñā viprāsya sārthakā ata eva hi ।
purāṇaṃ vedavedāntaṃ tathānyatsāṅkhyayogajam ।।

pañcaprakāraṃ vijñeyaṃ yatra rātryāyate abjaja ।
phalotkarṣavaśenaiva pañcarātramiti smṛtam ।।

sadāgamākhyaṃ mūlaṃ tu parabrahmaprakāśakam ।
divyasiddhipradaṃ caiva śāntikṛd vighnakarmaṇām ।।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ adhikāranirūpaṇaṃ nāma aṣṭātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha ekonacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pauṣkara uvāca 

pramāṇam āgamānāṃ ca sasaṃjñaṃ parameśvara ।
jñātumicchāmyahaṃ śaśvat saṃbandhaṃ vibudhādikam ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

saṃkṣiptaṃ triprakāraṃ ca kanīyomadhyamottamam ।
anuṣṭup chandobandhena baddhaṃ ślokaśatāt tu yat ।।

pādasaṃjñaṃ hi tacchāstraṃ mūlākhyaṃ dviguṇaṃ ca tat ।
yat sārdhaṃ śatasaṃkhyaṃ tu taduddhāram iti smṛtam ।।

nyūnabhedāstrayastvete ūnādhikyena vai saha ।
bahudhā cāpi sarveṣāṃ na saṃjñā calate punaḥ ।।

sārdhaṃ śatadvayaṃ yad vai parijñeyaṃ taduttaram ।
bṛhaduttarasaṃjñaṃ ca yad etad dviguṇaṃ bhavet ।।

sārdhaṃ sahasrasaṃkhyaṃ tu kalpaṃ tat samudāhṛtam ।
trayasyāsya parijñeyam ūnādhikyaṃ punaḥ śataiḥ ।।

evaṃ saṃjñāntarāstvanye āgamāḥ santyanekaśaḥ ।
kalpaikadeśāste sarve parijñeyāstathābjaja ।।

ā sahasratrayāt sārdhāt ṣaṭsahastraṃ hi sottaram ।
dviṣaṭsahasraparyantaṃ saṃhitākhyaṃ tadāgamam ।।

ye cānye cāntarālaṃ vai śāstrārthenādhikaiḥ śataiḥ ।
sarveṣāṃ saṃhitāsaṃjñā boddhavyā kamalodbhava ।।

sapādalakṣaparyantā ye ca śāstrāṇyatordhvataḥ ।
sahasraśatamānena ādhikyena prakāśitāḥ ।।

kalpaskandhāt tu te sarve parijñeyāḥ krameṇa tu ।
lakṣādhikaistu bahubhiḥ sahasraistu śatānvitaiḥ ।।

sārdhakoṭitrayāntaṃ ca tacca tantrākhyam āgamam ।
navaprakāramityetad bhedamuktaṃ trayasya ca ।।

yatrāntarālasaṃkhyānām asaṃkhyeyaṃ pravartate ।
yugānusārabodhena traiguṇyavalitena ca ।।

divyādyavāntarāntena saṃbandhena ca bhūriṇā ।
aprameyābhidhānaṃ ca ata ūrdhvaṃ samāgamaḥ ।।

kālena saha niryāntam asaṃkhyaṃ parameśvarāt ।
tad vai viditavedyānāṃ siddhānāṃ saṃsthitaṃ hṛdi ।।

yaiḥ svabodhapramāṇena koṭisaṃkhyaṃ prakāśitam ।
pādāntā yasya vai bhedāḥ kramaśaḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ।।

yatra yatrecchayā jātaṃ matabhedena vai saha ।
kriyāntarāśca bahavaḥ śuddhā rājasa-tāmasāḥ ।।

ādyaṃ sarvāgamānāṃ ca pārameśvaram āgamam ।
pramāṇapariśuddhaṃ ca hitam abjaja sātvatam ।।

siddhānte bhagavat tattvavedinaḥ paramārthataḥ ।
kramāgataśca taiḥ prāptaṃ muktaye bhavināṃ tu vai ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

vibhoḥ sarveśvarādyena svīkṛtaṃ pārameśvaram ।
aprameyaṃ mahat śāstram anantaṃ gaganopamam ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

sarveśvarasya ca vibhor avyayasyācyutasya ca ।
vācyasya vāsudevasya aprameyākhyam āgamam ।।

apṛthaglakṣaṇaṃ viddhi svasya śabdaṃ yathā dvija ।
jñānātmasaṃjñam ātmānaṃ nītaṃ vai svecchayā dvija ।।

svabhāvamāptakāmasya tasyaitat svavaśasya ca ।
jñānāṃśenābhimānākhyaṃ guṇaśaktimayaṃ mahat ।।

gṛhītasvayam ātmānam atīndriyam anaśvaram ।
śabdamūrtiḥ sa bhagavān svecchayā svayametya ca ।।

viśrāntaṃ jñānamūrtau tu sa ca saṃkarṣaṇo vibhuḥ ।
svayaṃ vīryam anantaṃ ca mūrchitaṃ jñānamūrtinā ।।

guṇaṃ śaktimayaṃ yasya prakāśākhyaṃ tu vigraham ।
ābhimānikam akṣobhyaṃ pradyumnākhyaṃ tu śāśvatam ।।

mahatā tena bhūtena śāstraṃ vidyutprabhojvalam ।
śvasitaṃ vīryamūrtistu praviṣṭaḥ svayameva hi ।।

atha vīryātmanā vipra prasaraṃ taijasaṃ mahat ।
janitaṃ cāniruddheti dhatte yo anaśvaraṃ vapuḥ ।।

guṇaśaktiguṇopetam aparājitam akṣayam ।
tyaktam udgāravat śāstraṃ pradyumnena mahātmanā ।।

ādāya vidhṛtaṃ tad vai aniruddhātmanā hṛdi ।
guṇavyaktimayaṃ devaṃ vāgīśam asṛjat prabhuḥ ।।

aniruddho avyayātmā ca arthayugmaṃ tadāgamam ।
anuddhṛtam asandigdhaṃ gataṃ cāvyayatāṃ tataḥ ।।

yadaṃśād viditaṃ tad vai jñānamūrte svavigrahe ।
avyayīkṛtamādye tu svarūpaṃ jñānamūrtinā ।।

nītaṃ samarasatvaṃ ca pratiśāstre prakāśite ।
vāgīśvarācca siddhānāṃ tairuddhṛtya yathoditam ।।

samyak samuccayīkṛtya navanītaṃ yatho dadheḥ ।
vibhorvidyādhidevasya brahmaṇo asya prakāśitam ।।

rudrādityendrapūrvāṇāṃ devānāṃ coditairdvija ।
svāṃśotthānāṃ ca rudrādyaiḥ svāṃśotthairarthināmapi ।।

brahmaṇā nāradādīnāṃ svasutānāṃ prakāśitam ।
tebhyo lokatrayāntasthaṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

svābhiprāyavaśenaiva nānākālavaśād api ।
nānādeśavaśāccaiva nānājātivaśād api ।।

ityetat śāstrasaṃbandhaṃ kathitaṃ te yathāsthitam ।
sarahasyaṃ mahābuddhe boddhavyaṃ hi yathārthataḥ ।।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ āgamanirṇayo nāma ekonacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha catvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pauṣkara uvāca 

parijñātaṃ mayā deva doṣopaśamanaṃ mahat ।
śāntikaṃ paramaṃ yad vai vyatyayāt saumanasyakṛt ।।

śāstrasaṃbandhaparyantaṃ prasaṅgāt tvadanugrahāt ।
nānādharmapratiṣṭhā ca bhavināṃ svargadā ca yā ।।

idānīṃ jñātum icchāmi tvattaḥ saṃkṣepatastataḥ ।
sarahasyaṃ jagadyoneḥ pratimālakṣaṇādikam ।।

saṃvidhānaṃ pratiṣṭhākhyam aśeṣaṃ pūrvacoditam ।
kṣatadoṣāstu yer'cānāṃ madhūcchiṣṭoditāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

tāstvayoktāḥ purā deva mānonmānādikairvinā ।
āmūrdhadeśakeśīyaṃ caraṇāntaṃ hi lakṣaṇam ।।

mayā yathāvanna jñātaṃ naipuṇyena jagatpate ।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ purā kṛtvā tu pauṣkara ।
mokṣārtham ācarecchuddhāṃ pratiṣṭhām ācyutīṃ parām ।।

sulakṣaṇe tu bhūbhāge gavyair bhaktena vai purā ।
prāgdiksiddhisametaṃ tu vasudhālakṣaṇaṃ ca te ।।

sphuṭam uktaṃ pratiṣṭhārthaṃ vijñātavyaṃ tad eva hi ।
jalāśrayādikā yā bhūrvividhaiśca vibhūṣitā ।।

vanaughavanasaṃyuktair grāmaiḥ saha purādikaiḥ ।
pratigrahaṃ pratiṣṭhārthaṃ pūrvavad vidhipūrvakam ।।

saṃpādya kusumārāmaparyantaṃ ca suvistaram ।
uttamaṃ vanayātrāntaṃ tataḥ kuryāt sadeśikaḥ ।।

horādyena ca lagnena muhūrtenārcitena ca ।
śakune gāgane bhaume cittasaukhyaprade śubhe ।।

kiñcid adhvāvaśiṣṭe tu vastavyaṃ ca vanād bahiḥ ।
śubhe grahe anukūle ca nakṣatre vāsare api ca ।।

kuryād vanapraveśaṃ ca tatreṣṭā vanadevatāḥ ।
ādāya lakṣaṇopetam upalaṃ vai sitādikam ।।

susnigdhaṃ susvanaṃ śuddhaṃ doṣairhīnaṃ sphuṭādikaiḥ ।
vṛkṣaṃ vā lakṣaṇopetam akṣataṃ saralaṃ dṛḍham ।।

phalaṃ puṣpapradaṃ sthūlaṃ sakṣīraṃ vā tadujjhitam ।
nānājāti ca karmaṇyaṃ yajñāṅgānāṃ guṇāvaham ।।

sattvādyaṃ tad adhiṣṭhātṛbalidānapuraḥsaram ।
kṛtvā visarjanaṃ caiva madhvājyāktena deśikaḥ ।।

śastreṇa praharaṃ dadyācchetavyaṃ śilpinā tataḥ ।
candanaṃ syandanaṃ tatra tathā surabhicandanam ।।

agaru karṇikāraṃ ca kāśmaryaṃ raktacandanam ।
bilvāmalakacūtāśca tālavarṇakasiṃhakāḥ ।।

śrīparṇī nālikeraṃ ca nāgamātṛkapīnakam ।
gavyaṃ kapitthaṃ ca tathā hima-tālatamālakam ।।

badaraṃ khadiraṃ phalgu madhūkaṃ kiṃśukadrumam ।
phālavetaṃ ca kharjūraṃ nīpanāraṅgaśiśupam ।।

pippalaṃ vṛkṣam aśvatthaṃ pippalīviṭapaṃ mahat ।
suradāru harītakyaṃ bakulaṃ cāpyudumbaram ।।

kālākhyaṃ puṣpakūlaṃ ca vairaṃ cānyat phaladrumam ।
phālāsyaṃ bhūrjavṛkṣaṃ ca palāśaṃ kṛtamardakam ।।

tindukaṃ bījasāraṃ ca mātuluṅgadrumaṃ mahat ।
rājavṛkṣaṃ kohitakaṃ sunābhikuṭakārjunam ।।

saralaṃ kuṭajaḥ śākaḥ śamīśrīveṣṭaketakāḥ ।
asanaspandanākhyaṃ ca stabachastabaketi ca ।।

sāravanto makhīyā ye susiddhā lokapūjitāḥ ।
grāhyāstarūttamāḥ sarve karmaṇi sthāpanādike ।।

ekaikatālavṛddhyā tu dvādaśāntakarāvadhi ।
dviraṣṭakaṃ tu bimbānām evaṃ syād aparaṃ tu vai ।।

prayojanavaśenaiva taravo bimbakarmaṇi ।
vihitāḥ kramaśastvete svalpānām ādināṃ mahat ।।

kecit phalavaśenaiva vihitāśca phalārthinām ।
niṣkāmānāṃ ca vihitāḥ sarve sarvaphalapradāḥ ।।

etaiḥ pūrvoditāḥ kāryāḥ saptāṅgaistoraṇāḥ śubhāḥ ।
agnikāryopayogyāni sruvādīnyuditāni vai ।।

agnāvindhanakāṣṭhāni samitparidhayastathā ।
ārādhanārthaṃ mantrāṇāṃ bhadrapīṭhāni puṣkara ।।

mantrabimbānyaśeṣāṇi tatpīṭhāni tathaiva ca ।
prāsādādīni citrāṇi prākārasahitāni ca ।।

śayanānyāsanādīni devopakaraṇāni ca ।
rathādirathayātrārthaṃ vaiṣṇaveṣūtsaveṣu ca ।।

ketudaṇḍāni dīrghāṇi śikharāṇāṃ śiropari ।
āhareta yathāśāstraṃ chāyāśuṣkakṛtāni ca ।।

bhaṅgabhedakrimicchidrasiṃhaṛkṣanakhakṣataiḥ ।
doṣair aśanipātādyair nāhared dūṣitāni vai ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

bhagavan bhadrapīṭhānāṃ pratimānāṃ ca lakṣaṇam ।
devīyapiṇḍikānāṃ ca prāsādānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।

yathāvad jñātum icchāmi rathādīnāṃ ca saṃsthitim ।
pramāṇaṃ dhvajadaṇḍānāṃ maṇḍapān maṇḍayanti ye ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

svānukūladine śuddhe gurūṇāṃ saṃmatena ca ।
mānam ādau tu sarvatra cintayet saha śilpinā ।।

suniveśena saha vai sarvam āpādayet tataḥ ।
yānyuktāni purā brahman vyaktisthānāni vai vibhoḥ ।।

dvayaṃ tebhyaḥ śubhataraṃ bhadrapīṭham akṛtrimam ।
mānonmānapramāṇāḍhyaṃ divyam ākāram abjaja ।।

tatra tāvat suvarṇādyair lohaiḥ śubhataraiḥ smṛtaḥ ।
śubhā bhagavadākārāḥ śailajāḥ samanantaram ।।

kāṣṭhaṃ lepaṃ tathālekhyam iṣṭaṃ bhūtivyapekṣayā ।
tatrāptānāṃ dvijārcāsu sthitirmokṣāptaye smṛtā ।।

sevāparāṇāṃ āptānāṃ bhūtaye amarayājinām ।
makhahomaparāṇāṃ tu divi devāsanāptaye ।।

yatīnāṃ muktasaṅgānāṃ hṛdi sarveśvare harau ।
ehi śreṣṭhataraṃ vipra arcādeśaṃ sulakṣaṇam ।।

cittaprasādam atulaṃ yatrābhyeti samarcanāt ।
yatnena ca samāpādya mantraiḥ saṃskṛtya vaidikaiḥ ।।

mṛdbhūtitīrthatoyādyair mūladravyaiḥ supāvanaiḥ ।
saṃsmarecca maṇisvarṇatāratāmramayairvinā ।।

svadehavad upādeyair nāḍīvyūhaiḥ savāyavaiḥ ।
dhātubhiḥ somasūryāgnisahajñānādikairguṇaiḥ ।।

guṇakāraṇataḥ kṣmāntaṃ yad anyattattvasaṃgraham ।
dravyam āśritya vai baimbaṃ vartate yad idaṃ mahat ।।

tatra hṛtkamalākāśe mantraratnaprabhojjvalam ।
brahmabhāvanayā nyastaṃ yacchati prātimaṃ phalam ।।

śraddhāparāṇāṃ kartṝṇāṃ phalatābhyeti ca sthiram ।
pratipattiṃ parāṃ brāhmīm ākāraṃ prati sarvadā ।।

prāpnoti sadvaśād ante jñānam ātmaprakāśakam ।
pratimānām ato mānaṃ sāṃprataṃ cāvadhāraya ।।

tālapramāṇād ekaikaṃ hrāsayet aṅgulaṃ kramāt ।
caturaṅgulaparyantaṃ yāvanmānaṃ punastataḥ ।।

ekaikaṃ vardhayed vipra śamaparyantam aṅgulam ।
tāladvayonnatiṃ yāvaccalārcānām atordhvataḥ ।।

acalānāṃ dvijārcānāṃ vdyaṅgulaṃ vdyaṅgulaṃ kramāt ।
catuḥśamāvadhiṃ yāvad atordhvaṃ tu samācaret ।।

ekaikaṃ tālavṛddhayā tu dvādaśāntakarāvadhi ।
vardhayed ata ūrdhvaṃ tu sapādaṃ tālameva ca ।।

ādhikyena dvijārcānāṃ jāyate anyaccatuṣṭayam ।
dadyāt tadunnater bhūyo vṛddhyarthaṃ dvādaśāṅgulāt ।।

tṛtīyāṃśaṃ tṛtīyāṃśāt pratimātritayasya ca ।
bhūyastadunnater dadyāt tālārdhaṃ tālam eva vā ।।

dvitīyapratimānāṃ tu ucchrāyeṇa varaṃ bhavet ।
śamam ekaṃ tatordhvaṃ tu unmānārthaṃ tu vardhayet ।।

ekaivārcā bhaved anyā vardhayed ata ūrdhvataḥ ।
kramācchatāvadhiṃ yāvat sāṃśāt tālādvijottama ।।

yathābhimata ucchrāyasiddhaye abhimatāptaye ।
bhūyo bhūyonnatiṃ kuryāt prādurbhāvākṛtervaśāt ।।

prayojanavaśāccāpi mahattvaṃ bimbakarmaṇi ।
vihitaṃ kramaśaścaiva svasvamānādinā saha ।।

tathā phalavaśāccaiva vijñeyaṃ hi phalārthinā ।
niṣkāmānāṃ ca kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sarvaphalāptaye ।।

mānato bahudhā proktam ityevaṃ pratimāgaṇam ।
dhātumṛcchailadārūtthaṃ yathāsaṃpattito dvija ।।

adhirudhya svavṛkṣotthabhinnair avayavasthitiḥ ।
varṇakaiḥ samavetā śca baddhaiḥ śastrāmbarādikaiḥ ।।

bhinnaiḥ snāyvasthimāṃsādyairjīvānāṃ vigrahaṃ yathā ।
mantrāṇām evam abjottha vyaktirdhātvādikī smṛtā ।।

aprabuddhaiḥ prabuddhairyā caturvargaphalāptaye ।
pūjyate vividhairbhogair antaḥ saṃpūjanād bahiḥ ।।

citraśailamayīṃ muktvā pratimāṃ mahatīṃ ca yām ।
mṛddhātudārujaṃ vipra ghaṭate katham anyathā ।।

pramāṇapariśuddhaistu bhinnair avayavair vinā ।
etāvat pratimāṃ vipra mānamātram udāhṛtam ।।

bhaktiśraddhāparāṇāṃ ca pūjārthaṃ hi calācalam ।
tatrāyatanatīrthānāṃ yātrāyāṃ gamane calā ।।

pratimāprayatānāṃ ca dadyād doṣadikaṃ vinā ।
pūjitāmuṣmikīṃ siddhim aihikīṃ ca prayacchati ।।

ato bhinnāsanārūḍhā svāśrame svāśramāntare ।
tasmāccalānām arcānāṃ bhinnaṃ pīṭhaṃ śubhapradam ।।

calasthiravibhāgena vihitaṃ sarvam eva hi ।
mṛṇmayā leśataḥ proktāḥ prāntapīṭhāstu kevalāḥ ।।

idānīṃ saviśeṣeṇa vakṣye bhaṅgāsanāttu vai ।
sāṃprataṃ bhadrapīṭhānāṃ dārujānāṃ ca lakṣaṇam ।।

vyāpakaṃ hi yad anyeṣāṃ śailahemādikātmanām ।
dviṣaṭkāṅgulamānācca dvihastāntaṃ mahāmate ।।

kuryād aṅgulavṛddhyā tu bhadrapīṭhagaṇaṃ śubham ।
trividhair aṅgulaiḥ prāgvad yathābhimatalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

dvidaśāṅgulaparyantāḥ sarve saṃkṣiptalakṣaṇāḥ ।
sarvaikahastaniṣṭhāstu madhyamānāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।

ata ūrdhvaṃ dvihastāntā mānato vitatāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
ādyārcā kramaśo viddhi prādhānyaṃ cottarottaram ।।

phalādhikyena saha vai arghyapuṣpādinārcanāt ।
sapraṇālāścatuṣpādāḥ sarve sadracanānvitāḥ ।।

ekapādāmbarasthā ye boddhavyāḥ pārthivairvinā ।
pranālarahitāste vai pādagātravibhūṣitāḥ ।।

darpaṇodaravat kāryāḥ pariśiṣṭā mahāmate ।
muktāmālāsamopetair ardhacandraiḥ sadarpaṇaiḥ ।।

karṇikāvitatopetaiḥ karṇikākamalacchadaiḥ ।
haṃsairvidyādharaiścāpi saṃyuktair antarāntarā ।।

yathā śobhānurūpeṇa evaṃ saṃpādya sāṃpratam ।
bāhulyaṃ bhadrapīṭhīyaṃ praṇālenopaśobhitam ।।

tadārādhyasya vai kuryād uttareṇa tu sarvadā ।
svātmano dakṣiṇe bhāge tallakṣaṇam athocyate ।।

vistṛte bhadrapīṭhasya tṛtīyāṃśena madhyataḥ ।
pūrvoddiṣṭena dairghyeṇa ślakṣṇaṃ vā racanānvitam ।।

prollasantaṃ yathā bhāti snānābhaṃ nikhanet tataḥ ।
samāṃśenāgrato bhāgairvibhajya susamaistribhiḥ ।।

mūlataḥ kaṇṭhadeśād dvau bhāgau bāhyād viśodhya ca ।
tridhāgraṃ mūlataḥ kṛtvā madhyamaṃ vrajanirgatam ।।

jalopabhogakānto api viddhi bhāgadvayopari ।
racanoparyududdiṣṭā kāryā karmāṇinī ? ca sā ।।

makarānanarūpā sā tyājyā kāpilalakṣaṇā ।
tṛtīyāṃśena vistārād bhūgataḥ sāṅghrisantatiḥ ।।

samudgatā na vai kuryād bāhulyaracanānvitā ।
sarvato bhadrabimbaiva madhyato gātrakānvitā ।।

bhūṣayed gātradeśebhyaḥ puṣpaiḥ patraistu sāṅkuraiḥ ।
bhavecchaśikalākāralāñchanaiḥ svadhiyāthavā ।।

kuryāt taduttare padmaṃ sacakraṃ kevalaṃ tu vā ।
ānataṃ taṃ bahiḥ kuryād ābhogaṃ vānanaṃ mahat ।।

tadānanaṃ tatheśānye bhāgāntena susaṃyutam ।
vidheyaṃ ca tathābhogaṃ dakṣiṇāvartalakṣaṇam ।।

saṃniveśama taḥsvāṅgaṃ gātra[madhyāntaṭagaiḥ saha ।
na ca prāsādabhadraṃ ca ekāgram avadhāraya ।।

ardhenārdhyācca pīṭhāt tu vistīrṇaṃ pṛṣṭhadeśataḥ ।
vidheyaṃ caturaśraṃ tu suvṛttaṃ vāmabhāgataḥ ।।

bāhulyavantaṃ bāhulyāt tasmiṃ[ścaiva] śiro nyaset ।
stambhaṃ suvṛttaṃ vihitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vā caturaśrakam ।।

aṣṭāśram athavā ramyaracanāracitaṃ tu vā ।
bāhulyāt triguṇād dīrghaṃ vihitaṃ stambhaveṣṭanam ।।

latāvitānapatrāḍhyair vanair upavanaiḥ saha ।
dhyānāsaktairmunīndraistu vedādhyayanatatparaiḥ ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmamūrtāmūrtairmahāmate ।
sākṣasūtrakarairvāpi siddhestu bhagavanmayaiḥ ।।

ityeṣāṃ racanāṃ kuryād aparāṃ vābjasaṃbhava ।
praphullapadmairāpūrāt karṇikākesarānvitaiḥ ।।

uparyupari saṃmūḍhaiḥ karmabhistvevameva vā ।
sragdaṇḍavad vidheyaṃ vā nālaṃ bhadrāsanīyakam ।।

pṛṣṭhadeśe tu yad bhaktaṃ vṛttādyaṃ parikalpitam ।
cakrādhārasvabhāvena ūrdhvavaktrāmbujātmanā ।।

nītvā tad bāhyataḥ kuryāccakraṃ sarvāṅgacihnitam ।
caturbhiḥ kūrmavat kuryāt staṃmbham ādhāram uttamam ।।

samatvenāsanīyasya vistārasya mahāmate ।
vistāraṃ tasya tenaiva sārdhena vihitastu vai ।।

māhendramaṇḍalākāraṃ vṛttaṃ vā vasudhāvane ।
samaṃ vā mastakoddeśād anupātena saṃkaṭam ।।

tribhāgaṃ samatulyaṃ vā budhnadeśācca vistṛteḥ ।
samāpādyaiva saṃskṛtya prāgvad vai bhavanānvitam ।।

saṃnidhīkṛtya mantreśaṃ mantraṃ mokṣāptaye tu vai ।
yaṣṭavyaṃ parayā bhaktyā svaśaktyā vā phalāptaye ।।

mahatā vibhavenaiva sādhakaiḥ svagṛhasthitaiḥ ।
ete bhedāsya vihitā aṣṭāśrāḥ kamalodbhava ।।

ṣaḍaśrā vartulāścāpi caturasrā athāpi vā ।
svadalena samopetaṃ caturaśrasya kalpayet ।।

tadāsya sattvasiddhyarthaṃ sarvadaivaṃ mahāmate ।
vibhavānuguṇenaiva proktamānāt tu sādhitam ।।

racanāsaṃniveśena samabhyūhya samāpya vai ।
iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ bhadrapīṭhalakṣaṇaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha ekacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pauṣkara uvāca 

uktamārgeṇa coddiṣṭaṃ māntraṃ saṃsthāpanaṃ tu vai ।
yathāvad uktaṃ tad ahaṃ jñātum icchāmi sāṃpratam ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

nṛṇām ārādhakānāṃ tu mantraikaniratātmanām ।
mantrākṛteḥ prabuddhasya guptaṃ kṛtvārcanaṃ hitam ।।

atha dārvādikānāṃ tu dhātūtthānāṃ samāhitaḥ ।
racanāsaṃniveśaṃ ca sastaṃbhānāṃ nibodhatu ।।

tathā staṃbhavimuktānāṃ bhūbhāgāṅghriniveśinām ।
bāhulyaṃ ca svavistārāt tṛtīyāṃśasamaṃ smṛtam ।।

praṇālaṃ tatsamaṃ dairghyād vistṛtervārdhasaṃmitam ।
vibhajya susamair bhāgair adhamaṃ balavatpurā ।।

svalpā dvādaśasaṃkhyaistu madhyamāstu dvisaptakaiḥ ।
dvir aṣṭasaṃkhyair vitatāstatrādyānāṃ tu madhyataḥ ।।

vidheyaṃ ṣaḍbhir aṃśaistu pīṭhaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ samaṃ śubham ।
suvṛttaṃ caturaśraṃ vā svapadmaṃ kevalaṃ tvatha ।।

cakrāmburuhayuktaṃ vā taducchrāyaṃ vidhīyate ।
ardhabhāgena bāhulyāt tatsārdhaṃ sakajasya ca ।।

samaṃ sacakrapadmasya tayoḥ pūrvoktalakṣaṇam ।
vihitaṃ kintu viprendra caturaśrasya kalpayet ।।

koṇeṣu śaṅkhanirmāṇaṃ śaṅkhādyaṃ vā catuṣṭayam ।
vartulasya na te kāryāstathaiva kamalodbhava ।।

cakrapadmaviyuktasya caturāśrāśrayasya ca ।
yaduktaṃ cakrapadmābhyām ardhe tuṅgatvam abjaja ।।

na kevalasya vihitaṃ mantrāspadasya ca ।
tad abjaṃ nikhanenmadhyād dvyaṃśaṃ dvyaṃśaṃ samantataḥ ।।

khātaṃ bhāgaṃ samaṃ caiva sārdhaṃ dairghyād vidhīyate ।
jalāśrayaṃ tu paritaḥ khātād bhaṅgasamaṃ bahiḥ ।।

sopavītaṃ ca vihitam antarekhāśrayasthite ।
dvādaśāṃśakṛtānāṃ ca ityeṣām aṃśakalpanā ।।

vihitā kāṣṭhavargāṇāṃ śailajānām api dvija ।
bhaṅgād vibhaktibhirbhāgairmātraṃ yatkalpitaṃ purā ।।

tanmadhye munibhirbhāgaiḥ sarvaṃ pūrvoktam ācaret ।
bhāgadvayaṃ dvayaṃ caiva parito nikhanet kramāt ।।

janmāśrayaṃ tu bhāgena sārdhena paritaḥ smṛtam ।
tatordhvam uktamānaṃ yat tatra tad vihitaṃ tu vai ।।

vibhajya tat ṣoḍaśadhā madhye bhāgāṣṭakena vai ।
vidheyam akhilaṃ prāgvad bhāgāt pādena vai saha ।।

parito nikhaned droṇīṃ brahman bhāgadvayena tu ।
jalāśrayaṃ tu vihitaṃ pādonena dvayena vā ।।

āpādya cakraṃ prāguktaṃ kamalādyaṃ yathoditam ।
navapadmamayīṃ kuryāt saṃsthitiṃ cārcane vibhoḥ ।।

yathāyathā ca vistāraṃ samabhyūhya tathātathā ।
ādāya khātapūrvebhyo madhyadeśe tu yojayet ।।

vibhaktaṃ bhavate yena kṣetraṃ ced ambujasya ca ।
navānām api padmānām atha mantravarāśritam ।।

padmaṃ sādhāraṇājjālaṃ yujyate abhyarcitaṃ yathā ।
iti vistīrṇabhāgānāṃ vibhāgaṃ hi yathoditam ।।

kṛtvātha racayed yatnād bāhulyaṃ mekhalādikaiḥ ।
jalāśrayasamenādau tad uddeśāt krameṇa tu ।।

śodhayitvānupādena bāhulyaṃ dikcatuṣṭayāt ।
tricatuḥ pañca vā ṣaḍ vā tataḥ pucchāśriter bhajet ।।

tridhā vibhaktaṃ soṣṇīṣaṃ sapadmaṃ mekhalātrayam ।
catur vibhaktenoṣṇīṣaṃ mekhalāṣaṭkamadhyagam ।।

kuryād vai kiṅkiṇījāladvayena nalinīṃ śubhām ।
munibhakte tu bāhulye ṣoḍhā kamalasaṃbhava ।।

bhāgenoṣṇīṣavargaṃ tu ślathagātrāgravad bhavet ।
tadadhaḥ śuktikākāraṃ sūtraṃ chinnaṃ vidhīyate ।।

adhastācchuktibhāgasya vṛttaṃ kuryāt sakarṇikam ।
vṛttāsanaṃ ca vihitaṃ caturaśraṃ samantataḥ ।।

tadadhastritayaṃ kuryānmekhalānāṃ sulakṣaṇam ।
sapādāścoktapādebhyaḥ kiñcitkiñcid yathākramam ।।

sthitirantarasūtrīyā vibhāgajananī hitā ।
santyajyoṣṇīṣapīṭhāṃśaṃ garuḍaṃ ca kṛtāñjalim ।।

svavaktreṇāpareṇaiva yuktaṃ pāṇidvayena tu ।
kuryāt pūrvāparābhyāṃ vā manye bhadrāsanasya ca ।।

gaṃgāyamunayor madhye varuṇaṃ yādasāṃ patim ।
madhyatastad udagbhāge bhadrapīṭhasya kalpayet ।।

pārśvadvaye pramāṇasya samudraṃ ratnapātradhṛt ।
vidheyaṃ saumyamūrtiṃ ca divyair jalacaraiḥ saha ।।

dikcatuṣkam ataḥ śeṣam āpūryaṃ kiṅkiṇīgaṇaiḥ ।
dravyaje calabimbe vā aṅgulaiḥ parinirmite ।।

athordhvaṃ tu nṛpādīnāṃ hitaṃ nānāniveśanam ।
mahādhanānāṃ cānyeṣāṃ śubhepsūnāṃ ca kīrtaye ।।

nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ tatra tāvat samācaret ।
rājā vā sādhakaścānyo lokadaṃ svargadaṃ hi yat ।।

vṛṣotsargaphalenāśu nivṛttiṃ tasya karmaṇaḥ ।
kṛtvā tadanu vai kuryād hareḥ saṃsthāpanaṃ punaḥ ।।

viśeṣakarmanicayaṃ pratyastama ti yatra vai ।
saṃkalpād eva nādharmamājīvam abhivindati ।।

samyak samāpto yenaiva tenānyasmin hi janmani ।
vivekajaṃ paraṃ jñānam āpnuyānmokṣasiddhidam ।।

nānyena karmaṇā yasmād viṣakīrṇena karmaṇā ।
jāyate parayā śāntirdharmavaśyo akṣayapradaḥ ।।

pauṣkara uvāca 

nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।
jñātum icchāmi bhagavan tvattaḥ saṃdehaśāntaye ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

pañcāyatanūparvaṃ prāk kṛtvā devālayaṃ śubham ।
kāmanārahitenaiva cetasā vimalena tu ।।

dharmārtham āśritaṃ tasmin puraṃ kuryād dvijāspadam ।
sarvalokeṣu sāmānyaṃ sarvadoṣakṣayaṅkaram ।।

sarvadharmottamaṃ caiva sarvadā sarvakāmadam ।
pravaraṃ pañcakālajñasamūhaṃ bhagavanmayam ।।

ṣaṭkarmanirataṃ cāpi trayīdharmaparāyaṇam ।
jñātiśuddhaṃ parijñāya nirdvandvaṃ ca parasparam ।।

dāśāgnihotrasaṃyuktaṃ vedādhyayanatatparam ।
nadīśailavanopete duṣṭaprāṇivivarjite ।।

sasyaśāliphalāḍhye tu snigdhaśaṣpasamākule ।
svādutoyaprade deśe suprākāravibhūṣite ।।

tam āsādya śubhaṃ tatra pūjayitvā jagatprabhum ।
tataḥ snātvānuliptaṃ ca vastrālaṃkārabhūṣitam ।।

tāmraśāsanapūrvaṃ tu brāhmaṇaṃ viniveśya ca ।
āsaneṣu samūhantaṃ pādyārdhyakusumair yajet ।।

taṃ ca dhūpaiḥ sugandhaiśca tāmbūlena mahāmate ।
yathākramopadiṣṭeṣu dadyāt pāṇau kuśodakam ।।

dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa pramādyam iti pāṭhayet ।
pratiṣṭhāsīti vai sāma kuryād vai prārthanāṃ tataḥ ।।

yathāvad arcanīyaśca madanugrahakāmyayā ।
svagṛhe puṇḍarīkākṣa svakulotthena karmaṇā ।।

sahasaddharmacāriṇyā vyaktavedyāṃ yathāgamam ।
samidādīni cāgnīnām agnervā śaktyapekṣayā ।।

traikālyamā ca kartavyaṃ svadharmaḥ paripālyatām ।
praveśaṃ na samāpannā dā tavyaṃ pāpakarmaṇām ।।

saṃskāryā svasutāḥ kanyā bhṛtyāmātyāḥ svavaṃśajāḥ ।
vaiṣṇavena vidhānena kāryāste bhagavanmayāḥ ।।

ā muhūrtāt tu vai brāhmād yāvadādityadarśanam ।
snānapūjājapastotrapāṭhaiḥ saṃdhyāṃ samācaret ।।

yāgasādhanabhogānām upārjanam anantaram ।
tataḥ snānaṃ tu vidhivad yathoktaṃ vidhinā hitam ।।

sāyam ābhūtaśuddhiṃ ca antaryāgam anantaram ।
yathoktavidhinā cātha kuryād ārādhanaṃ bahiḥ ।।

tato agnihavanaṃ caiva kriyāṃ paitrīm anantaram ।
balidānaṃ ca bhūtānām atithīnām athārcanam ।।

bandhubhṛtyasamopetam ātmayāgam anantaram ।
ṛksāmapūrvaṃ svādhyāyam itihāsādicintanam ।।

ācartavyaṃ samādhānaṃ svahṛtpadmāntare tataḥ ।
trayodaśāṅgam ityuktam āhnikaṃ bhagavanmayam ।।

kāryaṃ vai pratyahaṃ bhaktyā kṣīyamāṇe kṣapāgame ।
saṃnyāsam ācared bhūyaḥ kuryādgrahaṇam asya vai ।।

deśikendramukhenaivam ājñātuṃ gṛhamedhinām ।
dattvā nirgatya vai tatra kartā kuryāt pradakṣiṇam ।।

iti brahmapratiṣṭhānaṃ vidhānaṃ kathitaṃ ca te ।
vaiṣṇavīyaiḥ pālanīyaṃ nṛpendraiśca svasiddhaye ।।

svasiddhāntapratiṣṭhānam athedānīṃ nibodhatu ।
maṭham āyatane kṛtvā vṛttipūrvam akṛtrimam ।।

vaṇikkuṭumbabhṛtakairyuktaṃ dāsagaṇena tu ।
vāpyo gharaṭṭajā[liṭanyaḥ saha vātāyanaiḥ sthitāḥ ।।

tatrānnaṃ vyañjanopetaṃ bhakṣyakānnādikaṃ bahu ।
vividhaṃ sādhayitvāṃ prāk snātvā tu guruṇā saha ।।

dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu mantrair nyastatanuḥ sudhīḥ ।
arcayitvā jagannāthaṃ parameśvaram acyutam ।।

abhyāgatān samāhūya brāhyaṇān vedapāragān ।
idaṃ tad amṛtaṃ cānnam idamāyuḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।

idaṃ viṣṇuridaṃ prāṇam idaṃ jīvam idaṃ param ।
sarvasattvahitārthaṃ ca anuyāgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।

pañcabhūtajagadyoner annamūrte janārdana ।
ā bhūtasaṃplavaṃ kālaṃ bhava sannihitastviha ।।

codayed ṛṅmayān prāgvat sāmajñād dve pare śrutī ।
gurur abhyarthanīyaśca sakuṭumbena vai purā ।।

abhyāgatagaṇenāpi saha cānyaiḥ pareṇa tu ।
yoktavyaṃ pālanīyaṃ ca madanugrāhyayā dhiyā ।।

tarpayeta tato annena annād arcārcitena tu ।
samūham upaviṣṭaṃ tu ucchiṣṭaṃ śodhayet tataḥ ।।

yāyāt pradakṣiṇīkṛtya abhyāgatagaṇaṃ tatam ।
idam annapratiṣṭhānam uktam acyutabhāvinām ।।

jñānapratiṣṭhānam 

param uddharaṇopāyaṃ tathākhilasukhapradam ।
atha jñānapratiṣṭhānam idānīm avadhāraya ।
yatkṛtvā jāyate jñānaṃ vivekasahitaṃ hi yat ।।

pariśuddhān samuccitya pañcarātrīyasañcayān ।
sadāgamādikān kṛtsnān vedevadāṅgasaṃyutān ।।

smṛtismṛtyantaropetān itihāsasamanvitān ।
ānvīkṣakībhir vidyābhiḥ saśabdākhyābhisaṃvṛtān ।।

nadī nāgarakairvarṇaivividhān varṇasaṃcayān ।
pūrayitvā vinikṣipya saṃpuṭeṣvakṣayeṣu ca ।।

grathayitvāsitādyena sūtreṇa sudṛḍhena tu ।
susthire suprasiddhe ca nṛpanāgarasevite ।।

dvijoṣitebhyaḥ saṃkīrṇe satsamūhena pālite ।
samīpe aśmamayaṃ veśma lohayantrasamanvitam ।।

sakavāṭārgalopetaṃ sudhādhavalitaṃ śubham ।
kañjasthayā vāgīśvaryā bhūṣitaṃ citrabhūṣayā ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmakaraprodyatayā tayā ।
prodvahantyākṣamālāṃ tu śāstrasañcayahastayā ।।

varadābhayadāyinyā siddhādyairvāntayā paraiḥ ।
tataḥ prāgvat kṛtanyāsaḥ śuklāmbaradharaḥ śuciḥ ।।

lohayantrāyane tasmin praṇavādhiṣṭhite arcite ।
yathākramaṃ samāropya śāstrasaṃgrahapustakān ।।

pūjitāṃstu samālabdhānnetravastraistu veṣṭitān ।
dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa pūjayitvā paṭhed idam ।।

viśuddhajñānadehāya viṣṇave paramātmane ।
supratiṣṭhitam akṣayyaṃ tiṣṭha śāstrātmaneha vai ।।

ajñānām upakārārthaṃ prabodhajananāya ca ।
muktvā tvāmevam akṣayyaṃ kṣayavanto amarādayaḥ ।।

uktvaivam arcayed bhūyo vedavedāntavigraham ।
sadāgamādyairbhagavatpurāṇādyair alaṃkṛtam ।।

pratyahaṃ parayā bhaktyā vidyāpīṭhasya cāgrataḥ ।
śabdabrahmamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ bhadrapīṭhe purodite ।।

niyuktaṃ cārcane kuryād apramattaṃ dvijottama ।
tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya dhūpaṃ dattvā kṣamāpeyat ।।

sañcāradāne arthināṃ ca saṃcayaṃ tatra saṃcayet ।
śāsanāvanibandhāṃ ca tasya vṛttiṃ supuṣkalām ।।

kṛtvā tacchāsanaṃ dadyād jñānakośānupālane ।
tasmin devagṛhe paścād brahmacārīṃstu pāṭhayet ।।

mantradvayaṃ puroddiṣṭaṃ svayaṃ baddhāñjaliḥ paṭhet ।
ajñānatimirāndhānāṃ janānām avivekinām ।।

śāstrapīṭhapratiṣṭhānāt jñānam eti ca nirmalam ।
etasmād utthitenaiva phalena mahatā hariḥ ।।

prītim āyātu paramāṃ phalaṃ me nopayujyate ।
vidyāpīṭhapratiṣṭhānam idaṃ samyak prakāśitam ।।

phalārthināṃ jñānaniṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ yacchati cepsitam ।
vāpīkūpataṭākānām ārāmāṇāṃ ca mokṣaṇam ।।

pratiṣṭhāpanapūrvaṃ ca svargadaṃ hi phalārthinām ।
karmasanyāsināṃ viṣṇostatpunastatpadapradam ।।

kāraṇaṃ jagatām īśo bhūtaḥ sarveśvaro acyutaḥ ।
śabdātmikām amūrtāṃ ca jñānakarmātmalakṣaṇām ।।

samāsādya svarūpeṇa jagatyām avatiṣṭhate ।
tanmayaṃ deham āśritya yatsatyāhlādam uttamam ।।

sāmarāṇām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ mahāmate ।
evaṃ nānārasamayīṃ śaktiṃ viṭapavigrahām ।।

dāvānalasthasa karīṃ nānāvyaktamayaiḥ svaraiḥ ।
pravālapatrakusumamārutāmbuvimiśritaiḥ ।।

ajaṅgamāṃ pādapākhyāṃ patrapuṣphalapradām ।
mūrtiṃ devopavaraṇīṃ bhūmiṃ vai prathamāṃśakām ।।

aparāṃ jaṅgamāṃ mūrtiṃ saurabhaṃ saṃśritāspadām ।
tatastad utthitaistāvat pañcaupaniṣadātmakaiḥ ।।

mantritaiḥ pañcabhirmantrairgomayādyair yathākramam ।
saha ṛksāmapūrvaistu kuśodakasamanvitaiḥ ।।

śuddhaye api ca tatkhātaṃ paryukṣya paritaḥ purā ।
nayet pāvanatāṃ paścād ambunā paripūritām ।।

kṣmāgatenāthavādye na ko penālpena vā dvija ।
akṣāreṇa sutoyena sāṃprataṃ śītalena ca ।।

saṃbhave sati he mena deśakālavaśād api ।
krītena tāṭakīyena pallave noddhṛtena vā ।।

gobrāhmaṇānāṃ sāṃmūlyaṃ gatvā śatapadādikam ।
khātamadhye vinikṣipya sa khāto vitato mahān ।।

bahukāle jalasthāyī yathābhimatavistṛtaḥ ।
kāryo vai sarvadiksevyo anavasthā jāyate yathā ।।

kulastrījanavṛddhānāṃ sneham āharatāṃ bhṛśam ।
dhanurdvayasamaṃ kuryānnimnatvena tu sarvadā ।।

sārdhakārmukatulyaṃ vā ekajyāniṣṭhameva vā ।
dhanurdvayāt samārabhya yāvad dhanuḥśataṃ tu vai ।।

vihite khātavistāre hyata ūrdhvaṃ yathā ca te ।
tatpārthivaṃ ca vāyavyaṃ saumyam āgneyameva ca ।।

caturaśrāyataṃ caiva āpādya śubhalakṣaṇam ।
samūbhāgavaśāccaiva padavīgaṇabhūṣitam ।।

vṛkṣavallīgaṇopetaṃ śāḍvalasthalabhūṣitam ।
pāthikāvāsakairyuktaṃ tathā viśrāmatoraṇaiḥ ।।

evaṃ kṛtvā yathoddiṣṭaṃ yatra govigrahakṣitau ।
avadhārya ca sandhārya khātahrāsaṃ ca kurvatī ।।

kālaṃ pravṛttiparyantaṃ tarpayantī ca tajjalam ।
evaṃ saṃskṛtya ca tataḥ prāgbhāgam api vīkṣayan ।।

pratyagbhāgasthitaḥ kartā guruṇā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha ।
taduddhṛtenāmbhasātha athavānyena sāṃpratam ।।

mṛdā gomayayutayā tatkālaṃ lepayet sthalam ।
dvādaśārṇena gāyatryā sāmnā vai vāsudhena tu ।।

pūrvadakṣiṇasaumyānāṃ digbhāgānāṃ yathākramam ।
homārtham ṛgyajuḥsāmapāṭhakān viniveśya ca ।।

sthaleṣu vālakīyeṣu kuṇḍeṣu suśubheṣu vā ।
dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa kṛtanyāsasvakena vā ।।

mṛtpiṇḍam ekam ādāya svātamadhyāt tu pātrakam ।
kauśeyakusumopete āsane viniveśya ca ।।

toyapūrṇaṃ tadūrdhve tu kalaśaṃ kāñcanodaram ।
vastreṇa veṣṭitaṃ samyak kuṅkumādyair vilepitam ।।

puṣpasraṅmañjarīdūrvādarbhabījaphalodakam ।
sitopavītam āśubhraṃ netram uṣṇīṣabhṛnnyaset ।।

pārthivena ca śūnyena jīvayuktena bhāvayet ।
sabindunāmaye nātha sāmṛtenācyutaṃ vibhum ।।

nārāyaṇaṃ parāṃ mūrtim utthitāṃ madhuradhvaneḥ ।
padmamante niyoktavyam asya bījatrayasya ca ।।

nārāyaṇāya bhagavaṃstato bhūtātmane namaḥ ।
snānapūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhānam ācartavyaṃ yathāvidhi ।।

dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa athavāṣṭākṣareṇa tu ।
ṣaḍakṣareṇa saṃpādya pūrṇāntā havanakriyā ।।

arcayitvā yathāśakti gurupūrvān dvijottamān ।
samādāyātha kalaśaṃ pūrṇaṃ palvalajaṃ hi yat ।।

kartā vinikṣipet pūrvaṃ mṛtpiṇḍaṃ puṣkarodare ।
kalaśodakam utkīrya imaṃ mantram udīrayet ।।

āmūrte bhagavan nātha vāsudevāmṛtātmane ।
ācandratārakaṃ kālaṃ tiṣṭha tvaṃ supratiṣṭhitam ।।

māmakasyāñjasā trāṇaṃ nātha sānugasaṃyutān ।
devān pitṝn sasādhyāṃśca bhūtānyāpyāyitā sadā ।।

phalena tu ihotthena yātu prītiṃ parāṃ bhavān ।
tṛptirbhavatu bhūtānāṃ trailokyodaravartinām ।।

ityuktvā pāṭhayet sāma dhruvādyau ṛṅmayāṃstataḥ ।
pratiṣṭhāsīti vai sāma sāmajñān brāhmaṇottamān ।।

pūjanair vividhaiḥ paścāt tadutthena tu sāmbhasam ।
tarpayed brāhmaṇān sarvān khātakartṝna tathākhilān ।।

prasādya dānapūrveṇa deśikān vibhave sati ।
dīnānāthāṃstathā bhṛtyānanantaphalasiddhaye ।।

suvarṇavasudhādānaṃ yathāśaktyā samācaret ।
kanyādānaṃ vṛṣotsargaṃ pitṛśrāddhapuraḥsaram ।।

vadhabandhotthitaṃ doṣaṃ dhanadaṇḍotthitaṃ ca yat ।
vicāraṇīyaṃ lokānām arthayitvā nareśvaram ।।

kintu vī dhyantaram idaṃ vihitaṃ sati saṃbhave ।
pradhānaphalavṛkṣaṃ tu aśvatthaviṭapaṃ tu vā ।।

ārāmasaṃpratiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃskṛtya snānakarmaṇām ।
samālabhya svalaṃkṛtya upavetya yathāvidhi ।।

vāsasā veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā puṣpasrakparibhūṣitam ।
homāntam akhilaṃ prāgvat samantraṃ tatsamācaret ।।

tena yāti paraṃ kartā pāraṃ saṃsāravāridheḥ । phalamūlānnādipratiṣṭhā 

phalamūlānnapratiṣṭhāṃ śṛṇu vakṣye phalārthinām ।
nānnadānāt paraṃ dānaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vidyate ।।

sadyaḥprītikaraṃ hṛdyaṃ prāṇadaṃ prāṇināmapi ।
utpattāvapi saṃskāre rasam annasya kīrtitam ।।

annād bhavanti bhūtāni tasmāt sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
tacca pratiṣṭhitaṃ yena tena sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।

ātmanā saha loke asmin svarloke brahmasaṃjñite ।
yāvajjīvaṃ ca nīrogo vased duḥkhavivarjitaḥ ।।

putradāradhanair annair vṛddhiṃ yāti kṣaṇāt kṣaṇam ।
prāpnoti paramāṃ pūjām utkṛṣṭebhyo mahattarām ।।

devatā ṛṣayaḥ siddhāstasya saṃcintayanti ca ।
nityam eva parāṃ vṛddhimāyuṣaḥ saha connatām ।।

hṛṣṭaḥ puṣṭastato bhūtvā tṛpto bhavati sarvadā ।
bhuktvā bhogān suvipulānante nārāyaṇālayam ।।

yāti candrapratīkāśairvimānairdevanirmitaiḥ ।
svargādau sarvaloke tu sthitvā kalpaśatān bahūn ।।

kālāt punar ihāyāti deśe sarvottame śubhe ।
satāṃ kule samāsādya janma jātyuttamaṃ mahat ।।

jāyate rūpavān vāgmī vidyājñānaparāyaṇaḥ ।
dviṣatām api sarveṣāṃ pūjyaḥ priyataraḥ sadā ।।

śīlavāñ śauryasaṃpanno dhṛtyutsāhasamanvitaḥ ।
dvijadevaparo nityaṃ dātā bhūtahite rataḥ ।।

ekāntī dharmavettā vai nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ।
trivargam akhilaṃ bhuktvā yathābhimatalakṣaṇaḥ ।।

janmābhyastaṃ śubhaṃ karma kṛtvānantaguṇaṃ punaḥ ।
jñānam āsādyate yena prayāti paramaṃ padam ।।

na hi vai kūpavāpīnāṃ surabhīṇāṃ ca pūjanam ।
dadyācchuddhaṃ hi tādātmyaṃ vidhānaṃ sarvam ācaret ।।

nītvāṅgabhāvam asmiṃśca gogaṇaṃ bhagavadgṛhe ।
snānopabhogapūrvāṇāṃ vibhor analatarpaṇāt ।।

prītyarthaṃ surabhīṇāṃ tu pratipādyaṃ tu śāsanam ।
tam agniṃ govrajopetaṃ dhṛtadīpasamanvitam ।।

devavat pālanīyaṃ ca yāvad ācandratārakam ।
aniśaṃ jvalamānaṃ ca vaset karmakaraiḥ saha ।।

ṣaḍaśītimukhādyaṃ vai kālam āsādya puṇyadam ।
kuṇḍaṃ sulakṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā divyādyairveṣṇavairgṛhe ।।

svayaṃ pratiṣṭhite vāpi dharmaskandheṣu vai purā ।
dvādaśākṣaramantrādyaiḥ śubhaiḥ sūktaistu vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।।

ṛgyajuḥsahasāmaistu devadevapraśaṃsakaiḥ ।
evaṃ hotā śanaiścāpi saṃpaṭhecchāntike kṛte ।।

ghṛtādyair akṣataiḥ pītaiḥ sitakṛṣṇānvitaistilaiḥ ।
saṃskṛtya cānalaṃ kuṇḍaṃ prājāpatyena karmaṇā ।।

āhutīnāṃ tu juhuyāt sahasrād ayutāvadhi ।
śatādyaṃ ca sahasrāntaṃ tāmrajena sruveṇa tu ।।

pālīyenāṣṭamāṃśena dhṛtaṃ tu juhuyāt tataḥ ।
akāmo vā sakāmo vā dadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ ।।

nārāyaṇastu vedātmā sahavedamukhena tu ।
dadātyabhimatān kāmān upāyaṃ naiṣṭhikaṃ tu vai ।।

evaṃ kṛte tu saṃpādyād badhnīyād dhiṣaṇopari ।
saptāhaṃ vasudhārāṃ ca trirātram athavā śubham ।।

ekāhaṃ vā svaśaktyā tu tad vidhānam athocyate ।
nirdhūme vitate kuṇḍe dṛḍhaiḥ kāṣṭhaistu yājñikaiḥ ।।

kṛtvāgniṃ mekhalābhūmer adhikaṃ śibikopamam ।
dhanurdvayocchrite vātha tadūrdhve tāmrajaṃ tatam ।।

kaṭāhakaṃ yojanīyaṃ kāṣṭhaje valaye dṛḍhe ।
sthiravaṃśacatuṣpāde padavīsahanakṣame ।।

aṅgulair atha mānīyaiścatuḥsaṃkhyaistu connatam ।
haimīṃ suvarṇamānotthāṃ śalākāṃ sarvataḥ samām ।।

tatpramāṇasamopetaṃ madhyame tu kaṭāhake ।
vedhaṃ kuryācca lohena vastrāpūtam athāharet ।।

vyājahīnaṃ ghṛtaṃ havyaṃ sugandhi śubhalakṣaṇam ।
kaṭāhake samutkīrya yatna [pūrva]parikṣaya m ।।

pravahaṃ dinarātrīyaṃ kālaṃ yat trividhaṃ smṛtam ? ।
etāvad uktam ārabhya devam ātmānaṃ akṣamam ।।

āprabhātā[ntama]thavādyaṃ vāharayet praharaṃ ghṛtam ।
praharadvitayaṃ vātha praharatrayam eva vā ।।

praharāṇāṃ catuṣkaṃ vā svasāmarthyādyapekṣayā ।
ādau ṣaṭprasthamānāt tu catuḥprasthāntameva hi ।।

pravāham āharecchaktyā pālikaṃ tu ghṛtasya vā ।
adhibhūtādhidevāḍhyaṃ stṛtvādhyātmatayā ghṛtam ।।

pavitram amṛtaṃ brahma ājyam adhyātmameva hi ।
adhidevaṃ paraṃ vahnir adhibhūtaṃ ca gogaṇam ।।

smṛtam uktaṃ mamaivaṃ hi vasu matvā svarūpadhṛk ।
tadvāraparimāṇena vidhitvena ca vartate ।।

svadaridram imaṃ lokaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vai yatprabhāvataḥ ।
vitatena tu pātreṇa sthagayitvā kaṭāhakam ।।

daivatvenārcanīyaṃ ca bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ ।
sāṃprataṃ cārghyapuṣpādyair vasugarbhakaṭāhake ।।

anugrahakarastvāste svayaṃ śraddhāvatāṃ nṛṇām ।
ārambhād eva niṣpattiparyantaṃ śubhakarmaṇām ।।

arcayitvā namaskṛtya dvādaśārṇena cācyutam ।
tato anulepanaṃ dadyāt puṣpasragdhūpam eva hi ।।

naivedyaṃ madhuparkādyaṃ sabhakṣyaṃ saphalaṃ mahat ।
atha sarveśvaraṃ bhaktyā vibhum āyatanasthitam ।।

mahatā vibhavenaiva snānapūrveṇa karmaṇā ।
pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ satsūktaiḥ samyaguttamaiḥ ।।

rahasyamantrapūvaistu sāṣṭārṇadvādaśākṣaraiḥ ।
jānubhyām avaniṃ kṛtvā natamūrdhāgrato bhavet ।।

tadekakṣema pūrvaṃ tu viniveśya idaṃ paṭhet ।
paraṃ vasu ghṛtā ṛktvaṃ sarvaṃ saṃpūritaṃ tvayā ।।

tāreyaṃ paramā śaktisvamiyā deva pūjitaḥ ।
vāsādyānanam āgneyatulyaṃ yajñasya vai phalam ।।

sumahadgokulopetaṃ grāmaṃ yad viṣayoditam ।
tatpālakānāṃ viprāṇāṃ śāsanena samāpya ca ।।

yathā nocchidyate caiva kīrtidharmaparaṃ mahat ।
nṛpeṇaitat tathā kāryaṃ yaśodharmavivṛddhaye ।।

ṣaṭkād yad adhikaṃ caiva saśubhaṃ kīrtitaṃ trayam ।
goṣṭham agniṃ ca dīpaṃ ca aṅgam āyataneṣu tat ।।

dharmajñaiḥ pālanīyaṃ ca vicchedo na bhaved yathā ।
yasmād vahnimukhenaiva trayastriṃśattu koṭayaḥ ।।

pratyahaṃ tṛptim atulāṃ vibudhānāṃ prayānti ca ।
dadhikṣīrājyapūrvaistu vividhairgosamutthitaiḥ ।।

prītim abhyeti bhagavān upahāraistu sāttvikaiḥ ।
paramādityavat sarvam ābhāsayati tejasā ।।

prabhāvāccaiva dīpasya nityaṃ sannihitasya ca ।
yo adhikṛtya jagannāthaṃ ṣaḍaśītimukhāsu ca ।।

tithiṣvarcyastu bhagavān kalaśe maṇḍane anale ।
sopavāsaḥ śuciḥ snātaḥ kṛtakautukamaṅgalaḥ ।।

praṇavādinamontena mantreṇānena bhaktitaḥ ।
prīyatāṃ mama deveśo dharmādhyakṣo vṛṣākapiḥ ।।

gohito gopatirgoptā sarvamāvṛtya ca sthitaḥ ।
tato anulipte bhūbhāge kutapaḥ kevalaṃ tu vā ।।

abhuktamahataṃ śuddhaṃ prastīryaṃ satilākṣatam ।
samastabījaṃ sakuśaṃ siddhārthakasamanvitam ।।

tad bahistejasaṃ dadyāt pūrṇaṃ prāgāditaḥ kramāt ।
pātrāṣṭakaṃ payaḥ śālidadhyakṣatarasaistilaiḥ ।।

ghṛtena sarvabījaistu vastrairyavanikā bahiḥ ।
iṣubhiḥ saha sūtraistu barhipakṣaiḥ suviṣṭaraiḥ ।।

jātabījaśarāvāśca pūrṇakumbhamukhasthitāḥ ।
pūrṇaśākhāsametāśca taruśākhābhyalaṃkṛtāḥ ।।

dikṣu prajvalitair dīpaiḥ saha nyasya ṛgādikaiḥ ।
tato avatārya tanmadhye surabhiṃ kṛtamaṇḍanām ।।

sālaṃkṛtāṃ savastrāṃ ca ghaṇṭācāmarabhūṣitām ।
saratnahemakumudāṃ tacchṛṅgaparibhūṣitām ।।

muktāpravālalāṅgūlāṃ rajatāṅghrim abhipriyām ।
lalāṭadarpaṇāṃ śrīmatsraguṣṇīṣabalāṃ mahat ।।

evam evātha vīryadhvaṃ surabhiṃ kṛtamaṇḍanām ।
yauvanasthāmadhṛṣṭāṃ ca vāmabhāge vṛṣasya ca ।।

kāṃsyopadohasaṃyuktāṃ pūrvedyur adhivāsitām ।
nandāsunandāsurabhiśītalākhyapadānvitām ।।

catvāro dhenavaḥ sthāpyāḥ prāgādau tatra saṃmukham ।
suśaktivibhavopetā dugdhadohapradakṣamāḥ ।।

sagarbhāśca savatsāśca prasūtāśca sakṛt sakṛt ।
iṣṭadevam athoddiśya digbhāgān sāṃprataṃ tu vai ।।

hetinā ca tadīyena candanenātvacotsṛjet ।
vṛṣṇikṣetrasametaṃ ca tasya cāsaṃbhavāt tu vai ।।

ānuguṇyaṃ yathāśaktyā tanmūlyaṃ tu na kalpya ca ।
caturṇām agnihotrāṇāṃ bahiḥsthāḥ pratipādya ca ।।

vastrālaṃkaraṇopetaṃ mūlyaṃ ca surabhīyakam ।
vasudhāṃ vasudhārthaṃ vā vṛṣopakaraṇaṃ hi yat ।।

praṇipādya gurorbhaktyā vṛṣabhaṃ surabhiṃ tyajet ।
dakṣiṇe skandhadeśe ca hetinābhimatena ca ।।

lohenānalataptena mudraṇīyaṃ kṣaṇena ca ।
evaṃ kṛtvā vṛṣatyāgaṃ taduddeśena vai punaḥ ।।

prabhūtam annadānaṃ ca dadyāccaiva sadakṣiṇam ।
samantranātham uddiśya hyātmanor'the parasya vā ।।

vṛṣotsargaṃ hi yaḥ kuryād brahmalokaṃ vrajatyasau ।
vṛṣo hi bhagavān dharmo loke kāmārthabandhataḥ ।।

tena tyaktena saṃtyaktaṃ janmaduḥkhaṃ hi śāśvatam ।
prakṛtyā saha vai śaśvat surabhī savinaśvarā ।।

tad viśeṣācca tisro yāḥ śaktayo madanātmikāḥ ।
buddhir asmīti pūrvā ca pañcendriyam athāparā ।।

vinivartanti sarvāstā gotvamāśritya ye sthitāḥ ।
nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ vṛṣotsargeṇa vai saha ।।

uktam abjasamudbhūta idānīm avadhāraya ।
apavargapradaṃ divyaṃ sūcitaṃ yat punaḥ punaḥ ।।

pratiṣṭhāpanam abjākṣa ācyutaṃ bhuktimuktidam ।

iti śrī pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma ekacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha dvicatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

śrībhagavānuvāca 
dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu mantraiḥ sarveśvaraḥ purā ।।
ārādhyo bhagavān bhaktyā vedyāṃ vā kalaśe sthale ।
santarpyājyādikair bhaktyā mantraiḥ śrutimayaistataḥ ।।

bhagavān viśvakarmātmā sagaṇeśaṃ tu yājayet ।
vividhair upacāraistu puṣpadhūpānulepanaiḥ ।।

visarjane kṛte viṣṇau sānale kamalodbhava ।
śilpino yatra ye dakṣā mānyāsti tadanantaram ।।

yathāprasannabuddhyā tu śaśvannirvartayanti ca ।
tair api prayataiḥ snātaiḥ tarpaṇīyaḥ svakaḥ patiḥ ।।

tataḥ parigṛhītavyaṃ kṣetraṃ tvabhimataṃ dvija ।
abhuktam athavā bhuktaṃ vasudhāguṇalakṣitam ।।

niḥśalyam anukūlaṃ ca sthapatīnāṃ ca saṃmatam ।
samādāya pratiṣṭhārthaṃ yathābhimatavistṛtam ।।

mahendro apāṃpatirvāyurvirttapeśānadikṣu ca ।
padam āsādya vai kuryād divyād āyatanāśritam ।।

pañcāyatanapūrvaṃ tu śubhaṃ devagṛhaṃ mahat ।
siddhaye tatsvamārgāt tu vimārgāt tadasiddhaye ।।

etāvad arthanānmuktaṃ ato anyeṣāṃ tu doṣakṛt ।
svamārgaṃ paramārgaṃ vā yeṣāṃ sarvagato hariḥ ।।

sphuratyavirataṃ buddhau guruṃ taṃ śāstrataḥ svayam ।
śubhe anukūle nakṣatre namaskṛtyācyutaṃ vibhum ।।

nirvartya nityaṃ vighnena pūrvam arcāpayed dvija ।
saha ekāyanaiścānyai ṛgyajuḥ sāmapāṭhakaiḥ ।।

sāṃlaṃkāraiśva soṣṇīṣaiḥ sitāṃbaradharaistathā ।
samālabhanamālyaiśca bhūṣitaiḥ sāṅgulīyakaiḥ ।।

śaṅkhavāditranirghoṣair gītibhir māṅgalīyakaiḥ ।
phalapuṣpākṣatakaro jālasiddhārthakādikam ।।

samādāya śuciḥ kartā deśikena saha dvija ।
sthānam āsādya sarveṣāṃ vāsudevaṃ hṛdi smaran ।।

puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā ca gāyatrītritayādikam ।
uddhoṣya śākunaṃ sūktaṃ śivasaṃkalpameva ca ।।

śrīsūktena samopetaṃ bhadraśrīsāmam uttamam ।
karmārambheṇa saha vai svasti bho ityayaṃ paṭhet ।।

camaṣaṭkāṃstatodīrya śāntādyāstadanantaram ।
japannaṣṭākṣaraṃ tiṣṭhan kartāste deśikastataḥ ।।

bahiḥ kṣetrasya caiśānyāṃ prācyāṃ vā kamalodbhava ।
tatāṃ parṇakuṭīṃ kṛtvā vātavṛṣṭikṣamāṃ śubhām ।।

tatra puṣpārghyadhūpādyaṃ kṛtvā vai bhadrapīṭhagam ।
pañcagavyaṃ samāpādya sārdhaṃ mantrairvilakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

nārāyaṇam apāṃ mūrtiṃ hemādye kutape śubhe ।
sannidhīkṛtya saṃpūjya sarit tīrthāmbupūjite ।।

hemasarvauṣadhīratra darbhavargasraganvite ।
mantrāstrakalaśābhyāṃ tu saṃpādya racanāṃ tataḥ ।।

sādhāram āsanaṃ tābhyāṃ jñātvā kuryāt tadarcanam ।
hṛdi mantreśvaraṃ sāstraṃ pūjayitvā yathāvidhi ।।

nyastavyam āsane kaumbhe prāṇavanmanasā saha ।
saumyanāḍīpathā caiva tato hyastraṃ samantrarāṭ ।।

dakṣiṇena tu mārgeṇa tvapasavyaghaṭe vibhoḥ ।
avatārya jvaladrūpaṃ dahantaṃ vighnasaṃcayam ।।

mantratrayaṃ tu sāmānyaṃ sarvatra vihitaṃ dvija ।
ṣaḍaṣṭākṣaramantraṃ yat tathā vai dvādaśākṣaram ।।

hetīśaṃ yat sahasrāraṃ parijñeyaṃ tadāyudham ।
kṛtadīkṣeṇa yallabdhaṃ suprasannācca vai guroḥ ।।

astraṃ tadaṅgam āpādyaṃ saviśeṣam idaṃ śubham ।
sāṅgaṃ samarcayitvā tu bhogair mātrāvasānikaiḥ ।।

satsūktair yajubhiḥ sāmair yathāvasaralakṣaṇaiḥ ।
vyañjakair atha sarveśam atha homaṃ samācaret ।।

sahasraśatasaṃkhyaṃ yat pūrṇāntaiḥ sākṣataistilaiḥ ।
kuṇḍamantrāstradṛkpūtairevaṃ kuryāt tu deśikaḥ ।।

sthaleṣu vālukādyeṣu prāgādau viniveśya ca ।
catvāraścāturātmīyā mantrajñāḥ kṛtamaṇḍanāḥ ।।

ṛgvedādyāścatasro ye īśād vāyupathāvadhi ।
bhaktyā kriyāparā yājyā homārthaṃ kṣetrasaṃgrahe ।।

hotavyaṃ bhramiliṅgaistair mantrair ājyādikaṃ bahu ।
caturbhiścāturātmīyair dviṣaṭkārṇapurassaraiḥ ।।

hotavyam aparair vipraiḥ smaran sarveśvaraṃ harim ।
upadraṣṭā catuṣkoṇe ekaikaṃ viniyojya ca ।।

homārthaṃ sarvakuṇḍeṣu mantravinyastavigraham ।
śucayaḥ saṃyatā dakṣā vāstuśāstrakṛtaśramān ।।

viśvakarmakulodbhūtān āhūyāgre niveśya ca ।
pañcagavyādinābhyukṣya sitāmbaradharāṃstu vai ।।

mālyacandanasoṣṇīṣair bhūṣitāṅgulikādikān ।
saṃvīkṣya pāvanīkṛtya hyādāya ghaṭikānvitam ।।

kārpāsaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ sūtraṃ sahasrārābhimāntritam ।
sthapatīnāṃ kare dadyāt saha caikaśalākayā ।।

prokṣitān pañcagavyena sahasrārābhimantritān ।
vikīrya lājasaṃmiśrān bījān siddhārthakānvitān ।।

japannastraṃ sacakraṃ ca tridhā kuryāt pradakṣiṇam ।
prākpadāt tatpadaṃ yāvat saha ghaṇṭāravaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

kṣetramānam athādāya karair abhimataistataḥ ।
śiṣyadeśikakartṛsthair viśvakarmāṃśakaistu vā ।।

īśakoṇādi tatsūtraṃ caturdikṣu prasārya ca ।
śaṅkubhiryajñadārūtthair mudrayecca diśāṣṭakam ।।

tato bhūtabaliṃ dadyāt prādakṣiṇyena buddhimān ।
tilapiṣṭaṃ niśācūrṇaṃ salājadadhisaktukam ।।

bhūtakrūram iti proktaṃ tena bhūtabaliṃ haret ।
bhūtāni rākṣasā vāpi ye atraṃ tiṣṭhanti kecana ।।

te sarve adyāpagacchantu sthānaṃ kuryāmimaṃ hareḥ ।
śaravetralatācarmapuñjādyair grathitān drumān ।।

mṛdaṅgordhvasamākārān pāṇḍumṛdgrahaṇakṣamān ।
nacāṅgahomāsyustīkṣṇān kuddālākhyakhanitrakān ।।

sudṛḍhān yajñakāṣṭhotthān hastipādāṃśca pūjayet ।
kṣetrabrahmapade sthitvā yathābhimatadiṅmukhaḥ ।।

saṃsmṛtya dvādaśārṇena bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।
adhibhūtādhidevākhyaṃ smared adhyātmalakṣaṇam ।।

saptadvīpavatīṃ tatra samudrādisamanvitām ।
saptapātālasahitāṃ bhūtairyuktaṃ carādikaiḥ ।।

śaktibhiḥ śabdaniṣṭhābhiḥ sarvabhābhiḥ samāvṛtām ।
brahmabījasametena lakāreṇa sabindunā ।।

svasaṃjñānātiyuktena mānayitvā purā tataḥ ।
bhāvayitvādhibhūtatvam ādhidaivamataḥ smaret ।।

sāmarthyaṃ yad bhagavato viṣṇoḥ sarveśvarasya ca ।
param adhyātmarūpaṃ ca vārāhaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ mahat ।।

etāvad uktaṃ sāmānyaṃ dhyānaṃ kṣitiparigrahe ।
devālayavaśād anyad viśeṣaṃ cātra saṃsmaret ।।

caturaśre caturmūrtivyaktivyūhaṃ vicintya ca ।
caturaśrāyate dhyāyed divyaṃ vidyāgamaṃnvidam ।।

vṛttaśāntoditaṃ cakraṃ saṃvṛtāvayavaṃ smaret ।
anantaśayanaṃ devaṃ dhyāyed vṛttāyate gṛhe ।।

puryaṣṭakaṃ yad amalaṃ kālapuṣkaradehabhṛt ।
nābhirandhrodbhavaṃ viṣṇoḥ sthitam aṣṭadigātmanām ।।

devālaye dvijāṣṭāśre smartavyaṃ vasudhāgṛham ।
dhyātvaivaṃ dvādaśārṇena mantreṇa ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।

ṣaḍakṣareṇa saṃrodhya mudrāṃ baddhā dvijācyutam ।
adhidhyānasamādhānād yāvat kalaśasannidhim ।।

prāgvad vilakṣaṇair bhogair athāṣṭārṇena pūjayet ।
saha vipraiḥ svayaṃ dadyād agnau pūrṇāhutiṃ punaḥ ।।

sarvakarmasamādhyarthaṃ kṣetre kṣetrīkṛte sati ।
kuryāt pādapratiṣṭhāṃ vai suśubhe divase pare ।।

atha karmakarā dakṣā niyoktavyāḥ krameṇa tu ।
saṃtoṣya cānnapānādyaistoṣam āyānti vai ।।

śrībhagavānuvāca 

evaṃ parigṛhīte tu kṣmāṃśe śalyojjhite sati ।
ādhṛṣṭe sopalā bālā vasudhā vasubhūmidā ।।

śuddhiṃ sopekṣate kiñcit kṛtrimām udapāsara ? ।
yāvannopavanastāṃtu ? cirarūḍhair mahādrumaiḥ ।।

saṃkīrṇā tat prasūtaiśca mūlairvyāptā nirantaraiḥ ।
jñātaṃ tasyāpi bālatvaṃ śuddhirvai bhāvinī smṛtā ।।

tyaktā saritpravāhair na nagaragrāmadeśikāḥ ।
mahāntaṃ prekṣate śuddhiṃ bhaṅktvāśā bahuśo yataḥ ।।

svātvā vai bhāvam uddhṛtya dādyād abhyeti mṛcchubhām ।
sitāmaśarkarāṃ snigdhāṃ ।।

dṛṣṭvā jalaṃ samabhyarcya tarpayedyādasāṃpatim ।
nāganāthasamopetaṃ surasaṅghamatasthitam ।।

sthityartham upalaiḥ sarvaiḥ saha saṃpūryate mṛdā ।
mṛdopalaiśca saṃpūrya jātiṣu snigdhayā tayā ।।

ākoṭaya paunaḥ punyena bālād vai vāparisecanā ।
samīkṛtyopalipyātha gogaṇāṃstatra vāsayet ।।

bālavatsasametaṃ ca vṛṣendragaṇasaṃyutam ।
satoyāḥ śālayaścaiva prabhūtatṛṇasaṃcayam ।।

vikīrya satilaṃ tatra santyakte gomayādikaiḥ ।
apāsya gogaṇaṃ paścād upalipya punarmahīm ।।

samarcayitvā sūryātmā prāgvad diksiddhim ācaret ।
prāsādaṃ bhagavad rūpasametaṃ kamalodbhava ।।

yathābhimatadigvaktraṃ niścayīkṛtya vai purā ।
bhūbhāge sati vai kuryāt tadagre yāgamaṇḍapam ।।

diktraye tadalābhe tu saumyayāmyadigāyatam ।
ānuguṇyāya śuddhiṃ ca sukhaṃ nirbādhamiśritam ।।

śaraiḥ kāśaiḥ śaraiḥ kūrcair acchinnaṃ vā paraistu vā ।
sāntaraṃ vihitaṃ tatra pārthivaṃ pīṭhapañcakam ।।

saptaṣaṭpañcahastaṃ ca vibhavānuguṇaṃ tataḥ ।
caturhastaṃ tu vai sārdhaṃ caturhastam athāpi vā ।।

suvistṛtai ṣṣaḍaṃśena sarveṣāṃ parivarjya ca ।
antarālāni viprendra tad ucchrāyam athācaret ।।

caturviṃśatimāṃśena svena svena mahāmate ।
tad vistārocchrite sarve koṇastambheṣu bhūṣayet ।।

tanmānena samāropya stambhānāṃ śirasopari ।
racanāracitāścānye daṇḍāstiryakprasāritāḥ ।।

sarve sthūlābjasaṃbhūtāścaturdiktoraṇānvitāḥ ।
tṛtīyāṃśena vai pīṭhāt toraṇāvistṛtirbhavet ।।

suvistṛtaistribhāgena sarveṣāṃ unnatiḥ smṛtā ।
sacakragaruḍāḥ sarve tricatuḥpañcasaṃkhyayā ।।

sāntarālapramāṇena sastaṃbhāstoraṇākhilāḥ ।
viniveśyāḥ kṣitau kṛtvā sarve caiva sulakṣaṇāḥ ।।

caturaśrāstvatho deśā hyaṣṭāśrā madhyato dvija ।
vartulācordhvabhāgāśca samāṃśena vibhājitāḥ ।।

vīthī prākpaścimā bhāgā ubhayoḥ pīṭhasaṃmitā ।
sottaraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bhāgam ekaikaṃ pīṭhavartakam ।।

kṛtvaivaṃ bhagavad yāgamaṇḍapaṃ sarvakarmaṇā ।
udagdikpīṭhataścordhve dhiṣṇyaṃ kuryāt kajaṅkitam ।।

vartulaṃ caturaśraṃ vā prakāśākhyaṃ sulakṣaṇam ।
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaiścihnite mekhalāvanau ।।

dravyāṇām adhivāsārthaṃ tatsamīpasthitāṃ mahīm ।
madhyame maṇḍalaṃ pīṭhe mantrāstrakalaśārcanam ।।

catuṣkaṃ snānakuṃbhānāṃ soṣadhīnāṃ niveśane ।
anyatra śayanaṃ tasmin snānapīṭhe tu vinyaset ।।

snānakuṃbhasamīpaṃ tu snānadravyasamanvitam ।
pīṭhaṃ tatpañcamaṃ viddhi vālukābhiḥ supūjitam ।।

sadvāraṃ sagavākṣaṃ ca sakavāṭaṃ hi sārgalam ।
kṛtvaivaṃ adhivāsārthaṃ prākāravalayaṃ mahat ।।

prāsādakṣetramānaṃ ca santyajya paritaḥ sthitam ।
samekhalaṃ sapīṭhaṃ tat dikṣu kuṇḍāṣṭakaṃ likhet ।।

anukalpe tu vai kuryāt prācyāṃ diṅmaṇḍalādbahiḥ ।
tatpāścātye tu vā bhāge ekapīṭhāḥ satoraṇāḥ ।।

stambhā vā pṛthakpīṭhā viviktāśca parasparam ।
prāgbhāge cakrapadmākhyaṃ dakṣiṇe kevaleśvarī ।।

caturaśraṃ tu vā kalpyaṃ gadāmekhalam abjaja ।
padmād uttaradigbhāge śaṅkhaṃ koṇacatuṣṭaye ।।

eṣa pādapratiṣṭhāyāṃ kuṇḍānāṃ saṃsthitiḥ smṛtā ।
cāturātmyādidevānāṃ brahman sthāpanakarmaṇi ।।

saṃsthitiṃ śṛṇu kuṇḍānāṃ vividhā digvidikṣu ca ।
mahavibhavasaubhāgyaāyurārogyavṛddhaye ।।

siddhaye sarvakarmāṇāṃ vighnānāṃ vinivṛttaye ।
vyatyayācca phalaṃ viddhi muktaye samatānasau ।।

gadādvandvadvayopetaṃ prāgdikturyāśrameva ca ।
cakradakṣiṇadigvipra śaṅkhaṃ pratyaggate tataḥ ।।

padmam uttaradigbhāge yathābhimatapallavam ।
āgneyaṃ tu samāpādya kuṇḍam aśvatthapatravat ।।

vimuktakamalaṃ kuryāt trikoṇaṃ pūrvavartulam ।
homārthaṃ yātudikkuṇḍam aṣṭāśraṃ vāyave pade ।।

dhiṣṇyaṃ śrīvatsasaṃjñaṃ yat prāgvad ardhendulakṣaṇam ।
aiśānyāṃ tu samālikhya lakṣaṇenopalakṣitam ।।

ato aparaṃ saṃniveśam ekāgram avadhāraya ।
dhiṣṇyaṃ pūrvapade vṛttam āgneyyāṃ kaustubhākṛtim ।।

cakraṃ dakṣiṇadigbhāge śārṅgākāraṃ tu yātudik ।
āpyaṃ gadākṛtiṃ prāgvanamālākhyā vāyave pade ।।

udagdikkamalākāraṃ śrīvatsākāranīśagam ।
vistārasamamānaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vihitaṃ tu vai ।।

prāgvad dvādaśamāṃśaṃ tu oṣṭhārdhaṃ parimṛjya ca ।
susamaṃ mekhalābandhaṃ kuryāt tadvistṛteḥ samam ।।

samekhalā vai viṣamāḥ sarveṣāṃ pūrvavad dvija ।
yathoktalakṣaṇā kāryā yoniḥ pippalapatravat ।।

madhyadeśe suvṛttaṃ ca turyaṃ śrīvatsalakṣaṇam ।
prāsādakṣetrabhūmer vā tamevaiśapade bahiḥ ।।

saṃpādya mānayuktaṃ vā tarpaṇe sarvakarmaṇām ।
vāstvaṅgavibudhānāṃ ca lokeśānāṃ mahāmate ।।

vighneśadvārapālānāṃ kṣetreśasya tathā kṣiteḥ ।
saṃpādyam evam abjottha sakuṇḍaṃ yāgamandiram ।।

tato antarāt sabāhyaṃ ca ūrjanaṃ paribhūṣayet ।
suvicitrair dhvajai ramyairvaijayantīgaṇaiśca taiḥ ।।

procchritaiḥ kadalīrūpair drumāṅgaiḥ pāvanair dṛḍhaiḥ ।
savastraiḥ pūrṇasughaṭaiḥ puṣpairvai mañjarīgaṇaiḥ ।।

vitānaivividhākārair vinānalagṛhaṃ tu vai ।
saśarairbarhipakṣaistu sūtrairbhūtādhidaivataiḥ ।।

prāk prāptair lokanāthādyair dvāḥsthaiḥ kṣetralatāgṛhaiḥ ।
darpaṇaiścāmaraiścitrair ghaṇṭāvṛndaiḥ svarānvitaiḥ ।।

madhvājyadadhisakṣīrasupūrṇaiḥ kāṃsyabhājānaiḥ ।
upakuṃbhānanasthaiśca haritaiḥ pālikāgaṇaiḥ ।।

śālitaṇḍulapātraistu sahiraṇyaiḥ phalodvahaiḥ ।
lājasiddhārthakair bījabhājanaiḥ ṣaḍrasānvitaiḥ ।।

satsugandhaistvagelādyaiḥ pātraiḥ pūgaphalaistataḥ ।
madhūkabadarīlākṣāubhistriphalaiḥ phalaiḥ ।।

yathā tatprabhavaiḥ puṣpaiḥ bahubhiḥ prakarīyakaiḥ ।
ityevamādyair vividhair bhogapūgaistu pāvanaiḥ ।।

bhūmayaḥ pīṭhabāhyāstu sarvadikparivārya ca ।
saṃpraveśyākhilaṃ tatra saṃbhāraṃ bhūrisaṃbhṛtam ।।

śubhe grahe anukūle ca nakṣatre susthire tataḥ ।
lagne sthire sthirāṃśe ca pariśuddhe guṇānvite ।।

prāsādāṅghripratiṣṭhārthaṃ kartā vai bhagavanmayaḥ ।
kṛtāhniko dvijendrādyair deśikena samanvitaḥ ।।

bherīpaṭahavāditraśaṅkhaśabdādikaiḥ saha ।
ṛgyajuḥ sāmapūrvāṃśca praśastāḥ saṃpaṭhan śrutīḥ ।।

dvārapālārcanaṃ kṛtvā yāgāgāraṃ praviśya ca ।
saṃsmṛtya svāsane vyāptim arcayitvopaviśya ca ।।

madhyapīṭhasamīpe tu prāṅmukhaṃ paścime pade ।
prāgdikpratyaṅmukhaṃ yojyamṛṅmayāścāsaneṣu ca ।।

udagdakṣiṇadigyantraṃ yajurvedāṃstu yojayet ।
prāṅmukhaṃ paścime bhāge sāmajñānviniyojya ca ।।

saha caikāyanair viprair mūrtisaṃjñopalakṣitaiḥ ।
diguttarasyāṃ ca tato nityakarmaparāyaṇān ।।

niveśyātharvavedāṃśca sarve dvidvikasaṃkhyayā ।
pṛṣṭhataḥ susahāyādyaiḥ samyagjñānapratīkṣakaḥ ।।

upadeṣṭā ca mantrāṇāṃ dvijādīnāṃ samarcane ।
dakṣiṇe svātmanaḥ kuryād ekacitraṃ samāhitam ।।

tataḥ samācaret nyāsaṃ dvādaśākṣaramūrtinā ।
mantrābhimānaśaktiṃ vai samālambya dhiyā tataḥ ।।

athāṣṭākṣarapūrvaistu mantraiḥ śrutimayaistataḥ ।
prākproktavidhinā pādyaṃ bhṛṅgārakamalaṃ purā ।।

pādyārghyaiḥ pañcagavyaṃ ca kṛtvābhyarcya dvijātaye ।
samālaṃbhanapuṣpādyaiḥ savastrair aṅgulīyakaiḥ ।।

sapavitrakaistu hemāḍhyair dhūpayitvā yathākramam ।
prayataḥ sasahāyaśca sthapatiścopaveśayet ।।

dattvājñāṃyarjamānasya karmabhūmau sthitāni ca ।
suvarṇarājatotthāni navatāmramayāni vā ।।

śailajānyanukalpe tu mṛtkumbhānyathavābjaja ।
tatra madhyamakumbhaṃ yat caturviṃśāṅgulena ca ।।

vistṛte madhyatastacca dvyaṅguladvyaṅgulonnatam ।
vaktram aṅgulaṣaṭkena tatrāsyaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ smṛtam ।।

mekhaloparito jñeyā tryaṅgulā kamalodbhava ।
ye tu dikkamalānyevaitad ardhenonnataiḥ samāḥ ।।

phalaiśca vividhaiścaiva saha saṃpūrya vai mṛdā ।
ākoṭya khādiraiḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ prabalair ambusañcitāḥ ।।

pūraṇārtham aśeṣāt tu kṛtvā khātaṃ tu sādhakam ।
samīkṛtyopalipyātha prāgvad diksiddhim ācaret ।।

bhūṣayecca dhvajair anyair vaijayantīḥ samutkṣipet ।
śobhayet kadalīpūrvair drumāṅgaiḥ pāvanair dṛḍhaiḥ ।।

vastraiḥ pūrṇaghaṭaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kauśeyair mañjarīgaṇaiḥ ।
śubhe grahe anukūle tu nakṣatre śubhadarśane ।।

lagne sthire sthirāṃśe ca pariśuddhe guṇānvite ।
prāsādāṅghripratiṣṭhārthaṃ kartā vai bhagavanmayaḥ ।।

kṛtāhniko dvijendrādyair deśikena samanvitaḥ ।
bherīpaṭahavāditrasarvaśabdādikaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

vandivṛndasamopetair gīyamānaiśca maṅgalaiḥ ।
sāmaṛgyajupūrvāstu praśastāḥ pāṭhayecchrutīḥ ।।

sahasaṃbhṛtasaṃbhārakṣmākṛtaṃ kṣmāmalaṃ viśet ।
samācamya kṛtanyāso dvādaśākṣaramūrtinā ।।

athāṣṭākṣarapūrvaistu mantraiḥ śrutimayaiḥ saha ।
pādārghyapañcagavyaṃ tu kṛtvābhyarcya dvijottamam ।।

sthapatiścārghyapuṣpādyaiḥ pravarteta sukarmaṇi ।
oṃkārapūrvāṃ gāyatrīm ekaikaṃ pāṭhayed dvija ।।

gāyatrīsāmapūrvaṃ ca kanikrandam udīrya ca ।
evam oṅkārapūrvaṃ ca karmākarambham anantaram ।।

paṭhed ekāyanaṃ paścāt śivasaṃkalpam eva ca ।
ṛgvedajño yajurjño atha bhadronaṃ samudīryaṃ ca ।।

bhadraśrīsāma sāmajñaḥ śatādyau kṛtyadharmavit ।
vibhajya pūrvavat kṣetraṃ pavitrīkṛtya sāṃpratam ।।

pavitramantrair akhilair vaidikaiḥ pāñcarātrikaiḥ ।
kanyāṃ ca saumyadigbhāge aiśānyāṃ vālayāvane ।।

maṇḍalaṃ pārthive pīṭhe vinivartya catuḥ same ।
aśubhaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ vaśyāgāradvayānvitam ।।

bhadrapīṭhāsanasthaṃ ca sodakaṃ ca ghaṭadvayam ।
stragādyair bhūṣitaṃ kṛtvā ekasmin sādhanaṃ yajet ।।

dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ ।
śrutyuktair mantramukhyaistu tadastraparake ghaṭe ।।

mantrair hetīśaliṅgaistu caturvedasamutthitaiḥ ।
maṇḍapāgramathāsādya hārdam āpādyam arcanam ।।

avatārya bahiḥ kuryāt pūjanaṃ prāgyathoditam ।
pūrṇāhutiṃ vināgnau tu tarpayitvā yathāvidhi ।।

yajed vāstu narādyaṃ vai surasaṅghaṃ tadaṅgakam ।
śataṃ śatārdhaṃ pādaṃ vā āhutīnāṃ samāpayet ।।

tilānām ājyasiktānām ājyasya tadanantaram ।
sāmarair vāstuliṅgaistu mantrair devavratādikaiḥ ।।

susamaṃ kalaśānāṃ tu navakaṃ tvatha dhātujam ।
yathāśaktipramāṇaṃ tu nālpaṃ vai dvādaśāṅgulam ।।
