śailajaṃ mṛnmayotthaṃ vā supakvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ śumam ।
bhṛṅgāratulyam aṣṭāśraṃ śaṅkhākāraṃ tu vocchritam ।।

valihīnaṃ viraktāsyaṃ dravyāṇāṃ grahalakṣaṇam ।
śuddhyartham atha sarveṣāṃ snānakarma samācaret ।।

adhivāsyāmbaracchannān sadyo vānye ahani dvija ।
kramaśaḥ pūrayed dravyaistalliṅgaiḥ śrutisaṃpaṭhaiḥ ।।

gāyatryāṣṭākṣareṇaiva dvādaśākṣaravidyayā ।
suvarṇasikatābhistu ratnair muktāphalādikaiḥ ।।

dhātubhiścākhilair dhānyair athānyaiḥ pāratādikaiḥ ।
siddhārthakānvitair bījair dhānyair nīvārapūrvakaiḥ ।।

karpūramalayakṣodakuṅkumāgarumiśritaiḥ ।
paṭṭastrakcandanādyaistu bāhyataścopaśobhayet ।।

evaṃ saṃpūjya saṃskṛtya caturṇāṃ madhyato nyaset ।
padmāsanagatāṃ lakṣmīṃ nidhibhiḥ parivāritām ।।

caturṇām atha cānyeṣāṃ ratnarāṭ kaustubhābhidhaḥ ।
samantreṇa svanāmnā ca nidhināthaiḥ samanvitām ।।

bhagavān sarvaśaktyātmā ekasmin paricintayet ।
ṣaḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa niṣkalaṃ śabdavigraham ।।

brāhmaṃ catuṣpadaṃ kṣetraṃ nayed aṣṭacchadātmanā ।
nyasya sārveśvaraṃ kumbhaṃ madhyataḥ karṇikodare ।।

ratnakuṃbhacatuṣkaṃ tu dikcakreṣvaṣṭadikṣu ca ।
prādakṣivyena prāgbhāgān mantrān vā laukikān dvija ।।

lakṣyaṃ kumbhacatuṣkaṃ yad īśād vāyupadāvadhi ।
evaṃ nyastvā tataḥ kuryād arcanaṃ madhyagasya ca ।।

catuṣkaṃ hṛdayādyaṃ vai ratnakuṃbhagataṃ yajet ।
caturṇāṃ mantram ekaṃ tu śrīkumbhānāṃ tu pūjayet ।।

purato netramantraistu madhyakumbhe ca tasya ca ।
kṛtvaivaṃ niṣkalaṃ nyāsaṃ sarveṣāṃ sāṃprataṃ tataḥ ।।

vidhānanavakaṃ dadyāt tāmraṃ vā śailajaṃ samam ।
suvṛttaṃ caturaśraṃ vā sudhanaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam ।।

catuśśaktiniruddhaṃ ca tatra madhyagate dhaṭe ।
śaktirvā yā parā devī viśvasandhāraṇakṣamā ।।

prabhāsā vaiśvarī dikṣu jñānaśaktyāmṛtā ca sā ।
vidigghaṭasamūhe tu smared ānandalakṣaṇā ।।

kriyākhyā yācyutī śaktiḥ śuddhā śaktasya janmadā ।
nyastvaivam arcanaṃ kuryāt śriyādīnāṃ svasaṃjñayā ।।

nidhīnāṃ nidhināthānāṃ mantraṃ sāṅgaṃ yajet tataḥ ।
mudrāṃ pradarśayet māntrīṃ sarvasāmarthyalakṣaṇām ।।

dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa japtavyaṃ ca samācaret ।
sannirodhaṃ dviṣaṭkārṇe na sannidhim ।।

yajurjñaṃ tvatha sañcodya yujyateti ca yadyajuḥ ।
ṛcaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ sāmajño viṣṇusaṃhitām ।।

atharvāyeti ṣaṭpādya dvijam ekāyanaṃ tataḥ ।
ātmavyūhādikaṃ kuryāt saṃjñāmantracatuṣṭayam ।।

namaskārasamopetaṃ tataḥ sāma rathantaram ।
āhutvā harṣapūrvaṃ vai ṛnvedaṃ samudīrayet ।।

pratiṣṭhāsīti vai sāma sāmajño atha udīrayet ।
ato antaraṃ tu kumbhānāṃ ।।

āpādyam atha sarveṣāṃ sudhālepena caiva hi ।
digaṣṭakaṃ mudraṇīyaṃ kṣetraṃ śaktyaṣṭakena tu ।।

śilāntaḥ sannirodhena śilānāmasamāstu vā ।
kāryā ūrdhvasamāḥ sarvāḥ sarvatobhadralakṣaṇāḥ ।।

snānādyaiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ vāsastragvarṇabhūṣitā ।
ratnāṣṭakāsanasthā ca aṣṭānāṃ ca suvinyaset ।।

mantram akṣarabhedena praṇavādyantaṇaṃ tu vai ।
prāgādāvīśadiṅniṣṭham aṣṭakaṃ vyaktigaṃ nyaset ।।

praṇavena svanāmnā ca namo antena mahāmate ।
balavīryavatī nityā anantākhyā sthirā dhruvā ।।

sandhyākhyā dhṛtisaṃjñā ca sthitirnāmnā dvijāṣṭamī ।
vedādyantaṃ samuddhoṣya yajurvedavrataiḥ saha ।।

haye ca vidyā ṛksūktā brūyād ekāyanaṃ tataḥ ।
yadivāyo savetyādiva hutvaivaṃ kamalodbhava ।।

dattvā pūrṇāhutiṃ brūyāt mantram āśrāvikaṃ hi yat ।
kartā ca deśikendro atha saṃsmaran mantrasaṃhitām ।।

nyastaśriyādikair nāmamantraiḥ sarvaiḥ samanvitam ।
eṣāṃ buddhiḥ saptadheti mantram ekāyanaṃ paṭhan ।।

dadyād āhutikaṃ sarvaṃ karmaṇāṃ pūraṇāya ca ।
etāvad uktam abjākṣa mukhyakalpaṃ mayā ca te ।।

anukalpamato vakṣye sarveṣāṃ ca hitāvaham ।
etasmin kalaśe sarvam anyakṣetragaṇārcitam ।।

mantravyūhaṃ yathoktaṃ ca sthalagopalagaṃ nyaset ।
sarvaśaktimayīm ekāṃ śaktiṃ vai pārameśvarīm ।।

niveśya madhyatastasmin dadyāt kośaṃ sudhādikam ।
varṇakaiḥ kuṃkumādyaistu tatrordhve abjaṃ likhet tataḥ ।।

bhūbhāgaṃ khātaśeṣaṃ yat samantāt samatāṃ nayet ।
prāgvadākoṭṭanādyena sarvāṅgairipubhistataḥ ।।

pañcaraṅgeṇa sūtreṇa śaṅkubhir yājñikair dṛḍhaiḥ ।
astramantreṇa mantrajño jīmūtam atha saṃpaṭhet ।।

catuḥ strakcandanopetāṃ baliṃ vai sācca kāmikīm ।
dadyāt pūrvoditāṃ dikṣu samācamya praṇamya ca ।।

dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa tristhānasthaṃ ca mantrarāṭ ।
kṣāntvā tadopasaṃhṛtya prāgvadarcanapūrvakam ।।

sāṃsārīnāṃ bahiryāvad ācaret sthapatiṃ punaḥ ।
viśvakarmā puraskṛtya anyeṣāṃ piśitāśinām ।।

dadyād dvijendrapūrvāṇām aśanaṃ dakṣiṇādikam ।
anyeṣām arthinām annaṃ dhanadānaṃ svaśaktitaḥ ।।

nānādeśavaśāccaiva kuryād evaṃ gṛhāsanam ।
vibhāgena samāyuktam ālayaṃ vividhaṃ tathā ।।

dhvajāsanāvasānaṃ ca vibhajya svadhiyā tataḥ ।

iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ prāsādasya pādapratiṣṭhā nāma dvicatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha tricatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

śrībhagavānuvāca 

prāsādāvāsataḥ koṇe samārabhya yathāruci ।
prāṅkaṇaṃ sarvadikkṛtvā prākāraṃ parikalpayet ।।

grahikāsapratolīkaṃ kevalaṃ vāmarānvitam ।
prāsāde tu catudvāre caturmūrtir alaṃkṛte ।।

dvidvikaṃ tu pratolīnāṃ dikṣu prākāragaṃ hitam ।
catuṣkaṃ ? prāṣṭakaṃ kuryāt prāsādānāṃ mahāmate ।।

ekarūpaṃ hi vā nānālakṣaṇaṃ bhagavadvaśāt ।
yathābhimatamānaṃ ca prāsādābhāsamātrakam ।।

pakveṣṭhakāśmadārutthaṃ tatra koṇacatuṣṭaye ।
catuṣkaṃ vihitaṃ vipra aṣṭakaṃ kalpayed yadi ।।

parasparamukhaṃ kuryād dvāroddeśadvaye tataḥ ।
sāntaraṃ diktraye kuryāt prāsādānāṃ dvikaṃ dvikam ।।

sapīṭhād devamānācca dvārocchrāyam udāhṛtam ।
pramāṇenonnatānāṃ ca devānāṃ ca mahāmate ।।

nānāhṛsvapramāṇānāṃ pīṭhenonnatimānayet ।
vaitatyenonnatattvena lakṣaṇāniyamojjhitam ।।

dvāraṃ sukhapraveśaṃ ca saṃkaṭānāṃ guṇāvaham ।
kṛtāyāṃ śuddhavihitaṃ ṛkṣeṇānugataṃ tu vai ।।

vistārāyāmayoścaiva ādāyāṅgulasantatim ।
śubhāya ṛkṣalābhārthaṃ guṇayecca parasparam ।।

śodhayed vātha lābhārthaṃ muṣṭibhiścāṅgulisthitiḥ ।
ekatripañca vai sapta śeṣāḥ sarve śubhāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

dhvajaśārdūlavṛṣabhagajendrāḥ kramaśo hi te ।
evaṃ nakṣatralābhārthaṃ śobhayet tāṃ sthitiṃ punaḥ ।।

ādekāt saptaviṃśāntaṃ śeṣāntaṃ hṛṣṭam ācaret ।
varayed aṅgulaṃ caikaṃ pādayorvā prayatnataḥ ।।

nūnam aṅgularāśair vai śubhaṛkṣāya siddhaye ।
vicāryaivaṃ purā samyak kuryād bhūmisurālayam ।।

śayanāsana āsīnaḥ suparṇasthasya vā vibhoḥ ।
diktraye abhimate caiva evaṃ vā diktraye trayaḥ ।।

upaviṣṭaṃ tu yāmyāyāṃ paścime yā digutthitam ।
udagdigdakṣiṇadvāre prāsāde garuḍāsanam ।।

catuṣṭayaṃ caturṇāṃ tu koṇānāṃ yat prakīrtitam ।
tatrānale dignyastham udagdvāre tu prākcaram ।।

svabodhaparimāṇena sattvenābhimatena ca ।
kalāsaktā iyattākhyāḥ paricchedavaśāt smṛtam ।।

tam āsthāpanasaṃjñaṃ ca viśeṣaṃ kamalodbhava ।
saṃpanne brahmapāṣāṇasaṃskāre paiṭhike api ca ।।

udvartanābhyañjanena mṛdbhūtigomayādinā ।
śilpidoṣopaśamane snānamātre kṛte sati ।।

niṣpanne netradāne tu snāne saṃpādite pare ।
utthāpya mūrtipālaistu gurvādīn bahubhirbalāt ।।

niveśanena mantraṃ yad vividhaṃ sāṃprataṃ kṛtam ।
tritaye caikatāṃ prāpte vajralepena pauṣkara ।।

prokte lagnodaye mantranyāsam ācaraṇāt tu vai ।
yacchakter anusandhānāt tat sthitisthāpane tathā ।।

prāsādāntarabhittīnāṃ likhitaṃ vāmbarādike ।
sidhyarthaṃ sādhakendraistu siddhikālāvadhiṃ tu vai ।।

calabimbasya yanmantraṃ nyāsaṃ vai sāsanasya ca ।
nityam ārādhanārthaṃ tu karmārcāyām api dvija ।।

taṃ vipra calanākhyaṃ tu sthitisthāpanam eva ca ।
kṣmābhaṅgair jalapūrvaistu doṣairyā cātidūṣitā ।।

uddhṛtya yojanānyatra sthāne tu śubhalakṣaṇe ।
samyak saṃsthāpanād bhūyaḥ saṃsthāpanam udāhṛtam ।।

vidyutprapātapūrvaistu doṣairyā cābhidūṣitā ।
tadutthānakṛte śaśvannirdeṣe cāsane sthitim ।।

tatsamā lakṣaṇāḍhyā ca pratimānyā mahāmate ।
anyasmin vā neva pīṭhe bimba tpariyojitā ।।

boddhavyaṃ tad viśeṣaṃ ca sthāpanotthāpanaṃ tu vai ।
jñānasaṅghojjhitatvācca ekadiksamamīkṣaṇāt ।।

prādhānyenātha dikcakraṃ svagātrair iha vāsanāt ।
śayanāsanasaṃsthānacalācalavaśād api ।।

pratiṣṭhākhyaviśeṣāśca bahavaḥ sarvasiddhidāḥ ।
sāmānyasanniveśācca tad viśeṣaguṇāt tu vai ।।

sthitaṃ cākṣarayā śuddhyā sāmānyārccā phalārthinām ।
phalasāmyaṃ parijñeyaṃ kiṃ tvanyasmin hi janmani ।।

cāturātmyapratiṣṭhā ca jñānaṃ yacchati śāśvatam ।
yatprāpya na punarjanma punarevāpnuyānnaraḥ ।।

phalakāmastu yaḥ kuryāccaturmūrtiniveśanam ।
śraddhayā parayā bhaktyā saṃkalpād eva padmaja ।।

paitṛkaṃ mātṛkaṃ caiva jāyākhyaṃ saptasaṃkhyakam ।
kulam uddharate tasmin janmaprāptau kṣitau punaḥ ।।

dharmopetāṃ harer bhaktim āśraya ntyabjasaṃbhava ।
jātajanmā tṛtīyā tu ? prāpnuyāt sadvivekavat ।।

samuttarati vai yena ghorāt saṃsārasaṃkaṭāt ।
rūpam ādyapratiṣṭhāyā ityuktaṃ dvijasattama ।।

viśeṣasanniveśebhyastvidānīm avadhāraya ।
manīṣitaṃ phalaṃ bhuktvā divyeṣu bhuvaneṣu ca ।।

janmāsādya samutkṛṣṭam ācaret punareva hi ।
daivī brahmapratiṣṭhādyā yā parasmin hi janmani ।।

prāgvad yacchati vijñānaṃ parameśapadāptigam ।
etāvad uktaṃ vaiṣamyaṃ sati sāmyaṃ mahāmate ।।

yajñottamasya divyasya saphalasyābjasaṃbhava ।
acyutasyāvināśasya bhavakṣayakarasya ca ।।

bhedaṃ yad vastumātreṇa sthitaṃ tad avadhāraya ।
varṇā nāṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ gṛhāśramaratātmanām ।।

ādīkṣitānāṃ prāgvipra bhītānāṃ maraṇādike ।
vyavahārasthitānāṃ ca pratiṣṭhādyā mahāmate ।।

nirvarjitāḥ prayacchanti phalamuktaṃ hi yanmayā ।
nirvāṇadīkṣitānāṃ ca guruṇācyutavedinām ।।

bhaktyā prāptādhikārāṇāṃ nityaṃ ārādhanaṃ prati ।
samyaksamādhiniṣṭhānām iha janmaikaśeṣiṇām ।।

vikalpakṣīṇacittānāṃ pratiṣṭhā vihitābjaja ।
trāṇārthaṃ svakulādīnām anantānāṃ ca saṃbhavāt ।।

yāvajjīvāvadhiṃ kālaṃ teṣām āsthāpanaṃ tu vai ।
vihitaṃ paritoṣārthaṃ buddher buddhimatāṃ vara ।।

jñātvaivaṃ dharmalabdhena dhanena ca balena ca ।
ākṣipan grahaṇāt sarvaṃ dhvajāntaṃ vai samāpyaya ca ।।

viśvāvāsapadāvāsaṃ dakṣiṇānanam āsthitam ।
pīṭhastham upaviṣṭaṃ ca prāgdvāre nirṛte gṛhe ।।

evaṃ khageśapṛṣṭhasthaṃ vāyudiṅmandire hitam ।
divyabhogaphalāvāptiṃ saha diktalpagāt tu vai ।।

prajāpatitvam āpannā uktadigviniveśanāt ।
sthitiṃ triviṣṭapādīnām upariṣṭāt tu śāśvatīm ।।

vihāyasagatiṃ divyāṃ yānagāt prāpyate pumān ।
bhaktānāṃ phalalipsūnāṃ sthānasthalaphalādikam ।।

phaladiksaṃsthitāḥ sarve nagarāṇāṃ phalārthinām ।
utkṛṣṭajanmūparvaṃ tu janma cātmaprakāśakam ।।

tad viddhi bhavaśāntyartham acirād eva padmaja ।
yathoddiṣṭakrameṇaiva diktraye viniveśya ca ।।

nṛsiṃhakapilakroḍamūrtayo vā mahāmate ।
prāgvadvidikcatuṣkeṣu caturṇāṃ vihitaṃ kramāt ।।

vājivaktraṃ tu muktānāṃ siṃhādīnāṃ niveśanam ।
diktraye kacchapādīnāṃ kuryāt saṃsthāpanaṃ tu vā ।।

mīnavāmananāthānāṃ devānāṃ prākphalāptaye ।
vidikṣu viniyoktavyaṃ yathoddiṣṭakrameṇa tu ।।

trivitramakuṭhārāstrakaraṃ kāntāvapurdharam ।
sarvadevamayaṃ viśvarūpaṃ tu parameśvaram ।।

etāvad uktaniyamam ato anye ye akhilāstu vai ।
prādurbhāvāntarāścaiva prādurbhāvābjasaṃbhava ।।

gurūṇāṃ saṃmatenaiṣa yoktavyaṃ nānyayājakaiḥ ।
sadevāṃ hi kuṭīṃ ramyām āpādyābhimatāṃ tataḥ ।।

dvārāgre maṇḍapābhāsaṃ sopānapadavīyutam ।
vedīvibhūṣitaṃ kuryāt sthitam ārādhanāśrayam ।।

bhogānāṃ sthitaye anyeṣāṃ vātavṛṣṭikṣamaṃ śubham ।
prāsādāṅghripratiṣṭhārtham āpādyābjaja vai tataḥ ।।

pañcānāṃ vā navānāṃ ca ekasmin vā ghaṭodake ।
sarvaratnamayopete nyastaṃ yatparameśvaram ।।

āṅgaṃ salāñchanaṃ māntraṃ parivārasamanvitam ।
svaśaktikhacitaṃ caiva pratyahaṃ pūjayecca tam ।।

mantrabimbapratiṣṭhārthaṃ kālavighnopaśāntaye ।
anyathā jāyate vighnam anivāryaṃ mahāmate ।।

gacchanti sannidhiṃ mantrā nityaṃ traikālyam arcanāt ।
yacchantyanarcanācchokaṃ rodhitaṃ yatra yatra ca ।।

padāni prāṅkaṇe caiva devānāṃ viniveśane ।
uktāni padmasaṃbhūta idānīm avadhāraya ।।

madhyadeśe tu tadbhūmeḥ prāsāde abhimate tate ।
sanniveśavaśenaiva nānāsaṃjñāvasaṃsthitaḥ ।।

pīṭhabrahmavaśāsthānasta mba ? sya ? caturātmanaḥ ।
caturdigvīkṣamāṇasya yānusandhānalakṣaṇā ।।

boddhavyaṃ sā pratiṣṭhā ca digvyūhaparipūrakī ।
dhṛtiśaktisvarūpeṇa amūrtenātyayātmanā ।।

sthitaye prakriyārthaṃ ca brahmapāṣāṇatāmratā ।
sarvaṃ brahmaśilāniṣṭham ākṣiteḥ kamalodbhava ।।

vyāptamāmūlataścaiva tenāmūrtena vai punaḥ ।
dravyamūrtim amūrtāṃ ca gṛhītastamba ? lakṣaṇam ।।

ekasyācyutabījasya bhinneṣu prativastuṣu ।
saṃsthitā sthitir acchinnā sā pratiṣṭhita eva hi ।।

bhinnānāṃ vyūhamūrtīnāṃ kevalā khilasya ca ।
prādurbhāvasamūhasya vdyādikasya tu yad dvija ।।

ekasmin viśvapīṭhe tu sthitirekasya cecchayā ।
pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ viśeṣaṃ tat sthāpanaṃ samudāhṛtam ।।

cicchaktim anuviddhaṃ ca avyaktaṃ tattvasaṃgraham ।
dravyamūrtau calākhye ca nītam ekātmanā dhiyā ।।

bimbasaṃskārakāle tu adhivāsābhidhe dvija ।
acalatvena sanmantraṃ calabhāvanayā punaḥ ।।

sāṅgaṃ salāñchanaṃ caiva kṛtvā abhimataṃ tu vai ।
ārādhanārthaṃ hṛdayanyastaṃ taddhṛdaye punaḥ ।।

samāharet kṛtārthatvānnityaṃ kālāntareṇa vā ।
sadākhyam aparaṃ tattva ।।

nānāsaṃjñaṃ tathā nānāpramāṇaṃ tadvadeva hi ।
racanābhistathā nānāvividhābhistu rañjitam ।।

bahvībhirbhūmikābhistu citritābhir alaṃkṛtam ।
āpādabhūmeraṇḍāntam anurūpaṃ ca yattrayam ।।

uttarottarataḥ kuryād bhūrbhuvasvādikotthitaiḥ ।
sthāvarair jaṃgamaiḥ siddhair vividhair mañjarīgaṇaiḥ ।।

nagaindrair nāgarājaistu suśubhair nalinīvanaiḥ ।
murajaśṛṅkhalābaddhair divyair nānālatāgṛhaiḥ ।।

purujādyair jalodbhūtaiḥ prāṇijālaistathaiva hi ।
vanajair nagajaiścānyair mṛgarāṅgaṇapūrvakaiḥ ।।

vāraṇāḥ śabarāścaiva haṃsapadmasamāśritaiḥ ।
śaṅkhasvastikakahlārapūrvair anyaistu vārijaiḥ ।।

nandikaiḥ kesarai ramyaiḥ śatapatravad utthitaiḥ ।
sakiṅkiṇīkaiścamarairātapatrair dhvajādikaiḥ ।।

bhūmigābhūmigaiḥ sarvaiḥ samudraiḥ saritānvitaiḥ ।
navopakaraṇair devaiścandrārkajvalanādikaiḥ ।।

prādurbhāvāntarair dvivyaiḥ prādurbhāvasamanvitaiḥ ।
dvīpair dvīpāntaropetaiḥ pātālaistajja ? nānvitaiḥ ।।

maharjanastapaḥsatyalokanāthair mahāprabhaiḥ ।
dhyānamaunaparair brahman vahnidevayutair dvijaiḥ ।।

ityevam ādikaiścānyair jaṅghāstambhavatīḥ śubhāḥ ।
bhūṣayet kamalodbhūta sarvadiṅnāsikaiḥ saha ।।

garbhagṛhāmbaramadhyāt kuryāccakrāmbujāṅkitam ।
pitāmahādyair vibudhaiḥ siddhavidyādharaiḥ saha ।।

puṣpajapamālādharaiḥ prahvaiścāmarair vyajanoddhataiḥ ।
vanamālāgadāśaṅkhacakrapadmaśriyādikaiḥ ।।

khageśavedavedāṅgair akṣasūtrakarāṅkitaiḥ ।
āvāryāvarakatvena cakrapadmādbahiḥ sthitaiḥ ।।

antarbhittigaṇaṃ sarvadevadaityādikairgaṇaiḥ ।
nṛttagī paraiścānyair nāradādyairvibhūṣayet ।।

praṇavena svanāmnā ca natiniṣṭhena tatra vai ।
sannirodhya ca tanmantraṃ bhūlokaṃ pādamākṣiti ।।

evaṃ prāsādapīṭhe tu bhuvarlokaṃ yathāsthitam ।
jaṅghāyāṃ svargalokaṃ ca mahacchikharabhūmigam ।।

stambhaṃ ca talapaṃ caiva caraṇaṃ jaṅghameva ca ।
sthānaṃ sthūṇaṃ ca pādaṃ ca paryāyavacanāstvime ।।

janarlokaṃ ca tad vedyāṃtastapaḥsaṃjñaṃ ? ca daṇḍakam ।
satyasaṃjñaśca tallokaṃ tacchikhāyāṃ surālaye ।।

bhāvayecca parāṃ vyāptimeva vai sāptalaukikīm ।
bhuvanordhvamayīṃ vipra prāsāde abhimate tu vai ।।

anuviddhaṃ pādapādyair anyaisvattāsvarūpakaiḥ ।
parasparaṃ hi sarvatra vyāpakaiḥ paralakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

bhūrlokāṃśaṃ vinā brahmaṃstathānyair ujjhitaṃ hi tat ।
rajastamomahattvācca īṣat sattvaguṇāt tu vai ।।

sattvaikaguṇarūpāṇām anyeṣām ata eva hi ।
bhūrlokaṃ ca pṛthaksaṃsthaṃ padādyadhvagaṇasya ca ।।

kūrmabrahmātmasaṃjñāyāṃ śikhāyāṃ ca padatrayam ।
nyastavyaṃ jāgradādyaṃ yad ratnanyāse kṛte sati ।।

turyabrahmapadopetaṃ mantrādhvapratimāsane ।
tābhyāṃ taṃ pādato anyasya tattveyaṃ kamalodbhava ।।

ānābhemūrdhaparyantaṃ kalādhvaṃ bhāvayet tataḥ ।
tad brahmarandhrakamale mantrabrahmatalakṣitau ।।

karṇikāyāṃ paraṃ brahma sāmānyaṃ śāśvataṃ vibhum ।
dīkṣākāle yathoddiṣṭā mayā te adhvamayī sthitiḥ ।।

prāsādānāṃ tu sā siddhiḥ śikhāntānāṃ mahāmate ।
pratimānāṃ sapīṭhānāṃ sādhibhūtādilakṣaṇam ।।

tatrādhyātmaṃ hi bhagavān mūrtaṃ śāntaṃ mama ācyutam ।
sa eva hi virāḍātmā hyadhidaivatamavyayam ।।

adhibhūtaṃ dvijāvyaktaṃ sarvatattvamayaṃ hi tat ।
vidyākalādikaiścānyaiḥ parārthaira laiḥ saha ।।

sabīje vilaye yadvat susūkṣmādyair vyavasthitaḥ ।
tattvāḥ śabdādayaścaiva buddhiniṣṭhā mahāmate ।।

tadvatprāsādadehe tu te devādhiṣṭhite smṛtāḥ ।
sarvaśaktimaye vipra śuddhaṃ satsattvalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

yathopacād vihitaṃ mantraṃ sarveśvarād vibhoḥ ।
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ caiva sarvakartāram īśvaram ।।

mantramūrtestathā viddhi upacārāt tu tadgṛham ।
saṃskṛtasya tvato yatnāt sapīṭhasya yathāvidhi ।।

devavat sthāpanaṃ tasya vihitaṃ sattvajasya ca ।
sopānapadavī yuktā jagatī yā sulakṣaṇā ।।

prāsādasya ca pīṭhaṃ tat parijñeyaṃ yadātmakam ।
ekībhūtatvam āpannaṃ sudhālepaistu sāyasaiḥ ।।

pakveṣṭakāsametaiśca sthiramṛccopalaistathā ।
pramāṇalakṣaṇopetaṃ viśvavid racanānvitam ।।

rañjitaṃ rāgajālena phalaṃ yacchati śāśvatam ।
jīrṇatvācca kṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ svayaṃvyaktādibhirdvija ।।

ākāreṣvācyutīyeṣu vividheṣvarciteṣu ca ।
phalaṃ sahastraguṇitaṃ kartāpnoti mahāmate ।।

toyāśayeśayā vṛkṣā kṣetraṃ puṣkaramādiyat ।
paunaḥpunyena sadbhaktaiḥ kṛtaduṣkṛtaśāntaye ।।

anādyajñānasaṃsargāt kālahrāsavaśād api ।
naṣṭaṃ narendranāthā ye pālayantyarcanādikaiḥ ।।

dehānte yānti te svargaṃ rājyadoṣair anāvṛtāḥ ।
kālenetya punaḥ svargāt jñānam āsādya nirmalam ।।

yena sāṃsārikaṃ duḥkhaṃ duḥsahaṃ nāśameti ca ।
phalam etāvad uktaṃ hi devālayasamāpanāt ।।

savittānāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ nṛpāṇām api padmaja ।
sarvādhvabhāvanopetam āstāṃ tāvat surālayam ।।

bhuvanādhvamayīṃ vyāptim āpādayati kevalāt ।
anugrahecchayācāryo bhaktānāṃ saṃpradarśayet ।।

lakṣmyā lakṣaṇayuktasya sthapateraśaṭhasya ca ।
prāguktaṃ labhate kartā susaṃpūrṇaphalaṃ dvija ।।

prāsādānāmamantraṃ tu svayaṃ śilpikarāt tu vai ।
yatphalaṃ labhate kartā hemakṣmānnādikaṃ hi tat ।।

phalaṃ sarvasvadānād vā labhate vidhipūrvakāt ।
mṛdā dārviṣṭakādyaistu svalpaṃ vā madhyamaṃ mahat ।।

pramāṇalakṣaṇopetaṃ surākīrṇaṃ surālayam ।
yathoditair guṇair yuktaṃ grāmyaṃ vā kuṭisaṃjñitam ।।

digvidiksāntarād bāhyād yuktaṃ prasthāpitaiḥ paraiḥ ।
vibhavavyūhasaṃjñaistu prādurbhāvāntarāstu vā ।।

avanīcalanādyaistu doṣaiḥ saṃcālitaṃ yadi ।
dīrghakālavaśenāpi snātānāṃ dhanakarmaṇām ।।

kuryād yathāvad uddhāraṃ gurūṇāṃ saṃmatena tu ।
rājā vā tad amātyo anyaḥ sadbhaktaśca nṛpājñanayā ।।

vratārcanādikāryāṇāṃ labdhvānujñāṃ parāṃ vibhoḥ ।
anantaśayane dārbhe uttānasthaṃ smared vibhum ।।

dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa svargeśaṃ bhagavān hariḥ ।
ayutaṃ tvayutārdhaṃ ca śatam ardhādhikaṃ tu vā ।।

athānukūle nakṣatre nṛpasya nagarasya ca ।
śāntyarthaṃ jīvabhūtaṃ yanmantreśaguṇamūrtibhṛt ।।

traiguṇyaṃ yacchate hastam arcayitvā yathāvidhi ।
tarpayitvā ca dehānte samidbhirbahubhiḥ kramāt ।।

bhuvanādhvamayaṃ śaktirvyaktisaṅghaṃ yathoditam ।
tathā varṇādhvapadasaṅghaṃ sattābhūtaṃ hi pañcakam ।।

tarpayitvārcayitvā ca sādhibhūtādhikaṃ tu vai ।
bhūtaśaktigaṇaṃ tadvat susūkṣmam aparaṃ hi yat ।।

devapīṭhālayaṃ vipra ruddhaṃ kuryād yathākramam ।
udayārkasamaṃ jñātvā saṃjñāmantrapadaiḥ svakaiḥ ।।

praṇavādyair namo antaiśca vyaktisthaṃ punareva hi ।
prātimaṃ rakṣa bhagavan mantravṛndaṃ hi cādhvajam ।।

udumbarārdhamānasthaṃ digvidigbhūmikaṃ hi yat ।
buddhidharmasthitair darbhair vyāptāmā baimbalakṣaṇe ।।

samyak tadaparijñānād anusandhānam ācaret ।
tad utthāpanakāle tu kṛtanyāsastu sāṃpratam ।।

upoddharaṇaliṅgaiśca sāṣṭāṅgair vedikaistathā ।
ekaikam ātmasākṛtvā pūrakeṇārkabimbavat ।।

susaṃmate arcite kuṃbhe hemādyair mūrtike tu vā ।
nirodhyodakasaṃpūrṇe pūjayet pratyahaṃ tataḥ ।।

saṃpannotpattaye samyagavatārya yathoddhṛtāt ।
saṃskṛtasya pratiṣṭhānam ācartavyaṃ hi vai punaḥ ।।

nṛpendrarāṣṭrasthānānāṃ godvijānāṃ ca vṛddhaye ।
yatpadaprāptaye śaśvat sakhilasyākhilasya ca ।।

prāsādapratimānāṃ ca evam utthāpanaṃ dvija ।
gobhūhemādikānāṃ ca rāṣṭrasya sanṛpasya ca ।।

jāyate śubhaśāntyartham ihaloke paratra ca ।
ato anyathā mahān doṣo bhaved vai padmasaṃbhava ।।

prāsādagrāhikānāṃ ca bahiścābhyantare tu vā ।
bimbānāṃ cālyamānānāṃ mantrair aṣṭākṣarādikaiḥ ।।

prāgvannyastasvamantrāṇāṃ samāharaṇam ācaret ।
maṇinā sūryakāntena ādityād analaṃ yathā ।।

samāhṛteṣu mantreṣu cālyamāneṣu pauṣkara ।
bhaṅge karmavaśājjāte pratimāsu pramādataḥ ।।

prāktanenaiva pāpena prāyaścittaṃ caret tadā ।
cittaprasādajanakaṃ kīrtiśarmakaraṃ tu vai ।।

tatraikarātrapūrvaṃ tu trirātraṃ ṣaḍahantu vai ।
vrataṃ dvādaśarātraṃ ca svaśaktyā tu samācaret ।।

snānādihavanāntena karmaṇāvahitena ca ।
tilāni sahiraṇyāni dānaṃ sarajatāni ca ।।

śāntipūrvaṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ sājyakṣīrodanādikam ।
bhojanaṃ tu yathāśakti bahūnāṃ vai mahāmate ।।

sadānamevaṃ nirvartya vrataṃ vai deśikādijam ।
vased āśritya vai kṣetraṃ prasiddhaṃ siddhasevitam ।।

suprasiddhaṃ tu vā tīrtham ekāhaṃ vā dinatrayam ।
āvartayan mahāmantramasakṛd dvādaśākṣaram ।।

kālaṃ muhūrtasaṃjñaṃ yat pratisandhyātrayaṃ tu vai ।
pūrṇam āyatane kuryād divye vā siddhasaṃjñake ।।

sati vai bhaktisāmye tu prāyaścittam idaṃ smṛtam ।
sāmānyaṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ manasaḥ prakaṭe tu vai ।।

uttarottaram ādhikyaṃ japakarmaṇi vai smṛtam ।
śūdraviṭkṣatraviprāṇāṃ bhaktānāṃ nānyayājinām ।।

uktaṃ hyetat prakāśe tu atha yāvatprasannatām ।
tāvatkālaṃ japenmantraṃ bhakṣayet pāvanaṃ matam ।।

yāvatprasādam āyāti svabuddhir manasā saha ।
aprakāśe dviṣaṭkārṇaṃ mantram aṣṭākṣaraṃ hi yat ।।

ṣaḍakṣaraṃ dvijaśreṣṭha kramāt sandhyātrayaṃ tu vai ।
snānaṃ yathoditaṃ kuryājjaped antarjale sthitaḥ ।।

trimantrasahitāṃ śaktyā snānakāle tvananyadhīḥ ।
aṣṭārṇamuktasaṃkhyaṃ tu prātarmadhye dinakṣaye ।।

deśakālaṃ tu vai kuryāt pratisnānaṃ tu vai sakṛt ।
pañcāṅgam abhiṣekaṃ ca śeṣaṃ sandhyādvaye hitam ।।

jaghanāntamadhaḥkāyaṃ saṃprakṣālyāmṛtāmbhasā ।
adhovāsaḥ parityajya śubham ādāya cāmbaram ।।

dinatrayaṃ ca ṣaḍahamaṣṭāho dvādaśāhvikam ।
śūdrādīnāṃ dvijāntānāṃ hitaṃ cottaratottaram ।।

kramam etanmahābuddhe manasaḥ śuddhikāraṇam ।
phalenānugataṃ bhūyo vidhyantaram athocyate ।।

saṃkṣiptaṃ sarvasāmānyaṃ yathābhimatabhūmikam ।
caturhastadviṣaṭkāntaṃ kṣetraṃ kṣetra kam ।।

uttarottarapūrvābhyāṃ nyūnaṃ nyūnatarāvadhi ।
bhāgaistridaśaparyantair bhaktaiḥ pañcaśatādikaiḥ ।।

bhittayoṃ'śadvayenaiva pañcāṅgād antaraṃ tu hi ।
garbhaṃ sārdhatrayenāto bhittayor'dhadvayena ca ।।

viddhi ṣaṭkaramānasya bhūbhāgasya ca kalpanā ।
aṣṭamāṃśojjhitair bhāgair garbhaṃ saptapadaṃ tu vai ।।

parijñeyaṃ caturbhirvai tacchiṣṭair bhittayoṃ'śakaiḥ ।
caturbhir aṣṭabhāgaistu sārdhair aṣṭakarāgraham ।।

bhāgatrayena sārdhena bhittivyūhaṃ samāpayet ।
sāṅgaṃ pañcakaraṃ garbhakṣetraṃ navapadāt tu vai ।।

śeṣeṇa karasaṅghena bhittayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
ṣaṭkaraṃ daśahastasya garbhakṣetrasya vistṛtam ।।

karadvidvitayenaiva bhittisaṅghaṃ vidhīyate ।
ekādaśakarakṣetrāt garbhaṃ sārdhaṃ ca ṣaṭkaram ।।

sārdhaṃ catuḥkaraṃ caiva bhittimānam udāhṛtam ।
kṣetradvādaśabhāgāt tu pādonaṃ samasaptakam ।।

devālayaṃ parijñeyaṃ pādonaikaṃ catuṣkaraiḥ ।
vidheyā bhittayaścaiva vibhajyaivaṃ tameva hi ।।

kṛtvā trayodaśāṃśaistu phaladībhittayoṃ'śakaiḥ ।
navāṃśe vabhabhiḥ pūrṇe vidheyaṃ bhagavad gṛham ।।

śubhāpacaya siddhim āpādya vdyaṅgulenāṅgulena vā ।
eṣāṃ prasādagarbhāṃśabhittibhyāṃ pātayenmanaḥ ।।

mānādhikaṃ vinikṣepya kṣetrāṇāṃ ca nipātayet ।
paramāṇusamaṃ mānaṃ kiṃ punaścāṅgulādikam ।।

matā vṛddhikarī nṝṇāṃ vṛddhipātam aśobhanam ।
samānīyaṃ hi yatnena mahatā tacca pauṣkara ।।

racanābhirūpetaṃ ca vihitaṃ ca caturmukham ।
cāturātmyavyapekṣāyāmekadvārathā ।।

yathābhimatadigvaktraṃ nānāsiddhiphalāptaye ।
cirāyuṣārthī prāgvaktraṃ yaśor'thī dakṣiṇāmukham ।।

kuryāt pratyaṅmukhaṃ caiva vṛttyarthaṃ ca svatantrake ।
udaṅmukhaṃ ca prāsādaṃ dhanadhānyaṃ prayacchati ।।

etāvat uktaṃ hi phalamaihalaukikam uttamam ।
nānābhogasamopetaṃ sarvāsāṃ viddhi pauṣkara ।।

svakṣetre vitate ramye svatantraṃ svāṅkanakṣitau ।
saha pūrvapratiṣṭhāyām athavāyatane hareḥ ।।

svāyambhuve vā siddhākhye mukhyakalpam idaṃ smṛtam ।
anukalpamato anyatra boddhavyaṃ vibudhāṅkaṇe ।।

prākprāsādadhvajacchāyāviniyukte tate pade ।
iṣṭakāṃ ca sudhācūrṇaṃ doṣaiśca pariśodhite ।।

tadantare pratiṣṭhāpya homādyuktaṃ hi sonnatam ।
prāsādadvāramānaistu sapīṭhaṃ viśvam ācyutam ।।

saṃpūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaiḥ sarvairārṇavāntarakīrtaye ।
ṣyātītasya vaṃśasya svakasyoddharaṇāya ca ।।

yadaivaitatkṛtā buddhiḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ pādayāmyaham ।
tatkṣaṇād eva tatkīrtiḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ labhate acyutām ।।

bhūlokādyakhilānāṃ ca sthānānām api kiṃ punaḥ ।
vibhavena jagadyoneḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ yaḥ samācaret ।।

pitrāsū nāṃ gatāsūnām anyeṣāṃ vā karoti yaḥ ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ ca pratiṣṭhānaṃ svaśaktyā vibhavena vā ।।

acirādeva te yānti śaśvadevāntakāspadam ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ ca paraṃ sthānaṃ tataḥ kālāntareṇa tu ।।

kṣityaṃśaṃ śubham āsādya kulaśīlādikaiḥ saha ।
ācaranti śubhaṃ yena prāpnuvanti punarbhavam ।।

kṛpayānantu pratiṣṭhāṃ yaḥ samācaret ।
jātīnāmathavānyeṣāṃ tadutthaṃ ca phalaṃ ।।

praviśanti ca mantreśāḥ praṇavadhvanisādhitāḥ ।
karṣayanti vibhūtiṃ svāṃ kiñcitkālāntareṇa tu ।।

kṛtā vai dhvastadoṣāśca nirvighnam amalāṃ punaḥ ।
niveśitāḥ susiddhādyaistīrthaiḥ kṣetrāvaneṣu ca ।।

nivārayanti ye mohād vibhavavyūhamūrtiṣu ।
saṃsthānamānam ākāraṃ na doṣaṃ kālāntarotthitam ।।

smartavyā vāsudevādyā dvibhedāḥ pārameśvarāḥ ।
catvāraścāniruddhāntāścaturvyūhavyavasthayā ।।

evamanye va rāhādyāścaturvyūhena vai saha ।
tathaiva keśavādyā ye anyenānyatareṇa vā ।।

mandamandatarād bhāvavaśād amarapūjita ।
evaṃ yad adhikāreṇa kuryād ārādhanaṃ hi yaḥ ।।

bhogair yathoditaiḥ śuddhaiḥ kriyābhirvividhaistataḥ ।
niṣpattau tu kriyāṅgānāṃ hṛdāstrārghyaṃ samantrarāṭ ।।

nānarcitaṃ vibhorbhogaṃ kalpitaṃ vinivedya ca ।
praṇavādyantagenaiva ।।
